multyplied chyldren grewe encresid tytan eldest sone ffoul euyl fauourid counterfet saturne merueylleusly fayr amyable whiche cause vesca moder louyd moche better saturne tytan nature ffor naturelly moders loue better fayr chyldern fowle wherfore saturne norisshyd lappe moder tytan put maner bannysshid whan saturne grete beaute cunnyng scyens vertues gate hooll loue peple thys tyme hyt whatsomeuer man practyqued fond ony thynges prouffytable comyn w lehe recomanded solempnly called named god theyr folyssh derke custome saturne named god ffor hys yougth hys cunnyng fyrst ffyndar gyue instruccion ecryng labouryng erthe sowyng repyng cornes thys inuencion applyed saturne wyth dyuyn reuerence wyth loue vpon loue onely anenst vesca vranus hys kynnesmen aboue mesure ayenst peple crete march contrees lyyng ther abowte thus hys name aroos renomed place men chyldren noble vyllaynes cam scole lerne dayes tht saturne began thus floure xx yere age broder xl vranus fader sekenes dyed detid world leuyng wyf vesca endowed largely possession deth noyous soroufull vesca wife whyche causid wepe mesur sone doughtirs also dide obsequye reuerently habondyng grete bittir sorow obsequye doon ther wepyng sorow yet vesca saw tytan eldest sone pretended haue enioye succession ffader day callid der sone saturne wyth tytan contre reherced said vnto yong sone saturne sholde succede haue herytages husbond tytan heryng wyll hys moder redoublid hys sorow causid hym wepe grete plente teeris knelyd fore moder humbly sayd thys wyse moder ryght infortunate whan ye wyll right patrymonye put naturelli ought haue ryght shold gyuen fro yat tht well formed membres broder satorne y whiche sorow passyng noyous ye wil putte ffortune burthe whiche ye may lawfull reson first sone ye haue norysshid wyth substace blood chyld born bely ix monethes also first dwellid enhabited femynyn chambres none fore toke ony seasyng whan toke tho ye gaf due loue sortyd succession herytages whens cometh thys ye subuerte destroye nature hath one ioyned gyuen euery moder bounden hold conseruacion ryght chyld ala moder ye wil make bastard fro ryght bastard vranus fader ye glad fore tyme ye felte fyrst conceyued lawful bede fader husbond ye bare gaf souke brestes oft tymes kyst saye tendre dayes tyme membres softe tendre ha moder acquyte yow ayenst ye beholden bounden ryght knowleche ye tht tytan moche lasse well adressyd broder saturne moche ye ought desire mocion furdering whan dame vesca herd sone tytan speke sadly perfoudely pyte hym yet pyte hye vertu myght surmouut grete loue roted bytwene saturne sayd tytan sone tytan sone forsake tht thou tokest thy substance bytwene side wer brought thys world knowe veryly loue entierly desire thy wele hyt clere euydent euery mannes sight deffault lothlynes abhomynacion thy membres thou art man sufficyent deffende thy fadres herytages grete labour payne ffor yf hit happend ony man wold make warre thou able resiste hym woldest thou shold thy broder hath loue peple beaute hys vertucuse manicres euery man holdeth hym reuerence derision skorne thou contente thou shall lakke thyng yf thou lakke speke shall remedye hit speke neuer heritage ffor saturne shall obteyne fauour hys wysedom mekenes benyngnyte also cause comyn wy iuggeth hym seeth tht shall one man hys lyf shall shyne gloriousli tytan sore troublid wordes hys moder began chaunge colour wex reed hauyng suspecion saturne contryued mater agaynst hym wherupon drewe hym apart hym sayd saturne thenuye thou hast regne aboue hath engendryd hert thy mortal myschief wherof hate shall endure vnto mortal separacion thy lyf myn child thou knowest wel tht eldest sone fader vranus hou art thou hardy psumptuo tenhause thi selfe aboue conspyred ymaginacion wyl thou knowe verily lyke thou hast conspired temporel domage semblably shal conspire thy eternal domage hurt name hen forth thy mortal enemye whan saturne herd brennyng enflamed menasses hys broder tytan excusid hym selfe answerd neuer thought lyf come succession ther fader ner neuer ymagyned ner conspyred hit vesca ther moder cybelle cere toke wordes fro saturne said tytan thretenyng saturne nought ffor shold regne lord maistre tytan full ffelony angry fore sayd playnly tht shold suffre hyt saturne grete parte peple assysted hym gaf hym fauour tytan also hys syde whiche began murmure oon partie agaynst alle companye sore troubled began threste enployed sece noyse acorde tytan notwythstandyng yf hit hard doo alwey wold haue ronne vpon saturne yf hold etted allewey ende wyse men shewed tytan grete reson feble saturne fauour peple wold modere hym self lytill sayd shold agree graunte regne saturne condycion yf maryed shold bounden putte deth alle hys child male shold begoten hys ed yf ony ffor wele bothe partyes vesca wyth doughters auncyent wyse peple accorded tytan thys condycion laboured saturne brought temple theyr god mar cyte oson wherof lord myghty man callyd mellyseus fore ymage god mar saturne swore tht yf hym happid marye ony chyldern male shold slee hem alle thus tytan content hys broder shold enioye lond crete pee maad betwene hem boothe phow saturne crowned first kyng crete fond first diuerce science wher fore peple held hym grete honour god trayttye maad pee tytan saturne tytan syhe hym selfe tht myght worshipfully abide dwelle beyng vnder yonger broder leuer goo serche auentures place thral yonger brother toke wif child frendes departid alauenture dyuerce place wher fond ffortune good happy tht armes strenght made hym selfe kyng many diuerse royalmes whiche departid vnto child commysed ordeyned certayn espies espye wayte yf broder saturne maried hym selfe yf wife broght forth men child whether put hem deth duryng sayd thingis saturne dwellid wyth moder susters cibelle cere began regne wyth grete magnificence contre seeyng neyghbours dide make ordeygne kynges regne suche noble vertuous assemb id gider day maad saturne kyng vpon vpon theyr synes crowned hym wyth grete glorie crowne lawrer wyth grete ioye saturne anon toke acceptid rial honour worship toke ceptre hand bare crowne heed regned meurely indusyng peple lyue honestly loue vertu naked swerd born afore hym sygne iustyce dyde iustyce malfacteurs enhaunsed good dyde bylde cyte whiche named crete yle bare said name fyrst enhabiteur dwellar whan founded cyte ordeyned palais dwellyng place myddel example hert myddes body mynystre membres wold ensigne mynystre peple chose honderd foure wyse men whiche institued ordeyned counceillours gouernours royame crete seeyng right grete wysedom kyng assemblid gyder dyuerce tymes named hym god yet founded vnto hym temple awter ydole beryng oon hand ziekle signyfiance destroyed vice suche wyse ziekle cuttyth herbes destroieth wedes hand held serpent tht bote tayll moche saturne said euery man shold byte tayle serpent saye euery man shold ffere flee euyll ende ffor ende oftymes venymous tayle serpent apperyth yet dayly ende many euyll dysposed enuenymed men moyen thynges renomee kyng saturne grewe worlde tyme gold saye hyt moche better haboundant dayes mannes lyf plente frutes erthe ony tyme poetes thys colour compared world tyme gold whiche moste precyous alle metal well dyuerce men saye saturne fyrst man fonde maner melte metall affine gold made hys vessell vtensilles hows dyuerce metall vnder thys colour figured tyme worldes ben gold began men doctryne saturne vse gold myne roches persshe montaigne perillo haunt thorny desertes fyght adaunte orguyllous serpentes fiers dragon dedely griffon monstrowous bestes sprede brood theyr wordly engyns excersites saturne fourbesshour begynner style lerne men take bestes fyrste fonde maner shotyng drawyng bowe gold maad saturne hys hows chambres halle shyne meruayllous werkynge stronge hardy feer ne doubte serpent montaigne ner monstre desert ner beste dwellyng caues knewe vaynes gold erthe coude decerne vaynes syluer edefyed ryche thynges gold ioyous vnto eye syght hoot courageous herte ffor tyme courage pardurable fyre chauffing affeccions man maner contagious heet syngulerly alleway coueyted desyred accomplissh tyme golden world creature lyuyd endured gretly longe alle world laboured edyficacyon scyence connyng vertue tyme men vertuous bodyly edyfyeng euer syn amonge alle saturne neuer ydle one laboured cornes erynge sawyng malte fyned gold metalles enduced taughte hys men drawe bowe shote hym self fonde fyrste bowe manyer goo saylle see rowe lytyll bootes ryuage toke owen playsir endoctryne teche hys peple alle thynges grete abondance wordly goodes reseruyd onely dorste marye sworne putte deth alle men child shold come hys seed wherof oftyme anoyed hadd grete displaysir etc phow saturne wente delphos hadd answer shold haue sone shold chace hym oute royame maryed hym hys suster cybell etc whan saturne sawe hys palays flo ysshe shyne gold sawe peple obeye hym sawe hys goldsmythes werkers breke montaigne pikois instrument sawe maryners cutte wawes see wyth theyr oores sawe hys dyscyples lerne laboure erthe sawe hys archer shote wyth arowes smote toke byrdes dwellyng hye tree fleyng ayer myght enbrace grete glorye enhaunse hye hys trone hys felicyte syde whan remembryd trayte made betwene hym broder tytan lyke vnto pecok proud fayr fethers diuersly fair colourd wiche spreded roound whele wyth loke hys foot leseth ioye saturne like wise traittye lost alle ioye glorye hys plaisance long tyme ledyng lyf ioyous sorowfull growyng alwey encresyng royame daily thought poysed hym selfe yf myght marye ffor thyng world wold false hys oth iust trewe dede word neuertheles nature meuyd hym cyted hym haue generacion come compaignye woman meuyng tymes refresshid renewed contynuel syght dayly passyng fayr mayde tht wete suster cibelle whiche saw continuelly deffaulte alle goodes nature apperteyning woman owt mesure ryght humble spekyng wyse werkes honeste conuersacion flowryng alle vertuys fo cause saturne behelde oftymes happend tyme beheld affaire werkes caste eyen vertues plesid hym gretli end desirous loue wherof moder vesca grete ioye pleasir ceyuyng desyr saturne gaf hym courage wyll marye hym laboured solicyted mariage effectuelli tht wyth grete worshyp triumphe saturne spousid wedded cibelle suster vsage first quene crete liyng wyth payengin wyse dew dette maryage thende ix monthes cybell sone whiche saturne dyde put deth acquytyng hym self oth maad vnto hys broder tytan thys sone bochace maketh mencyon laye gyder agayn cybell conceyued seed saturne another sone doughter space tyme apperyd grete moders bely thys tyme whan lawe nature vygour strength men maryed wyth susters especyal paynems yf content souffisance oon wyf myght take moo wyth reproche whan saturne knewe hys wyf wyth chyld second tyme deth hys fyrst sone cam fore hym sayd hym self wold hys wyf ben barayne tho began ful dyuerce fantasy sorowfull thoghtes desyred knowe shold befalle fruyt wombe cybell wente hym self forth yle delphos vnto oracle god appollo gaf answer peple demaunded thynges shold falle happene whan hys sacrefyce maad prayer preste temple put hym cloos vnder awter forsayd ydole herd grete whirlyng wynd troublyd hym wytte vnderstandyng maner spasme swowne whiche fill groud tht whan aros hym thought god appollo apperid vnto hym wyth dredfull face said thus hym saturne meueth knowe thyn euyll destyne thou hast engendrid sone shal take diademe crete shall banysshe thy royame shall pere aboue alle peple fortunat man euer borne grece aftir wordes saturne cam agayn hymselfe remembrid hym euyll prophecye touched botom hys herte sore anoyed right pensyf wente oracle wyth troublid herte al bare gladnes al oppressyd enuironed wyth wanhope cam folk departid then went ship whan ship henge doun heed whiche held vp tyl cam crete whan hys heed enclined began thynk pensif many right sorowful syghes engendrid roote malencolie said wise hela saturne pour kyng auayleth dignyte first kyng crete wat prouffyten dyuyne reuerences ner good science whan fele puttyng back fortune fortune sone torning fraile varyable ployng euery wynd lyke rosier leste areste whele tht torneth wyth oute end may speke saturne inuentor ffynder comyn wele thu wilte lene thi clere lawhyng visage leste leue thy large eeres thou hast gyue triumphe glorie corowne thou suffrest falle fro grete shyp goddes wytnes hit thou hast consentyd prosyte conspyrest mendycite fall shamefull end entendest shall named vnhappy saturne yf lyf hath ben nouryshyd happynes end vnhappy wofull shall callid said vnhappy happy fortune ewres shall torne reproche shame preysyng ony worshyp ffortune thyng haue offended haue foughten agayn haue doon ony folye agayn magnyfycence goddes haue rebellyd offended ayres worldes heuenes planet sonne mone erthe see haue trespast telle god art thou hast thou enuye cause haue ben thoracle forsayd god appollo hath shewyd vnto ruyne ceptre ffroussyng brekyng dyademe troublyng clernes regne enhaunsyng chyld puttyng royame shall cede insurreccion ala remede grete sorow tht haue haue slayn oon soones fore haue grete bitter sorow haue concluded self neuer wole cruelly spyll lyf chyldren dye wyth hem thys conclusyon muste verray force sore agaynst retorne contynue fyrst vnnaturell cruelte ffor yf sone wombe wyf suffryd lyue shall exyle put royame doun trone whiche shal ryght hard peysant bere suffre pacyently therfore hyt better sle hym ala yf sle hym hit semeth shold resiste wylle goddes whiche perauenture reyse hym agayn shold worse shold callyd homycide manslear vnnaturel murderer geant strange man nother land right litil child yssued propre vaynes bone fflessh prenosticacion goddes p electe chossen grettest lord grece souerani kynges tyme saturne thus felyng hym grete sorow trowble alwey wors wors fore sayd began chaunge colowr wex pale ful malencoli fantasy cowde appese vnfortune moste preuy men famylier wyth hym durst approche vnto hym seyng sorowful maner disconfort desolacion sorowful sorow angry wyth anger short tyme greth turbed inpressed wyth eygre inpression sorow face lyke vnto asshen ded alwey many thoughtis opend mouth spake softly sle self malencolye aman gretely abused haue mad oth vnto broder tytan tht shall put child male deth shall come fflessh parauenture goddes wole suffre shal sworn haue late haue knowleche god appollo tht wyf hath conceyued sone shall put royame end shold slee hym ffor moche concluded self haue broken myn oth haue spared lyues chyldren ffor moche hyt shall lenger spare yf hit happen sone borne lyue certayn shall put deth ffor hit better dye chyld shold wexe man wex rebelle ayenst enhaunse hym self abone hys malyce insurreccion wyse im wille sorowful saturne retourned hous contynuyng thys estate sorowfull syghes melancolyous fantasy wyse cybell durst come psence coude gete hym ioyous syght wherfore gate hym surname sorowe named saturne tryste sorowfull hit whan hous certayn space sawe day approche wyf shold delyuerid chylde ffor execute hys sorowfull courage callyd hys wyf said dame hit apparaut shortly thou shalt delyueryd ffruyt thy wombe yf thou delyuerid sone comaunde vpon payne deth thou slee hym thou sende herte whan cibell hard wordes rigorous innaturell volente anon ffill ground swoune ffor legges fayled releuyng swoun kneled fore foot saturne saide thys wise syre haste thou shame husbond woman murdryng owen child requyre mercy grace besechyng haue regard thy wyf haue hert woman tyraunt murderar dame answerd saturne requyre thyng towchyng thys mater hit iuggid forseen counterpeysed sentence tht yf thu haue sone shall ded ffor haue promysid sworn broder tytan aboue thys haue answer god appollo thy wombe sone shall caste royame therfore e birth ded dere thou louest thi lyf also haue said send herte medled wyth wyn may drynke hit syre answerd cibelle knowest thou woman propre synguler inclinacion haue verray loue smale chyldren must gyue hem ete souke wenest thou haue herte diuerce foylle handes wyth blood sone pray requyre reroque thy sentence pietous thy wyfe generacion thou art wyse iugement thy peple partye thou shewyst thy selfe good ffor thy oth thou art bounden ner holden sle thy sone hou wel hit trouth alle othes maad agayn good maners ought holden ffor slee thy sone hyt vilayn caas contrarye honour reson pyte equyte iustyce hit synne ageynst nature ageynst vertu ageynst good maners thy oth sle thy sone noght thou oughtest anulle hyt thou art kyng vpon payne deth defendest thy peple make murdre homycyde thys thou art myrour example oughtest content appease thy selfe semeth side thou interpretest construest euyll sentence god appollo sayng tht haue wombe sone shall put thy kyngdome ffor hit ought vnderstande sone bere shall ouerlyue put thy kyngdome saye thy sepulture day thou shalt departe world yf may appese yf hit happen haue sone thou mayste hym kept strong towr sette suche warde vpon hym shall neuer power enhaunse hym self agayn saturne tho herte passyng grete semblable compassion vesca moder cybell cere wepte gaf grete plente teres like wyse assistentes place wepte mesure haboudantly yet neuertheles hit myght softe attempre hard comaundement kyng saturne conclusion said cibell shold procure respyt tthe lyf sone shold ded also hym yf dide comandement sorowful conclusion cibell detid then traunse half ded castyng abrood armes handes wyth grete excesse teres ran lyke ryuer tendre eyen entrid tour moder desolate lady folowed sshe beyng chambre forfrusshid distemperid sorowe began trauayle anon delyuerid doughter sone doughter born fore sone sente cere born norysshe cyte perthemye named iuno sone began laughe comyng hys moders wombe named iubyter whan cibell vesca sawe childe lawhe theyr teeres began growe double taken grete regard hede chyld tyme cibell angrye corrupt wyth wanhope wyth syghe feble speryt sayd moder ha moder pietous caas shal gyue sharp cuttyng knyf shall murder sone innaturel errour agayn wyll vyllayns dede absolucion grete synne shall murder self also myn oppynion ffor cruell dede werk notwithstandyng ony excusacion wyll neuer lenger lyue moder cibell tho wepte greth dismayed whan herd ayer tendre mouth doughter redounde eres hard cruelte beyng affrayed sayd doughter thynkest thou doo art thou enraged thi witte folyssh moder answerd cibelle ye veryly verily ye saye enraged wytte folissh yet furio wood make lenger languyssh gyue cursid mortal knyf forgyd euyll houre ffor force muste obeye kyng saturne right welbelouyd sone ryght redoubtid husbond tht hath comaundement ouer wil schamely put deth yf acomplyssh fulfille comaundement deth sone whiche hath chargid slee amone vesca consideryd doughter said errour tht toke chyld armes pluckyd hyt force alwey chyld laughed whan cibell sighe sone armes moder woman araged wytte began crye shold slee chyld gyue hyt agayn elli wold aryse bed go playne kyng saturne thise wordes vesca delyuerid child damysell hows onely hem bad shold go slee child presence saturne som place theyr sight poure damysell excusid vesca gaf comaundement charged wyth grete menasses shold go forth take chyld knyf slee hy comaundement two lady toke knyf many tymes put hit throte child cutte hit sonder alwaye noble child laughed knyf whan damysell saw hyt innocent myght fynd hert hit ony harme sorow payne varyacion vesca cibell damoysel longe tyme iugged hym deth put knyf throte sodeynly damoysell reuoked hit swere wold neuer secuteresse oon fayr child thus began thre wepe sobbe bewaylyng child grete affeccion hit pyte whan longe wepte sobbed bewailed tendre wepyng payne cibell began lityl attempre hert began retorne moderly pyte cibell called held child requyred petously tht wold gyue sone kysse hold armes promyttyng wold hym none harme damoysel wyst shold falle delyuerd tendre chyld whan cybelle beheld child face bewept alle distemprid wyth teris kyssed laughyng mouth c tymes cam agayn nature knowlechyng syn began saye chyld wel infortunat yf taken thy lyf thee haue contended thi deth right swete sone ala shal secute wyll thy fader kyng saturne hyt comaundement owe hym obeyssance yf obeye culpe synne due hym yf obeye make selfe culpable deth thys shalt thou dye handes handes thy propre moder ha shall thy moder thy marterar shal thy moder thyn enemye bitter mortall aduersarye doubte deth wot saye woley woley thou art sone euery moder loueth chyld may hate hyt moche better dye thou haue liuyd longe ynowh thou art first borne veryly thu shalt dye thys tyme shal saue thy lyf shal dye thy helth requyryng goddes euyll wyll ayenst saturne comaunded sle iupiter tht new born hys moder cybelle sente hym kyng mellisens wher norisshid right sorowful lady cam better self toke hert kyssed chyld tht alwey laughed vesca beheld contenance newe satte doun bedde side doughter laye two began speke geder saturne ffortune child ben grete auenture mysid oon vnto wold saue child vnto power mysse ende dyuerse pourposes concluded send child secretly vnto two doughtres kyng melliseus whiche vesca norisshid yong age two doughters oon named almachee mellisee conclusion fully fynysshid taken vesca lappid wond child hit ought delyuerid hit vnto damoysell beyng psent thynges gaue charge bere hit secretly vnto almachee mellisee good damoysell enterprisid said charge detid crete child aventure worshypfully guyded brought child leuyng sauete cite oson whiche psentyd almache mellisee rehersyng vesca sent hym hem grete loue truste hem saturne comaunded moder shold slee hit anone two damoyselles sawe child vnderstoode saturne iuggid hit deth resseyued hit wyth pyte fauour vesca promysid nouryssh hit secretest best wyse mochte forthwyth oure bare chyld vnto montaygne nyghe cite wher dwellyd theyr nouryce depe hole caue whyche rychely entaylled coruen wyth chysell dyuerce instrumentis sent agayn damoysell brought chyld crete maner lyf chyld saued almache mellisee norisshid child wyth melk goot ffortune hym propice helpyng nature shall saye begynnyng whan put caue hys nouryces day sawe wepe crye pre inclinacion c dhood cause shold herd toke tr pe tympane cymbales maad sowne gretly gret multitude bee ffleyng aboute montaygne herd theyr soun wyth sown entrid caue toke hooll chyld ffleyng aboute hym wyth ony greef harme doyng child yet maad hony wher child ete norisshed then forth whiche merueylous thyng allewey tachieue mater begynnyng damoysel tht born thys child theder whan cam agayn reherced dame cybell vesca besoyne werk gaf hem ryght grete fort towchyng child two ladyes meur deliberacion toke abbeste whiche precious stone brayded hit pouldre medlid hit wyth wyn cuppe gold dame vesca bare hyt sone saturne habowndyng bitter teres bewept sayd hym sone thy wyf hath sent drynke knowe thou veryly day hath rendred yelden fruyt wombe sone doughter hath sent doughter nourysshe cite parthemye obeyng thy strayt comaundement haue defetyd sone put hym deth body fflessh lityl tendre bone torned asshis hath sent right noble herte temprid wyn whiche present thende thou thy plesir doute thy sone put thy royame anon saturne herd petous wordes hys moder vnderstandyng newe tydyngis said shewd hym began frowne yd maner pyte oute pyte ne ought herte terryble angry restraynd pressurs sorow whan hit force myn hert present hert yssued blood rootes gyuen mete pasture estaunche descouenable honger myn inhonest desire thise wordes accomplisshid saturne gretly displesid full renewyng sorow drank drynke wenyng hyt ben moder done hym vnderstonde went chambre began gretly melancoly fo thon purposid trowed abstayne hym self paye wyf deu dette maryage ther sorow ne ouer passeth space tyme forgate sorow lyyng wyf engendrid sone whiche sauyd like iupiter sauyd well saturne charged put hym deth child born atthenes kept norysshyd named neptune yet laye wyth wyf engendryd sone doughter whiche time couenable born deted moder tyme told sone hid hit saturne whiche sone named pluto dide hit kepe party thesaylle afterward named hell content husbonde saturne whan delyuerd two childern sent hym doughter whiche callid glanta dyed tendre yeres thus generacions saturne supposid tht non reseruyd iuno doughter wente oftymes visite parthemye dide hit nourysshid wyth many noble virgyns eage also many auncient gentylwymen enduce teche hem gentilnes vertu wyl tarye also iupiter neptune pluto wyl shewe dardanus put broder iasius deth couetyse rengne cyte corynthe detid corynthe sette fyrst ston cyte dardane whiche afterward named troye phow deth kyng corynthus corynthe two sone dardanus iasius strof shold haue kyngdom dardan slew broder iasius trayson wherfore dete contre tyme whan crete began aroyame kyngdame possession fyrst kyng wyse cyte corynthe whiche stant naples regned corynthus ther fyrst kyng corinthus wyf oon doughters kyng athlas libye named electra regned geder achieued prossly theyr lyf lefte hem two sone wherof oon named dardanus iasyus saye dardan sone iupiter bochace trowed lawful sone corynthus hit apperith sixte book genelagye goddes dardanus iasius deth theyr fader corynthus moder electra wold succede royame wyse coude accorde dardanus hihe hauntayn courage iasius like wyse argued stroof gyder oon ayenst often tymes mater conspired made secretly menasses vnder couert suche wyse dardanus day assemblid peple coude gete spryng destroie broder iasius fredes whiche tho assemblid secrete place treete pee see myght contente plese dardan whan iasius sawe hys broder come armes blood began chaunge seeyng broder esmeuyd full euyll demyng mater shold torne grete myschief ascried saide ala auayleth speke counceyll seke menes pee betwene broder ben betrayed lo broder cometh vpon v armes eche man saue hym self may wordes dardanus cam consistorie smote broder vnto deth said iasius thou maist abstayne thi self thy machynacyons thou hast enhaunsed thy self ayenst shal make ende iasius fill doun ded among foot hys frendes ther clothes sprenct bled blood whan frendes iasius saw tyrannye saued self well coude power fledd then araged dardanus retorned riall palays frendes iasius gaderd ad wente armes made noyse murmure grete lityl space alle cyte strongly troublid deth iasius whiche gretly grace fauour peple corynthe ffor whan herd reherced deth iasius toke grete sorow manaced dardanus deth forthwyth effect assemblid grete rowtes stretes sayd oon ala ded loue corynthyeus amytye loue comyn wele dardanus late v goo auenge deth gowe punysshe malefacteur late v lenger tarye shall meritorye werk euer doth iniustyce tyrannye worthy chyef heed clemence ner iustice yf suffre murdrer reygne vpon v neuer shall ther good come ther wher heed seke euyll membres may hoole ner good dardanus hath slayn broder iasius wrongfully hyt vray semblable h shall slee v wyll late v take hym puissance late v shewe men distroyers vyces enemyes vnto seken engenderen tyrannye courage svche clamour corynthyeus suche noyse semblable clamour chauffyd selfe end assemblid oon place ful ardent appetyt correcte malefactour dardanus complices tempest swellyng ffurour went pallais dardan put hym self reffuge fonde yates shytte coude entre hyt wherefore assieged place makyng grete noyse grete tempeste dardanus abasshid anon assemblid hys frendes axed councel answerd sayd grete auenture paryll peple meued myght lightly appesid said hym saue thy self v also thou hast slayn thi broder iasius peuple louyd crueyllously benyugnyte trespaas grete syn hit best wey ought taken councell thou leue palais ffynd maner yssue shall folowe goo wyth serche auentures landes ffor hit shall grete payne possibilite euer contente appese peple well corynthieus terryble haue hate despyte dardanus heryng wordes began sighe conscidered moste departe cite mysfait culpe desert smote hym self brest sayd ha ffortune vnstedfast befalle handes ben foule filthid blood laufull broder insurreccion rebellyon peple hangyng fore myn eyen hit force flee saue lyf purpose lyue rauayn thefte meschunce euyll happe syn hyt yelde fugytyf shall go way alauenture hyt whan ffrendes dardanus vnderstande concluded purposed saue lyf ioyned hym appoynted gyder next morn first krekyng day wold departe pallays take thauenture passe theyr enemyes sayyng yf myght ascape shuld go ryuage see take kynges barge sware helpe accompanye eche vnto deth nyght passyd day aperyd dardanus restyd nyght plesir wacchid wyth armed men redy take thauenture goddys fortune wold gyue send hem yssued pallays found parte enemyes slepe threstyd among vyllayns passyd forth wyth lityl resistence notwythstandyng wakyng coryntheus cam ryal shipp toke see sauvid self wherof corynthyeus grete sorowe whan dardanus sawe quyt fureur corynthyeus wente saylyng see descended first port cyte samos beyng trache vytaylled hym went see agayn arryued asye quarter wher land ioynyng see hellespond fyndyng land right good fruytefull enhabite made habitacion sette first stone ryght grete cyte began achieued cyte tyme named dardane name dardanus afterward hit callyd troye dardanus peupled fyld cyte wyth men woman whiche gate swetenes fayr promesses te conquerryd force thefte pillerye made hym self kyng dardane dyched cyte aboute wyth grete diches longe tyme passyd thys world dyed lefte sone wif candame second kyng dardane kyng named erutonius regned seuyn fourty yere en augmentyng encresyng cyte peple last consumed end yeres regned hym trops sone troos thirde kyng dardane stronge man fiers hardy en armes encresyd gretly hys seygnourye crowne moche dardanyens said ther kyng troos named troians thus troyes enhaunced royames grece hihlye kyng tantalus ffrigie grete enuye gaf hert courage myght anulle put doun name tros neighbour began tessaie bryng hit doun shal said pof grete werre tht meued betwene pelagiens epiriens kyng lichaon pelage destroyed iupiter cause man put hym ostage whiche kyng lichaon rost wise subtyl virgyne menerue saint austyn reherseth shewid self tyme stagne riuer callid triton gretenes subtilte engyne ffor fonde maner forge make armes purpos ovide reherceth foughten agayn geant named pallas slewe hym flood triton tyme armes founden science mynerue practiqued world fiers descension engendrid bytwene epyriens pelagiens tht named archadyens maketh mencion bochace fowrt book genelagye goddes amonge pelagiens regned tyme kyng named lichaon eldest sone tytan epiriens enterprysed vpon pelagiens maad right grete noyse aroos sourded ffor whiche cause assaylled eche fete armes felounous aspre booth party suffryd many fowle mortall shoures wyse men epire sawe thys warre disolute partye iniustly vnrightfully attamed begon thys warre knowlechid fault went kyng lychaon beryng braunches olyue signyfiance pee loue hym requyred wold condescende acord pee bothe peuples lichaon consideryng peple moche lost wonne discencion bataylles perylous accorded thepiryens pee condicion shold delyuere hym oon thyr moste noble men suche wold demaunde seruaunt space tyme token vnryghtfully engendrid discencion epiryens consentid condicion delyueryd kyng lychaon seruitude noble man mong thus ended warre terme tyme drewe ouer thepiryen seruyd kyng lichaon due tyme whan tyme expired epiryens assemblid geder deliberacion counceyl sent enbassade lichaon trete delyuerance thepiryen thise enbassadeurs departyd epire cam pellage shewid kyng man seruyd long bounden requyred hym wold rendre delyuere hym ratefie pee end euer myght frendes gyder whan lichaon hard courage fiers euyll vnto men also vnto owen peple vnderstood wordes requestes epiriens grete sorow angre hym sylf sayd mouth thynkyng contrary hert morne wold feeste hem haue hem dyner shold doo lyke demaunded wordes epiriens departid ioyously fro presence kyng lichaon morn cam feste richely ordeynd maad gret plenteuousnes whiche ryght fayr begynnyng ende right foul abhomynable whan hit cam performyng feste kyng lichaon roos table went vnto kechyne toke body thepirien seruaunt murdrid nyght rostid soden brought hit grete plater feste presentid hit thepiriens sayng lo thepirien hath seruyd whiche cause escheweyng ruyne perdicion epirye said yesterday shold delyuere hym thys day take hym wole discharge put handes hym wole hym alle tho psent wel ser uauntis stranger aswell epiriens pellagiens anon grete horrour whan herd vnderstood wordes kyng lychaon grete shame furcur beholde hounteuse abhomynable werk oultrageous synne troubled blood wente fro face leyde handes afore eyen abhorred behold pour martir epiryen ther man wyste saye infamye kyng lychaon vnnethe whan kyng sawe troubled euery man began frowne grugge part lefte hem wente then vnto chambre euery man rose fro table abhorryng eschewyng sente sauour dede man wold haue departid goon way confuse ne ben iupiter sone saturne whiche epiriens brought legacion enbassade moche fair child able gentill whan sawe euery man drewe parte waye putte hym self myddes thepyriens began glorious enterprise said wise blood epyriens bannyd hardynes exyled valoyr honneste whiche epiryens force wole expose self vengeance foule horryble dede caas born terryblete tyrant lichaon redoubtyd whan hit bleuyth vnpunysshid ye see pelagyens make semblant euyll payd hym muste punysshid saye shall neuer haue pleasir lyf tyll se hym refrayned tyrannye tyme epiryens conceyued grete courage iupiter yonge age thanked goddes brought hym hem said hym oon wy childe blessid wombe bare blessid goddes forseyng iniure wronge v hath enspyred v brynge wyth v ben courage hardines well ben hardy haue taken ony terme vengeance thy wordes haue awaked envertued spirytes whiche ded aslepe passed countrepesed infamye tiraut lichaon thy hardynes hath maad v hardy thy vayllyance hath maad v vaylliant louers vaillyance thy wisedom hath enlumyned v cause thou shall conduitour ledar werke comaunder shall obeye vnto etc ivpiter answerd sayd worshipfull lordes sir wise ynowh resseyue honour ye ner tendre yeres shall accepte hit allewey forme counceyle humelyed vnder alle correccion well saye yow thynketh erpedient doon yf ye fynde man saie better ye shall counceill aduyce ye shall take poure epiryen estate delyueryd yow bere hym vnto comyn place cyte ffor hit day sabate haliday pelagiens ben grete nombre multytude passyng tyme wyth dyuerce playes esbatementis ye shall shewe pour ded man ffor hit sayd kynge well belouyd owne peuple vnmanly werkes mesfeet trespaas passyng foull pyetous anone shall knowe hath doon foul werke ye shall wel secyf shall take synne pleasir dysplaisir yf pleasir hyt abuse folye speke therof present tyme ony muste seke remedye retorne epire yf take displaisir ye may playnly disco ure courage prouoke calle purge cryme cursid wene shall right lyggtly entende v none amytie betwene hym shal domyne ner regne vpon hem tyrannye ffor naturel lord sone tytan broder saturne kyng eleccion force alle herd iupiter thus speke merueyled gretly hym accorded hys counceyl suche wise man contraried hit ner agayn sayd hyt sodenly toke murdred epiryen bare hym comyn place ther shewid hym openly euery mannes sight whan pelagyens sawe dede man skyn scorched fflessh rosted senewes shronken bone aperyd ioynturs assemblid al aboute hym grete nombre castyng eyen vpon hym grete orrour abhomynacyon abasshement hertes trembled playned eche othir many went awey compassyon wepte araged trembled angre toke duste pouldir casted ayer signe sorow cuttyng clothis sayng liftyng handes highe goddes almyghty peple ben epiriens haue rosted mannes body haue brought hit fore v mene eters mannes flessh bryng hit v shew cruelte courage come ete ded man among v fere v ivpiter ther beyng awaityng leyyng eres seyng eyen maner pelagiens contenances conceyuyng condescended contempnacon enemyte hym wrought pietous werke whan herd reason seen wondringes adressid hym self amoge said wise ye men pelage ye esmerueylle yow vnmanly vnnaturell werke haue ye lerned knowe tiranies kyng lichaon hath murdrid man man epirien delyuerid hym traytte pee yow v serue hym lo guerdon reward hath hym hath tirannysed right euyll hath hym euyll good grete infamie yow peple folk euery cyte haue regnyng kynges noble men vertuous crowned eleccions vertuous dedes ye defferent fro nother nature tyrant kynge murdrer iniuste man synnar worthy infamous deth vnworthy lefte lyue vpon erthe considere ye considere vnder who hande ye nyghe ye fynde self maladye parcyll deth whan heed aketh alle membres suffren payne ye may hooll sound shulle doo thynke ye counceylle ye v come reffuge demaunde yow ought behaue v ayenst oon fowl kyng lichaon telle v verray trouth yf ye confesse trouth ye louers rayson iustyce equyte ye shall iugge condempne hym ye shal leye handes puissance correccion hym ye shall depesshid malice amon pelagyens vnderstood iupiter lichaon kyng commysed villayns cryme also presentyd eryepins body frend ded beyng table condempned synne murmured agaynst hym sayng wold gouerned norysshyd vnder rodd peruers vnfamous tyrant sayden epiryens wold abide put theyr abandon wyth wordes iupiter putte hym sylf among epiriens hardynes amonesshid conspire agayn kyng wyth whiche conspiracion acorded alle cyte wordes iupiter agreable hem hys maners put hand deth destruccion kyng lichaon thende shold truste haue affyance sent theyr armes habillemens warre armed assemblid aboute iupiter said hym shold capitayne conduitur tachyeue sayd werke ivpiter beyng ioyous grete honeur worship excusid hymself excusacions place epiriens pelagiens ordeynd constytuted hym heed ouer constituted dignyte sette peple ordre hem marche toward palays longe goon way whan sighe kynge lychaon yssue palais grete companye ffrendes armed ben aduertysed sayd conspiracion maad agaynst lychaon ffelyng enemyes cam tassaylle hym ffor shewe hym self man fyers corage cam gaynst wenyng presumtuously haue ouercomen anone began taproche escryed eche deth counceill strongly esmeuyd assamblid batayll right merueyllously sharpe lychaon setted ladd peple ordre agaynst iupiter medled hem hastely geder wyth lytill stryf wordes wyth grete stryf horyons stroke stryf coste moche especiall lychaon ffor peuple lasse puyssance myght men iupiter whiche stronge grete enterprise fought smote vpon pelagiens caste hem doun uow fiersly desmesurably none mochte abyde afore amonge alle iupiter wonder meruaylles well doyng putte lychaon passyng grete errour noyance thys grete anoye sued passyng fast haue come ronne vpon hym whan fals tyraut sawe hym come sawe iupiter sette stroke myghteli araught smeten doun erthe confounded alle hys herte began faylle hym wente hym syde long abiden whan iupiter vaynquysshid ouerthrowen pelagiens made hem fle place fore hym like hit ben thondre tempeste maner whan lychaon sawe complices felawship suche extremyte fledde hym self kyng pour man comfort hope desolate durste take non complices wyth hym helpe hym away comforte hym doubtyd iupiter deth fleyng way said durst entre palais yssued cyte wente vnto grete forest nyghe then forth brygant theef cause poetes faynen torned wolf saye lyued wolf proies robberyes allewey purpos mutacyon leoncius reherceth lichaon fleyng sayd supposyd sued iupiter put deth putte hym self ryuer grete lake ther saued hym self ffelyng water ryuer synguler prete wete men putteth self water shold torned wolues terme ix yere ix yere exspired yf wold putte self water agayn shold recouure agayn first liknes hit myght well lychaon putte hym self water transumed wolf space abouesaid lyuyd thefte pillerye wodes forest waytyng oftetymes pellagiens gouerned self ende whan accomplisshid penaunce retorned ryuer toke agayn mannys forme knowlechyng cyte pelage myght neuer recouerd retorned poure myschant vnto fader tytan shall tarye lytill shall telle iupiter began amerous calisto doughter said lichaon etc phow iupiter disconfiture kynge lichaon transformed hym self guyse relygious woman goddesse deane loue calisto doughter said lichaon dide descomfiture kynge lichaon whiche transformed guyse wolf began rauyssheur substance men contre eter child murdrer wilde bestes ofte tyme assaylled rage hunger whiche constrayned hym cherissh kepe myserable lyf whan epiryens syghe iupiter vanquysshid enemyes abode maistre place brought hym grete ioye glorye palais soughte longe lichaon ffyrst place bataile chambres palais fonde hym quykner ded ner coude tydyngis hym hit happend iupiter sought hym thus chambre chambre fonde hiest tour doughter kynge lichaon named calisto whiche passyng fayr yonge ffresshe coloure damoysell bewepte right sorowffully losse fader whiche newly vnderstonde whan iupiter sawe desolate discomforted sette hym doun said damoysell comforte self speke sece wepyng ala syre sayd damoysell shold recomforte self epiryens han slayn kyng fader ought take consolacion ruyne ought angry ought myn herte wyth sorow stomake sihghes myn eyen wepyng c thousand infortunes trauerse body corrompe se poure gentyl damoysel doughter kyng desire deth lyf wanhope hope whan iupiter knewe wordes damoysel tht doughter kyng lychaon grete pite fore moche doughter kyng said damoysel appese hert wote well hit fo ce nature acquyte hym self ye ought considere inordinate werkes fader whiche ye ar bounden bewayle lasse resonable man kyng ought ded hath put hym self som place secrete saue hym self synnes infamo shal beplayne sorow hym goddes fortune haue suffrid rabaisshement casting doun pride tiranies hit rightwys thyng ye take haue pacience rightwis aduersite ffor demerytes gyue yow cause take pacience nature enclyneth yow vnpacience ye ought inpacyent rephension castyng doun ffor like wise hyt losse tyraut torneth alle contrey ioye conforte self damoysell oultragious synnys ner vnmanly furours fader shamefull dedes shall thynge dampnable vnto yow ner torne yow preiudice man shal missaye ner yow ner attouche yow ony maner wyse yow assure certaynly etc syre answrd mayd thanke yow courtoysies fayr wordes wyche ye profere saye vnto wote well pouerte hath maad indygne vnworthy whan see infortune fader irrecouerable infelicyte hath recourance renonce world pray yow hit plese yow trete vnto epiriens myght goo yelde self relygion dame deane noble virgyne doughter wise iupiter somtyme kynge actyque born londe vpon ought remembrid right auncyently yssued pellage wyse noble man named iupiter bochace maketh mencion first book genelagie goddes whiche iupiter kynge actyque moche introduced peple honest lawes dide first ordeyne halowe maryage ffor fore tyme acticyens maried hem vsed woman comyn iupiter cam doughter named diane whiche willyng tabide thestate virginyte maad cloistre wood archade assemblyd many virgyns passed tyme huntyng chacyng wild bestes ffor torne purpos noble virgyne deane lyuyd tyme subuersion regne lychaon whan iupiter vnderstod calisto wold yelde silf vyrgyne behelde said vnto damoysell ye dispeyred litil tribulacion toucheth persone ye yong fayr amonge none yow go religyon may growe fruyt child aduyse yow wel hit better ye abode amonge worldly peple enplenyssh world many woman also men entre religion yougth repente age syre said calisto tempte yf ther ony gentilnes yow resseyue praier request oon desolate infortunat gentyl woman desirous helth sowle temporel plaisirs duryng deuyses iupiter beheld cessyng damoysell coude nough complayne beaulte moche wold religion wyth grete payne whan herd answer seen swetly taken hit wold torned fro wyll said h requeste shold accomplisshid called epiriens requyred wold content suffre virgyne entre religion shall say epiriens put requeste iupiter iupiter moche conduyte led religion virgyns serchid palais kyng lichaon maad thepiriens sease riches iupiter abode certayn tyme wyth grete worship pelagiens epiryens wold haue crowned hym ben theyr kyng wold neuer consente ther considered ouer yonge age variacions fortune said hit auaylleth man hym sure maad kynge olde age yougth dyuerce parylls may fall alleway acorded wold capitaine royame man grete iustice swete debonnayre vnto manyer peple etc first comyng vp right noble child whan submysid playsance pelagiens beryed thepirien lichaon murdrid hit said afore obsequye solempnly dide brenne asshen pelagiens ben slayn helpe lichaon sent word alle thynges knowen shewed epyriens lefte home epire kynge melliseus wherof epiryens kynge melliseus gaf thankyngis vnto theyr goddes moche muste telle gaf herte courage moche accomplissh thynges tht otherwhile gaf hym self remenbre thynke beaulte seen religyose calisto wherof sparkle loue enuyronned strongly herte suche wyse day nyght wisshed hyre armes repentyd hym consentyd wente relygion laboured thys manere reste nyght taken hym bastard fro franchise courage encresid loue desire virgine see made passe time haunte woddes continuelli hunte wild bestes forest wyth dame deane wherof fortune anenture suffrid otherwhile recountrid mette mayde calisto whan one seen day enioyed yf sawe aboundance many thoughtes ran redely intendement may alday tarye thys mater thoughte ynowh myght come grace religieuse calisto alle thoughtes reduced brought concluded day hym self wold putte hym habite relygiouse woman wold go cloystre dame diane faynyng woman requyryng resseyued virgynes conclusion taken ratefied iupiter many deliberacions dyuerce day dide make hys woman clothyng secrete werkman whiche promysed hym kepe secretes whan clothyng maad assemblid thepiryens euenyng toke leue certayn time sayng wold goo allone certayn secrete thynges thepiriens dismayed desolate whan herde thentencion iupiter prayed goddes wold conduyte spede hym iorney requyryng hym instantly tht wold retorne shortly agayn promysed hem wolde drewe hym chambre toke key grete gate morn betymes whan arayed adoubyd vesture clothyng mayde departyd then alone entrid woode exploytid cam habitacion relygiouse maydens ivpiter yet berde whyte fayr colourid visage whan cam relygion knokked yate cam hym passyng fayr mayde named athalanta wyf vnto kynge melleager achaye demaunded hym wold iupiter answerd noble virgine ala poure woman noble hous haue auowed goddes virgynyte pray yow ye wole presente vnto lady place thende myght serue goddes nombre virgyns yf hit plese goddes shall deserue hit anenste yow athalanta meuyd compassion mayde accorded hym requeste presentyd hym dame deane iupiter spake also swetly demeurly made humble femenyn manyers semed proprely mayde diane behelde hym well longe said neuer seen fayr mayde ner grete welcomed hym resseyued hym iupiter thanked dame diane grace athalanta courtoisie good hoope enterprise whan sawe hym self sone resseyued wythout knowyng iupiter began lerne spynne werke silke done excersitees maiden hit becam hym well ben mayde humble solitary conuersacion laboured handes eyen herte handes mad corporell werkes eyen beheld oftetyme secretly beaulte calisto wyth herte ymagynyng edifyyng mene myght begyle deceyue calisto ofte tymes conuersid felawshipt etc hys hert alwey right grete payne otherwhile meuyd grete heuynes otherwhile conforte hope spede well wiste saye ner doo muche shame drede hym hardynesse shall saye long payne douteuous shamefast hardy ende auentured hym self ffyndyng day calisto beside well refresshid wery ronne longe dame deane chassyng huntyng wilde beste sat hym doun said suster calisto yelde thy grace man nothyng woman thy beaute hath ouercomen corage come poynt haue clothid lyke woman mayde ala require thou resseyue vnto thy loue shal lyue gyder religion shall take deduytes plesances man hath nothyng world lyf haue moche eureus happy thou hast withdrawen hether displaysir losest thy flourisshyng yougth calisto ynowh complayne ner bewaile domage may preyse ynowh haue ben desi rous fynde secrete place force hath ben mescried tht haue enterprised auenture hopyng fortune tht shal gyue grace suffre oure yougthes vsed gyder secretly ffor may comune geder tht oon knowyng ony parsone chambres also busshes woode suster take hede saye resseyued exhaunced late thy prayer pray resseyue exhaunce requeste desdayn hym thou mayst see verray louer etc whan calisto herd iupiter knewe man alle affrayed roose vp wenyng haue fledd myght ffor iupiter helde faste clothyng maad sytte doun hym clippyng aboute nekke kyssyng force moche calisto ascryed said iupiter folye wenest thou ouercome thy flateryng wordes moche leuer erthe wold opene swalwe wombe suster answerd iupiter ther remedye may lette wyll accomplisshid ye shall pleasir hit force hit loue word calisto began crye myght iupiter began accomplissh pleasyr ther neyther man ner woman ther aboutes herd hit well cry calisto grete notwythstondyng iupiter dide body knewe flesshly engendrid sone conforted promysed helpe alle thynges take wyf yf wold retourne world wyth hym fayr speche ne promesses myght conforte ner thynge coude say coude come grace calysto allewey sware grete othes wolde complayne vnto maystres dyane maad moche iupiter departyd desplesid displaisir went woodes thynkyng hym befalle also phow calisto moche childe goddesse dian putte order compaygnye tyme began ryse thentendement iupiter many thoughtes better concluded hym self retorne agayn pellage fro whens cam fro well displesid enforsyng lady dame calisto loue departid fro wood exployted morn among thepiriens first habite whan thepiryens saw iupiter comen agayn made hym right grete chier grete honour day iupiter faigned hym wold go huntyng wente fonde maner speke calisto requyred wold loue wise wold assente hym retourned chasse anoyed passe melancolye departed contre fourth daye folowyng ordeyned folk gouerned peple retorned hous kyng melliseus hym resseyued sone dwellid longe tyme auentures whereof ony mencion maad also calisto dwellid pee whan herd telle vnderstood iupiter goon passyng ioious ffor hym leuer ferre nyhe allewey tyme passid fruyt wombe grewe dayes cam diane athalantha wyth virgyns apperceyued childe wherfore assamblyd alle chapitre callid calisto spack deane said calisto doughter thou hast doon fornycacon man fornycacion excusable virgyns place sory thy synne haue abhomynacion thy shame ffor cause hit force thou departe hous thou shalt lenger theyr felawe thou hast maad thy self worthy departe brekyng losyng thy virgynyte take thyn ray gere go thy wey som place thou mayste delyuerid fruyt restith ffor thou shalt lenger etc whan calisto herd goddesse deane knewe sayd trouth grete teeres fylle eyen wepyng grete habondance excused vpon iupiter rehersyng myschief auenture deane maydens grete meruaylle iupiter deceyued calisto cryed mercy right humbly many tymes offrid self punycion maydens withstondyng well hold excused resseyued mercy condempned go cloyster moche wente mater forth pour religious woman departed fro then bewepte shamed wold go toun cite ner hous depe caue seen afore tyme woode first made prouysion herbes rote moche winter comyng entrid caue ther helde also longe tyme bere holdeth hym denne wherfore archadiens faynen torned bere forgoten duryng tyme delyuerid sone whiche named archas child grete huge membres calisto nourisshid hym among wilde bestes rote fruytes herbes propre mete proyes cruel terrible bestes lyueden ther beste dide hym ony herme ner none hardy hym ony greuans cruell fiers eage seuyn yere hys moder angrid troublid hym day lift vp hym silf ayenst wold haue slayn moche calisto constraynd flee fore hym busshes yet yssue wood goo iupiter whiche tyme cyte pellage archas poursued calisto moder vnto cam cyte forth entrid palais held two handes grete rounde stone whan calisto entrid palais auenture encountrid met iupiter knewe kneled doun erthe fore hym requyred hym affraied spirite wold iustice sone wold sle iupiter nothyng knewe calisto moche euyl clothid half wilde sauage beheld chyld made hym taken demaunded calisto sire said calisto tht thy synne long syn bannysshid religion haue child thy seed suche thou seest thy sone haue nourisshid alle child male etc tyme yonge archas crowned kynge pellage named cyte archade name kynge saturne grete puysaunt ample encrece splendure natyuyte named hym self saturne sone heuen erthe began studye maner myghte enhaunce resplendour felicite dyuyue mysteryes ffortune torned back hym ward ther ne nothinge erthe may abide endure hit happend titan acertayned quene cibell dyuerce men child kepe secretly sauyd lyf bochace recounteth historie iiij book genelagie goddes saith mene titan knewe thyng allewey suspecion enuye glorye saturn broder secret aduertisment vnder colour determyned hys courage wold assaylle saturne armes cause dide assemble day sone required tht wold ayde helpe hym gete lond crete sayng wold make warre agayn saturne broder right iuste tytle good cause put deth dyuerce men child wif cybell conceyued seed lyke promysed sworn child tytan tht oon lychaon tyme lenger wolf ner kynge archade another name typhon kyng secile cipres thirde callid bryarius kynge nericos fourte named ceon kynge yle cea fifth named egeon kynge see egee yle deserte sixte named eperion kynge plipheros whan herd fader pourueyed alle royames conquerid departyng crete desiryng please hym coueytyng recouurance ther ancient heritage tho grete renome sayde hym oon wy redy accomplissh good pleasir goo crete armed hand sworen shuld constrayne saturne seke feche sone persecute hand vnto deth olde tytan herte grete ioye whan behelde free grete courage sone promysed swere geder shuld employe recouerance herytages whiche comuracion ordeyned suche wise gaderd hem geder porte secyle sente vnto lordshippis assembele men armes warre wente made suche diligence exployted assemblyd grete armour harneys moche peple said porte whan day comen desired laboure mater departyd secyle grete oost took see made iournees wyth auenture fewe dayes sayled vnto crete porte arryued toke londe entryng fiersly lande destroyed wasted afore cruelly contynued theyr warre mortally cam vnto cyte crete kynge saturne dwellyd resident saturne aduertysed comyng discent tytan myght ferther passe bataylle assault sente saturne lettre wherof tenour foloweth saturne englottid wordly honneur couetyse glorie moche thou art ocupier seygnourie right langeth titan thy lord elder brother furthermore cause thou art falsely periured ffor thy wif hath dyuerce men child thou hast put deth like wise thou bounden knowe come take possession thy kyngdom apperteynyng wherfore come mercy meke thy self grace ellys make sure thy parsone ffor yf hit possible shall come haue reson whan saturne redde lettre man esbayed sent wyf cibell toke part coniured charged saye trouth telle hym wyth child charge poure lady changid colour seeyng constrayned saye trouthe sayd syr thou knowest woman herte woman naturelly doth werkes pite haue ben nature abhomynable monstre yf shold haue deuourred hande child wombe moder shal murdre child certes hand neuer man slear ner neuer shall haue erred agayn thy comaundement fauour nature syn hit must nedes said leuer murdrid murdrere named pietous cruel ffor murdre cruelte apperteynyng vnresonable bestes tyrantes pite naturelly apperteynyng woman therfore confesse haue born thre sone conceyued thy seed whiche haue nourisshid secretly demaunde ferther shal liue longe hit plesith fortune wil tytan ther deth wherof ony woman may turmentid shall make place dyscoueryd saturne herynge wordes wyf esbayed wist answere withstondyng better assemblid wise men cyte sayd brethern frendes best doon tytan broder hath begon warre royame wyf hath confessid hath resseyued thre sone whyche hath nourisshyd strange land vnder colour shold slee tytan assaileth shall syre answerd wyse men force enhaunsed ouer grete presumpcion ther muste craft conduyte wiseli put hand withstand hit thou hast stronge cyte fulfillid grete peple thou art wyse gouerne hem put thy self armes take regard quarele titan man worthy kynge yf hit vertu gentil maners crete neuer royame tytan hath ben lyue enclyned vice enuoluped synne whyche purpos maynteneth come thy crowne yf enhaunce hym self thou muste rebasshe put hym doun remedye helpe thy self shall helpe fleeth causeth enemye chasse hym thus hit may fled hit must wythstande gyue arrest enemye ryght coragiously ffor man may day late hym put hit ouer tyll morowe arme well sewerly assayle thy cyte thyn enemyes yf thou doo thou shewest thy corage enhaunced gretly lyghtly ouercomen thou mayst attempre somwhat pryde presumpcon yf thou mayntene otherwyse thy self late take reste shall mater cause encorage vpon whyche shall enflame self hoping come aboue whiche shal harmyng vayllable ffor corage hope ofte tymes men saie make men attayne grete hye victoyres notwithstondyng thou art kynge thy accomplisshid fulfilled saturne answerd said brethern frendes hit grete shame v suffred hyt dissypate destroyed hit force warre begonne open euery man dispose hym saue worship titan assaileth myn honour requyreth dyshonour syn hyt force mater armes warre iugges shall arme v hour poursiewe thentertenement ryght good auenture tht fortune come v herte telleth also sodeynly enemyes ben entrid land also sodeynly shal make goo yssue agayn thys answere alle wyse noble men crete took grete plesir saturne gaf answer messanger tytan said hym yf tytan retourne two houres wold come take batayll ayenst hym answer massanger retorned tytan said hym thentencion saturne tytan swore wold neuer retorne backward tyl attended abiden batayll saturne man grete valure hye wyll whan messangier tytan departid made sowne armes whiche sowne yong olde adowbed made hem redy shall make long processe short tyme redi poynt whan saturne sawe enemyes made semblant meue went ascended chare ffor tyme kynges went bataill chares yssuyd cyte rengid peple aboute hym anone dide marche agaynst tytan etc ferre tytanoys sawe saturnyens come right glade made self grettest chiere worlde uyd silf ioi usly ayenst grete crye grete sheldes tree mace pollaxes guysarmes strange facions fote reseruyd tytan sone whyche rynges theyr curres chares whyche brought caried force hors puyssance men approched nyghe cam fightyng began werke archer kynge saturne began drawe shote maad tytannoys arest stande also longe shotte dured slowe hurte many whan shotte fayled tytanuoys grete sorowe seruid saturnyens esmeuyd hem self agayn swore oon wold auengid cam fight hand oon hand whiche enployed aygrely noise dene ax guisarmes smote vpon sheldes hit semed hit ben thonder counteryng batayll right ffell lychaon egeon creon typhon encheladus first front ther many shelde broken weight clubbes polaxes many heedes broken ceon tiphon begynnyng maintend hem self right vailliantly conduyte folke batayll rigour stroke moche mette saturniens bete hem doun well doyng knowen doubtyd enemyes moche saturne maad chare lad wey grete bruyt noyse made aboute hem grete effusion blood ffor tytanuoys enforced haue endured bruyt crye saturnyens saturne putte payne abate hit breke hit comyng saturne cause prouesse vpon prouesse many oon deed entended oon acertaynly werke part day maad grete stryf none myght enioye hym victorye ne trouble disconfiture ende whan titanuoys sawe sonne declyne couetous glorye worshyp oon crye tytan made vpon saturne lychaon egeon many enclosed aboute hem beyng diskled chare broken force polhaxes gaf hym many woundes finably toke hym brought many saturnyens deth ouerthrewe disconfeture werse discoragid whan vnderstode saturne taken loste viguers strength hertes myghtis armes turned backis fledd desroyed tytanuoys entred hem cyte toke hit wanne hit ony resistence betyng doun peple wyth grete murdre men woman smale child tyme men myght se lady matrones crete take duste caste hit ayre renne stretes ther dessheuellyd hangyng aboute hedes castyng ferre atyre lityll child cry hem wise men toun semed witte cyte trowblyd myght amonge cybell vesca seres maad grete sorow semblably cessyng ffor tytan neuer louyd cam tho palays putte prison saturne wyf swore shold neuer departe then tyll put deth sone come furthermore tytan dide hym crowne kyng crete ne auayled infinite praiers orison dame vesca made tytan compassion sone saturne cybell delyuerance ner fayr spekyng cere ne teeres meuyd charite valu moo prayer made vnto tytan fonde hym vncourtoys felon malgracyous dyde execute put deth alle held apparteynyg partye saturne space four dayes vexid troublid crete robbyng shedyng blood cytezeyns ne persecuted onely men also woman chyldren toke theyr goodes departyd amonge helde hys partye whan vessca sawe alle thynges happene cyte sone tytan gouerned hym malicyously allewey worse worse ony compassion peple cam pryson saturne cybell sayd hem wyth mouth widyng dolorous sighes ala child shal ye shall come yow shal ye sauyd land crete drowned teeris wepyng best frendes blood blood wiues child herte tytan terrible harded indured ye shal dye myserable payne ye muste put sone deth syn hit better put deth ye sende seke hem whan lyf none remedye anger cibell right aspre sharp sorowfull tidynges moche herte faylled saturne moder thought whan come agayn self escryed saide ha moder saye ye v haue grete payne kepe child shold oure abandoune deth shal trayson child begyn floryssh right clere fame shall neuer beyf hit plese gooddes haue well leuer haue regard semblant iupiter sone hath grete name hath wonne loue pelagiens thepiriens world preyseth hym holdeth hym oon vailliants men world sone shal sende hym late hym haue knowleche myserye damoysell bare hym vnto montaigne oson shall requyre hym socours hope man hye corage ewreus comyng vp shall socoure hath hym merite worthy haue socours tht saued hym tendre dayes hert telleth shal trowblyng crete thankyd damoysell torned hym vnto kyng said hym syre ye may knowe vnderstand hows damoisell witnesseth fader moder ben handes enemyes praye yow faueur ye wyll helpe socoure goo hastely oppressyng hym hath oppressid haue singuler hope truste fortune shall helpe v fayr sone answerd melliseus knowe haue affeccion recourance thy lignage shewe make semblaunt signe promyse helpe moche possible iupiter assured damoysell swore vnto wold put hym armes agaynst titan bad retorne vnto saturne cybell comforte hope right short socour damoisell departyd then wordes iupiter retorned crete told vnto saturne cibell doon anone damoysell departid iupiter sent archas sone hastly archadiens also sent epiriens parthemyens cite anlacre thise peple louyd iupiter grete loue cam comandement grete nombre men warre iupiter welcomed well couthe told cause sent told sone vnto kynge saturne thise thynges dide maad redy alle thyng necessarye vnto hys oost departyd fro cyte oson wyth ryght fayr compaygnye ignorance thou knowe thou arte firste sone heyr kyng saturne dame cybell kynge saturne thy fader euery man knoweth longe syn maad oth vnto broder tytan shold slee alle child male shold come seed whiche cause day thy natyuyte comandyd thou sholdest put deth thy moder pyte saue thy lyf sente secretly vnto hows geuyng thy fader saturne vnderstande persecucion eschewe fureur thy fader thou hast ben norysshyd thy dayes knowest thy self thou thou art certayn ioye certaynly grete thou oughtest go ioyously vnto thy fader moder presentyng thy self vnto grace yf hyt thyse tydyngis ioye whiche muste nedes shewe vnto iupiter tidyngis thy moder hath sauyd thy oncle titan holdeth pryson saturne hath norissh hath ouercome venquysshid thy fader bataile newly take hym royame yet hem dye wherfore praye requyre thou haue pyte thou wilt employe go delyuere daunger daye kynge melliseus iupiter heering thise tydyngis damoysell meruayled right gretely iupiter right ioyous whan vnderstand sone kynge saturne otherside sore vexid resseyue tydyng ryght grete ioye knowlechynge place natyuyte ffor gretter ioye may haue ner come hym knowe fyrst sone auncyent hous crete shall torne hym souerayn gladnesse whan shall see requyred come make recouerance fader moder contre phow iupiter wyth ayde kynge melliseus epire deliuerid saturne fader cibell moder prison tytan slewe tytan bataill whan saturne vesca herde cibell speke vesca said aduyse ryght good saturne esbaied ffor thought iupiter seen dyuerce tymes wyth kynge melliseus shold wise sone vnnethe coude beleue hit gyue faith vnto wordes cybell said yf iupiter wold socoure hym man hit content cibell shold sende seche hym sayd cybell sent damoysell knewe alle guydyng iupiter gaf charge go vnto hym fornysshe werkis damoisel ioyeus enbassade departid secretly taried til cam vnto hows melliseus fyndyng iupiter kynge reuerence made adressid orison iupiter sayd hym iupiter esioye glad brynge tidyngis gladnes neuerthelasse amonge sorowes ffortune hath hold long tyme ignorant knowyng place thy ryght noble natyuyte hath certaynly suffred discouerture knowleche tha men arme vnto nombre sixe thousand fightyng men well spedde short tyme brought hem vpon myle nyghe cyte crete jupiter wold tarye vpon toppe montaigne callid hym sone archas tyme ne xiij yere age right wise well bespoken gaf hym charge shold go crete gyue sommance vnto kynge tytan go cyte de u hym fader saturne moder cibell yonge archas hardy herte hye enhaunsid worde fader wente vnto crete kyng tytan dide hym presentid sayd vnto hym thise wordes folowe tytan j come vnto thobeissance fader jupiter first sone kynge saturne thou holdest captyuyte hath ben aduertised thoppression thou hast persone fader moder deth sone signyfieth sone saturne moche thyn enemye thou sone art enemye vpon whiche j somone legat one twyes thries thou yelde cyte vnto fader kyng saturne hastely thou hast entrid therin like wise thou departe childe answerd tytan thou tellest tydynges ben full plasirs exultacion whiche j knowe thy wordes saturne hath sone yet lyuyng ffor moyen j see clereli also seeth world good juste quarele j maad kyng cyte late jupiter thy fader knowe j doubte hym sette nothyng alle hys comyng also thynge hys comandement tytan sayd archas moche thou abidest wyll tyme ocupie make good wacche iupiter tarieth none cause answer fro deuoyr recoure cyte etc word departid archas fro presence tytan retorned agayn vnto fader whan iupiter herd answer tytan full gladnes ffor desyred thyng armes concluded peple morn shold assaulte cyte caas tytan ffurnysshed hem batayll anone tentes made bowes leeues tabernaclis osonyens archadiens epiryens laye vpon grene verdure maad oost wache tytan crete hit wete whan archas departid fro presence assemblid alle sone told hem thise tydyngis whiche plesant agreable ffor desired nothing stryf debate assured hem self haue victorie iupiter well saturne hour sent four spy espie nombre enemyes made redy harneis spy went ferre sawe oost iupiter made report tytan place enemyes nombre peple bee report said spyes titan concluded moche enmies myle cite shold make hem redy go batayll agaynst hem morn eerly nyght passed fast day cam aboute sonne rysyng tytan mountyd vpon chare right riche made titanoys renge batayle lefte honderd wyth cyte kepe hit rebellion fro trayson toke hym vnder conduyte sone espyes etc ivpiter ydell houre sette men ordenaunce brought folk fayr playne hopyng bataile thus tytan ferre ryden ne sawe ooste jupiter ffor playne disconuerte sydes ferre eche myght see eche full joye enforced make showtes cryes grete desire marched tht oon agaynst vnto comyng smytyng stroke jupiter put hym self front batayle hauyng bowe hand arowes hym shotyng began medlyng right fiers ffor oon side ther ryght good archer many caster polisshid stone failled neuer cause deth many whan shotte castyng stone faylyd began go geder speres tho began mortall fyghtyng hand hand sharp brekyng speres sheldes hit resouned vnto walles crete cam eeres saturne cybell noyse wherof began reioye ffor verr hope iupiter shold obteyne victorye agaynst tytan hour vesca went vp vpon hye tour myght see vnto feld ther sawe fightyng batayle tho helde iupiter glayue hand sheld glayue smote thykkest enemyes sheld sauyd hym self strookes oon strook glayue departyd body encheladus oon sone tytan caste hym ground foot tytannoys right sory deth felaw iupiter assayllid right sharply oon cryed slee slee cryed slayn non th handes iupiter destroied blood aduersaires stronge fiers yonge boystous aspre entrepryse defended hym vigourously lion myghtely olephant eigrely tygre ne entendid vnto deffence body saue rescowe alle parell vnder warant merueilleus alle side noyse bruyt doublid redoublid aboute hym tytannoys began ouerthrowe grete route oon fill sholders sheld charged sore vpon stroke myght susteyned men strong puyssant etc bataile felono hard begynnyng bothe two tie ther many titannoys tharchadiens thepiryens hurte dede cast vnder foot archas accompaignied fifti archadiens commysid vnto garde body moche yonge yet made put hym self right gode deuoir emploie hym self armes melliseus failled ner titan lichaon egeon syde also eche man dide beste tht might saye many men ded ground ne often tymes oon gate vpon ye shall vnderstande ther none comparable vnto iupiter en strengthe conduyte ner prowesse ther thynge hym inpossible ouercame ouercomers slowe slears smote doun smytars put hym self forth many place batayle tytanoys destrayt cam fonde tytan chare confounded epiryens stone rounde plomettes caste cried tytan tytan moche thoughte faught well whan iupiter knewe tytan drew toward hym titan auauncyd arme smyte vpon one epiryen iupiter haunsyd swerd dishargyd sore vpon arme smote hit departid hit fro body wherof grete ioye cryed iupiter iupiter tytan hurt grete sorow fyll doun wyth chare poynt epiriens began corage self tytannoys discoraged lychaon egeon ther fast sawe faders arme fle feld began tassaile iupiter men dispayred began newe medling moche blood spild notwithstondyng fierste lichaon iupiter longe tyme hate moche taken hym lordship iupiter entendyd eygrely put tytan vttrauce brak chare peces helpe epiriens swerd smote arme departyd lyfe body vnhappy tytan mortall strook gaf vnto herte gaf entente prowesse persecute lychaon egeon gyuen hym many stroke horions adressyng swerd vpon hede lychaon swerd wente herte wherof egeon grete sorow drede fledde sauyd hym tempest whiche tempeste ranne vpon titannoys vnmesurabli put deth flight feldes som ther reseruyd oon sone titan named typhon seyng discomfiture cam vnto iupiter said iupiter see thyn enemye fflee flee hit shall vnto honourable fyghte agaynst deffieth renne fugytifs neuer yet founden ffleyng fore myn enemy ner yet shall thou hast slayn tytan fader broder slayn venquysshyd fforce strength behoueth thys royame muste thyn myn late v see shall best yf may shalle vaynquysshe yf ouercome certaynli thou shalt dye glayue ne swerde water fflood renneth alle reed died blood kyn thende thou drynke blood thou hast maad renne body wherof haue grete anoyance endure hyt ffor cours nature ought take displaysir anoye also torne grete dispyt dysplaisyr thou hast doon etc phow iupiter vaynquysshyd felde thyphon caste hym ryuer etc typhon grete full orguyell pryde whan said laye herte iupiter beholde vnderstand answerd hym vaissale hast thou knowleche rayson right goddes fortune thou art stronge membres procedeth fro herte ou trageous wise alleway moche thou demaundest batayle thou art welcome make redy shortly best thou canst haste caas requyreth hit worde thyphon smote iupiter rudely vpon hede shelde bare away grete quarter made iupiter stoupe wyth ryght legge ther ther many epiryens seyng iupiter smeten ranne cam rescowe hym iupiter wold suffre hem shold helpe hym ony maner bad melliseus archas shold folowe chaas fled began assayle typhon grete vertu force suche wise gaf hym many woundes body thus began batayle typhon iupiter bothe stronge able craft armes charged one vpon dolorously eygrely hit nede declare many stroke oon gaf vnto muste telle iupiter fought smote hys enemy toke hym swerd shelde whan poynt chargid hym vpon sholdres force armes bare hym ryuer dyed wyth blood dede men ther dyde hym dye miserably castyng hym flood hede vnder moche menaced iupiter suche deth shall say batayll deth typhon iupiter wente agayn pursuyt enemyes vnto sonne began tenclyne weste sued grete slaughter processe tyme whan sawe tytan part sone ded reste peple feble dispersid feldes myght neuer aryse agayn sowned retrayt reassemblid folke best wise myght toke ryght way cyte hauyng grete ioye exultacion victorye ne taried longe foure cytezyns crete cam vnto hym told hym partye tytan fled taken pryson fader phow iupiter saturne reconsiled gyder iupiter comandement fader wente destroie kynge apollo paphes medecyn esculapius etc ivpiter ressayued cytezyns tidyngis ryght grete gladnes desiryng herte fader moder moche ametus thessayle paas men saye tyme iupiter began mounte hys regne enbrace honour esculapyus sone appollo whyche ryght expert medycyne serchyng day hys aduentures wente woode side sawe ferre herdeman lityll horne fought agaynst basilique nature slewe peple syght whan esculapyus sawe gretly esmeruayllyd taryed longe abyden herdeman ouercome basylique constraynd hym wythdrawe hym vpon rocke nyghe esculapius alle esbayed thynge wi saye ffor hym thought hit impossible man ouercome oon mortall beste whan tyme basylyque wythdrawen vpon sayd rock esculapyus went hym hastely vnto herdeman fyndyng vpon hede chapellet garlond made many diuerce herbes flowres iuged incontynent thys forsayd chapellet herbe suche vertu kepte hym deth also subtyll venym basylique dide moche herdeman shepard gaf hym hys chappelet garlond innocent sayd herdeman went agayn tassaile basilicque sodeynly oon propre sight eyen poure shepharde fyll ded vnto erthe etc esculapius well assured wel thought chappelet herbe suffisid withstonde agayn malicyous entoxicacion thenuenymous eyen beste wyth sayd chappelet went rocke fought agaynst basilicque slewe hym wherof grete ioye herte entendyng worship myhht haue whan thus done went vnto herdman hauyng pite hym toke herbes oon wherof chappelet maad put hem diuysably eche hym self mouthe fynablely touched leues vertueuse herbe brusid hit vpon mouth sodeynly roos deth lyf merueyllous vertu herbe men rede thys herbe ipolitus whiche cam vnto deth mene styfemoder accusid hym falsely afterward reysed lyf agayn longe ded drawen busshes egghes montaygnes thornes whan hys body founde fonde hym leyd hym medowe vpon plante herbes like vnto herbe wherof spoken fore vertu whiche woundes heled lyf gyuen yelde vnto hym agayn holde matier whan esculapius reysed herdman shepherd toke herbe basilicque bare hem vnto cyte paphes tellyng aduenture forth reysed men fro deth lyf vertu herbe fought ouercame basyliques thys cause gate hym hye name iupiter glottyd glorye toke warre agaynst hym slewe hym wherof fader appollo toke grete sorowe hym self enterprysid warre agaynst iupiter iupiter ouercame hym constrayned hym suche extremyte hyde hys name wente seruyd kynge ametus thessayll sayd fore thus whan iupiter vaynquysshid appollo oon manyer retorned crete grete glorye fonde neptune pluto brethern iuno suster maad hym grete chyere iuno beauteuous hym mortall hate agaynst iupiter vnto hym many good dedes also seeyng euery man helde hym loue besy please hym adioustyd fayth gaf credence vnto cursid prenosticacyon suffryd hym self enuolupped wyth tyme ye depryued crowne loste hit delyueryd yow made yow quyt enemyes yf cause charge adiuracion touche mater counceyll oppynyon yf kynge haue puyssance myght ouer hym doubtyth haue cause euydent kynge ought kepe hym seur man daungiers certes sayd saturne thauys counceyll resonable ynowh moche must declare yow saye yow mene kynge speke man doubte iupiter sone fere drede moche deth moche may endure ner take reste hym ffor slepyng dreme ryseth ayenst assailleth armes grete multitude archadyens epiryens resteth vayne qucur victorious ouer wakynge haue alle weie myn eeres opene herkene espie whiche cam gate axed portiers yf iupiteer iune porter whan vnderstood axed answerd iupiter cyte yf wyth hym shold fynde hym pallays passid tyme wyth sone archas newly come toun visyte hym whan crete execute comission whiche may sonner come ruyne trouble pea saturne thy fader comandeth thou allone come speke hym hath sought place parthemye doughter iuno thy wyf thynkyng euyll hath acertayned hym thou art come hether comen armes knowe thynketh doo neuer angry ne tri te ne fiers ben hys seruauntes fforce hath constrayned v obeyssance gyue day appere persone fore hym hour excusacions cessyng etc whan iupiter reteyned well putte hys mynde adiournement wyth hys eyen full teeris maad answer said thus meruayll ryght straunge conduyte fader parauenture hit wyth grete cause royame pea haue putte sette hym agayn hys royame hath putte hym self armes wyth oute knowleche syn sendeth shold allone come speke wyth hym strange thynge vnto gouerneth hym ought ffor ought preyse haue deseruyd hit valu haue auayled hym moche royame worth hath othertyme sente make warre wote neuer euyll wyll hath may haue come armee hath thyng notwithstandyng come demandeth thynge aloonly thynge countyd debatyd haue thyng world pea pea norysshyth prouffit pea ar norysshid men chyldren townes cytees ar vnyed knet geder charite anexed amerous comynycacion pea royames prouffyten en decoracion bildyng fair house labour ereyng erth length lyf pea mannes bodyes ben hole quy te hit thynge causeth man demande souerainte saturne hit semeth thou rekkest good vertu regnyng pea tranquyllite kynge ner prynce dar shewe hym agaynst thee thou hast troublid thy royalme thou art abuser warre haue pea man ought putte hym dispose hym warre thou doost otherwyse ne seest thy sone iupiter hath delyueryd bondes thyn enemyes hath sette thy dyademe seuerte pea thou myght doo wyth oute hym ne seest thou make hym warre thou ne mayst haue pea thou destroyest brekest pea ne seest thou thys thy sone ne seest thou thou art monstre nature fadres naturelly loue child wise rude brute bestes kepe holde condycion nature thou sekest woldest destroye blood thy sone whens cometh dysnaturell appetyte myght hit satysfye thyn appetyt de errour goodnes wele thou hast receyued late reysyng thyn interyor rancour permanent shall thy fantasyes neuer cesse shalt thou age lasse sympler child men growe age wyse thou hast lasse knowleche thou haddest thy paryllous yougth fro whens cometh deffaulte heuenly influence yf hit thus rayson equyte wher loue fader sone knowest thou ne iupiter thy sone ben thou haddest ben yet grete derkenes languysshyng sygnefye aduocat iupiter loueth hys owen fader furthermore praye thou wilt pea yf thou wille hym good yet leste wille hym harme ner encombrauce sholde sone vaynquysshyd answerd
