bataill saturne iupiter ther fader sone sone agaynst fader ther loste nature fayr recomaunded propertes fader sought blood engendryd promysid grete yeftes vnto myghte take hym batayll rygourous harde wrought foughte well iupiter archas soueraynly noble iupiter enploied hardly swerd temprid stele smote doun sheldes helmes cutte heedes armes man myght resiste hys prowes inuyncible made tremble moste hardiest ther made resorte go abacke auaunced self power vertu brak wynges batayle strength entrid encountryd many tymes saturne fader well power puyssance greue hym wel saturne caste hym gaf hym grete stroke greuous horions yet wold neuer smyte agayn said hym ofte time ala fader wherfore sekest thou theffusion blood thy sone thy seruaunt thou hast cause persecute shal enploye myn hand vpon beware take fyance archadiens ffor yf may haue gete power thou shalt fynde lytyll pyte ne mercy etc saturne notwythstandyng fayr wordes wold neuer refrayne ire smote euer vp iupiter also fiersly mocht iupiter alle stroke toke non hede sette lityll ther wel concyence fight smyte fader yet allewey torned stroke cocience occupie trenchant swerd vpon crete fermly euery strook wyth faute dyed newe blood enforced hym self shewe hit saturne faught ayenst hym vayn hym thyng inpossible alle thynges saturne toke regarde ner ensample crye grete aboute iupiter armes gretely exercysid ground coueryd theffusion blood dede bodyes laye oon vpon beheded smyten pecys right hard sore batayle saturne enuolupped obstynacion blood men wetyng armes cours large woundes iupiter maad vnto myght modere yre ner herte hys eyen blynde ire sawe nought ryght euydent domayge sought propre moyen whiche put royame dowbtyd ayenst whiche entendid resiste eschewe myght phowe iupiter vaynquysshid batayll ayenst saturne fader saturne fledd see batayll iupiter sauved often tymes saturne among glaiues tharchadiens dide good ayenst euyll many crete fought herte knowyng saturne meuid cause warre howe well put handes werke yet alleway variacon amonge cause losse right grete nombre peple doubtyd iupiter power withstande fight suche wise wold haue yf felte querele good maner bataill demenyd grete preiudyce saturnyens iupiter put hym self deuoyr vnto fader ofte tymes cryed ere shold wythdrawe hym er batayll went worse lost wythstood hys stroke grete whyle awaytyng wold conforme conuerte hym self fro euyll oppynyon last whan iupiter toke hede sawe wold wyse hym opende desployed hys vertu grete myght armes swerd maad suche affray vnto aduersaryes brekyng helmes hewyng harnoys manere man hauyng alday susteyned foot grete stroke peysant saturnyens manere champion ffresshe newe strookes redowblid thus hit semed vnto saturnyens multiplieng horions stroke strength puissance iupiter began norissh growe hys well doyng vayllyance gaf vnto tharchadyens strengthe vpon strengthe vnto enemyes grete losse blood also lyf ther ground bedewed newe blood ther ded body coueryd newe ded men ther chare saturne smyten peces saturne held longe bataile also longe might wold endure wise wold flee coclusion whan men sawe thynge wente allewey euyll worse began flee torned back fledde saturne torned fledde also like wise tho folowed chasse asperly dedly som slayn way sauyd hem self amonge saturne nyhe poursiewyd archas tharchadyens leyser retorne crete dryuen force tyll cam vnto porte see ther sauyd hym self moyen shippe ther fonde ther wente vnto see wyth fledde sore greuyd anoyed moght speke etc thus thys batayll ended fader sone whan arch sawe saturne sauyd see retorned iupiter hys fader assemblid peple told hym tydynges also ouer assemblid counceil wete iupiter shold doo counceyll oppynyon iupiter shold goo crete wold make hym kynge sayyng goddes shewyd clerly wold shold succede kynge royame wherof fader fled fro also moche heed counceill accorded iupiter wente crete space tyme resseyuyd kynge ffor cytezeyns durst agaynsaye hit moche wiste neuer wher saturne become well cibel vesca maad grete sorowe infortune saturne allewey torned theyr sorowe gladnesse coronacion iupiter sente iuno began iupiter regne desirybuyng departyng vnto archadyens tresours hys fader wherof grete ioye gladnes cause sayen poettes iupiter geldyd fader caste genytoyrs see engendryd venus saye castyd tresours hys fader belyes men wherof engendryd alle delectacion whyche comparyd lykenyd vnto venus etc phw acrisius doughter named dane whiche shette tour moche answer shold haue sone whyche shold torne hym stone etc dayes whan iupiter crete flourysshid honour strength prowesse nd vaylliance cyte arges regned ryght myghty kynge acrisius doughter dane beshitte kepte tour ffor knowe genealogye kynge acrysius partye hit noted iupiter born archade damoysell named ysis cam sone named epaphus epaphus engendryd sone doughter sone named belus regned partye egypte doughter name libye dwellyd affryque conceyuyd sone named busiers vnhumayn tyraunt shall said dedes hercules belus engendrid two sone danau egistus danau fifty doughters egistus many sone thise sone doughtres conioyned geder maryage wenyng egistus right well haue maried sone deceyued wenyg ffor danau enuye couetyse haue succession maad doughters trayterously shold murdryd alle fyfty sone said egistus fyrst nyght theyr esponsailles slepte concentid foule horrible cryme synne exept oon allone named ypermestra whiche stedfast herte pyte ffor whan shold haue persecutid husbond linceus saued hym lyf mercifully also conceyued seed sone named aba kynge arges engendryd kynge acrysyus wherof maad mencion begynnyng chappitre parentes progenytours kynge acrysius ryght puyssant rychesse named hym self poure ffor chyldren oon doughter whyche named dane haue sone wente day day temple oracle goddes ther made many prayer sacrefices ynowhe fastynges almesses suffrage alle thynges myght helpe ner brynge exaudycion accompllysshement desire wyf cam vnto bareyn yeres alle hope haue ony chyld maale confortyd hym dane doughter sette hys loue gretly pleasance beholde purposyd neuer noman shod haue ner wedde yf moste noble vayllyant man world moche world thinge pardurable loue lityll enduryng purchas kynge acrysius ffor loue dane grewe ampliacion naturell ielowsie wente hym thoracle god belus old grauntfader serchyng shold destynee doughter dide hym answerd shold come sone shold torne hym stone etc answer acrysius began falle grete loue doughter retornyd sorofull pensyf hows becam melancolik takyng ioye ne plaisir ony thyng sawe doughter yonge sawe often tymes otherwhile cruelte tyme pite remors trowed transformed stoon hym destine shold born doughter meuyd hym cruelte suche wyse often tymes determyned wold put deth spille blood ende remedye infortune whan take hand glayue wherwyth wened slee nature began medle put hym betwene bothe cruelte maad hym condescende pyte put way glayue late shedyng blood come owne blood whiche shold come succession crowne whiche auncyent progenytours ordeyned fore etc saye verite kyng acrisyus then forth toke reste trauerse many syghis coude assured doughter grewe becam woman passyng fayr right well adressid many kynges grete ertheli lordes desired haue mariage wold endowe noble crownes kynge acrisius refused requyred ymagyned doughter grete beawte might taken away rauysshed whiche myght auenture haue sone shold torne hym stone ende eschewe parcill daunger thoughte wold make tour strengest world tour shold doughter closed shette duryng lyf wyth comyng ony man ffor ielous leuyd well whan sawe ende sent werkemen forgiers stele copper alle partyes brought hem vnto stronge place alle enuyronned wyth water entre oon place etc whan brought theder werkemen sayd wold haue tour made alle copper wyth gate departyd tour put four twenty men armes kepe tour yf hyt nede werkemen bargayned kyng acrisyus make tour gate sette hande werke towr maad processe tyme whan alle achieued acrisyus brought theder doughter latyng knowe entencion also sone tour sayd doughter hit comen vnto knowleche serchyng thy prosperyte god belus haue ben aduertised shall come sone whiche shall conuerte torne stone thou knowest euery man naturelly coueytyth desireth thenduryng lyue lyf loue passyng well thynge world moche sauf lyf certayn lyf toucheth ner herte thy loue wherfore sekyng requyryng remedyes ayenst myn predestynat infortune wolde neur gyue maryage ony man hath required desired also thende generacion descende thy body thou sholdest haue knowleche man duryng lyf haue forgid tour copper wille thou closed shytte therin man see pray doughter accorde vnto desire take pacyence thys place passe thy tyme shall accompanye many noble virgynes shall gyue vnto alle thou canst mayst thenke etc whan noble damoysell dane vnderstode fader behelde tour copper kepe shitte faste therin conciderid shold neuer marye duryng lyf fader kynge sore troubled thynges grete bitternesse sorowfull herte began wepe said ala fader born vnder vnhappy constellacion marteresse prisonner ende myn yeres yonge tyme pryson stone symet tour copper laton suche wise shold dwelle therin perpetuelly fader hast thou thought thou enterpretest euyll sentence god belus sayng shall born sone shall torne stone ffor sentence ought none thynge vnderstande shall haue sone shall regne shall torne stone saie shall putte thy sepuliure beholde symplesse shall hit hold thus enfermed shitte tour doughter answerd acrisius thou interpretest prenosticacion god belus liketh thy ioye prouffyt hit lieth sore herte yf thou haue sone shall putte deth iugement ne wythsaye ayenst thy fader lorde mayster ouer thou shalt abyde eyther loue otherwyse thys conclucion whan dane sawe myght contente ferfull fader wyse sage agreed accorded playsyr sayng hyt mouth wyth herte kynge sente virgynes also olde matrones alle royame aboute delyuerid doughter vnto accompanye serue kepe maad hem shette closed toke leue comandyng vpon payne deth ne souffryd ony man come speke wyth doughter oute wytyng knowleche whan thus doon retorned cyte arges assemblid fourty stronge woman whiche gaf wage sowldye sente hem kepe gate entre tour aroos renomee thynges grete soun noyse grece full meruaylles ther kyng ne prynce ne complayned losse youth fayr dane holden named fair alle grekesses doughter kynge etc phow iupiter gyse messanger brought vnto tour darrayn damoyselles dane many iewels faynyng cam iupiter tour moyen acrisyus thought ouercome pdestynat infortune well cased doughter seur place alle world spacke tour compassion coplayned hit moche spoken caas iupiter eeres full therof onely eeres also herte ffor heryng recomendacion thexcessiue perfeccion virgyne dane amourous gretli desirously like mariage hym iuno consumed began alle herte thenke whan maner myght come see damoysell dane moche thoughte studyed mater ther none thynge wold ner deuyses men saue spake pryson dane spak gladly deuysed good coueytyng instantly well psence iuno wise whiche said many tymes wold goddes wold gyue hym grace power brynge damoysell dane tour etc mene deuyses iuno doubte began fele firste sparklis ielousie castyng infynyte curse malediccions vpon dane vpon sowen tydynges fore husbond couert stomack openly presence husbond shewyng euydently thataynte ielowsie notwithstondyng iupiter ne lasse desirous see dane fore malediccions ne curse myght lette ne withdrawe affeccions whiche grewe ende fonde hym self surmounted ther contynence founden diffinycon deuise entencions conclusion concluded go vnto gardyens kepars damoysell dane wold bere vnto largely many owches gold iewels wyth monye gold wold torne hem yeftes acorde hym late hym entre tour dane sente iewellers tht wonte serue fader saturne maad hem make moste ryche bagues owches euer seen thought whan werkmen made apartye iupiter toke hem charged hym euyll clothed lyke ben seruaunt allone departed crete drewe hym arges moste secretli myght wente cam sechyng tour darayn whiche fonde euenyng sawe walles shynyng cam vnto gate fonde many matrones syttyng dore recreacion etc whan iupiter comen salewed matrones said vnto noble dame good nyght come yow tour thys noble stronge facion ffayr sone said eldest ye contre moche ye knowe name tour knowe ye certaynly hit named tour darayn propre place kyng acrisius hath make kepe doughter virgyne dane whiche accomplisshed vertues honorable manyers lyke alle thys worlde poure mayde moche tour seeyng hit imprenable ony assault well strength place hit founded hit nyghe cyte arges whyche right stronge considered hym self come see mayde coude obteyne moyen woman thus answerd old woman thanke good aduertisement moche beholden vnto yow shall yet say vnto yow yf hit plese yow sent vnto damoyselles place fro right myghty kynge iupiter crete delyuere certayn presentes behalue wherfore concyderid ffor yf hit knowen faute shold put ffyre perauenture yf ye founden kyng cometh often tymes hether wolde put yow deth wherfore pray yow hit please yow excuse v yenst maystre comprysyng answer iupiter fonde nought soughte helde hym ner dyspayre dyde hope remembrid beggar shold go away one warnyng sayd vnto olde woman begynnyng answer dame ye well yf ye fere drede kyng whiche meruayll fauour tye madame concideracion wordes ye may see lyf deth ye may ligtly make iugement yf humylite condescende knowleche pyte haue yow disposing self dahger might sure nyhe ieoparde whiche ye may saue recomendacyon maad yow presence poynt entreprised delyuere tour helde self right ewro happy cause hye enterpryse seeyng parels fynde self syn wote neuer may saie self ffor moneth vpon moneth weke vpon weke day vpon day name hath domynacion ofte tymes hath constraynd rauysshed yet traunce desire speke yow ymagyne shold come poynt also fynde mercy yow pray requyre yow right humbly amerous yefte mercy ye acorde thus doyng ye shall mercy self haue pyte yonge day whiche ye haue consentyd lese folyssh fantasy kynge fader ye knowe well lyf shal suffre yow maried ony man hit possible fader shall lyue longe ye ffor stronge membres hard boistous also ye ought conceyue yf ye wyll beleue lyf hath welthe ne playsanse playsances come vnto peple syght beholdyng dyuerce thynges woman syngulerly haue pryncypal plaisus husbondes generacon lignyes ye ne may come yf ye haue mercy self hit consait knowleche man hath lyf world ffor moche ye obeie complaise folish comandement fader kynge acrisius ye shall woman loste beyng place hit possible take haue pacience hard thynge vnto yonge herte put prison oute demerite knowe humayn affeccions vnderstande naturelly euery creature loueth prouffit fore prouffit ayenst prosperite vtilite ye shitte inne may ye haue loue vnto hym whiche cause two euillis lasse euyll chese syn ye fele yowe condempned vnto ende dayes fader dowte ye hys ende ofte desired myschef sake meschief may ye oute grete charge conscience thynketh better hit yow dyuerce facions fynde manere yssue go place take husbonde man noble puyssant wold entreprise carye yow awey secreth wyf contrey moyen ye shall delyuered fro payne ye ye shuld eschewe deth fader lasse euyll ye shold fleyng folissh comandement abyde poynt wher hath putte yow madame ala thynke ye hereon honour helthe haue sayd yow seruaunt yf hit please yow departe place ye shall fynde man redyer kepe yow conduyte gyue self vnto noble comandementes furnissh wyll power bereth allewey remembrance yow deppest place mynde slepyng see yow wakyng thynke yow haue neuer reste self ner neuer shall haue yf hit plese yow fortune destynee happe vnhappe come yow yf ye take vnto mercy fynde grace anenst yow shall moste happyest happy yf ye otherwyse hit may sayd among vnhappy none shall go fore whan suche fortune shal come rygour shall take hit pacience noblesse see yow allewey require yow herte pryued ne put yowr herte moche hit toucheth alle tonges men saye ner expresse quantite loue haue yow pronounce propre name sterres heuene loue allewey thoughtes laboureus en sighis anguysshous ofte tymes grete fere gaf lityll fors etyng iupiter ete lasse bodyly spirituelly traunces doubtances feeres answer whiche coude glose thyng prouffyt saauf oonly hopid dane shold discouuere hit vnto damoysselles suche wyse darrain wyth damoysell dane whyche engendryd noble persens longe dured ffeestoyng iupiter hit oure tyme wythdrawe dane toke leue iupiter dyde conueye hym secrete chambre damoyselles whan iupiter departyd entryd chambre accompanyed wyth olde woman maistresse whishe charge aboue sone olde woman pryuely chambre malicio sayde doughter telle tidynges must nedes knowe thinge messanger hath sayd yow dame answerd dane woll ye wete ye sayd olde woman answerd dane muste come hym self make raiport hath sayd many thynges tenthe part mynde doughter said olde woman thinke well comen hether wyth cause hath sayd yf ye haue mynde telle leste abideth resteth mynde dame answerd dane ye knowe well neuer mystrusted yow secretenes myn herte yow hath alwey ben open wyll make newe customes shorte mater nameth hym seruant iupiter iupiter self raport hath maad grete othes hath maad thyse presentes yeftes speke dede hath shewyd lose tyme hath requyred wyf whiche haue yet consentyd haue taken day gyf answer morn hopyng take counceyll therfore pray yow ye counceylle haue answere shall haue ye knowe haue suffrid yeftes resseyued muste contentid som maner fayr speche wyse olde woman ben tyme hous kynge melliseus seen iupiter tyme retorne conqueste ar hade pertye knowleche syn first day cam theder notwythstondyng doutyd persone moche men otherwhile ben like oon alway eye hym whan vnderstande dane told iupiter seure hit hys persone grete ioye saynge doughter certaynly knowe hym speke deuyse longe tyme past persone assure yow hit hath yow vnderstonde vnto regarde counceylle yow yf ye take hym vnto husbonde saye none wyse yow oon vailliantest men world entrepryses ben right hye yf doughter moste best manerd world ther man leuyng wold gyue sonner vnto hym yf hit plesid hym take ye see wythstandyng symple aray goodly man noble ryche wyse kynge ye fele self corage yf ye wole vse obserue comandement fader ye may hym hold consistorie ne parlament yf ye wyll absente yow place good moyens ther man iupiter may helpe yow counceylle yow neyther oon ne chese ye take beste waye etc moder sayd dane shold chese self ther neyther wytte ne entendement take shold chese ne discerne good ywell shall put hit deliberacion wole ye knowe tour wold fayn bee myn honour sauyd honour sauyd felawshyp wyth thys cam alle damoyselles hous sayd made right good chere theyr ghest thus faylled secrete deuyses dane aged woman damoyselles wente fette theyr iewels newly presented hem departed eche porcion saynge kynge iupiter none like amonge moste large honourable kynge kynges mayde dane toke beddes theyr chamber iupiter liyng bed hour fonde hym self surmountyd wyth couetyse loue constraynd aryse loke wyndowe beholde yf day approched liftyng eyen agayn sterres heuene rauysshed herte remembrance fayr dane sayd noble dane hath beaulte sterre shynyng ye shyne souerayn clerenes ala ye houre payne endure cause ye knewe grete ieopardye paryllous paas haue put attayne loue vnkendenes may haue place yow desdayn rygour fiersnes whiche ben myn enemyes enuenymed mortall venym dane remembre self thou fortune haste couryd alle myn affayres coure present nede word complaynt cessed gaf clamour fledde grete short tyme kynge troos aduertysid wherof affrayed cyte well garnysshid peple also made redy resiste aduersaryes suche dyligence whan herd tydynges morenyng foure oures yssued troye wyth xxx thousand fyghtyng men drewe vnto place frygyens entryd noble kynge tros compaygnye two sone whome eldest callyd ylion cam doun heuen palladiu yonger callyd gammedes two sone vayllyant hardy comen feld requyred theyr fader troos departe arme two wolde graunt hys vawarde preue theyr myght vpon theyr enemyes troos considering separacion hys peple fowled put back myght socowryd whan hit sholde come stroke acorded request ij sone toke vnto xij thousand fyghtyng men ylion gammedes thankyd kynge troos fader toke leue hym went forth fyghtyng men suche wyse mile fore batayll kynge kyng troos sued batayll ij sone ylion gammedes rydars betwene bothe comysid reporte kynge tros whan sone founden tantalus enemye also ij noble sone fore hem diuerse espies way tar sente diuerce place espies raportyd demanded councell oppynyon shold suffre oste reste yet good houre shold breke faste lityll lightly thende haue better longer breth also corageo also cause hem better awakyd shold departe goo assaylle theyr enemyes oppynyon semed god vnto fyue sone kynge signyfied theyr entencion ryders vnto theyr fader troos wythdrewe hem take lityll theyr reste gaf charge vnto kept wacche awake whan sawe tyme lityll restyd whan awakyd callyd eche man shold take armes folowe troians obeyed knowe well hit tyme make redy lightly neuer ioyous ther whan knewe shold go batayll ete dronke attemperatly full oon good wyll garnysshid hem wyth theyr armes shewid oon wold fight batayll confunde theyr enemyes menassid euyll recountre houre mone shone right clere whiche shynyng light ylion gammedes putte theyr peple araye fayre ordenance whan take shorte refection began marche toward put hem self fore came nyghe mone light guydes wer herd kept wacche theyr enemyes soughte whiche fledde vnto tentes kynge tantalus awoke hym tolde hym troians come tassaylle hym seen hem grete noumbre tantalus beleuyd lightly hys wacche defferryd hys arysing nede longe abyden troyans cam vpon ofte smote doun right vpon ffrygiens desmesurably redoundyng stroke cam fill eeres tantalus whyche aroos sprange foot terrybly affrayed wyth affraye awaked frygiens generall mortell woundes cryes smyten anguysshously vnto deth comynge thus troians domaged gretly enemyes cause many garnysshid wyth armes whyche smyten doun gleyues troyans beten doun labouryng mortally aglowtyng blood wyhtstondyng well answerd gammedes ben comen crete correcte sone sette yow agayn siege shall doo may doo power furnyssh fighte frely wyth oute doubtance feer vnto ende reproche inposid vnto v shall sende somone sone first ony swerd drawen strook smyten thende yelde hym vnto obeyssance come amende mesdedes gammedes dide come troians consent saturne sette hem ordynance batayle whan doon sente oon auncyent knyghtes noble man vnto iupiter gaf hym charge make somacion suche sayd fore troyan departyd oost comandement gammedes dyd moche presentyd fore iupiter sayd hym iupiter thou oughtest knowe euery sone oweth obeyssance vnto fader thou doost contrarye thynges shewest thou art sone kynge perdicion thou despysest thy fader stede reuerence thou hast hym hate thou makest hym warre thou sholdest holde hym loue thou puttest hym grete dishonour thy self wher thou art holde bounden hym worshippe iupiter shall gyue absolucion thy lif dwellyng venym shall excuse thy synne thou art enemy thy fader caas greuous theyr mercy ne excusacion yf hyt departe fro naturell clemence thy fader beholde iupiter beholde ende thyn insurrexion alle lawe po ityf alle lawe wreton condempne vnto deth curse anathematyse hit grete pyte thou art goodly yong man knowe thy regne may longe dure thou shalt shortly punysshid thou wenest perauenture time gamynedes oon soones troye helpe saturne thy fader twenty thousand fyghtyng men whiche meneth thou retorne mercy thy fader yeld hym hys royame alle excusacions set part messanger answerd iupiter yf suchon ye saye wyth iuste rayson ye might gyue sentence condempnacions vpon ought bothe parti e trowe yf gamynedes ye haue spoken herd myn excuse wold myn enemy answer yow loue fader saturne moche fader saye yow part hath often tymes wyllyd putte deth shewyng hym self mortell fiers batayll troians oute fere dide grete prowess manly conduyte saturne gamynedes saturne mette iupiter often tymes sought grete stroke iupiter knewe hym well wold neuer abyde sayng wold neuer sette agayn amended spack ynowe prowess oon souerainli held theyr deuises egle spack moche hym iupiter nyght toke pece cremesin sa yn conteynyng yerd half square made theryn remembrance egle golde sette hit spere made banyere sayng wolde bere banyere alle bataylles euer vnderstood egle hit tokene hym shold abide victoryous hys enemyes shold souerain kyng crete like egle kynge alle fowlys phow iupiter disconfited agayn kyng saturne bataylle saturne putte flight see svche deuyses kyng iupiter nyght whiche passid moste ioyously coude visityd hurte men confortyd concluded ixion day folowyng centaures shold haue bataylle foughten day afore shold reste slept grene restid hym vnto tyme centaures put hem aray wente hors back dide iupiter leuer deyed haue ben ydell tyme saturne slept ner lachesse founde hym gamynedes iupiter seur shold met alle assayled theyr enemyes agayn adoubid arayed beste wise couthe aboute sonne rysing rengyd wente vnto oost iupiter encouragyng eche smyte fyghte assaylle theyr mortell enemyes hardyly auenge blood theyr felaws dede bataylle day make shorte troians strongly achanffid appetyte vengeance firste felde wherof grete ioye hertes maad right grete cry thys ioye anon vnto hem abaysshid doon sodeynly iupiter centaures herd theyr crye toke banyer wyth egle gold theyr speres theyr sheldes wyth ioyous soune trompes clarion tabour prickyd forth theyr hors whiche redounded ayer reimyng helde heuen ne erthe vpon theyr enemyes began fighte certes whan troians sawe centaures mountyd horsback rennyng wynde aferd affrayed wend neuer haue seen light day wel toke corage abode centaures fought myghtily among hem eche oon bare erthe troian wyth poynt spere among gammedes born doun erthe among som hurte parte releuyd hurtyng wyth oute hurte whan gammedes felte hym self among hors foot herte terryble angry sayd wold shortly auengyd anon aroos lightly tooke swerd seyng centaure smyten hym doun doyng merueyllous armes among grete meyne folk myghtily wythstood vnmesurable strookes gaf vnto hym grete strook lenyng right side haue smyten troian gaf hym grete wounde whyche astonyed drowe hym doun hors hym self leepe vp sadel centaure named eson yonge afterward fader iason conquerd golden flees whan receyuyd strook gammedes gyuen made cry grete x centaures cam rennyng deffended fro presse castyng doun oon bete doun troians caste hem doun sparpelid blood place died reed fond eson gamynedes oon nyhe seeyng gamynedes approuued hym self conduyte gouerne hors seeyng theyr felaw put doun hors passingly supprisid grete yre mortall yre ascryed gamynedes vnto deth troians approchid beyng fought manly agayn centaures centaures castyng smytyng gamynedes troians dide theyr power defende hym put hem self iupart deth many slayn many sore hurt centaures strong huge grete lothly troians courage body place gamynedes shewid ynowh prowesse valeur well deffended hym awhile ende fortune hym aduerse suche wyse suffryd many assault seen put caste ground mo thousand troians beheld side sawe saturne torne playn desconfiture sawe troians lete hym put aback put deth wyth oute turnyng fyghtyng agayn alle breke turne back also aboute hym gaf hit vp fledd knowyng disconfiture remedye ner recowerance allone myght bere ne abide batayll put hym self flight fled oder susteynd wel myght porsuyt centaures maad vpon men ende guyded hem vnto poort theyr shyppyng saturne alle dyspayed entryd shyppe wyth grete losse troians gammedes entryd ryght angry dysplaysant reherce entre shyppys oon partye troians left peryshyd see another partye peryshyd swerd toke shyppyng iupiter yxion thankyd theyr goddes gretly victorie concluded gyder wold yet poursuye theyr enemyes see moche yet grete nombre yxion sayd hit expedient brynge hem plain vttrance moche fortune wyth ende shold neuer reassemble agaynst iupiter accorded poursuyte gretly anoyed hym semed taryed longe yet shold tarye yf entryd see myght wyth dane day promysed wyhtstondyng hopyng allewey excuse hym vnto made hym redy hastely goo poursuyt enemyes sent maryners went temple ther dedyfied vnto god mar phow iupiter sacrefied egle poursuyd troians strong batayle agaynst gammedes ivpiter sone temple egle entryd also sette hym awter whan iupiter sawe many thoughtes took egle maad sacrefice anon cam tydinges mariner redy went temple recomanded hym vnto god mar cam maryners made thyng redy wente see accompanyed wit centaures two thousand men crete sayled enemyes desired troians fledde force maad sayle couthe two dayes iupiter often tymes wy hed hym fayr dane thought longe taryeng shold noyous vnto whan two dayes past day folowing thre clock crete troye began mete gyders vpon see troye grete sorowe crete grete ioye tyme saturne troians durste retorne shame befalle discomfyt self dispayr passed wawes see drawyng eest whan gammedes aspied shyppes crete fro ferre supposid fyrst hit saturne taryed auere proces tyme whan ga ynedes sawe shippis comyng grete force nerre sawe banyere abandonned gyuen hit ouer ought abyde tarye euery man saue hym self gammedes wold fayn abyden bataylle proue yf fortunat happy see lande whan knewe wyll troians desired nothyng reste made drawe vp ankres sayle forth fleyng wythdrawyng crete also moche possible iupiter centaures seyng troians lyeng ancre began araye doube wyth theyr harnoys whan sawe theyr enemyes take vp theyr ancres began showte folowe pursuyt strong dured thre dayes thre nyghtes morenyng fourth day gammedes felaws aspyed lande troye sawe drewe porte wyth grete ioye sone entremedled wyth sorowe whan taken lande behelde sawe theyr enemyes foloweden cam porte arayd redy bataylle shame losse smote vnto herte gammedes suche facion ascryed sayd wyse vnto men mi brethern felaws fortune hath doon v grace whiche ben brought conduyt hether grace v lityll prouffit may playnly conceyue lo kynge iupiter whyche hath doon v grete shame chasse v vnto owen terrytorye shame shall hym wyll flee ouer holde bridell teth behoueth flee hit behoueth fighte force necessitee venge loss blood recouuer worship ben owen contre yf auenge v shall torne perpetuell dishonuer socours may fayle troians ben vpon walles gon vp hyhe edifice cyte beholde londyng ther make redy well come v well couragid neuer fare well late euery man enforce vertu strength hewen piece shall flee pray yow ye take courage abide two thinges happend while spack shewyd thise remonstrance vnto felawis troians aduertised comyng theyr men descendyng landyng theyr aduersaries disposid resiste wythstande iupiter men approchid port gamynedes lefte warnyng theyr blood iupiter wyth yxion centaures lete estemed vaynquisshid ouercome adressid ayenst kynge troos ylion folowyd well ben feblid eyer beyng see whyche lityll prou ited centaures grete huge stronge olifantes hard lyon aygre tygres tyme weder fayr cleer sonne shone fayr whan began medle hit fayr thyng see recountres good noyse cryes ther many spere tronchonnyd many arowe shotte many theyr puyssance wyht oute ende wrought fought wyth theyr enemyes makyng theyr glayues reed blood troians folowed grete force suche wyse faught alle day otherwhile afore somtyme behynde hit soo ende whan sonne began go doun gaminedes thenkyng grete losse desiryng recouure worshippe took terrible myghty axe enflamed right noble courage faught banyer egle gold strengthe smote doun oon side dismesurabli axe changed lightly colour cryed wyth hye wy troyes troyes ivpiter way eye banyer whan herd crye gammedes sawe hys exployt knewe hym wherof grete ioye sought man hym gaf ouer place ioiously addressid hym vnto hym sayde vayllyant troian thou hast shewde thy prowesse day thou manyfestestt shewyst thy self grete fete armes grete bruyt thou arte seche amonge vayllantes troye presume vayllyant armes thou moche thou art haste assayllyd crete haue poursiewed hether thou hast assaillid fought wyth puyssance ayenst puyssance late v fighte body ayenst body take hit may gete hit gammedes wyth worde lyfte vp axe castyng eyen iupiter herd made hym answere happy wreus kyng crete knowe thou art worthy haue grace fortune thou art wyse stronge thou seest fortune wyth neuerthelasse thou enhaunsest thy self aboue alowe preyse moche thou dost worship honour thyn enemye dispreysest hym ymagynest hath corage hert knewe thou thou doste thy self honour worshyp mespryse blame another man man ought auaunce hym self wolde hyt plesid goddes thy fader saturne whiche beleft see myn entent helpe shold haue reson shall come ther yf hit possible shold recouuerid hurtes loss yf myghte adaunte ouercome wyth oute wordes gamynedes late fle axe smote iupiter iupiter couueryd shelde whiche smyten two piece cuttyng axe iupiter enuertued self day sousteyned spared poys fete armes comandyd folk shold lete hym allone gamynedes moche allone place approuyd self ayenst axe gamynedes employeng steell swerd best wyse hym possible thus began bataylle two champion crete troy bothe right expert
