woundes dede toke hym hys axe mene grete wounde ryght arme myght haue put hym deth yf wolde make short processe whan taken hys wepen hym pytie hym sauyd hys lyf dyde take hym foure hym foure centaures anon hit began wexe derke nyght toke day light wherfore hit behoued hem take reste leue feete armes troians wythdrewe theyr cyte crete vnto porte see phow kynge troos ylion sone made grete sorowe gammedes wyste wher becomen iupiter wente see goo arges whan troos ylion wythdrawen abode yate vnto tyme troians comen agayn cyte knewe gammedes becomen whome sore desired haue founden bataylle troians entrid ther man cowde telle kynge tros sone gammedes whether lyue ded whan sawe mo men lefte felde retorned pallays sorowyng gretely anoyed sente comen agayn fro crete enquyred tydynges wyth sone touchyng sone answerd euenyng prees amonge hys enemyes wyst comen hym touchyng tydynges crete told hym sped theyr iourne ayenst egle appered vnto iupiter ouercomen strength centaures wyste saturne becomen tydynges gaf vnto kynge troos sorow vpon sorow ylion also teres fill doun fro theyr eye especyall ylion wept sore bewayling broder manyre ala broder ala gaminedes belefte glorie troyes maleureus vnhappy saturne whiche hath fayled thy nede lefte yf thou haddest comen agayn geder shold haue put v deuoir haue auenged thy losse shold haue assayed bodyes fraternall loue haue recouured thyn honour art thou perisshid parell harde doleance sorow befalle saye thy mesaduenture myshappe preiudiciable vnto hous troye ilion fayr sone answerd troos oon aduersite hit behoueth abasshid warre non aduenture haue ferme courage warre gyueth day victorie oon morn taketh hit away gyueth hit nother putte h eche vertuous manly man vnto singuler deth ought effrayed yf gamynedes ded bataylle yf taken remedie hit expedyent eyther avenge deth socoure hym oure enemyes ben lityll nombre shall morn fyght agayn late goddes theyr wylles v shall discorage otherwyse lyon noble troye conforted wordes kynge troos confermed go morn assaylle theyr enemyes while thinges comenyng cyte iupiter felde made grete chyere wyth yxion centaures beyng sette soper vpon ground alle aboute grete stoon iupiter sente fecche gammedes made hym soupe wyth gammedes sore meuyd herte grete troble wel toke lightly refection wyth felte ryght grete ache smerte woundes recomanded iupiter hym sayng vayllyantyst man euer seen among moste vayllyanst troyes moche mercy late wyth fader descended crete gladly planted name worship yf fortune wold haue souffryd hym shalle warre fore troyes shal entre agayn morn see goo putte execucion thyng lyeth sore herte wyll well ye knowe haue entencion go vnto royame arges vnto tour darrain deliuere acording promesse tour fayr dane kynge acrysius holdeth fast shytte wyth oute rayson conclusion plesid kynge yxion centaures moche herd spoken strength tour darrain thought wel argyens myghte holde agayn theyr strength whan eten entred theyr shippis thought among thynges woundes hurte also gammedes afterward leyd hem doun strawe slepe aboute two oures fore day disancred departyd secretly troian knowleche therof morn betymes whan kyng tros ylion yssued troyes bataylle rengid good ordenance fonde man haue doo alle ner coude see ner parceyue theyr enemyes coste see fer saylid fro port tyme sight thus grete sorow meruayll usly cam vnto place batayll ben buryed dede men tarye iupiter retorne vnto historie dane phow kynge acrisius whan sawe doughter dane grete chylde sente exyle put lityll vessell see aduenture fortune etc noble damoyselle dane abode childe seed iupiter said fore iupiter retorned contre abood passing longe hoope tht shold retorne strengthe peple shold lede roiame vnto promised hope mounted ofte tymes vnto hye wyndowes tour castyng eyen hether theder vpon mountaygnes weyes stretes awayte yf came myght see men armes peple warre oute ende alway eres epen herken yf might trompes ta clarion hope duryd longe vnto last day iupiter promisid sore complayned tyme abiding said vnto self wold come certes whan euen comen day sette comen ner herd tydynge hym whan sawe cam fruyt bely apperyd wente doun fro wyndowe hye tour alle rauysshyd dispayr entryd allone chambre ther began beholde bely sayde poure bely may lenger hyde haue couerd vnto tyme hopyng comyng iupiter day come past shold haue comen ther tydynge hym ala hath also forgoten art thou iupiter arte thou ded liue yf thou ded speke spyryte excusing thy defaute telle shall wyth thy seed yf thou lyue ryght euyll auenture holdeth art thou wery dane thou enforcest reynyng golde thou moche desiredest ala thou promysist thy loue gauyst hit vnto receyued yeft good gaf vnto myn herte like caas yet thou wenest shall iupiter loue frende art thou nature false men ypocrites payne deceyue poure woman late dishonour ala thou art oon verayly thou haste brought pardurable shame hast abandonned gyuen ouer malewreus man fals liar thow cursid thy rychesses acursid euer sawe euer putte shame myn ende approcheth may lenger hyde thy werkes shall childe become euery man shall see knowe trespaas ala fader shall put deth may faylle hit deth hit shall greue saue fruyt bere yet shall kepe hit well self auenture come may come therof etc thyse semblable wordes dane passid ouer nyght oute slepyng reste fro forth began alle melancolious toke sore herte fyll right greuous maladye whan maydens thyng knewe caas sawe euyll disposid signeffied hit vnto kynge acrisius cam kynge visite doughter betoke vnto cure fisicians medecines demanded maladye answerd hym presence dane grete childe short tyme shold deliuerd dane answerd fayllyd saye trouthe neuer knowen man deuyed caas moche possible hoping alwey liue knewe well fader wold dampne deth yf knewe childe alle maydens hous stryued agaynst maisters sayng well seurly kept tour man saue kynge spoken yf come inuysible syn receyuyd gouernance wherof kinge gretly abasshid sore wondryd whan kynge herd debate sawe state doughter sore troblid experyence sawe well semed dane wyth chylde trowed beleuyd better fisiciens excusacions maydens doughter knowe trouthe sente alle maydens place prison arges betoke dane kepyng woman comanded vpon payn deth shuld telle hym yf happend delyueryd chyld nay wyth certayn tyme whan dane sawe termes began falle wepyng kynge accrisius fro day forth cam euery day knowe dyde wept wyth oute cessing spack vnto herte bewayled loue complayned fortune sorowfully whan labouryd longe wepynges fayr eyen maad grete reed aboute xv dayes fore tyme chyldyng began remembre cause put tour goddes prenostykyd shold haue sone shold kynge arges remembrance confortyd lityll whan tyme cam ix monethis brought forth passing fayr sone whiche ladyes woman receyuyd named hym pers n signefied hit vnto kynge burthe chylde excusid put oute blame alle damoyselles sayde alle innocentes hir caas anone kynge acrisius knewe veryte doughter fayr sone herte sorowe ioye condempned deth dede comanded two marouners shold take moder child put hem lityll boot bothe allone shuld carye fer hie see shuld neuer man see ner haue knowleche marouners durste reffuse comandement kinge comandement wente vnto tour darrain toke dane sone perseus saide vnto damoysel charge praing humbly wold pardone aboute midnyght whan dane vnderstood shold caste see sone hope escape fro thys paryll mene fortune sone notwythstondyng tre e ran doun eyen wepyng tenderly toke leue ladyes damoyselles keping lete caryed vpon see making complainte pietous bewaylinges whan marouners brought vpon see lefte litill boote put lappe perseus fayr sone hastely mighte conduyte hye see oute mete drynke oute steer gouernail gafe ouer al wyndes ther many teer wepte among marouners dane perse yong childe maroners bewailed verray copassion tht see suche damoysel abandouned parill deth dane wepte coceyuing rigour fader fawte tht iupiter also perill whiche might resiste seus wepte blowing winde grosse aier see tendrenes might well suffre endure facon marouners retorned arges right disconfortyd damoyselle dane wente forth vpon wawes see gree wylle wyndes wawes right ferfull lefte hem ayer montaygnes wyndes blewe grete stormes lityl boot born caste vpon wawes often tymes dane wente supposid haue perysshid alwey hope fortune well hit happend aduersite caste see apulye naples founden auenture fisshar pyte charyte toke shippe sone brought londe moche hit grete nede tyme noble dane dede body half goon whan maronner brought lande toke rynge gold bare finger gaf hit good man prayng hym wold brynge hous myghte warme chauffe wyth chyld nyhe ded cold traunce maronner toke gold ryng broughte damoyselle lityll chylde hous made good fire broughte hem mete drynke asso e perseus felte ayer fire herte cam hym agayn began lawhe moder whan sawe alle sorowes torned nought toke hope fortune adoubid arayed sone colour cam agayn ete dranke shall saye fisshar behelde seeyng moche beawte like sawe neuer noon wente hym vnto court kynge naples tolde aduenture preising certainly beaute kinge sente hastely fecche kinge named pilonnus sone auncient iupiter whan dane come fore hym sodaynly waxe amorous demanded name contre cause aduentured see begynnyng excusid self alle thinges telle began wepe whan kinge sawe conforted said wold take wif beaute spak fayr graciously tolde hym lif doughter kinge acrusius shette tour iupiter deceyuyd fader putte see shall saye whan kinge pylonnus herd alle fortune damoysell pytye wedded wyth grete honnour dide norysshe perseus gate sone whiche named danu mater tarye torne agayn historie iupiter etc phow iupiter retornyng fro troyes see encountrid grete theef egeon whiche fought ouer came tydinges dane wherof passing sorowfull whan iupiter departid fro troyes afore sayd made marouners saylle rowe alle diligence withdrawe fro porte approuche crete knewe wel time promesse made dane expired tht displesid gretly might amende hit marouners dyde alle coude space day naturel day past ther roos tempest see terrible mesure hit bare many shyppys wyth theyr apparayll vnder water brake theyr sterne helmes drowned alle shyppys reseruyd shyppe wher iupiter wherfore wepte outragyously thys tempeste duryd two dayes two nyghtes sawe tyme heuen sonne ne mone ne sterres iupiter wyth hym wende neuer better haue dyed well escaped deth toke lande thyrde day whan tempest cessid thyng crete ner see europe occeane ferre knewe langage enhabyted porte cam ancre whan iupiter peple sawe dyuersite peple dwellyng porte theyr manyer lyuyng knewe fer theyr regyon iupiter disconfortyd suche wyse wysshed ner come see moche knewe wel myght accomplisshe promesse made vnto dane loue made many grete bewaylinges touchyng mater saye also complayned men lost storme tormente well complayned defaute promesse well whan felaws wete yxion centaures gammedes refresshid vytaylled well putte thynges poynt taken thynges necessarie theyr shippe disancred departid fro porte toke theyr waye eeste exployted day day moneth vpon moneth entryd see egee longe sayled whan egeon grete theef rouare whiche helde alle see disancred fro porte yle deserte acompanyed sixe galeyes thousand men armes cam fore iupiter apparayllyng bataylle intencion haue destroyed whan iupiter centaures sawe conduyte theef knewe lightly myght faylle bataylle sayng eche shold defende vnto deth longe hold parlament amonge garnysshed theyr armes displayed banyer egle gold displaing made grete ioye ben paradis tyme gamynedes wounde heled whan sawe eche man adoubed hym fighte sauf whiche prisonner cam kneled doun knee fore iupiter requyred hym right humbly wold comande deliuere hym harnoys helpe worshipp also defende lif promittyng trewe deuoyr iupiter toke vp gamynedes whan sawe hym meke hym self began sette loue hym suche wyse hit endured vnto deth made harnoys armes yolden sayng fro forth shall brethern felawis armes gammedes answerd hym wolde alway abyde dwelle seruaunt amonge deuyses egeon gallees aborded shippe iupiter escryed deth egeon fronte afore capitayne iupiter behelde hym knewe hym armes bare yet er ony strook smyten escryed hym sayd theef veray rouare pyrate darst thou escrye deth hym made tremble fle fore hym bataylle crete vnder regarde swerde dyed made reed wyth blood vnhappy tytannoys beholde see iupiter mortal enemye alle thy lignage thou lyke wyse art myn enemy arte come bataylle ayenst hit may well sayd shall renne eche vpon grete felonnye recountre shall right domageable late goddes doo theyr playsir whan egeon vnderstode iupiter sayd hym destroyar lignage herte surmountyd yre inpacience coude answere oon word grynyng wyth teth began smyte harde toward iupiter yf strook axe helde ben adressid ther neuer remedye lyf iupiter knewe foot warre whan sawe strook come auoyded hit haunsid glaiue charged hit vpon egeon seurly coude auoyde strook peysant astonyed made hym falle doun vpon plankes galeye made pirate theues grete crye fille vpon iupiter felawis gamynedes helde axe handes ydle dyde wrought vayllyantly puyssance dide centaures skarmusshe grete many dede partye iupiter partye pyrates laboured centaures died theyr galeyes blood theyr enemyes pyrates well x ayenst oon coude ner myght abide fore etc thus began mortell batayll pyrates centaures whan oon galeye fought longe myght another came thus iupiter gamynedes ynowh doo fighte faylled smote displaysir pyrates eche theyr stroke deth pyrate processe tyme egeon came gayn medle dismayed fulfild inpacience put hym prees fight moste strength alle dispayred wynne alle lose point bataylle terrible mortall galeyes closid shippe iupiter smote hit vnhapp ylfare moste parte slayn gamynedes iupiter entrid galeye kinge egeon foughte sore oon side enuie shold beste lefte oon man slain cast see reseruyd egeon whiche iupiter toke hand bonde honderd chaynes yron etc chaynes yron egeon acustome bynde prysonners vnto tyme doon wyll whan pyrates sawe myschyef ran vpon maystre ouercomen bounden wyth chaynes wonte tormente prysonners wyth entended saue self wythdrowe hem shippe iupiter sayng fought wyth men deuyllis vnhappy cam vnto handes iupiter oon shippe pirate sparklid abrood oon another whan centaures sawe sayde iupiter hit ought suffyse haue victorie enemye hit nede make poursuyt vnhappy theuys iupiter accorded entryd agayn shippe wyth gammedes egeon made maryners take cours agayn alleway memorie dane hit nedeth make longe deuyses bewaylinges iournees auentures yere long sayling see ende yere arryued royame ther fonde foure honderd hors whyche crete presentyd hym byen venue quene iuno wyf made hym grete chiere louyd hym wyth herte festyd hym presented hym horse put pryson egeon lete gammedes goo fre wold louyd gyder euer two brethern whan iupiter ben thre dayes toke foure honderd men moste puyssant made noble made hem knyghtes gyuyng eche oon hys horse taughte enformed foot armes discipline yxion centaures whan assemblid thousand pietons fotemen two hounderd archer compaygyne centaures knyghtes departyd fro crete fyften dayes retorn sente pluto ne neptune toke waye vnto cyte arges entencion haue rauysshid fayr dane fer goon whan encountrid mette oon citezeins arges noble man worshipfull recounted told hym lif dane moche demanded hym tidynges assured hym lif kynge acrisius caste see moche brought forth litill sone ayenst comandement whan iupiter herde caas infortune dane began sorowe sighe sore swete cam visage teres eyen callyd gamynedes yxion tolde hem viage broken kynge acrisius caste see made armee gamynedes yxion conforted hym best wyse coude brought hym agayn crete helde hym solitaryly laye wif iuno iuno aunte seres made good chere often tymes ofte came seres one axid cause hys sorowe behelde beaute allone dyde dyde moche doo wyth knewe flesshly conceyuyd seed doughter determyned wyll wold goo secylle conquerre contre wylling alwey ocupie hym self ony exercitees toke leue kynge yxion centaures shyppyng redy wente see cam secylle conquerd hit wyth yle lennos whan doon wente ytalye descended hous kynge ianus whyche receyuyd hym made hym grete chyer told hym fader saturne come newly dwelle therby souerainly louyd alle peple moche taughte hem laboure vynes cornes alle blode changed iupiter whan herde ianus spak hym fader saturne well wente see hym sawe hym fonde fader makyng foundyng newe cyte place stante capytole rome suche wyse submyttyd hym fader saturne toke hym grace made pee wyth hym also acorded hym shold enioye fro forth hys royame crete acorde makyng pee kynge ianus kynge euander dwellyd nyhe wete ianus cyte callyd laurence euander cyte beyng nyhe mount auentyn kynge ytalus cyracuse made tyme newe cyte named albe vpon ryuer tybre alle thyse kynges made grete chiere pee fader sone thus iupiter abidyng acqueynted hym wif kinge euander named nychostrate moche right experte science nygromancie charmes sortes lernyd science iupiter toke leue fader saturne neyhebours lefte saturne maryed agayn vnto woman callid philiris sone callid picus fader kynge famus husbonde quene fatua hercules amorous hit shall said second book retorned crete ther fond wif deliueryd sone vulcan acqueyntyd amite seres deliueryd hys doughter named proserpine wherof iuno ryght euyll plesid contente complayned iupiter dishonour iupiter sette nought ther laughed ioyous doughter hys sone hys doughter meruayllously fayr wlcan sone foull courbbackyd well liue pee iuno maryed seres vnto noble man named siccam gaf hem royame secylle cyte siracuse sente hem dwelle proserpina hit longe sente sone wlcan yle lennos whome betoke gouerne thre men callyd berroutes sceropes pyragmon thyse thre men kept hym well cam cage man ryght enhauncyd courage lerned alle science especiall nygromancie geomancie promancie made many meruayllous thynges beleue wherfore wyll tarye hym iupiter wyll trete sone perseus moche hym cam alcumena phow quene meduse cam athene worshyp temple goddesse pallas kynge neptunus wax amerous deceyuyd hym tyme whan iupiter dwellyd pesibly kynge crete sone vlcan waxed lerned craft nygromancie lande esperye passid world kynge named porcus man right grete enterpryse whyche esperiens callyd god see spaygne auncyently named esperye sayd kynge lefte thre doughtres oon eye poetes saye saye pryncipall charge vnto vanytees world therfore callyd gorgonnes saye cultyueresses labourer erthe moche entended vnto vyces behelde erthely thynges thyse doughtres oon named meduse ewryale thyrde scenno meduse eldest succeded thempyre royame poetes saye hede serpent gyuyng vnderstande sonuerainly wyse subtyl deth kynge porcus meduse gouuerned hyely royame held pyrates men warre begynnyng toke hauntyd see ewrope foot wyth right grete tryumphe descended aday porte attenes sente vnto kynge neptune requyre wold graunte vnto might entre cyte worshippe temple goddesse pallas whiche newly maad neptune dide grete honour vnto messangers meduse accorded vnto shold entre cite temple forseen shold haue none saue damoyselles whan meduse herde answere kynge neptune concluded wold go temple wherof grete renomee companyed many damoiselle richely arayed hit tryumphe see entryd temple cyte ther torned stone men behelde also woman among specially quene named yde bi hit vnderstande meduse excellente beaute passing ryche behelde gafe hem self ouer perfitly couoyte beaute rychesses therfore wryte poetes torned stone dispose gyue delices world ben lykned compared vnto hard stone wherof may good come thus meduse entryng athene conuertyd torned many men stone moche neptunus herd tydynges desiryng see quene wente hym temple contemplacion longe beholde whan felte hym couoytous loue said hym self shold wif shold neuer escape hym meduse longe space contemplacion duryng neptune desired beaulte herte iuged hym sholde come entencion anon herte made iugement lityll debated consideryng excellence another iugement trauersid ourded entendement constraynd hym saye wordes folowe ala matyer sorow right grete enflamyng payne ben ben brennyng loue longe space tyme begynne fynde somany sighes payne wote neuer may tyme come vnto lady requyre wyf shynyng beaulte right haboundaunt rychesses lackyth beholdeth amonge while prayer hit may happen well loue may torne herte make thaliance men saye loue hurteth man yf hit eyen yf eyen made see shal saye desire shall happe well wher put oute herte desir wote neuer thynke thought may abusion myn abuse may well reuersid myn eyen perauenture wene see see myn eres ymagyne yet ben deef finde self grete playne vayne ataynt yet superfluous errour ony man may haue whan see lady excellente beaute riches reson telleth comen hether whan beholde allone wyth oute men cyte shall agayn saye shall requyre wif hath deuocion yf accorde requeste werke shal doo well yf gaynsaye stande hit muste vse force auctorite royall thus whan neptune cam thys conclucion meduse aroos fro contemplacion lokyd right fayr neptune wente dide reuerence prayd wold goo ryall palays refresshe meduse thankyd hym curtoisie saide mighte well tarye tyme whan neptune vnderstood wyll retorne wyth oute areste hows ne cyte sore displaysid herte alleway held manyer drewe parte said vnto changyng colour madame sory ye reffuse take pacience hows kinge cyte goddes haue gyuen moche happe haue yet ony wif ony lady damoysell hit happend goddes fortune hath enspyred yow come hether certes hit right hye beaute perisshid eye herte hath made couoytous yow gyue vnto yow herte body goodes alle louer may gyue vnto loue lady ony king may gyue wherfore pray yow ye descende vnto palays ende may haue comynycacion secretly telle vnto yow right grete loue haue yow anone meduse vnderstood requestes kynge began frowne wyllyng wyse answerd hym syre kynge yf hit soo myn herte desired acqueyntance comynycacion oon man trouthe yf fonde shold holde self right happy findyng self grace eyen mater goth wyth otherwyse loue men moche oon haue entencion abyde contynue virginite ye kynge ye haue gyuen saufconduyt achyeue pylgrymage requyre yow ye holde yow plesid ye doo suche wyse ye neuer seen dame sayde neptune shall doo ye saye whan herte gyuen vnto yow syre answerd meduse hyt behoueth fyrst knowe loue haue told yow hyer haue entencion abyde virgyne may hit prouffite yow saye ye haue gyuen herte thyse ben loste wordes dame sayd neptune dyamond shyneth tyl hit pollisshyd ye neuer perauenture desired ne requyred loue wherfore ye haue loue oon man wherfore ye muste vnderstand hauntyse maketh loue yf ye come wyth make doubtes soiourne wyll shall change ye shall take alyance wyth syre answerd meduse wyll vnchangeable notwythstondyng sayd neptune hit muste change abaysshe yow syre answerd meduse see thyng yeuyth cause enbaysshement fele herte ferme stable operacions ye kynge haue gyuen saufconduyt furnysh deuocion temple goddesse cyte rayson honour shold gouerne corage dame said neptune yf beaute surmounted beaute woman shold consente anon retorne whan conceyue yow formed hye degre nature nothing lackyth yow whan see grete goddesse pallas hath enspyred yow thys cyte rayson may haue place hit loue force ye shall wif leuer dye renne alle deshonnours world faylle haue allyance whan meduse wise vnderstand wordes neptune sawe well outragyously achauffid amorous desire might ascape puyssance beaute yf hit ony auenture changed heer couleures saye force regned wrought subtilte said vnto kynge syre knowe ye grete puyssant lord loue hath meuyd yow force take wif syn playsir suche cotente suche wyse ye haue demanded day maad maryage yow solempnly halowe fefte espousailles requyre yow two thinges first may retorne vnto porte peple aray dresse triuphant riches ne may employe grete glorie day mariage secondly ye wyll araye adresse ladyes cyte receyue hit apperteyneth wyll well ye knowe alle remenant ladyes world ye shall finde ony haue meuable goodes ne riches haue neptune oon alle rauysshyd ioye whan herde answer meduse thankyd swete wordes agreed suche wyse deuysed anon sente agayn meduse vnto galleyes hopyng wold retorne agayn wyf whan subtylte wytte rendred agayn porte neptune puyssance stede retorne cyte dyde disancre shippis lete sayle falle haste wythdrewe hem fro porte stede aray vestementis nupciall toke armes made men arme thus ascapyd fro neptune whiche grete sorow merueyllously grete anger sayde hede serpent here torned coleuuers ende hyde graciously malice manyer deceyuyd begyled hym etc thus ascaped meduse handes neptune meen hede serpentyne neptune abood conuertyd tornyd stoone saye erthely affection riches meduse wente moche puyssance surmountyd moche alle puyssance atthenes thynge ran renomee thurgh grece beaute meduse recomanded tho party wente daye many knightes auenturyng theyr liues many torned stone many loste theyr tresors innumerable enforcyng armes conquere lady whiche withstood alle way assaultes assayllyng way abode vainqueresse meduse sette nowht kynge ne prince wold haue wyf alle sette gete gader tresors world yf fader ben strongly coueytous yet couetous comen agayn fro athene royame put vnder subiection grekes exposed ayenst said mountid pe swalowe couetyse auarice made warre vnto alle nyghebours dauntyd hem constraind paye yerly grete tribute wherby astate name aroos greet bruyt therof ran many ferre region amonge cyte naples regned kyng pilonne afore said tyme renomee meduse bruyt perseus sone dane iupiter verdour begynnyng tempryen strength dayly requyred moder kinge wold gyue hym leue serche hys auentures whan pylonnes herde speke haultesse meduse rapine auarice behelde sone lawe shold vertuous werk yf myght correcte told perseus wold sende hym theder perseus thankyd hym sayd wold enploye therto puyssance kynge pylonne sente men armes made redy thretty galeyes thexercyte perseus whan redy callyd hym aday perseus dubbyd hym knyght ordre cheuallrye began tyme vsid world hit ordonned day perseus shold go see pand whan kynge accomplisshed serymonye caas requyred paynems wyse perseus toke leue kynge pylonne moder dane damoyselles right ioyously entryd galeye dysancred departyd fro port naples wyth grete bruyt tabour trompes wyth banyer splayed saylyd hye see hit good fayr sight see departement ther many teer wept euery body loued perseus moche humble debonayr apulyens departyd neuer longe myghte see hym retorned home prayng vnto goddes good right happy myght fortune perseus noble knyght wente see porte wyth oute auenture shall saye exployted cam affrike named lybye tyme wolde haue refresshid hym port beside strayt gybalter kynge athlas grete astrologyen kynge put hym fro landyng porte cam armes ayenst hym shewyd fro ferre signe wolde kepe contre wyth swerde perseus whyche wold employe armee wythdrewe hym fro porte en entencion auenge hym another tyme rudesse yf fortune wold helpe hym passid strayte sought longe royame meduse anone fonde hit veray tydinges certain marchantes fonde labouryng see told hym susters soiourned cyte whiche stode ryuage grete ioye perseus whan vnderstood tydinges folk grete nede vitayll callid hem saide shold make hem redy arme nyhe place soughte saylid alway forth aboute thre owres fore euen sawe cyte meduse inne ouer sawe meduse susters grete nombre men warre renged porte richely arayed poynt hit meruaylle see whan perseus sawe dyuydyd armee thre egale bataylles eche ten galeyes ordeyned put capitaynes warre wysely enformed hem nyhe approche porte put hym self first batayll poetes saye goddes pallas gaf hym shelde cristall vnderstande approuchyd right wysely porte vpon grete see spayne conduyted hym self suche prudence likenyd cristall cam fought hand hand puyssance meduse shynyng ryght clere shelde hys prudence receyuyng yeuyng infinyte stroke gate lande constrayned meduse retorne cyte force force armes prowesse wyth grete dyscipline fightyng sowdyours tyme hede serpent meduse myght notwythstonde firste fortune acustomed put vnder foot ouercome alle exposed armes ayenst tyme put thextremyte put phow perseus vaynquysshed bataylle quene meduse fledde cyte svche entre warre betwene perseus meduse gorgonnes fortunat whiche meduse cherysshed right hye degree fille doun fro whele fortune whiche whele consented prudence perseus sholde cause humylieng mekyng notwythstondyng meduse took corage self reentryd cyte gaf charge oon men go vnto enemyes enquere chief captayn hem thinge soughte countre hisperyen comandement meduse departyd fro cyte cam ooste apuliens entended logge nyght moche cam perseus toke refection vpon table maad grete stoon marbell sayde hym wyse syre vaynqueresse men hath sente thee enquere thyng thou wylt doo contre ende may knowe hath messanger answerd perseus haue entencion fraunchise make fre men fro seruytude thy maystresse holdeth hem make hath oon eye conuerte torne men stone riches shall cause losse dicion knyghtes whiche wold haue mariage ayenst malice serpente shall armed prudence wel tht knowe morn oute lenger delaye shal gyue assault vnto cyte caas come agaynst batayll answere esperien retorned vnto meduse recountyd vnto herd meduse assemblid alle men warre said hit meruaylle though haue myn herte anguysshous whan haue vaynquysshyd grete companyes men armes see shamefully ben goon back withdrawen cyte prowesse handfull men anguysshe haue ben custome ouercome tryumphe alle maner warres ben hye enterprise whiche haue made alle see occidentall fere drede v ben glayues ben yolden v kynges trybutaryes ben armes strengthes hath made tremble mountaygnes roches libye day haue taken feer prowesse drede hardynes dishonour honour leste sin thinge gouerned hit behoueth passe best wise may hit behoueth also euery man corage vertue hym self morn hyt recoueryd v thys day loste enemyes thys cyte haue v vnderstonde knowe morn wyll gyue v assault ne furnyssh bataylle hit also ben trauayllyd ayer see hit moche better furnyssh bataylle tyme sholde abyde lenger oure enemyes ben straungers heth triuphe mortall mysaduenture yf ouercome hit shall memorye v ferre nyghe honour yf caas goo contrarye shall renne wyth losse lyues derision mocquerye alle peples shall blood spred brood haue made ground rede blood shalle honour wastyd loste also name haue goten wyth grete labour alle world taketh courage hope two thynges ben also couenable warre armes wyth oute shall neuer man attayne crowne victorye take herte yow dispose harnoys armes morn shall day ye muste nede shyne dedes beste wyse ye may kepe renomees tytles honourable prowesse dame answerd oon ther capitayns grete domage ye ne man yf hit hit apparant ye shold haue subiuged put vnder alle monarchye men ye saye muste nedes kepe oure renome yf fortune hath ben v day froward morn shal torn prouffyt woundes hurtes ben made worship blood moste bere hit take hit gree prowesse honour shall morn putte v fore shame shall esuert e v conne ye ryse erly myght fronte hem well rayed apparaylid laboure prosite requeste whan meduse herde good wille capitayne consentid right ioyous concluded puissance shold bespringe assayll enemy midnyght hope come vpon hem vnwares coclucion thought good vnto alle eche man withdrewe take reste make redy harnoys meduse slepte moche night herte alway grete sore chargid appetite vengeance midnyght sowned armes made hem redy adoubed toke banyers tht right riche men diligent nowh arme crafte well enduced whan redy assemblid fore palais riall meduse susters yssuid oute gate riche astate gyuyng good morow folk litill noyse myght deuidyd hem two companyes wherof made oon companye departe oon yates cyte self coduyted yate tht ayenste porte hauen etc tyme ayer pure net sterres twinklid mone shone put away derknes nyght acordyng celestyall offyce whan meduse feldes wente ryuage see supposid haue taken perseus folke faylled sone yssuyd cyte hit parceyuyd wacchemen ooste perseus signefied theyr comyng perseus hys men slept harnoys thus whan approchid vnto enemyes supposid haue distressid fonde arayed renged good ordenance bataylle wherof ther aroos right grete crye bothe party wyth crye ther engendryd grete scarmuche eygre fiers hit nede vnto alle put forth prowess theyr strengthes many man cast doun dede vpon sande ther many swerd dyed reed wyth blood cam seconde bataylle meduse makyng grete bruyt ioynnyng bataylle naples stronge partye maystrye etc tempeste perseus gafe hym reste alway eyen open eeres bent armes enhaunsed smyte quyk hys grene yougthe swerde trenchid cutted dispairly smote man ne shelde al frusshid hit slewe doun right meduse alway put strength frayes moste prees myghty grete corage entretene holde geder men seeyng often tymes appertisements noble fete armes enemy perseus grete sorowe conduyte helde apuliens estate aray ther none myghte resiste strength leste myght resiste hym thinge torned grete displaysir meduse alleway bare displaysir vsid prowesse beste wyse myghte dyde grete domage enemyes smote doun vaylliantly semed moche better man woman better became brandissh swerde spynne torne spyndell phow perseus bataylle slewe myghty suster meduse venquysshid bataylle scarmuche dured longe grete betyng doun men armes knyghtes thenuye meduse well doyng perseus gaf armes force strength nature gyuen full malice coude kepe well fro swerd perseus way enuyronned best men shall make longe counte fought facion vnto day oute ony wyste shold gyue victorye like sonne began sprede shewe bemes rayes semblable wise perseus began shewe rayes prudence braundisshid swerd seeyng oon side banyer royall smote prees drewe parte castyng men doun dede sandes moo honderd banyer square four foot made cremesin satin myddes ymage paintyd wherof body figure facion woman hede serpente etc meduse neuer ferre fro thys banyer moche drewe allwey theder rescuse whan perseus comen theder grete sute hys folk cryed perseus perseus liftyng swerd temprid blood ende hit happend first strook gaf place fille vpon oon susters meduse terribly confouded ded wyth grete wounde begynnyng heed doun stomack naples smote hesperyens alle puyssance tho smote perseus endlong ouerthwart right side lefte side stroke mortall affrayed feble enemyes alle strengest also asseured meduse grete occision point meduse enforced power wythstonde grete force perseus notwythstandyng fore tymes ouercomen men ouercomen hauyng late corage lifte vp herte fiers ony man veynquysshid despayr cheuaulrous conduyte perseus broken banyer smyten men piece partye slayn wyth swerd partye fled made reed swerd right hand wyth blood see smale goters made rede warm blood whiche meduse lost ferocyte alle presumpcion alle strength alle vigour euyll wente alle werke side whan seen banyer destroyed whan seen moste victoryous knigthes confounded tempest deth whan sawe men armes leue bataylle flee fore perseus fore ymage deth fynably sawe alle puysance torne destruction generall wherof ende eche man gaf hit ouer euery man myght saue hym self sauyd hym caues busshes oon sore affrayed hit pietous thing theyr cryes many sauyd cyte many slayn fleyng perseus men phow perseus conquerd meduse cyte smote hede wente fyghte ayenst kynge athlas septe myghty puyssant geant etc perseus thys disconfiture poursued meduse fleyng cyte entryd moste parte peple hym faylid hym neuer put deth alle men defensable fonde thende insurrection shold ayenst spared blood woman lityll child comandement perseus amonge perseus founde meduse put cisterne pytye hit smote hede suche facion blood yssuyd engendrid pegasus fleyng hors hede perseus smote meduse vnderstond toke royame depryuyd hit bannysshid poure nakyd fleyng hors engendrid blood yssued fro hede vnderstande riches issuyng royame founded made shippe named pegase moche saye good renomee shippe likened vnto hors fleyng moche good renomee perseus born fro region region suche wise vpon hors fleing moche perseus wente shippe dyuerce contrees gate hym grete name bi facion perseus conquerd hede meduse make pegase swyft shyppe alle world abode certayn nombre dayes seekyng serching tresours meduse rychesses whiche susters sette entencion herte fonde perseus stone precyous thinges meruayllous whan shippe made filde hit precyous bagues iuellis leuyng cyte men gouerne hit conduyte wente see toke armes armes meduse restyd tyll cam poort cyte regned athlas sayng wold put hym vnder subiugue hym afore er retorned contre thys cyte name septe athlas knewe well armes meduse fro fer sawe pegase shippe knewe armes therin thought meduse veynquysshyd strangyers doubtyd sore theyr comyng notwythstondyng dide putte men armes bewayled moche phylotes brother otherwyse named esperus kept gardyn wyth apple gold doughtres whan folk armed rengyd hem vpon porte good ordenance anon cam porte liuerd assaulte full dyuerce sharp fierstees athlas yong strong body puyssant peple defended hym vayliantly kepte porte wyth poynte hys swerd well thys assault perseus conquerd thing two dayes assault dured stronge nature porte strength swerd kinge athlas whan perseus sawe folk ynow take porte withdrewe hye see sente naples vnto kinge pilonnus half tresors meduse signefieng hym hye aduenture requyryng hym wold sende hym thousand sowdyours kynge dane grete ioye tydynges requeste perseus assemblid fyften honderd fyghtyng men whiche sente libye theyr propre sone danu ordeyned chyef capitayne armee whan perseus sawe come thyse fyften honderd fyghtyng men fro fer aspied see knewe hit socoure cam hym took hys hors volant wente mete hem fonde danu broder made moste grete chyer world entrid shippe abode day festyng whan hit cam nyght comanded maryners shold rowe sayle toward septe saide hym morn wold deliuere hym porte marouners put hem deuoyr theyr craft well nyght past aboute sonne rysing shewid perseus hauen porte septe perseus full grete gladnesse callyd danu sayd hym broder ben comen porte thou shalt gete day honour worship yf hit plese goddes yf good auenture helpe v honour shall appertayne vnto thee fore durst enbrase allone puyssance name alle goddes late v enploye hede meduse hit myn aduys tyme shall torne stone alle regyon vnderstonde thy men mene rychesses meduse comen hether cyte sette fore v shall constrayned abandone gyue ouer theyr poort flee betwene walles stone theyr cyte broder answerd danu haue good hoope truste fortune shall thy helpe honour worship werk hit shall torne prouffit vnto thyn arte sechar honourable awerk desire thyng partye name souldiour thy souldees enuyronned loue fraternyte come serue yf rychesses meduse comen naples wyth thy right good fame warryours comen libye conclusion hit conceyue yf werke honour hit torne thy glorye loenge notwythstondyng shall fayle thy loue worshyp shall expose assault may hold nature praye dubbe make knyght word perseus drewe swerd gaf danu ordre knyghthode sin comanded eche man shold garnyshe hym armures made dysplaye banyers standardes penous recognyssances knowlechinges dide sowne trompettes clarion tabour renged alle galeyes sette right fayr good ordenance dide moche cam poort whiche full enuyronned wyth libyens redy caste speres dartes stone contre right experyent warre also aborde poort ther right grete bruyt right greuous assemble perseus pegase assayllyd libyens ende danu another galeye assayllyd hem like wise putte hem bothe moste daunger assault grete sheldes large coueryd hem dredde strook glayue ne swerde ne stoones put hem self myddes porte gaf assault many dede oon partye plente fightars suche wyse thentree ther many apukens confounded put back hoote aspre thys whan goten land perseus danu began smyte dismesurably vpon libyens bete hem doun oute remedye right side lifte side alle made rede theyr blood also perseus gaf grete strook wyth hys glayue vnto athlas purposid haue come broken passage neuer athlas hope ne durst come amonge stroke well grete strong puyssant moche coueytous victorye perseus danu naples libyens accustomed finde fiers mortall armes perseus kynge athlas wyst saye encouraged peple beste wyse couthe notwithstandyng sawe hem beten doun enemyes wyth oute nombre wyth oute mesure sawe forther naples wan alway whan seen also behelde men vaynquysshid quene meduse iuged hym self puyssant ynowh resiste theyr strength hardnes bataylle shuld hym domageous vayllable sowned retrayt fled cyte right hye montaygne therby therfore saye poetes athlas sight hede meduse torned mountayn fro forth hille callyd athlas yet endureth name vnto day moche athlas sauyd hym among stone founded syn castell dwellyd vnto tyme hercules phow perseus torned kynge athlas stone quene auria wyf kynge pricus wax amerous knyght belleforon reffused wherof moche payne whan perseus danu sawe athlas alle folk put flight first chaced hem vnto mountayn torned stone dyeng theyr blood caues busshous weyes pathes secondly whan put hem vnto vtterance moche cowde drewe cyte wherof yates shette ner kepte noman entryng therin ne fonde litill nombre matrones yong child whiche made terryble grete sorowe alle yong men woman fledd vnto feldes abandonned theyr cyte theyr folk goodes whan perseus danu sawe hit abandonned hem peple alle fonde passid night grete ioye gladnesse makyng grete chier thankyng theyr goddes theyr victorie gyuen morn perseus made bete doun gate cyte comanded euery man shold take butin whan laden alle perseus danu wente see galeyes sayllyd forth leuyng athlas montaygne gafe hym vnto studie science astronomie tyme iupiter made aliance kynge tro moyen gaminedes signe loue frendshyp gaf vnto ylion vigue gold whiche sette palais ylion hit shal said thirde book hit longe kynge troos consumed cours ende regne obsequie halowed made solempnly troye grete haboudance teres ylion crowned kinge cyte liued peasibly apliacion encresing seygnourye lordship wedded noble lady cyte receyuyd sone named laomedon moche finde tht ylion dide ony thing coronacon ner made thing saue tht achieued made palais ylion shall speke hensforth laomedon sone regned hym shall leue faytes ylion yet er wryte laomedon shal poursiewe matere perseus come therto shall racounte historie fyll perseus torned kynge athlas mountaygyne tyme perseus began gyue lyf vnto righte digne ocuures werkes noble fame accrisius belefader perseus naturell fader dane put kyngdome royame alle seygnourye arges conspiracion pricus broder made ayenst hym ther left vnto acrisius alle royame tour darayn wherto fledde refuge acrisius pricus naturell sone aba lawfull sone linceus lefte lyue fifty sone egistus mercy wyf ypermestra doughter danau pricus hauyng vsurpyd fro broder acrisius seignourye royame arges wyf named aurea norisshid custome gaf charge habounde delyces day behelde amonge seruauntes oon well accomplisshid knyght nature thynge forgoten hym touchyng body enamoured yong husbond pricus auncyent werkes condycions moche lasse desired carnall desirs wif well bothe right nyhe oon eage knyght thus belouyd name bellorophon whan aurea put studye loue knyght solicited hym eyen semblauntes drawing delite voluptuosite trewe knight herte ferme stable whiche parceyuyd well countenance dissimilid fayned blinde partye ende whan lady sawe semblant ne signe amerous shewid employed one plese fled compaynie moste euill wyse myghte entended torne loue hate fayr countenance fierste enuenymed make hym dye accusid fore husbonde kynge pricus sayng wold haue enforced requyred iustice instantly accusacion maad bellorophon present sore abasshid surprisid begynnyng heering lady speke longe assewrid self excusid saing madame neuer plese hit vnto goddes couere myn honour discouere disworship fawlte another late neuer man aduance self deffame another knowing shall saye trouthe yf ther ony man worthely may proue tht ayenst ouercome litill noblesse herte shall remette iugement alle noble men residue dayes ala lady fro whens comen abusion impose shold haue willed enforce whan place ben withnesses cry tht ye made afray ben proues shal saye euer lif allone hit gyueth meruaylle fro herte departed dishonour tht ye note cause hit ymagined aienst wil wel tht al world knowe tht haue seruid trewly loially neuer thoughte dishonour vnto yow ne vnto kynge whome praye wille take make informacion vpon liuynge vnderstonde like wyse youris yf hit prouyd appere haue trespaced may punysshid praye also yf founde innocent may haue light basolucion sire sayd lady strongly obstynat errour make party ayenst hym yf accuse hym hit trouthe hit oughte demande wytnessis folye caas worth two wytnessis alle worlde knoweth whan ony ylle man wille dishonour woman callyd wytnesses ne proues therto doth damnable moste secretly hym possible wende bellorophon haue wyth wherof requyre sentence iugement hym wyth word pricus assemblid counceyll hit iuged lady shuld beleuyd bellorophon shuld culpable deth spack pricus bellorophon sayd fayr sone thou knowest felest haue louyd norisshid louyngly thou vnderstandest accusacion thy lady caas foull hit may purged denyeng yf hit euyll boyes garsons shold aldaye dyshonoure many woman coude finde caas ladyes haue prerogatyfe beleuyd nede brynge forth wytnessis moche thy maystresse hath vaynquysshid requyred iugement thy trespaas thou art condempnyd dye moche fore tyme haue grete loue vnto knowe vaylliant man thy body shall relece attempere thys sentence wyse thou shalt goo fighte aienste chymere secille yf thou maist adaunte maistrie geue thy lif gyue plain absolucion moienant neuer thou replicque ne reherce trespaas sire answerd bellorophon sin fortune consente attainte ony infelicite preuelage lady domyne go aboue reson moche leuer vainquysshid wrong cause euill iuste good cause thanke moderacion iugement make vowe presence haste shall goo secille proue ayenste chymere shall see yf fortune shall helpe gete lif whiche made lose iugement noble knyght departyd toke leue kynge ladyes damoyselles toke also armures goodes made couenant bargayned certain maronners bringe hym scecyll whan acorded wente see litill compaygnye euyll ease herte whan sawe fortune hym diuerse well conforted hym self good quarell sayllyng day see helespont maronners lokid weste sawe come right grete flote shippes warre whiche dysconforted sorowfully wonder awoke bellorophon tyme slepte sayd ded loste bellorophon confortyd maronners best wyse cowde told hem disconforte cowde helpe hem thus spekyng galeye auauntage wente oute afore felaws fleeyng see like vnto byrde adressid vnto shippe bellorophon aborded hit wyll demande name galeye men ther inne shall saye hym pegase perseus therwythinne seeyng myght speke maronners caryed bellorophon secylle axed demaunded regyon wold goo whan bellorophon herde perseus speke behelde mayntene countenance iuged hym self good hous sayde hym certes sire haue moche grete ioye see shyppe maronners ben well adressid good recountre youre ye seme well knyght noble feetes shall yow saye caas ye haue made arynge first poynt ye haue enquired bee knowe ye arges haue take birthe seconde answere yow haue entencion go strayt sccylle whiche constrayned rygour mortal iugement caste vpon thynstance lady callyd aurea iniustely vntrewly hath complaynd vpon saynge wold haue enforced lady speke wyf kynge pricus whiche newly fresshely hath bannysshid excylled broder acrisius royame kynge plese satysfye accusacion wyf hath condempned deth relecyng allway hope good agreable seruices haue acorded lyue yf hit plese goddes may possibilite vaynquysshe ouercome chymere secylle vnto whiche go assaye praye yow owr infortune lette yow neyther non compaygnye uallyant knyght answerd perseus hit trewe herte noble man taketh pyte compascion dystresse passion semblable recorde caas hath percyd myn herte charitable mys ricord pyte whiche ye may seurly vnderstande haue v ony enpeschement vpon infortunat lif moche hertes wold endured callyng crafte armes singulierly deliten auentures grete poys weyghte enhaunce shall accompanye yow two cause first expose self dissipacion destruction chymere yf hit ppen ye adaunte whiche presuppose seconde chymere vaynquysshyd may guyded yow vnto royame arges fro forth wyll enemye vnto kynge pricus fauour fader moder kynge acrisius late yow haue gretter knowleche matere telle yow sone dane properly tht conceyuyd tour darrain seed iupiter sone kinge acrisius made caste see notwithstanding shall take vengeance demerites honour blood wombe whome yssued shall hym socours ayde praye yow ye wyll felaw broder armes ye come galeye sende home agayn maronners contres yf hit plese yow whan bellorophon herde good wordes answer perseus made alyances wyth hym entrid galeye gaf leue maroners acompanyed hym wyth perseus danu loue hym toke theyr waye vnto secylle arryued space tyme toke lande day bellorophon armed hym desiryng finde chymere toke leue perseus suche wyse putte hym paryll deth poetes write tht chymere hede lion wombe chieure taylle serpent trouthe hit mountayne inhabitable heyghte aboue passing grete caue lyon myddell hill hit full chieures fote benethe hit aduyronned sette round aboute wyth serpentis lyon serpentes passing domageable noyous vnto contre aboute nyghe whan bellorophon sawe moutayne wente theder perseus danu folowed hym longe marchid whan sawe behelde mo thousand lityll serpentes wyth many grete dragon arestyd aboute bellorophon caste theyr venym passid forth come rennyng vpon perseus danu whiche promysid bellorophon shold doo foot ne entreprise armes yf hit constraynt defending theyr bodyes anone thre vayllyant knyghtes sawe cursed bestes toke theyr swerdes smote vpon many beheded grete payne traueylle bestes cruell full orgueyll hardyed eygrely hem yf ben well garnysshid abillementis warre ther sonner haue found deth lyf bellorophon went alleway fore smote doun right heded smote peces many perseus ne broder danu fought bestes cam vpon whan bellorophon litill holden stour bataylle ayenst vermyne founden aspre byting point egghe swerd made terribly blont smote ayenst hard scale skynnes lepe doun hooles chieures lion cam doun tassaylle knyghte grete nombre enuyronned etc bestes escapid fro cam seus gaf hym new ocupacion employe strength prowesse lion lepe aboute necke bellorophon som tyme suche nombre parte myght seen alleway hys abilite coude well saue hym self neuer ascapid ther cam moche vermyn vpon bestaill se danu whiche rachid assayllyd yf wonne roche vpon whiche gate vp grete payne right grete swete body go vpon roche ther oon strayt waye siewed hym lyon wyth hem bestes helde hem way roche fote roryng makyng grete noyse aboute hym terribly perseus danu non hope knyght hit ben laste daye many bestes aboute hym hit likly egghe cuttyng swerd myght longe dure oute hit ben worn broken lion myght touche bodye boot stone arachid wyth theyr clawes serpentes flewe vp ayer lifte vp theyr bodyes vpon theyr taylles caste fire smoke oute theyr throtes vnto roche moste hardiest lion oon rengyd bataylle ayenst hym shewid teth receyuyng stroke sore sette fled abode bestes famylier sore coueytous mannes blood whome regned souerayn fierste moche ony wylde beste world tyme harde meruayllous bataylle perseus danu behelde thoughte facion myght socoure bellorophon noble knyght defended hym power beheld myghte saue hym fro paryll caste eyen vpon grete stoon henge ouer weye roche wher vpon moutid thoughte yf myghte make stone falle doun shuld slee moste parte bestes began lityll lityll wagge ston seke ioyntu re helde hit moche labourid ende made hit falle vpon lion serpentes chienres suche wyse falling made alle roche tremble ferid generall vnhappy bestes forfrusshed like thonder ronne vpon yet tombling doun hit made roche bellorophon stood shake tumblid doun theron astonyed wiste neuer whether hit day night stone grete brought doun many stone hym perseus danu begynnyng wende alle mountaygne tumblid doun well assured hem self notwithstondyng beheld playnly ende seyng noyse tempeste theyr felawe laye vpright reuersid vpon toppe roche supposid ben ded made grete sorowe displaysant approuchid roche fonde bestes liyng vnder stone ded wente vp mountain knewe bellorophon ded wherof recouerid grete ioye cessyng theyr sorow toke knyght betwene theyr armes perseus demanded hym hit stood hym felte hym self etc phow perseus vaynquysshid monstre see exposid hym self agayn hym loue andromeda etc perseus danu awayted gladly answer bellorophon helde hym beste accomplissid knyght euer sawe shall make longe processe matere perseus danu serchid mountayn wente caues bestes fonde none alway satte bellorophon vpon roche myght goo frusshyng bruysing foote two knyghtes circuyd goon aboute hille retorned bellorophon perseus sayd hym broder well arte thou worthy haue preysing loenge thou haste day good holy werk thy worthy conduyte thou hast goten vnto thy name crowne gloryous fame thou haste passid strayte waye passage infortune fro whens thou art yssued cler sonne thou hast laboured thy wele vtilite wele prouffit regyon thou hast slayn wardes serpentes portyers lion kepte contre inhabitable whiche shall fro hen forward enhabited ocupied wyth peple bellorophon shamed whan herde glorye perseus gaf vnto hym mekenes humylite hym answerd yf ther ony worship werke hit shall torne well vnto hem hym began preyse echon ete vpon hille nyght made sacrefice vnto theyr goddes thedir camalle apuliens made grete chiere syn toke alle skynnes lion heedes serpentes ded signe victorie charged theyr galeyes bare hem theyr galeye bellorophon whiche myght goo finably wente vnto see sayllyd rowed toward poort athames whiche nyghe whan wende haue drawen vnto porte sodaynly ther roos tempeste see grete hidouse constrayned abandonne hem vnto winde passid forth hauen theyr fortune suche brought sirie vpon see palestyne brought hem porte hauen ioppen regned amon palestyne regned cephus phyncus etc tyme perseus arriued ther tempeste poort ful men woman child hit semed world assemblid perseus cam theder allone folk disparklid vpon see theyr galeyes whan siriens sawe hym arryue force winde assemblid grete nombre aboute hors volant kinge amon seeyng hit chargid hedes lion sore abasshid knowe fro whens galeye comen enquired maistre whiche inquisicion answerd perseus demanded kinge courtoysly contre arryued kynge tolde hym sirye royame apperteyned whan perseus knewe spack kynge sayde syre descended vnto poort disposicion fortune also men ben sore trauayllyd tempeste see hath ben longe troublous vnto requyre praye thou contente may come londe refresshe v yf hit happen tyme comyng thou ony thyne haue semblable courtosie naples whiche place domynacion promyse parolle word noble man meryte thanke shall rendryd vnto kynge answerd noble knyght ther ben many exploratours adayes sayllyng regnes contrees man may well knowe maye affye truste notwythstondyng see well facion trowe ye wyll gyue v vnderstande thynge trouthe abandoune yow alle contre pray yow ye wyll come take pacience hows furthermore counceylle yow ye departe come shippe yf ye abyde longe ye shall grete peryll moche knowe certaynly poort shall come anone monstre see shall deuoure right fayr virgyne mayde whiche bounden vpon stoon cryme moder sentence yf ye tarye tyll comynge hit doubte hit shall wors yow bocace genealogye goddes ne toucheth otherwyse cause mayde thus exposed monstre wherfore passe ouer demandeth name mayde bocace sayth named andromadas whan perseus vnderstonden bounden mayde desired see meruaillous iugement giuen vpon arayde riche vestementes clothes sin yssued galeye tooke also bellorophon whiche myghte yet sustene self wente vnto andromeda parentes cosins grete nombre whiche laboured sorow grete plente teres whan perseus sawe maiden passing fayr degre whiche neuer sawe like ne paralle pite sayd self yf mighte wolde deliuere fro peryll callyd frendes sayd vnto presence amon haue certainly grete pyte compassion fair damoyselle also esbayed goddes suffre endure fortuned tendre yeres yf hit happend myght finde ony knight noble man wolde vnbynde charyte expose body agaynst monstre loue shold quyte answerd ye sayde perseus yf wolde sake aduenture self werke yf hit fortuned grace ouercome surmounte monstre putte hym vtterance shall ye contente mayde wyf answerd yet ye promyse yow sayd perseus swere hath founden knyght shall putte body lif ieopardye etc worde perseus sente feche armes wente damoyselle vnbonde fro stone deliueryd frendes kynnesmen saynt augustin boke cite god reherceth yet poort stone andromeda bounden vpon ioppen kepe signe memorye victorye perseus monstre alle meruaylled gretly entrepryse knyght knowyng monstre iugged hym ded alowyng hardynes semed hit grete oon spack matere perseus armed hym ioyously whan armed cam andromeda kyste takyng leue saide fayr mayde praye ye vnto goddes champion loue submytteth hym self vnto peryll deth ende oonly suffragies may come vnto right stok loue gyder ioye ioyned mariage whiche bye pry lyf noble knyght answerd mayde beholden yow kennesmen frendes knowe ye yf suffrage maye obteyne anenste goddes ye shall retorne saulf fro entrepryse perseus went hym fore stoon andromeda kneled wyth grete humylite wyth bothe knee vpon erthe prouokyng goddes vnto helpe champion ther many matrones vpon bancke see compassion put hem contemplacion example alle siryens began praye prosperite knyght reseruyd kynge phineus whiche prayed deth cause moche fore iugement gyuen andromeda fianced trouthplight well willyd monstre deuoured perseus ende mariage hym myght haue ben ended shall saye whan perseus put hym self forth stone behelde toward see held hand good glayue passing stronge ne longe seen situacion taken leyzer see place whan ther sprange swolowe abisme see monstre grete horrible dredfull hit semed made destroye alle world rowhe went foure foot like beste fourme diffigured none wiste wherto myght likened whan siriens sawe hym put oute heed swolowe ther none well assured ne tremblid fere many afrayed fledde theyr howses reentred theyr cyte notwitstandyng perseus sone sawe hym sourdre ran hym hardy right well assewryd smote hym point glayue apoint vpon right eye side made hym blinde wherof monstre felte grete payne cam see open mowth wende haue swalowed perseus perseus wente aback litill put glayue betwene iawes throte fer forth coude drawe hit agayn force hit abode throte foure foot tt second strook monstre made meruaillo crye lifting vp heed wenyng haue caste tronchon glaue whiche abood throte hit wold bee alwey monstre assayllyd perseus wende haue swalowed hym throte perseus alwey roof hym wyth swerde put hym defence smote alweye throte aboute nyghe eye well entended werke gyuen hym many woundes made hym lifte eye like dyde righte eye monstre wente made many wentes wyth oute seeyng knowing wente poursiewyng aduenture perseus gaf hym many woundes serchyng herte laste fonde hit fynably adresshid persed herte whiche strook made hym falle doun ded phow phyneus wold haue andromeda perseus answerd hym shold wif passing ioyous esbayed siryens whan sawe good fortune perseus saiden oon another suche knyght ought preysed aboue men kinge amon toke grete playsir see conduyte seeyng monstre labouryng deth wente doun hym enbrasing hym sayde syre goddes gouerne thy fortune syn haue receyuyd fauour grace ther none may anoye good oure thou arryued demande thou wilte shall haue hit syre answerd perseus haue preseruyd fro deth damoyselle desire none thinge vaylliant knyght sayd phineus awayting thou thinkeste gloryfie thy self haue goten half day honour knyght shall gete honderd yere gretly thou oughtest recomanded forseen beaulte mayde deceyue knowe thou haue trouthplighte right ought wif many dayes ben goon exspired presence bisshop promised take eche mariage infortune comen thou haste releuyd wolst therfore haue begynnyng fayr ende fowle yf hit happe thou wronge late wete shall suffre hit contre kinge haue grete puyssance alle glorie thou haste goten shall quenchid wherfore praye thou forbere caas thou suffre take myn take thou longeth dvryng wordes perseus behelde toward see sawe fro fer galeyes comyng oon adressing toward th poort wherof right grete ioye saide vnto phyneus kynge make doute thy power grete contre knowe thou right well knowe man liuyng shall cause leue longeth whan comen hether fonde mayde condempnyd vnto deth tyme alle abandonned deth haue sauyd saye myn thou ougthest haue regarde ony promesse hath made ony haue entencion shall wif yf thow wylt debate fighte assemble thy power make redy thy bataylle loo come galeyes redy receyue yf hau peple yet haue cofres moste parte tresours meduse sende men armes alle place may gete hem whan phineus considerid answere knewe knyght vaynquysshid meduse wherof renome grete ronne thorugh oute world coude none otherwise answere perseus myght playsir alle kynnysmen andromeda angry phineus folie made ashamed departyd then wente cyte wente beholde monstre cam saillyng rowing apuliens vnto poort comen brought perseus andromeda ioppen grete triumphe yet perseus andromeda espousid eche day laye geder solempnyte duryd theyr weddyng xv dayes tyme siriens cam poort daily see beholde monstre plunius rehereith monstre born rome boon xl foot longe also grete oliphant late rede hystorye serche grete huge monstre whan oon bone grete romayns grete meruaylle haue kepe bone shall saye ende expiracion feste weddyng perseus andromeda perseus toke leue siryens garnysshyd galeyes vitaylles departid fro ioppen wente see ledyng hym wif andromeda fortune hym good litill tyme passid see syrie cam lande poort hauene thebe receyuyd courtoysly kynge creon regned yong chylde phow perseus restablisshid royame kynge acrisius slowe kynge euyll auenture thebe refresshid hem apuliens made allyance kynge departid fro then toke theyr waye lande toward arges vnder conduyte bellorophon hooll helid foot whiche knewe well contre whan bellorophon guyded hem nyhe arges hour myght renne fore gate signefied hit vnto perseus perseus made oost tarye valeye sente danu vnto kynge pryeus somene hym shold yelde royame vnto kynge acrisius danu wente arges accomplisshed somacion kynge pricus answerd hym kynge wold holde helde manaced perseus vnto deth yf departe fro contrey hastely danu retorned vnto oost perseus answere made hym reporte perscus hoped kynge prycus wold come hym gyue hym bataylle therof right grete ioye playsir desired nothing world armes entende take hede vnto werkes ordeyned nyght shold departe bataylle three wherof gaf charge first batayll bellorophon whiche requyred desired hym vawarde ryght grete instance hym self helde seconde bataylle danu betoke thyrde thus whan began sette forth bellorophon waye ferre gon whan sawe fro fer kynge pricus knewe theyr comyng espyes sette batayll arengid good ordenance bellorophon hym two thousand fightyng men whan kynge pricus sawe come lityll companye supposed hit perceus wende haue wonne afore hand auantage maa peple meue agaynst hem whiche hastely began cruell hard bataylle batayll pricus right ioyous thassamble well employed hys armes swerde dyde meruaylles tyme supposid force haue abiden victorious vainquer enemyes caste eyen toward thebe sawe perseus bataylle descouerd shewyd hem self wherof fortune suche beholdyng hede meduse whiche bare payntyd shelde cristall alle folk moment torned stone saye meyne lost theyr strengthes corages myght lifte theyr swerdes myght statue ymages pricus fledde alle flee myghte cyte feldes auenture perseus daygned folowe chasse cause theyr poure conduyte thus pricus escaped deth abandonned gaf ouer contre wente hem fledde calidonie afterward put deth hercules perseus wente cyte arges wherof yates open oute ony men made ony deffence whan cyte made edicte vpon capitayll payne none hardy ony force ne violence sente seke geant fader acrisius told hym deliueryd hym agayn cyte royame etc courtoysye acrisius helde hym self gretly beholden vnto perseus id hym enquyred doughter dane theyr aduentures perseus told hym alle knewe acrisius right sore desplaysant rudenes doon amende adoptyd perseus sone gaf hym full power gouerne cyte hym self withdrewe hym tour darrayn sente agayn vnto naples danu broder wente bellorophon gaf vnto hem theyr companye grete tresors theyr departement perseus sente many argyens li ye made enhabite contrey thus abode perseus arges wyf andromeda gate many child wete scelenus blache demon erictreus gorgophon whiche alle becam men took wyues yet regnyng kynge acrisius amonge alle gorgophon oon wyf two sonnes alceus electrion alceus engendryd amphitrion electrion engendryd alcumena cam visite kynge gardes kepars tour knewe hym fille vpon hym hurte hym whan felte hym smyten put hym self deffence noyse waxe grete kinge herde bruyt cam rennyng doun departe medle threstid prees suche wyse perseus knewe hym wyth glayue smote hym slewe hym alle porter hym anone whan cam fonde hym ded remembrid thought put hym deth prenosticacion goddes made grete sorow dyde ordeyne obsequye right solempnly obsequye happend iupiter sone vulcan whiche tyme practicqued geder science magike nygromancye etc tyme vulcan forged smote thonders vnto iupiter saye meuyd self smytyng tempestieng fire swerd royames theyr neygbours poetes saye make many fable hym wherof nedeth make mencion tyme perseus dyde grete honour worship vnto fader iupiter like wyse dyde iupiter vnto perseus eche told reherced theyr aduentures whan thobsequye doon kynge acrisius iupiter beheld sawe perseus heuy coude haue ioye retorned crete vnto wif iuno ther exercysed hym self science magique whan perseus fonde hymself allone arges sawe myght recouer ioye departed fro then wente vnto cyte micenes regned long moche deth acrisius renewyd weye coude put hit mynde departed then withdrewe hym grete ooste oryent couetyse loue ouer maister hit late hit passe toke bowe arowes entencion goo woode slee som wylde beste wente forth accompaygnyed gamynedes assone yssued gate ther cam recountryd hym oon knyghtes thebe dyd reuerence vnto kynge sayd hym kynge creon thebe sente hym vnto hym requyred hym wold ayde helpe hym warre agaynst kynge thelleboye trespaced agayn hym whan kynge iupiter herde message knyght ryght ioyous requeste kynge thebe toke knyght hand brought hym palays ther feested hym made hym good chere sayd ryght good herte wold socoure helpe kynge creon warre knyght thebe wyth answer toke leue kynge iupiter retorned vnto thebe thapparayll ordenance maad goo vnto thelleboye hit longe kynge iupiter made armye hasted hym moche myght shortly myght come hows thebe hoped fynde alcumena whan thyng redy toke waye spedde hym iourney cam thebe ryght honourably worshypfully receyuyd kynge quene lady kynge iupiter comyng forgate loke yf myght see alcumena sawe wher grete payne wyste loked amphitryon coude nowher see hym wherof abasshyd afore abasshement approchyd kynge creon demanded hym amphytrion kinge creon answerd shold hastely come assemblid men armes castell arciancie whiche gyuen castell stood betwene thebe atthenes vpon ryuer passing fayr place stronge anon iupiter vnderstonde kinge creon gyuen arciancie amphitrion ymagined sone alcumena place haue goon place ne ben dredd talkyng peple also fered make amphitrion ielous considerid kynge iupiter abode thebe well plesid moche myght see alcumena passid tyme best wise cowde till amphitrion comen departid fro thebe king creon wente laye siege cyte thelleboye accompanyed kyng iupiter many siege cyte assayllyd ofte tyme bataylle agayn theyr enemyes thebe way good fortune ende thelleboye yelded hem alle poyntes wille kynge creon thus whan kinge thebe ouercomen subiugned cyte retorned vnto contre wyth grete ioye etc whan amphitrion sawe enemyes ouercomen ther peryll grete desir goo see wif alcumena dispose hym sonner departid fro oost wyth leue kynge accompaygnyed squyer whan kynge iupiter sawe amphitrion departe vpon waye began thinke auyse hym grete subtylte come hys entente departyd fro ooste wyth gamynedes sone felde way two geder iupiter entryd deuyses gamynedes sayd hym gamynedes haue grete affiance yow ony man lyueth wherfore shall telle yow priuely thyng secrete whiche shall accomplissh semeth whiche ye muste holde kepe secrete trouthe amorous terrybly dame alcumena maner world may forgete ne put fro desyre wel knoweth payne loue haboudeth neuer hardy discouer caas ner neuer durste shewe hit moche knowe wise chaste vertuous consideryd thynking thyng werk fynde ful abusion confesse folie wel maner dispair supposid haue fouden fayt loue alcumena ne ben sodayn detyng amphitrion whiche yet grueth maner hope tyme sawe hym departe fro oost go see wyf companye squyer ymagined hast wold goo vnto arciancie ner shorter way knowe passage longe syn wold transfigure self forme amphitrion yow forme squyer goo alcumena opend chambre vnto iupiter whiche entrid grete ioye thentre chambre iupiter alcumena toke eche armes kyssid wenyng alcumena hit ben amphitrion whan beclipt eche others armes alcumena demanded hym fro whens cam iupiter answerd sayd cam fro thelleboye yeuyng ouer town yeldyng theyr enemyes departed fro oost loue accompanyed squyer come hastelier alcumena well contente wordes iupiter axed hym yf wold ete drynke iupiter answerd wold thyng go bedde shall saye laye desired kynge iupiter neuer grete ioye hym self goyng bedward bad gamynedes shold go chambre dore abide withoute gamynedes departid fro chambre iupiter approuchid alcumena grete loue complaysid loue moche power myght extende wise facion cam iupiter vnto secretes ioye loue deduysing hym self lady hym semed expedyent cradell put hem oon oon syde syde mounted vpon cradell theyr euyll case sone went vp hercules parceyued ferde cause fiers dredefull esuertued hym self toke armes suche myghte puyssance brak bondes whiche wrapped swaded dyde armes handes large whan serpentes ran vpon hym put hem backe naturell strength force many tymes fought wyth hem wyth fystes ryght longe fynably whan hercules sawe serpentes athene atticque dayly cam men woman child see hym elder grewe enforced strenghte whan x yer olde ther mighte man stande ne abide hande xiii yer age began doo sue armes propre mocion thought wold goo vpon mount olympus wold abyde answer alle maner men theder comyng space xv dayes receyue armes wrastelyng ony proof assaye strengthe come theffect enterpryse awayted day whan eristeus cam see hym sayd hym syre ye haue nourysshid vnto tyme lyke owne sone yf fortune contrarye nature knowleche shold infortunat childe euer born saye sonne iupiter saye amphitrion hit haue fader yow nourysshid substance wherfore drawe vnto yow fader aduer yse yow purposid mounte olympus hasty tyme goodly may ther shall abide alle theder shall come xv dayes duryng full furnyssh spere swerde wrastlyng nyng alleway forseen hit lycence leue hit plese yow courtoysye gyue hym shall beste som pry thende meue hertes noble men vnto vaylliance myghte attayne worshippe eristeus answerd sayde hercules fayr sone ye requyre thynge honest worshipfull shall therto agreable ye yong well ye strong puyssant wote well ther man may endure agaynst yow syn hit ye haue right well contente ye shewe proef strength yougth conduyte brynge enterprise vnto worshippe shall araye yow richely yf ye propre sonne fader answerd hercules thanke yow grace kyndenes sin hit playsir hit behoueth yow chese man grete vnderstandyng auctorite shall goo vnto alle royames march shewe vnto kynges prynces gentill men enterprise haue taken fayr sone saide eristeus ye saye trowth ye shall make lres conteynyng entencion sende whan haue receyuyd shall good diligence ye reson shall content deuyses many kynge eristeus went home hercules toke enke parchemyn sette hym wryte lettres forme paas whiche wolde make conteyned wyse gretyng alle kynges prince knyghtes gentill men ladyes damoyselles fro esquyer vnknowen well fortuned late yow haue knowleche first day moneth may next folowing esquyer vnknowen shall mounte olimpus dispose hym habillemens conuenyent vnto armes playsir goddes fortune resseyue alle ben noble hous name shall come theder maner foloweth begynnyng firste thre dayes shall holde paas wrastling shall beste iugement iuges therto comised shall wynne elephant sin golde fourth day shall renne forlong stade ayenst wole renne best renneth shall wynne courseur leuyng fyfte sixthe dayes shall shote wyth hand bowe first moste strayt nyghe moste ferre shoteth moste strayt nyghe shall wynne gloue golde best ferre shall haue bowe sheet arowes seuenth day shall caste stone ayenst alle men best doth ther shall haue ryche dyamont eyghte day folowyng vnto fyftenthe shall armes yf ony proue hym self oon alone ayenst hym shall receyuyd forseen duryng first sixe dayes shall come presente hym vnto iuges doth best shall haue riche swerde yf hit happe shall come feste wyll tornoye gyder maner batayll ioustyng wyth courtoys rochettis fyghtyng wyth swerdes rabatnes iuges shall ordeyne capitaynes suche shall seme conuenyent best doth excersite shall wynne chappelet lawrer alle thynges fore wreton sayd esquyer vnknowen promytteth accomplissh prayeth vnto noble men lady damoyselles wylle vouchesauf come see thassemble noblesse whiche shall parformed playsir inmortall goddes whiche wyll gyue receyuours thys mandement multeplyance honour encresynge good fortune etc whan hercules wreton mandement grossyd hit vp sente hit eristeus whiche red hit hym semed inuencion auctour makar good right digne put memorie callid knyghtes gaf hym charge office go publisshe mandement courtes alle kynges grece knyght enprised right good herte sayd office first officer armes euer wente athene thebe arges lacedomone archade achaye perelye magnefie crete ephese pepos triopolye thesaylle alle aboute publisshid mandement oute declaring shold kepe paas herde speke squyer vnknowen vnderstode hye enterprise iugyd hym cam noble corage myght fayle gete honour worshippe knyghte furnyssh viage iiii monethes terme acomplissh hit alle party cam theder many noble men ladyes damoyselles nombre myght extemed mounte full alle side nyght ther grete bruyt noyse oon make theyr tentes loggys bowes leues theyr tabernacle hit ought forgoten whan euen comen knight publisshid mandement assemblid comyn tente alle kynges comen theder requyred name behalue esquyer vnknowen wold chese amonge suche sholde iuges gyue pry whan kynges yuyte hercules amphitrion side beleuyd tht sone iupiter side sayde apperteyneth hym sente hem worde tht myght better come solempnyte whiche moste speciall thynge newe tht euer spoken tyme first day maye oure tyme sonne caste hete vpon erthe hercules dide sowne trompe make ladyes go vp scaffoldes place anone beyng mou tyd sette hercules lepe tente habillemens wrastle cam myddis place felde gentill men armes ladyes damoyselles esquyer vnknowen comparant persone vpon mount olimpus presentith self fornisshe contenu mandemet ordre manere chapitres make mencion wherfore yf ther ony man proue muste begonnen ende wordes accomplissid two noble esquyers approchid seasid eche theseus employed puyssance hercules suffrid hym moche wold cowde oute shewyng puttyng oute vertu myght agayn hym shoke lugged eche finably hercules caste theseus moste softly fauourably cowde wherof lawghter grete among ladyes damoyselles theseus departid fro place wente amonge ladyes damoysellys prayng wold take hit gree cam vnto paas many yong esquyers knowe name laboured traueyllyd largely gete honour worshyp theyr laboure prouffityd lytyll vnto regard pry hercules caste put erthe alle cam wrastlyng duryd foure owres contynually laste requeste ladyes iuges made wrastlyng cesse day cause semed hercules yong achyeuyd grete werke etc whan hercules vnderstand iuges made cesse wrastlyng ryght sorowfull wrastlyng singuler playsir iuges wyth eristeus cam hym made hym clothes araye hym brought hym comyn halle ladyes daunsyng syngyng ioyously sayd hym muste daunse synge lyke dide hercules excused hym sore excuse myght auaylle sette daunce hande right fayr damoysell named megere yong eage right well adressid witte vnderstandyng doughter kynge creon whan hercules sawe hym hand oon noble damoyselle sore abasshid shamed damoysell syde also shamfaste seen hercules wrastle sette alle loue hym wiste none hem bothe saye stede wordes vsid preuy couert regard hercules caught singuler plaisir beholde see damoyselle nere damoyselle hercules herte sette hym shall saye loue nyght submysid constrayned loue eche oute spekyng theyr awtes cause therof men shold haue founden grece two fayre child ne better accomplisshid yxion oughte haue horse sow e trompe redy iuste ran oon ayenst couragiously trowblid ayer duste pouldre roos theyr hors foot recountre eche mette often tymes ther ouerthrowen vnder hors som reuersid torned vp doun coopyng ther brakke theyr speris knyghtly cheuaulrously ther plente vaylliant knyghtes point whan knightes hors back theyr foot sette hande swerdes pietons footemen began renewe tornoye ioyous playsant forgyng theyr helmes hewyng sheldes coragyously especyall partye yxion partye kynge tandarus constrayned crye hercules vnto rescows etc whan hercules herde cryed hym passing ioyous hit noyous hym ydle see laboure nyhe tornoye beholdyng dyde beste swerde fyfte crye put werse made wente vnto theyr ayde helpe began tornoye syde grettest stroke gyuen plesantly hi ioye beholde kynge yxion cam agaynst hym susteyne faytes holde gyder folk certes byen venue hercules smote hym shelde suche wyse stonyed bare hym erthe doun hors tho began ther grete showte laughter well began entende fested hem foure dayes longe fourth day tydynges cam vnto poort hauene comen strange folk fortune whiche clothed righte plesante robe garmetes whan kynge eristeus herde tydynges sente anon fecche necessarie mannes lyf well telle yow place conuersacion haue hauntyse ther ben many yles lyyng aboute ferthest partyes maurce yonde ampolesye growe alle beste thynges men thynke ther kynge named mountaygne valeye hit suche wyse gardyn alle grene ther ben ther many sheep mouton meruaylle whiche ben kept cherisshid also diligently fyn golde mouton speke haue robe gownes maad may haue muste bye grete pris gold ete flessh clothe v skynnys knowe ye certayn yle oon entree entreth ther wold kynge philotes geant whiche ben wise subtill meruayllously stronge alwey kepe thentre yle allwaye oon sayd hercules shulle haue otherwyse sayde geant sayd hercules leste late v haue pris ye haue goten hem sayd geant kynge phylotes hath conquerd swerd yle mouton hercules answerd myn entencion like wise conquere yle vpon yf ye wole defende hit haste yow ye muste haue batayll ayenst elli late yle may ther wille anone geant vnderstande conclusion hercules made hym redy defende paas blewe grete horne hangyng tree atte sownyng horn doughters athlas awakyd philotes tolde hym gete paa geant blowen horn philotes wordes roose vp armed hym cam paas fonde hercules force putte back geant reseruyd philotes subtill man armes alle hisperye sore abasshid began sihe notwythstandyng longe soiorned whan hercules smote geant right sholdre suche strength vertu shelde geant falle fro hym armes alle frusshid wordes cam vnto paas helde grete bordone whiche smote sore vpon shelde hercules made hym disauale paas wherof philotes began lawhe thoughte haue smeten yet hercules bordon whiche shamed strook kepte paas whiche conteyneth well two cubites heighte whan hercules sawe knewe philotes kepte paas oute abassing aduenturyng come doun thoughte subtylly wold fayne hym self wery lityll lityll began smyte hercules cam place agayn gaf grete strook philotes made hym recule goo back foure foot philotes abasshid repentyd hym descended fro paas nought repentyng myght auaylle took corage enhaunsed swerd
