eristeus putte hem two wynges oon right side lyfte side cam rennyng vpon troians grete noyse grete tempeste alle troians felte well theyr comyng tyme wyste entende smyten afore behynde sore loste rowte pryant wiste becam etc entremetyng faytes laomedon oute prees refresshid hym herd saye sone pryant taken wherfore passing sorowfull grete payne swete cam herte fro then alle membris wente hym self agayn batayll half mynde batayll fell enuenymed hard fightyng augmente encrese ouergrete sorowe laomedon fonde folk worse losse lasse foughte side sawe horyons stroke grekes grete desmesurable men disrenged tharayes broken chargid heuy stroke heuy glayues wente torned back began flee whan hyt cam disconfiture laomedon abode laste entrid agayn cyte hastely mighte grekes folowed troians asprely nyhe entryd hem grete effusion blood hercules firste wan gate grekes portier putte alle knowleche many troians passid cuttyng swerd many fleed away feldes busshis shal saye whan laomedon sawe force cyte taken put handes gouernance grekes right sore disconforted despayr took doughters exione antigone moste precyous iewels bagues fled away preuely thenkyng enemyes shold make right grete destruction pyllyng dyde whan hercules put men within cyte abandonned robbe pylle thus troians secuted canellys tempryd theyr blood tthe howses beten doun grete rychesses put proyes alle goodes cyte ther lefte nothing hoole palays ylion ladyes maydens withdrawen hercules wolde wyse destroye palays moche ladyes made hym requeste spare hit pryse hercules soughte longe laomedon palays ylion alle place cyte cowde tidyngis hym wherfore sore desplaysant whan beten walles ben made wyth moneye goddes departed then retorned grece wyth grete glorye wyse troye destroyed first tyme wherfore shall thus make ende firste booke shall begynne seconde booke shall shewyd troye reedyfyed hit destroyed seconde tyme pryant areysed hit made hit agayn contynuyng noble labour hercules newe begonne etc thus endeth first book ueyll gadryng geder historyes troye phiere begynneth seconde booke recueill historyes troye speketh prowess stronge hercules deth etc phowe hercules foughte ayenst thre lyon foreste nemee slewe tooke skynnys hide etc fyrste booke begonnen faytes prowesse stronge puyssaut geant hercules destroyed fyrste cyte troye vpon kynge laomedon whiche foot conqueste retorned grece helde hym certayn space time doyng ony thynge founde writyng olde iuno euyll cursid enuye gaf ymagyne thynke myght make hercules destroied dye tidynges cam crete foreste nemee comen many lyon amonge ther oon sixteen palme heyght destroyed wasted alle contree iuno warre agaynst eristens haue aqueyntance hercules vnder fayned colour good loue sende hym clawes lyon maad pee cristens sende hym come crete conferme pee eristens thought thynge well wente crete brought hym hercules pe made iuno acqueyntid hercules cam speke lyon forest nemee etc moche spake iuno accountid hem said hercules hit wel faite gete hym honour worshipp go vnto foreste nemee employe hym conquere tho lyon hercules wenyng iuno counceillid hym goo assaylle lyon worship prouffyt enterprysed goo foreste iuno requyred hym yf wente whan vaynquysshid lyon shold retorne vnto hercules promysid wold doo departed fro crete fyrste wente thebe see gera make harnoys armes poynt whan ladyes thebe knewe hercules wold goo ayenst lyon nemee alle complayned yougth thoughte shlod dye ffor lion cruell terrible megera aboue passyng sorowfull required lady wolde praye euristeus wold kepe hercules fro going vnto daungerous voyage ladyes accomplisshid requeste megera wende haue broken voyage hercules meen curisteus myght wyse lette purpose hercules answerd euristeus vnto ladyes hit first emprise taken hand requeste ony ladie moche quene iuno made hym hit intencon accomplissh hit playsir tho goddes fortune hercules grete herte courage exalted honour leuer haue dyed haue thynge werof shold folowe ony dyshonoure whan armes redy adowbyd hym toke leue kyng creon euristeus amphitrion ladyes damoiselle accompanyed philotes whiche wold neuer leue hym detid fro thebe spedde hym iourney cam vnto foreste nemee whyche stood ser arges approching foreste wente two day findyng bestes men vnto tyme entryng foreste fonde pastour hierdman named melorcus herdeman mountyd vpon grete tree whan sawe hercules entre woode ascryed hym sayng syre ye ded yf ye goo ony retorne lightly fiers lyon ete yow elli come hether vp vpon tree hercules heeryng wordes molorcus loked vpon tree demaunded hym ala said pastour moste poure man alle lyon foreste theyr comyng haue eten grete herde bestes haue nourisshid aboue haue eten alle famyllye meyne haue deuoured saue allone whiche haue auenture grete sauyd self vpon tree ete thyng elli leues akehornes dare descende come doun fere thre lyon whyche ben whiche wyll sone assayle yow yf ye departe flee etc pastour fynysshyng wordes ther cam leepyng busshe thre lion marched ayenst hercules roryng criyng openyng eyen grete felonnye hit semed wold haue thurgh percyd hercules fell sight grete lyon cam fyrst heer stondyng vp hyhe olyphant grete auenant hede twyes grete hede abool hercules seeyng come took glayue clobbe philotes bare philotes notwithstandyng prowesse sore aferde wente vpon tree vnto herdeman hercules sette hys clobbe vnto tree toke hys glayue faste betwene fystes lyon approchyng brayed throtes hercules smote oon betwene eyen bare hym doun erthe satte vpon buttokes grete lyon wende haue sprongen vpon hercules haue taken hym clawes maad terryble leep whan hercules sawe knewe entente torned fro hym smote thirde lyon whyche lyght peert conduysed glayue right fermely throte rought hym herte som euer resistence made bytyng glayue lefte hit wythin body suche wyse fyll doun ded whan two lyon sawe felawe arayed sette clawes erthe howlid yrously hit semed thonder spronge stomakes foreste denned therof hercules toke swerd two lyon approched newe agayn ran vpon hym pawes hurte hym desmesurably losed armeurs nayles entryng flessh drewe hem alle dyed blood hercules herte sore troublid whan felte woundes lyon made hauncid swerd smote oon grete lion skyn hard swerd myght entre therm hit myght grete stedy thus began batayll lyon hercules lityll lyon passyng aygre fyers launched hym forth ofte tymes ayenst hercules allewey wende haue hurte hym clawes cutted lyke rasour launched ofte hit euyl helth ease hercules amonge many stroke made departe body ryght legge ryght nyghe sholdre smote hym doun foot lyon laye ded etc whan hercules sawe delyuerid two euyll bestes nomore doo grete lyon began haue hope good fortune ioye hym self bataylle whyche stronge susteyne ffor grete lion gaf hym grete stroke pawes putte hym ofte tymes parill deth swerd hercules myghte neuer entre skyn beste hit hard lyon toke swerd betwene teth nayles wyth grete payne pullid rachid hit hym ffynably whan longe foughten swerd knewe well therby myghte reyse blood lyon wold assaye yf clubbe hym prouffytable toke hyt fyrst strook lyon cam vp hym gaf hym strook wyth clubbe grete moutthe alle teeth braak fyll fore hym lyon felyng stroke maad grete meruayllous howling haunsed pawes wende haue pullyd doun hercules fledd comyng lyon lyon fill ground grete fiersnes failyng maad whan hercules sawe tht fallen leep vpon hym bete hym helde hym wyth handes aboute throte dismesurably brought iawes place ioynte made eyen flee heed stranglid hym slewe hym doyng foot werke hercules shewid synguler hardynes increable force estranglid wyth handes lyon skyn hard glayue ne swerd myghte entre ner ony harme put hym deth excessiue vailliance whan doon wente lyued yet brake tare hym yf hit ben lityll lambe called philotes pastour herdman meruaillously ioyous glad highe victorie hercules fonde manyer fle lyon take skynnes helpe herdman whan flayn hem hit nyght hercules demaunded herdeman yf ther ony hous loggyng ther myght haue mete drynke herdeman brought hym hous wher fonde prouision mete drinke wherwith good man feested hercules power hym semed paradys thus hercules passid day nyght forgate thenke woundes felle smarted litill nought slepte nyght notwithstanding whan day apperid toke leue herdeman deted toke iorney goo crete shewe quene iuno thre lyon skynnys thanke good aduertisment phow iuno sente hercules egypte slayn tyrant busire hercules slewe tyrant ayenst hoope iuno tyme regned egipte kynge busire sone quene libie londe egipte drye fertile barayne busirie remedye callid clerkes helden scence zorastes axed myght doo helthe royame counceylled goddes answere muste sacrefye vnto hem mannes blood whan busire naturelly euyll neuer doon good herde answer began tyrannyse hym self tiraut afore began first peple takyng pluckyng fro moders lytyll child fro men wyues fro wiues husbondes brennyng fowling teples egipte blood homysides slaughter droughte sessed augmentid waxe clerkes demauded gooddes cause dewes water ner rayne fro aboue answerd wold haue iuste true blood egypte strange blood whiche shold take make sacrefise therof goddes answer wold haue sacrefice blood busire strange vertuous policye ferre fro good clerkes vnderstood wold haue blood stranger busire aduertised answer cessed secute blood egipte tourned glayue vpon blood strangiers made edycte statute tht stranger shold entre cyte shold sacryfied goddes wold slee estrangers might gete edicte dampnable custome many estrangers noble putte sacrefice blood shedde egipte amonge oon noble man crete lignage iuno perisshed infortune swerd busire tydynges cam crete made hym grete sorowe sorowe cours hercules philotes cam vnto quene iuno fond charged teeres wepyng cyte tyme honderd cytees crete kynge iupiter held hym iuno many cause resons whan hercules retorned vnto lady iuno stepmoder made reuerence shewid skynnys lion slayn thanked hyhe auenture ensigned hym etc cursid stepmoder retorne hercules augmentyng sorowe vpon newe sorowe reseyued fested hercules made hym fayntly grettest chiere coude hit vpon poynt goo dyner made hym dyne ete wyth etyng dyuerce deuyces lyon thoughte remembrid howe myght make hercules dye myght better sende hym egypte tyme concluded self wold sende hym egipte yf myght doo chaunged propose lyon said hercules comyng agayn saefte recomendable name shall put perpe uell louyng preisyng amonge worthy beste world ye haue doon many fair enterprise fectes yong childhod ye made world wondre meruayle victorye serpentes yow enstranglid ye haue maad swerd braundysshe occidente ffrygie uow newly nemee thauentures place haue gyuen yow ryght moche honour worshippe wherof haue right grete ioye ffor eche sone ought glad enioye well doyng nother especiall noble man specyally whan putteth hym payne vaylliantnes euery persone holden bounden councelle hym vnto worshipp wele wherfor whan hit ye enuertue self fro day day seke peryls see fals daungers erthe thende surmout alle aduertyse yow egypte tyraut sacrefieth estrangiers come contre oute rescruyng noble man villayn semeth yf fortune helpe yow go conquere hym ye shold gete grete honour worship yow yowres helthe prouffit nacions world madame answerd hercules ner neuer shall liue suche recomendacion ye saye reporte notwithstondyng moche haue grete desyre doo werkes may plesyr peple helthe wele promette yow swere morn oute ony delaye shall put deuoyr way goo egypte shall neuer retorne agayn contree vnto tyme haue seen teraut yf leye put hand sacrefyse haue entencion shall hyt wyth smytyng stroke iuno heeryng thenterpryse hercules herte passyng grete ioye day passid many deuyses hercules took skynnes lyon delyuerid certayn werkemen make garment maner armour arme hym morn toke leue stepmoder departed fro crete longe iourneyed waye philotes oute fyndyng ony auenture wherof ony memoire day cam gate cyte menphyn egypte wher tyrant busire held residence whan hercules comen nyghe vnto gate toke clobbe philotes bare lefte philotes entrid hym self cyte ben longe ner ferre goon busire whiche aduertysed comyng hys espyes cam agaynst hym many complices oute spekyng ony word ran vpon hym hercules well assured knewe tyrant mayntien syngnes told hym lyfte vp clobbe whan sawe hym come tyrant wold haue smyten hym glayue oute ony word spekyng smote tirant clobbe vpon ryght syde desmesurably bare hym vnto erthe also brake rybbys body arayed hym myght neuer releue hym self egipciens seeyng busire ouerthrowen ran hym releue hym whiche coude doo heuy assailled hercules cyte ameuyd hercules right ioyous beten tyrant began lerne egypciens knowe clobbe slewe many remenant maad flee strookes heuy peysaut complices busire acustomed shede mannes blood blood shedd sparkled abrood coude ner myght remedie meschance grete hercules fillyd place dede body longe bataylle fonde hym silf allone ffor none hardy durste seen fore hym peples comonte egipcyens gaf charge rescous kynge whan sawe hym beten alle hated hym sawe bataylle fro ferre grete rowtes whan hercules moche doon fonde man fight hym sette doun clubbe adressid hym vnto grete companye egipcyens stood assured wold thynge vnto axed peple assailled hym answerd hym knelyng knee manslears hangemen peple vicious euyll lyuyng kynge first beten doun worste hem alle hadd purposed haue put hym deth strangier make sacrefice vnto goddes prayd hym wold sacrefyce sayd kynge hercules graunted petycion accorded hyt vnto peple anone toke cursid tyraut busire lyued yet bare hym vpon sholdre vnto temple whiche egypciens shewid hym fals tyraut cryed helpe terribly crye auayled hym egypciens cryed vnto hercules sacrefice sacrefice hym whan hercules cam temple sacrefised hym tht shewid hym hys cursid euyll lyf whan fyre put vnto sacrefice hit began rayne grete droughte began faile wherof egypciens ioyous none coude specifye songe louynges preisinges hercules brought hym vnto palais philotes also whiche seen ordeyned constituted hercules kynge ouer whiche refused ordeyned iuges gouerne departed retorned vnto quene iuno whiche grete sorowe kynge creon whiche grete ioye told recounted prowess phow hercules espowsed megera made kynghte thebe etc suche wise yonge wyne labour besynes labourer groweth heighte bowes spred brood full fruyte semblably hercules vertue labouryng hym grewe verdur well doyng fruyt noblesse werkes bowes hys braunches began spreed brood mounte ryse fro royame roiame secrete conspiracons iuno cursed enuyes myght hurte ner mynusshe vertue hercules wenyd abasshe hurte hym cause enhauncement yf puyssant stronge body yet stronge vertue hit sette hym precyous stone gold odour flour raye sonne beme sonne belouyd kynges prynces ladyes damoyselles noble villaines en especial megera doughter kyngt creon louyd hym certes deceyued ffor hercules loued also neuer houre thoughte well durst none speke matyere ashamed dyscouure whereof hope haue honour worship behelde eche ofte bewayled complayned self desyred day myghte take eche maryage moche wisshed day laste hit cam morow tyde hercules goon vnto wood take wylde beste remembrid hym lady began speke saie hym sylf softely shall alleway payne shall myn herte neuer eased alway languysshyng loue see oon grete ioye wyth loues ladyes wote neuer come poynte oon haue chosen aboue achyeue purpoos wote neuer begynne dar speke ner haue yet requyred loue ner haue assayed yf wold condescende shall speke wote neuer yf speke reffuse shall fall dispayre shall dye sorowe melancolye desplaisir shall neuer dar come noble assemblee foot ala payne considerid oon tyme must come speke yf frendes oon acorde gyue maryage contente ner pleased alle lost moste ieopardye haue good grace ffor grace may nought doo hyt necessite seke requyre yf may haue good wyll syn hit ffor yf slepe thus speke shall neuer achyue ner come pourpoos hercules ferme purpoos esprised enflamed grete desire departid wood abandoned wild beste gaf hit ouer come vnto megera thenkyng wordes myght come shewe laye herte wente ferre cam vnto gardyn palays many ladyes damoyselles made reuerences espied tyme myght speke megera waxe pensyf hit meruaille entremeted thynge deuyse ladyes drewe hym parte gardyn whan ladyes beheld hym pensyf dyuerce cam hym talked hym put hym thoughtes pensyfnes coude laste megera cam hym assone hercules sawe come hym began syghe cam agayn sayd hym hercules ye pensif put away fro suche melancolye telle tydynges pray yow lady answerd hercules thanke yow good visitacyon syn hit pleseth yow tidynges knowe shall saie yow paart first aduertyse cause brought put abisme swolowe pensifnes sighes day comen vnto contemplacion ffor wente wood hunte remembrance ryght noble beaute contynuelly beyng myn ymaginacon cam made entre secret debate wete yf shold allewey lyue vnguerdoned vnrewarded loue also yf durst saie yow haue sette myn herte loue yow madame debate grete ende concluded come vnto yow knowe conclucion fortune whether hit deth lyf deliberacion thynkyng myght spede vnto yow poynt partie comyng hath put right grete thought pensifnes ffor wiste neuer come poynte speke yow apart may enploye tyme saye yow trouthe syn tyme olympiade haue desired yow nyght day tyme putte myn herte seruytude concludyng loue yow pardurably madame knowe woot well haue enterprysed thynge indygne worthy notwithstandyng abide mercy requyre yow hit please yow resseyue grace suche wyse shortly may see day maryage etc whan megera vnderstood wordes loue hercules herte reioysed wyth grete solaas notwithstandyng ashamed shamefaste answerd hela hercules fortune fynde grace gentil man ye excessiue prowes gloryous labour respledant vertues ben moche value ye ar worthy haue wyf flour ladyes choys wordes many damoyselles cam vnto causyd sece theyr deuyses loue sayden megera hyt tyme withdrawe go dyne megera sorowful hasty departyng space deuyse loue ne myghte achieue purpoos constraynt toke leue hercules wente halle refeccioned loue hercules abood gardin glad ioious swete answer receyuyd etc whan ladyes lefte hercules gardyn also sone goon hercules assemblid euristus amphitrion said hem grete desire maried prayed wold goo kynge creon knowe yf wold giue hym doughter megera spake kyng creon mariage kyng herd hem speke ryght gladly ffor mater plesyd hym answerd myght nowher better bestowe hys doughter moste noble man world hercules louyd owen sone whiche vailliant noble felawe like vnto hym content gyue hym doughter wold demande euristus amphitrion thanked kyng courtoys answer megra hercules sente fore kynge made hem trouthplyte eche grete ioye bothe party processe tyme day espow sailles mariage halowed glorie tryumphe honour ioye shal saie laye gider auenture liuyd gyder right honestly anone solempnyte mariage hercules cam kyng creon praied hym tht wold adubbe make hym knyght moche royame ioonie comen vnto hym chosen hym kynge cyte good renomee kyng creon ioyous chosen kynge ycome answerd wold accomplissh desire wold shold certayn day assigned saiyng wold make right noble feste men shold iouste tornoye wold come theder alle kynges prynces grece hercules accorded agreed counceyll kynge kynge sente messagers vnto kynges grece praied hem chiualerie dubbyng knyght noble man shall hold paas day named sette furnysshe shall come ioustes renome forsayd ffeste none borne knowen vnto alle regnes grece apparayll ordenance grete thebe oon disposed tyme passed day cam many kynge knyght comen tyme thebe theseus iason sone kynge eson amonge kynges maad grete bruyt grete pompes aboute ten clocke fore none kyng creon wente place ordeyned arayed ioustes corner place tente tente hercules alle alone tyme ladyes damoyselles wente mounted vpon scaffoldes iousters cam place man knewe ne wiste newe knyght shall saye whan kynge creon sawe knyghtes comen sydes ladyes gon vp skaffoldes sente hercules made hym knyght statute hercules mountyd vpon hors toke spere hys shelde escryed ther thende eche man shold deuoyr oon desired haue worshipp toke speres ran ayenste hercules began ioustes right hoote sharpe speres stronge brake lightly mette often tymes ouerthrowen smyten doun horse myght iuste ayenst hercules assayed eche lyke lyke iason theseus iusted ofte tymes ayenst hercules pirothus sone kynge yxion lyke wyse alle name mayntened right vailliantly notwithstandyng aboue hercules abood men man myght abide stroke bare hem doun reseruyd iason whiche encountrid hym dyuerce tymes gaf hym many grete stroke hercules bare doun theseus erthe pirothus well fyfty stronge knyghtes dide moche man abode place iason lefte sessed ioustes vailliance hercules fonde iason euer specyall loue hym toke acqueyntance hym fested hym made hym grete chere ende ioustes knyghtes ladyes damoyselles wente vnto pallays hercules maad kynge yconye feste grete riche reherce stranger gretly fested hyghly thanked comune shall make longe processe whan feste passid honour glorye hercules wherof ony memoire saye pirothus praid wedding thessalonyque certayn day named eche man promysid hym go theder ther ate euery man toke leue hercules whan tyme come departing eche man retorned contre place coude ynowhe meruail glorye haboudynge apperynge habonde growe flourysshe fructefie hercules whiche courtoys humble grace temporall honour worship vertuous prowde ne enhaunsid hym self meked lowed hym self phow centaures rauysshed ypodame weddyng pirothus hercules recouerd agayn vaynquysshid batayll centaures contynue matiere whan hercules sawe approche day weddyng pirothus disposed hym go theder space tyme wente forth way toke philotes hym alauenture toke hym armures skyn lyon whan megera sawe hym departe sore troublid departyng tht toke armour hym thought yf hercules herd speke ony aueture wold goo theder put hym deuoir assaie hym self agayn hit grete sighes loked hym ferre myghte praiyng goddes wold bringe hym shortly agayn hercules phylotes wente forth contrey also moche myght exploited iourney cam thessalonycque wher resseyued wyth grete ioye pirothus ffrendes fonde right grete assemble noble men ladyes damoyselles theseus iason frendes iason wolde iason sholde maad kynght doo presented hym hercules whiche gaf hym ordre knyghthode hercules sayd seen hym good begynnyng noble man yf may lyue shall attayne one thynges right hyhe noble amonge thynges day weddyng cam cyte full noblesse centaures honderd geantes armed ran wynde whiche kynge yxion ordeyned thes saylle whome dwellyd mollose aphyte cyte epire wherof quene ypodame ladye bryde weddyng ther many kynges prynces haue name quene ypodame pirothus weddyd gyder lawe whan tyme dyner come sette ladye halle maad generall ffeste ffeste alle worlde amply seruyd manyer good wynes good mete especyall centaures made passyng good chyere dronke moche stronge wynes pryncypall capitayn named euricus wordes gyder troublid ffeste trouble foughte geder caste eche pottes plater wynes mete terrybly many hurte ded anone halle full noyse euricus fyfty geautes yssued pr e wente feche harnois armour whan armed entrid halle content trouble maad well hercules enteudyd appese slewe eche toke quene ypodame bare rauysshid fledd away whan lady sawe grete outrage escried affraied thaffraie grete hercules iason pirothus theseus ran vnto whan knewe centaures rauysshid lady fewe wordes wente armed anone etc hercules dyd skyn lyon toke swerd bowe arowes wente geantes wyth oute abidyng ony companye persone geantes withdrawen vnder tree renged bataylle wiste well seurly firste shold come shold hercules hatyd hercules secretly envie glorye swore deth hercules whan termes deuyses euricus aspied fro ferre hercules shewid hym felawshipp hercules alone cam paas softely man cam rennyng lightly also swyftely herte rennyth valeye semed flawe ayer swyftenes hercules ne abasshyd ne affrayed centaures well foure score alle grete corages toke glayues polha e swerdes habyllemens warre strengest wente ayenst hercules syde assone hercules approchid nyghe myght shote bente bowe arowe smote centaure named gryneus suche wyse arowe perced heed entryng visage nayled attachid hede vnto tree stoode hynde hym second arowe smote another geant named petreus breste thurgh armour hit wente thurgh body thirde hurte dorillas tarrible geant nailed hand vnto visage ffor whan geant sawe strook come held vp hand fore visage arowe entrid grete myght afore sayd made hand attachid visage whyche strook ded shotte many moo arowes also longe ony shotte none yf hurt slewe oon geantes whan shotte failled geantes strongly esmeuyd seen felawes dye shotte hercules escried vpon hercules enuyronned hym sydes cilarus pheotones nessus myncus astilo lodeum piseon firste smote vpon hercules glayues hercules toke swerd cam agayn pheotones grete axe grete hyt mannys burthon pheotones anone lyfte vp hys grete axe wende haue smyten myghty strook vpon hercules hercules knewe ynowhe warre torned hym strooke grete axe fylle doun ground sodenly hercules caught grete axe plukkyd hit handes forthwith gaf hym strook grete smote right arme sholdre etc svche begynnyng batayll hercules centaures cilarus smote hercules behynde myght piseon ledeum smote hym also oon tyme notwithstondyng hercules ast nyed one therfore retornyng cilarus gaf hym strook axe fermli helme hit entrid body confouded geant erthe seruyd lyke wyse piseon ledeum iason theseus put batayll well prouved yougthe theyr comyng gyue herte courage hercules threstid grettest pr e geants wroughte axe cursyd phiotones brought hit theder alle forged hit betyng smytyng doun fore hercules began seke ypodame fonde alle wepte right beside nyhe euricus spake euricus said hym thou euyll gloton thou haste day trowblid feste lady ffrende pirothus anone shall trowble thyn esperite word descharged axe smote euricus suche wise heed fill doun dede vnto grete enbassement geantes ffor beholdyng axe dyed wyth blood curicus capitayne abasshid began hercules smyte vpon geantes none seure aferde ner none ferme e began hyde hym tremble fere hys strookes sustenable put enemyes araye vnto flyght ffinably wyth helpe iason theseus pirothus meruaillousli vaillant vaynquysshid chassed vnto ryuer wher xij sauved passyng swymmyng ouer remenant persecuted vnto deth reseruyd lyncus hercules helde prisonner moche discomfiture praid hym mercy yelded hym vnto hym thus centaures destroied strength hand hercules ony whan hercules doon ther moo centaures vpon place hys felawys retorned vnto ypodame brought agayn vnto cyte grete tryumphe shall saye ladyes recourid ioye recourance ypodame recomenced began agayn feste dured eyght dayes ryght grete sumptuous etc phow pluto rauysshid proserpyne orpheus wente hell quene serum cam vnto weddyng pirothus theseus pyrothus foughte wyth cerberus porter sayd helle etc tyme wete lityll fore weddyng pirothus pluto kynge molose sone saturne broder iupiter saylyd wente see sechyng hys aduentures longe sayled arryuyd secyle fonde nyghe ryuage right grete assamblee secyliens halowed ffeste goddes whan pluto sawe feste dide arme xx felawshypp vnder robe garnementes wente maner see feste wete yf myght fynde ony proie pluto grettest theef moste lecherous man world hym geant named cerberus ynowh ylyke vnto pluto condicons corage moche strenger puyssant body alle grete geantes lerned thyng elli harme euyll coude none wise doo whan secilyens sawe pluto come felawes supposed hit neighebours cam see playes esbatementis moche cam clothed theyr garnementis sawe none armour ne harnoys enforced synge dauce certes songes daunces pardurable ner dured longe comyng vnto kynge pluto caste eyen side sawe quene march beheld feste doughter made chapelet flowres moder named serum doughter callid proserpyne maried vnto noble man named orpheus sat beside played harpe proserpyne passyng mervaillous fayr anone pluto seen desired coueyted aduertised folke secretly cam nyhe felte hym self surmounted coueytise beaulte sette handes leyde back bare way whan orpheus serum sawe proserpine rauisshid escried pietously anguisshously vpon pluto crye cecyliens lefte feste ran pluto grete nombre men woman hoping haue rescowed proserpine whan cerberus complices sawe murmure drewe swerdes shewid armes smote vpon approchid sleyng largely recuyellid wente vnto porte maulgre cecyliens orpheus guyded pluto shippe entrid disancrid caried way proserpine cecyliens dispourueid armes coude withstand rauisshement proserpine departyng fro porte made moste aspre ill sorowe coude proserpyne wepte sore side pietously cryed right hyhe lowde serum side cecyliens made skarcete teeres certes orpheus faylid furnysshe teeres parfound sighes loued proserpine loued hym also departyng hertes put hard greuous distresse harde anguyssh proserpine fill doun swone orpheus rauisshid anger retorned palais whan loste sight proserpine helde hym cloos hys chambre speche two dayes end two dayes serum cam visite orpheus wold nether ete ne drynke sayd hym knewe wel rauisshour doughteer hit pluto kyng melose dweld partie thessaylle lowe basse cite callid helle moche yle kynge pluto complices dide moche harme euyll compared lykened vnto deuylles cite named helle whan orpheus vnderstode proserpyne helle toke lityll hope hym self ete dranke made vowe wold neuer reste place vnto tyme ben helle see proserpine eten sente maronners bad hem make redy shipp whan shypp garnysshid hit behouyd leue congie taken quene serum habite disguysed entrid allone shipp harpe maad mariner saile forth see suche wise arryued oon poortes thessayll orpheus wente lande comanded maryners shold abide hym place vnto certayn tyme named departed wente fro contre contre longe spede mater came yate helle whiche cerberus kepte began plaie harpe right sweth melodiously whan cerberus herde sowne harpe lyfte vp hede hyghe cam gate knowe pleyed melodiously sonne harpe fond orpheus thynkynge pluto wold gladly hym reioye proserpyne allewey wepte maad hym entre cyte brought hym kynge orpheus began playe agayn harpe whan kynge pluto herd hym toke therin grete pleasir dide ther hym pluto sente seke proserpyne whan come herde hym playe harpe plaie knewe wel hit husbond sore abasshid yf sore wepte fore wepte moche pluto sory sorowe proserpine made sayd orpheus yf coude playe harpe lady shold sesse wepyng wold gyue hym wold axe hym orpheus promysid made hym seure wold doo hit pluto sware hym wold holde kepe promesse yf dide orpheus setted entuned harpe playd dyuerce songes swetely infernal cerberus many fill slepe also proserpine mene certayn tokenes signes orpheus maad eyen made cesse wepyng whan pluto sawe proserpine cessing wepyng passing ioyous awoke cerberus slepte spack orpheus sayd hym well harped man coude better wold shold demande som thynge wold gyue hit hym ony faute orpheus heeryng wordes pluto grete debate hym self knowe thynge myght beste demande ende sayd hym syre orpheus husbond ladye loue haue enterprysed come hether thys aduenture praye requyre yow ye gyue rendre agayn may brynge agayn vnto moder dyeth sorowe whan pluto herd requeste orpheus made passing angry also esmaied hardynesse orpheus hit answerd hym orpheus ye haue demanded proserpyne lady moost loue world neuertheles accomplissh promesse haue maad yow gyue vnto yow condicyon ye brynge cyte oute lokyng beholdyng behynde yow yf hit happen ye one loke behynd yow ye shall lose answer orpheus contente hym semed tht wyf good recoured wonne proserpyne passid ouer nyght good hope whan morn comen pluto delyuerid proserpyne vnto orpheus condicion afore reherced orpheus proserpyne toke leue kynge pluto thanked hym syn wente waie goon half way gate whan orpheus pryuely loked behinde hym see yf ony man folowed hym fonde heles cerberus toke proserpyne away fro hym yelded delyuerid agayn vnto kynge etc orpheus seeyng vnhappynes lost wif began curse day born cam folowed proserpyne began agayn harpe offre grete yestes recoure agayn hit said hym conclusion shold neuer haue agayn also yf vsyd foot armes strenges harpe shold armes haue dyed conclusion orpheus departed fro hell full sorowe anguyssh retorned secylle vnto quene serum tellyng auenture quene certaynd doughter hell aduertised thesayll shold halowed feste weddyng pirothus ther many knyghtes grete name wente see cam apoynt thessalonycque feste yet endured approching cyte none pirothus theseus feldes mette exersite grete theseus pirothus salewed salewed greted agayn axed thestate feste weddyng told recounted demanded yf ther knyghtes grete name hyhe enterpryses whan vnderstode enqueryd ferre wold wete demanded name sayd thys lady seres cecyll spake theseus said madame ye well come ffor occasion demande ye yf feste ben ony knyghtes entreprise well saie yow ther truly withstondyng aduertyse yow pray yow also requyre ye telle aduertyse vnto v cause ye haue demaunded etc syre said lady syn hit pleasith yow tenquere myn estate ferre knowe ye certayn haue maad yow demaunde moche pluto kynge helle hath rauysshyd doughter proserpyne whyche hurte vnto deth wold fayn fynde som knyght courtosie wold emploie hym gete agayn yelde assaylle cursid tyraut whiche pray goddes may dampned confounded pardurably demerites wherfore pray yow yf ye knowe ony propice hit plese yow charite adresse vnto hym madame answerd theseus ye besy fynde suche knyght ye seke ffor fauour lady shal knight werke promyse yow vpon myn honour shall transporte helle kynge pluto shall neuer haue pea vnto tyme hath restored doughter etc whan pirothus herde thenterprise began breke wordes said hym broder thynke ye doo whan ye enterpryse goo helle ye knowe termes ner situacion place helle stondeth behynde inner see betwene montaigne roches highe citezeyns dwelle ther ben contynuell vmbre shadowe entre stronge hit inpossible come cyte yf porter consente fore tyme many haue goon theder ben lefte bleuen ther goth man theder euer cometh agayn hit right helle eche man nameth hit helle well situacion therof derke tenebrous place inhumanyte terrybilite habitans indwellars allway wacche wayte euyll desplaysir alle world theseus answerd vnto pirothus sayd ther thynge inpossible vnto vailliant herte kyng pluto cruell stronge folke peple tyrannyse cyte standeth contre enuyronned mortall parelles notwithstondyng certes dowtance fere thinges shall neuer rebowte ne withdrawe corage shall deuoyr achyeue emprynse shall dye payne shall haue reproche shewyng maner knyghtes man kepe honour worshippe ought doubte ony paryll euer hit bee etc whan pyrothus herd noble answer theseus allowed hit gretely said hym wordes hym right agreable acceptable wold hold hym companye thys aduenture quene seres thanked twoknyghtes brought cyte palays resseyued feested hit apperteyned thauenture doughter told thenterpryse two kynghtes reporte aduenture thenterprise theseus pyrothus maad alle ffeeste trowblyd gayn newe amonge alle ypodame consyderyng husbond newely maryed vnto wold goo paryllous voyage helle herte began gyue oute wepyng teeres myghte gyue soulas ne comfort vnto eyen shall saye ffeste ended grete sorowe iason hercules wold gladly haue goon theseus pirothus spake therof wolde suffre hem departed hercules entrid shippe wold haue goon contrey eche man lyke wyse departed also theseus pirothus toke theyr way goo vnto helle aboute departing wherof hercules aduertised hercules made conduyte shippe vnto march hell ther descended lande allone concludyng hym self wold goo pirothus theseus loyall true felawe betoke philotes charge brynge lyncus vnto thebe put hym prison vnto retornyng comyng agayn departed philotes shipped see dolorous auenture hit shall said tyme muste tarye mater shall recounte hercules wente hell etc phow hercules fonde pirothus ded yates hell theseus daunger hercules vaynquysshid cerberus conquerd proserpyne vpon pluto etc paas hit ought sayd whan theseus pirothus departed fro thessalonyque goo assaie yf myght recoure fayr proserpyne moche diligence shorte tyme aryued valeye proserpyne valeye full synnes cursidnesse pirothus knewe contre fond straite way wente cyte entrid first therin way strayte ther myght man oon allone goon neyther right syde neyther lyfte side roches highe man myght goo nether syde whan passed waye fonde rooche entaillid cutte steyers grees maad hewyd chyselles sawe benethe lowe helle cyte stronge enuyronned water fyll doun inpetueusly ferd full fro roches maad terryble noyse rooryng ffor fyll right hyhe lowe swalowe abysme erthe cyte enclosid montaygnes ffor speke properly hit right helle hit oon entre oon yate ffor come doun yate pirothus theseus descended doun degree made roche descendyng sodaynly sawe sprynge fro gate grete geant oute mesure heed meruayllously mysschapen fyers blacke owggly nose hyhe wyde hys chyn longe teth grete hors teth eyen grete lyke vnto oxe eeres hangyng lyke hound sholdres large brood hys bely swollyn grete bolned legges thyes passyng strongly boned myghty thys terryble geant cerberus wherof touched rehersed aboue poettes named hym hound thre heedes concideryng right greuous vnhappy lyuyng whiche replyed lyckende vnto thre synguler vyces wete pryde auaryce luxurye lecherye pryde gloryfied hym self enhaunced hym aboue men worlde hys force strengthe ffor stronge man myght wystande hym auaryce couetyse apetyte insacyable gadre gyder tresours toke bare away myghte haue coude fynde luxurye ther noman lyuyng fowle lyff ffor neuer doon thyng alle lif fowle rauisshe woman maydens ladyes damoyselles good right poettes named hym hownd thre heedes fowle hound lyueth multiplicacon synnes dooth felicyte greuous felicyte whan theseus pirothus espyed enemye cerberus come vnto alle armed makyng whele marchyng prowdly vnto pirothus said theseus broder behold enemye putteth hym suche parillis loue ladyes setteth lityll lyf v behoueth lyue dye late v achieue ioyously emprise thende ye thynke leuyr dye haue reproche shall firste shall begynne bataylle theseus space ne leyzer answer ffor cerberus cam ascryed hem sayng seeken felaws hell come said theseus seche proserpme pluto hath taken away fro quene serum shall neuer retorne contrey vnto tyme brynge v truly answerd cerberus whan ye shall retorne contre ye shall rendre yelde agayn proserpyne shall deffende yow retourn day shall presente vnto proserpme glayue died blood ye shall buryed ye shall neuer see proserpme ner come nerrer ye wordes enhaunsed glayue gaf grete strook theseus vpon shelde bare away therof half quarter etc whan pirothus sawe felawe smeten toke glayue smote cerberus oon syde theseus smote hym side gaf hym two right grete stroke grete made cerberus esmeuyd sore began bataill dismesurably frusshid brake sheldes harnoys also made glayue died noble blood afore said bataill hard mortall begynnyng theseus pirothus resseyuyd many woundes aspre stroke armes hewen broken batayll endured longe pirothus dide right well auaunsyng hym self cerberus smote vpon hym dismesurably many woundes gyuen hym braste hys helme cleuyd heed two peces vnto stomake etc theseus sawe felawe dye enhaunced glayue grete anger smote cerberus fermli made hym auale goo back two paas cerberus wold auenge hym strook smote vpon theseus strook grete force yf noble knyght torned back cerberus born smyten hym vnto erthe strook cerberus fill vpon erthe entrid therin theseus smote agayn vpon enemye whiche herte grete began rore olde lyon smote theseus fiersly swerd brakke shelde ffrusshyd helme astonyed strook allewey theseus abood place cerberus shold haue brought hym vnto vtterance folowyng euyl auenture pirothus yf fortune brought theder hercules whyche cam apoynt rescousse theseus knewe saue hym poynt theseus astonyed hercules departyd fro see sayd cam vnto steyres cutte made rooche beholdyng theseus couerd blood pirothus ded began descende doun cryeng theseus shold aferd ner take drede whan cerberus sawe ande herd hercules began rebruyre rore assaylled theseus asprely quyte hym theseus myght well recomforted voys hercules began renne fore cerberus moche hasted hercules goo doun steyres degree entryng place hastely myght escryed cerberus said hym tyrant cruell late kynght renne come thou hast put deth vpon erthe good frende pirothus wherof sory certayn yf may shall take vengeance hym cerberus heeryng sentence hercules ran theseus taryed behelde hercules afyers looke answerd hym weneth auenge shame beleueth haue deuoured thy ffelaw vnto deth yf thou excede hym restier armes bodily strenght honderd fold double hit folye come hether ffor cerberus porter helle recorde name world tremblith thus endyng answer hercules fote roche clobbe vpon sholdre cerberus cam agaynst hym smote eche rudely thus began right hard batayll theseus passyng wery satte oon side way rested hym dreyng clensing woundes blood comen hercules behelde oon syde seeyng theseus purgyng clensyng parfond grete woundes began employe excesse strength myght suche meruayll strook gaf hym vpon helme vpon right side maad hym bowe lowte vnder clobbe knele ground lyfte knee second strook poursuyng hym hastely made swerd flee hys handes made hym falle armes ground thyrde strooke cerberus wende haue releuyd hym goten swerd hercules smote hym vpon body made hys hede hurtle agayn grete stone ther sprange vpon hym bonde legges strength force handes maulgre geant tare helme hede wold haue slayn hym theseus praid hym wold put hym deth wold brynge hym thessalonycque dye sentence quene ypodame etc cerberus putte deth requeste theseus notwythstandyng hercules bond handes behynde backe maad hym aryse toke hym berd made hym goon vp hyghe roche leyde hym doun boond feete handes necke geder suche wise myght ner durst remeue whan dooon soo wente doun entrid yate helle leuyng theseus wente ferre fonde palais kynge pluto cam halle pluto proserpme alle meruaylid hym whan sawe hym entryd ffor knewe nothynge ouercomyng cerberus lefte charge kepyng cyte cerberus haue ony doubte suspecion also ferre gate myght bataile ner knewe thing befalle porter whan hercules founde pluto proserpme grete ioye knewe token enseygnes beyng hit adressid hym pluto said pluto thy malyce secille alle full wepyng teeres rauysshyng lady whiche hast willed yelde rendre agayn husbond orpheus wote neuer pleasir thou haste therin shall saie thou shalt receyue grete displaisir folowyng euyll auenture cerberus haue vaynquysshid ouercome etc whyth worde hercules lyfte vp clobbe gaf suche strook pluto ouerthrewe hym erthe ne meued nether hande ne foot whan beten pluto wenyng ded assailid made grete murmure put deth lightly wyth clobbe presence proserpme whiche tremblid fere conforted proserpme sayd come vnto place deliuere brynge agayn moder shold sewe folowe hym herdely proserpme assured conforted wordes hercules folowyd hym etc hercules opend halle wente proserpme hym addressid hym vnto yate palays hit happend hym fond right grete companye citezeyns aduertised affraie ran vpon hym dismesurably escrieng hym deth whan hercules sawe said proserpme shold drawe parte enhaunsed lyfte vp clobbe began medle enemyes ryght vertuesly highe prowesse couerid al thentre palais myserable tirantes slewe smote doun fortrusshid putte deth foure honderd ffinably wrought soo fledde gaf hit ouer whan sawe euill willars ded disparc ed toke proserpme hand ladde gate cyte theseus abode taried gate said gretly reioysed whan sawe hercules come agayn proserpme aroos wait agayn salewed lady presented hercules chayne ademont yron found yate many prisonners bounden cerberus bounden hercules vnbond prisoner toke chayne bonde creberus wyth whan buryed pirothus departed thys hell toke waie proserpme theseus cerberus oute grete aduenture specifie maad iourneyes arryued thessalonyque delyuerid proserpme quene serum ypodane presented cerberus rehersyng ladyes slayn pirothus ypodane demened grete sorowe deth pyrothus recounte telle hit possible thessaylle semblably maad grete mornyng sorowe sore bewailed lord shall saie contreuenge deth ypodane bynde cerberus stake theatre cyte yonge olde noyed pyned hym thre dayes longe contynuelly drawyng hym berde cracchyng hym visage slewe hym inhumaynly horribly whan hercules theseus serum proserpme taried certayn space tyme comfortyng ypodane toke leue gyder hercules wente acompanyed theseus toward cyte thebe hym tarie shall come speke auentures lyncus etc phow andromadas deliuerid lincus enemyes slewe bataill kynge creon toke cyte thebe etc whan philotes receyuyd garde kepyng lyncus hercules goon socours theseus pirothus afore said maronners toke shippe wente see saylled day oute fyndyng ony aduenture morn tyme mornyng ffortune alleway torneth oute ony restyng brought grete shyppe drewe hys cours vnto place cam fro thys shyppe galleye capitayn chief andromadas kynge calcide andromadas cosyn vnto lyncus whan espyed shyppe lincus inne maad vyre hys galeye bord said wold knowe peple therin approchyng shippe thebe lyncus behelde galeye andromadas knewe hit thensignes tokenes hit bare knowleche andromadas spack demanded maronners shippe belongeth anone lincus sawe herde andromadas brake thanswere maronners escryed hym highe andromadas lo thy frende lyncus yf thou gyue socours helpe thou mayste lose grete frende ffor prysonner hercules hath sente thebe etc andromadas heeryng lyncus grete anger ffor louyd well lyncus escryed brought hym sayd hym comen vnto theyr deth also vnder warde philotes hys folke garnysshid theyr armes harnoys made hem redy defende hem self wyth lytyll langage calcyde assayllyd phylotes philotes folke employed defence batayll grete hard malehe myshappe tourned suche wise vpon felawes philotes alle slayn dede andromadas two c men companie robeurs theues see theues robeurs smote hard fiersly vpon philotes hewe armes worchynge gyuyng hym many woundes buried many see stronge resistence prouffited lityll ffor ende taken bounde lyncus delyuerd vnbounden bondes hercules etc lincus grete ioye deliuerance thanked good frende andromadas tolde hym take hercules discipate destroyed centaures amonge named many frendes ded wherof andromadas grete yre suche desplaisir sware incontynent wold auenge hit hercules slayn frendes like wise wold destroye cosyns kynnesmen lincus toke grete plesir vnderstonde oth andromadas whyche wold venge deth kynnesmen sayd hym hercules goon helle demanded hym wold auenge hym vpon frendes hercules vpon longe thynkyng ende whan longe take auys andromadas concluded wold goo assayle cyte thebe yf myght gete hit assault wold doo slee kynge creon blood etc wyth conclusion cam theder alle galeyes andromadas whiche folowed eyghte thousand fightyng men andromadas maad hem torne toward thebe also hastely myghte entrid royame wastyng destroyng contrey fyre swerd terribly tydynges cam vnto kyng creon whan kyng creon knewe comyng kyng andromadas oute deffiance maad hym warre sowned armes assembled grete puyssance knowyng andromadas comen certayn place yssued oute thebe armed brought hys peple vpon enemyes grete ioye theyr comynge sette hem ordenance agayn suche wyse cam smytyng strookes cryes noyse grete bothe sydes glayues swerdes dartes guysarmes arowes polhaxes put forth sette awerke many noble beten doun ded lyncus andromadas wrought mortally kynge creon amphitrion faylled blood largely shedde oon side bataylle felonnous aspre lytyll whyle andromadas hys peuple gate wan vpon thebe constraynd recuyell goo back wherof kynge creon ryght grete sorowe wenyng haue putte hys men agayn araye putte hym self grettest prees bataylle wher wrought mortally made grete slaughter betyng doun hys enemyes lyncus andromadas herd affraye cam theder lincus saw kinge creon doo meruailles armes gaf hym thre stroke swerd oon wyth fourthe strook brake helme hede slewe hym wherof thebe affrayed dispayred put descomfiture fledde whiche fleyng amphitrion myght remedie hit stronge grete corage etc euyll aduenture thebe right hastely aduertysed megera goon vp vpon oon hyghe toures palais sawe behelde bataylle place sawe thebe slayn oute remedie also torne backes tokene betyng doun kynge fader recougnossances slaughter maad ascrye sayd ffortune fortune meschyef hercules ala hast thou brought hym ala defende mete natiuyte kepe wif full annoye put hand sholdres bere grete fete dedes batayll whan sayd fylle swonne laye grete neuertheles kynge andromadas lincus folowed hastely thebe entrid cite moche theban heed put araye amphitrion many woundes vpon hym alle membres faylled werke vnhappy lyncus adromadas toke cyte slewe alle myght bere armes reseruyd amphytrion fonde hete wente vp palays ther fonde megera amphitrion grete desolacon many ladyes damoyselles sone lincus espied megera fair plaisant becam amorous cam said lady wepe nomore hercules bastard sone iupiter goon hell ther ded ye haue ben wyf man goten auoultrye hen forth ye shal felawe wyf man legitisme born lawful mariage ffor shall wedde yow shall doo good pleasir euer ye megra answerd fals traitre wenest thou folisshe gyfe fayth beleue wordes homycide fader enemy lorde hercules know thou wyf shal neuer haue husbond hym bastard sone lord amphitrion moste noble man world lady answerd lincus kyng cyte ye comandement ye ye shall shall put hit respyte souffrance till morn wordes lincus sente megera tour made kepte ther sente philotes lowe pryson amphitrion nother pryson fyndyng seruage myserye pryant sone kynge laomedon pytye hym sente hym agayn troyes receyued wyth grete ioye troyans etc phow hercules entrid thebe vnknowen habyte put deth geant lyncus complices wyf megera etc bi glayue lyncus andromadas thebe trowblid dolorously lyncus exercised many tyrannyes wickedness thys infortune andromadas departed wente doo thynges leuyng lincus foure honderd men warre kepe cyte hold hit obeyssance thus taken vengeance centaures tyme vengeance quene iuno cam thebe grete ioye whan fonde hit desolacion full wedowes orphelins enemyes handes hercules grete teeres lamentacions megera amphitrion nyghe vnderstood doleances comforted lincus cam many tymes vnto prisonn requyred swetely haue loue fayrest maner alleway swete faire wordes auailed fond constant ferme alleway kepyng rigour chastete gaf hym many vertuous answer wherof foloweth oon whiche laste lincus thou hast hande stronge hast brused thebe ffortune yll happe haue gyuen vnto tyrannye wherof thou hast enryched thy self vyces thou hast furthermore puyssance comette murdre thy power ne thy synnes ben stronge ne myghtt make vertu bowe ne folde megera alleway bewayled hercules bewayled hym moche day becam alle rauysshed traunce day hercules departed thessalonyque good whyle fore made iourneyes entryd roiame thebe accompanied many nobleman entryng march fonde contre destroyed goon ferre whan hyt told hym lincus lord thebe slayn bataill kynge creon enprisoned megera etc whn hercules receyuid tidinges enplenysshid grete anger said wold auenge hym yf myght cladde hym aboue armour mantel disgysed hym self moche myght whan lefte felawes entrid hym self thebe vnknowen passid thurgh gate bare hym wel porter lete hym passe forth like wyse entrid palais entre palais souldiour cam hercules demanded hym soughte ther hercules caste way mantell ferre toke hys swerd stronge wyth oute ony worde gaf grete strook souldyour armed clefte heed fro hyghest parte doun ground many souldiours seeyng strook cryed affrayed ran ax clubbes auaunced hem self take hercules hercules smote theyr heedes bete hem doun began ryse grete bruyt grete noyse lincus herd hit wenyng hit ben porter affrayed cam rennyng doun vnarmed make pee assone hercules aperceyuyd sawe hym comyng halle drewe vnto hym swerd haunced hand cryeng hercules hercules smote hym cutte right arme strook fyll doun ground smote vpon oon helmes heedes ne hauber backes knewe hit hercules slewe largely blood yonge wedowes wyues maydens ran vnto armes grete corage assailled aboutes men lincus terrible batayll gaderd geder woman ayenst enemyes lityll cyte trowblid whan hercules put deth fonde cloos palays reseruyd lyncus whyche put garde kepyng quene iuno many damoyselles cam vnto hym sprange vpon stretes shewid swerd smote doun ryght side skarmowshyng mortally men lyncus boute myght fynde hem helpe thebe made hem passe trenchyng cuttyng swerd thebe reiosed hercules retourned palais vnto place lady kepte lyncus hercules sente breke vp dore chambre wh r megera ffor moche coude fynde keyes kepte ded megera ful gladnesse cam vnto lord hercules aroos vp wold haue enbraced kyste ncus thought thynge euyll secrete introduccon iuno torned hym fro hyt sayyng hercules late concubine haue take flesshly desire myn acqueyntance moste luxirio lady euer acquented whan megera herd right grete iniurye wronge trayttre chargid fill bacward angre furyo oute saing ony word hercules full angre hoot full grete yre wenyng lincus said trouth smote heed linc swerd slayn trayttre put deth megera whiche chylde hit cronycques spayne telle hercules slewe wyf put religion ordeined thebe temple dyane renounsyng companye thys first religyon euer thebe thinges accomplisshed oon manere hercules toke pryson amphitrion philotes departed then anoyed sore gr uyd tyme longe spack wente way auenture kynge laomedon destroyed troye seconde tyme hercules theseus philotes departed thebe wente many dyuerce landes sechyng aduentures passyng licie hercules maad kynge day cam myrodonne vnto palays kynge eson iason whiche enprised saile yle colcos maad thynges redy whan hercules fested iason duc pelleus knewe thenterpryse iason wold goo conquere flees gold vowed promysed wold accompanye hym yf fortune wold wyth hym wolde aduenture brynge empryse vnto ende shall make longe processe iason hercules made redy right gode shippe wente see renewed vitayll tyll cam porte troyes yet renewid hem poort ffor kynge laomedon troye whiche fortefied meruayllosly cyte agayn knowyng ther descended porte shipp full grekes sente doun man comanded rudeli shold departe then enemye vnto grekes iason capitayn armee whiche waxe amerous iason hyt conteyned historye iason poort lennos hercules aduertysed kynge named phyneus whiche suffrid hym gouerned auaricyous woman phyneus ben maryed nother woman fore two sone two sone vnrightfully theyr stepmoder put exyle ffor saye veray trouthe seconde wyf corrumpid wyth auaryce tooke fro kyng rychesse helde gretter astate whan hercules knowleche herof wente spack kynge phyneus quene shewid vnto theyr vyces good manyer facion two child repelled fro exyle kynge helde astate royall retorned hercules lennos toke see wyth iason wente yle colcos iason lernyng industrie wyndowes oost enemyes right grete thought whether myght goo batayll agayn non hit happend hym thus pensyf behelde toward market place sawe thretty thousand armed men whiche enflamed herte suche wise wente hym arme thoughtis pen e put aparte cam peple warned desired parte deuoyr hym self trustyng fortune yssued felde batayll arenged good ordenaunce well supposed hercules armee descended porte often tymes vpon helme suche wyse myght saue hym enbarryd clubbe heed brayn strook slewe hym amonge plente grekes lyyng ded sand endyng ende hys lyf smote vpon bare banyer slowe alle rente banyer troyans alle discomforted cryed late v fle late v fle wyth crye impetuous began recuyelle goo back vnto cyte wenyng saue self grekes conueyed wyth poyntes theyr swerdes cuttynges theyr sharpe glayues hercules herde hym recomanded aboue alle maner men som euer cam vnto hym full ioye sayd hym lorde noblesse tresour vertu amonge peple moste myghty amonge kynges moste resplendant gloryous vertue salewe yow requyre may seruant frende sayng knee fore hercules signe humylite kyssed erthe whan hercules sawe salutacon manyer doynge man toke hym hande liftyng hym vp fro ground salewed hym demaunded hym name armee belonged sawe ther answerd hym named affer sone madyam sone habraham armee none capytayn ne chief hym self egipciens ordeynd hym duc ledar ooste goo libye destroye contre vengeance come hercules fonde sayd shippe affer wyf also doughter affer thys doughter name echee oon moste fayre damoysell alle worlde yonge fresshe dayly sight hercules becam amerous requyred wyf echee answerd due dette maryage suche wyse echee conceyuyd seed hercules shall make longe processe hercules affer sayllid longe fonde porte libye standeth cartage arryued toke land nyght whiche clere entrid hasteli haste renne vpon egypciens sette ordenance amonge hys peple wherof toke grete harme ffor whan cam batayll fonde hercules renged hys peple sette hem two bataylles whyche lad conduysed fyrst bataylle hit happend sayd felawshyp hercules force shotte mayntenyd hem self vayllyantly wyth stroke brought deth fyften honderd libiens whan shotte fayllid antheon sprange grettest prees moste vaylliant supposyd well haue scarmeshyd enemyes anone hercules sawe hym come scasid clubbe put hym forth afore gaf hym grete strook made hede bowe lyfte side antheon hys swerd lyfte vp haue smyten hercules whan resseyuyd strook hercules gaf hym whiche strook broken neuertheles sayd betwene teth wold auenge hym lifte vp swerd smote hercules dysmesurably wyth strook brake shelde knewe hercules geant man grete strength notwythstanding smote hym seconde tyme clubbe thus hercules antheon gaf eche grete stroke ther cam betwene hem two party libyens egipcyens grete noyse clynknge swerdes sownyng sheldes helmes broken hawberks dismaillid sheldes quarterd glayues broken ther blood largely shedd partyes hercules antheon departyd force prees antheon grete yre smote oute cessyng vpon fiers egipcyens hercules forfrusshed helmes largely clubbe maad libyens pleasir brought many deth clubbe lityll space passid thurgh oute puyssance kynge antheon many tymes waye couerid erthe waie held dede libyens firste scarmusshe stronge domaigiable antheon ffor agayn oon egipcyen slewe glayue hercules maad dye clubbe ten libyens aboute hercules thynge blood hercules made montaygnes redounde cryes renges tremble libyens flee goo back wynne lityll gayne shall saye also longe day endured held bataill vigueur aboute euen affer theseus cam medlee enuertued hym self suche facion ayenst antheon made hym flee alle charged horions stroke like wise fledde alle libyens phow hercules toke kynge athlas began studie scyence astronomye seuen science lyberall etc whhan hercules sawe lybyens torne flighte dide sowne maad right good chiere egipciens thopposite right good chiere libyens cyte made grete sorowe ffor well loste thretty thousand men souerainly antheon demened symple chiere god cause ffor hercules beten knewe mowthe hercules late conquerd philotes slayn geant felaw taken sheep also newly assaillid warre antheon promisid gyue socours also considerd tht wold sholde yelde hym hym herte began hym swelle anger pryde grete felonnye sayd hym thou presumptuous hercules art thou hardy come allone fore thou may loue knowe thou haue many displeasir thyn oultrage ffor philotes right grete frende thou art come renewe dysplaysance wylt shold yelde vnto myn intencion etc athlas thise wordes wente chambre ther faste comanded euery man shold arme hym dyde hercules allwey eye vpon hym ende shold escape hym whan armed cam ayenst hercules escryed hym deth gaf hym strook glayue fiersly crye strook fortresse assaylid hercules hercules put hym self deffense myghtly rigour clobbe xij stroke slewe xij enemyes forth fortresse durst assaile hercules ner aduentured hem rescowe ne releue athlas fledde then castell hercules abode allone athlas dede body ende whan hercules sawe gyuen hit ouer toke athlas maad vnto see syde place philotes abode hym etc whan philotes sawe hercules come athlas bokes grete ioye made know leche aqueyntance athlas whiche sorowful myght speke entrid galeye wente vnto see athlas sorowfull woo begon wounde heed hercules requyred hym instantly wold teche hym scyence athlas wold wise hit begynnyng sorowe whan conuersid taried hercules bounte sawe hym introduccon philotes whiche affermed hercules moste noble vertuous man euer ben began teche hym science wherein lerned prouffited quyk sharp engyne suche wise comprised afterward becam beste philosopher parfyt astronomyen world thus studyyng hercules retourned grete ho oofte affer fonde comyng hys wyf brought forth fair sone whiche egypcyens crowned kynge egypte regned afterward callid dedoum etc affer sawe athlas knewe ordeyned hym self kynge chief first batayll seconde ordeyned kyng ghetulye thirde kynge cothulye whan right well sette arraye renged mornyng made marche ioyously ayenst enemyes demandyd thyng comyng antheon grete prowesse hercules excessiuely grete lybyens fledde hym deth sawe hym tremblyd grete feer bataill fore swerd hercules alle blody grete rowtes lybyens right sore affrayed kepte none araye smote heedes leyde hem doun erthe folke disroyed antheon gadrid geder agayn made suche werke libyens worse antheon sente hastely kynge cothulye shold come helpe etc kynge cothulye sendyng antheon detid wenyng come medlee whan affer theseus sawe hym meue wente ayenst hym lettyd hym waye began stour grete mortall theseus affer slewe kynge cothulye bete doun banyers recongnoissances cotulyens smote sore yron vpon body wente aback constrayned crye helpe kyng ghetulie seeyng euyll aduenture cam vnto rescousse fonde cothulyens alle disconfited comyng cryes noyse tempeste stroke began renewe hys conquestes right well wysely also gaf yeftes aduysedly whan maad affer kynge enquyred lawes helde establisshid amonge hem sacrement maryage ffor tyme woman comune whan hit happend woman child gaf late ded abandonnynd contrey cause grete oultrage vexoses kyng egipte made fithee moche ye lygnage egypcyens sende yow ye submette yow vnto theyr obeyssance wyth yow shall plese hem elles ye come ayenst hem batayll elles eschewe theffusyon blood late yow wete haue good right subiugue yow yf amonge yow two kynghtes agayn two wolle doo armes vtterance shall delyuere yow two ladyes place couenable condicion yf ladyes vaynquyssh ouercome yow ye shall holden vaynquysshid theyr comandement yf men ouercome ladyes shall reputed ouercomen shall sugettis vnto yow etc hercules heeryng mandement message ladyes answerd vnto messanger damoysell syn ladyes fithee ben cheuaulerenses haue conquerid grete royames egypte capadoce asye ben sore doubte neuerthelasse eschewe theffusion blood deffende affrycans fro seruage ye shall retorne vnto saye batayll two knyghtes ayenst two lady acorded agreed vnto morn condicion ye haue sayd hercules affer many swore promysid hold thyse thynges dyde grete honour reuerence vnto damoysell damoisell hauyng message said retorned vnto ladyes whiche entred grete way affrycque tolde word word answer hercules ouerest maistresse lady named synope two susters experte stronge armes dredde knyght world oon named menalipe ypolite anone lady receyuid thise tidynges affrycans grete ioye holdyng oppynyon affrycque wonne strength ypolite menalipe whiche dide meruailles armes ordeind shold fight two knyghttes doo thay made redy ypolite menalipe whiche morn redy vpon feldes oure ordeyned hercules theseus sittyng two stronge horse grete siewte affricans rood place lady chosen doo armes two lady abidyng fayre place armed well mounted good stedes lady grete nombre also sone hercules theseus aspyed two damoyselles made folowed stand come nere sente vnto damyselles wete wold doo damoyselles answerd abode two knyghtes redy doo armes agayn vnder condicions querele yf come shold come forthe hercules theseus wyth thys answere toke speres spored horse made signe vnto damoiselle garnysshid sheldes speres ran agayn cheuauloursly hyt semed ne helde heuen ne erthe copyng theyr sharp speres stroke huge grete bothe sydes ypolyte theseus bare eche vnto erthe lyke wyse dide menalipe hercules affrycans meruaillid moche see two prynces born doun yet ladyes sythea meruaylled moche damoyselles etc whan knyghtes oon syde damoyselles fonde self lyyng oon erthe shame vergoyne smote hem vnto hertes neuertheles eche releuyd hem lightly grete corage toke swerdes approchid eche chargyng smytyng oon vpon radely armes ladyes knyghtes felte strookes ypolyte poursiewed man theseus menalype helde vnto hercules strookes ypolite grete dide grete gryef vnto theseus theseus enforced hym self strongly auenge hym myght well come purpose hercules put vnder ouercome menalype lightly swerd put mercy ypolyte mayntenyd force myghtely ayenst theseus put hym vtterance ne hercules ben sayd hym broder shall bee prowesse theseus shal daunted chyualerye damoysell yf hit certaynly men shall haue shame dishonoure thyse wordes began quycquen wake agayn blood theseus afore slepe lyghte courage suche wyse recouerd newe force strengthe put hym forth began smyte suche prowesse maad damoysell recreante toke fro swerd surmounted wherof ladyes right doleant sorouful especiall quene sinophe whiche sente hercules armes token vaynquisshid prayng hym wold yelde ayen rendre two damoyselles hercules toke armes quene sente menalipe made pee affrycans condycion shold gyue ypolite mariage theseus whiche amerous ypolite weddyng made affryque grete honour worship ladyes heeryng telle meruaillous feetes dedes hercules prei id hym alle helde hem happy ewrous vaynquysshid hym phow hercules began wexe amerous deyanyra achelous hercules bataill oon ayenst achelous vainquisshid conqueste lady theseus toke leue hercules affer retorned contre brynge home lady hercules wente see goo calcedonye whiche lyeth thoposite achaye archade see fayr lady exellente beawte herd gretly recomanded calcedonien companye dide moche see lande cam calcedoyne kynge place name oeneus two doughters oon named deyanyra gorge deyanyra fayrest hercules cam see whan oeneus vnderstandyng knowleche hercules cam hys contrey grete ioye wente ayenst hym resseyued hym enbrasing honourably hym possible entryng hys pallays quene hys two doughters gorge dyanyra wellcomyd hercules incontynent hercules caste eyen vpon dyanira moste fayrest thynge euer sawe desire right depe enrachyned roted hole place herte felte hym self rauysshyd meruayllously desire entrid hercules full rayes loue entryd herte also sodeynly rayes sonne passe thurgh glasse etc deyanira moche beaute well accomplisshid relused shoon amonge ladyes myght maad comparyson allonly beaulte tht wysedom bounte precious tresour calcedonye ther cam many ladyes damoyselles hys neyghbours amerous soueraynly kyng achelous strong puyssant kynge grete seygnourye marchyd royame calcedonye whan hercules ben space passyng tyme ioyously beholdyng conduyt deyanira hyt happend day messanger kynge achelous cam oeneus said hym achelous demanded hym yf wold gyue hym doughter yf wold gyue hym thys tyme wold moleste greue contre wold make hym warre mandement oeneus strongly troublid answerd messanger morn wold gyue hym answer day oeneus pensyf symple abode allone passe melancolie cam hercules whan hercules sawe hym pensyf coniured hym suche wyse shold telle hym cause pensifnes whiche told hym said lord hercules syn hit pleseth yow knowe myn anoyance greef shall anon telle yow cause ther kynge neyghebour named achelous grete fiers prowd whyche many tymes hath requyred haue wyf deyanira doughter haue ben accorde maryage ffor moche knowe kynge man ryght euyll lyf cause haue many menace hym also day messanger yet comen agayn hath sayd yf gyue hym doughter tyme make warre certes hercules yf ye see pensyf hyt cometh occasion ffor haue yet gyuen hym hys answer muste gyue hit hym morn neuerthelesse haue concluded self wyll gyue vnto hym doughter whan see veryly reffuse doughter hyt muste nedes bee warre open betwene forsayd kynge achelous knowe well dysplesyd ffor warre eternall exyllement contre perdycion waaste peple goodes etc sire sayd hercules hyt force vnto man take bere alle fortune wyll ye saye warre encresyng peple dymunycion allewaye hole hyt behoueth passe hyt expedyent man reioyse hys ryght ryght conforteth courage man also corage man conforted bryngeth hym ofte tymes gloryous victorye beste rurall disgarnysshyd raysonable engyne fighteth hole neste clawes foot teeth wyth becke shall man sensible endowed entendement rayson doo yf ony assault namely owen land terrytorye come nature wyll enseygneth corperall force faylleth vygour vertue courage werken fyghte contrey take courage yowr right late saye entente vnto enemyes ye haue receyuyd worshipfully receyuyng thise tydynges ben come shall helpe yow yf hit nede suppose yf achelous assaylle yow shall repente hym thyse wordes kynge oeneus conforted hym self gretly day drewe ouer morn oeneus called messanger achelous said hym come demande doughter auysed gyne mayster furthermore yf meuyd warre ayenst hym cause intencon defende hym vnto deth last man hys peple messanger retorned wordes told hem achelous fonde achelous euyll content kynge oeneus ouer moche smyten loue deyanira began assemble men armes intencion make warre kynge oeneus take fro hym doughter hercules calcedonye ofte tymes deyanira gracious deuyses fonde well adressid honeste manyers day parte nyghte dide dreme thynke hit said thynge touched amerous desire willyng fyrst shewe power armes hit happend day opend wyndowe gardyn deiamra castyng eyen doun sawe deyanira sat vpon grene place acompanyed many ladyes damoyselles sette entendement contemplare thexcessiue beaulte desired coueytyng desiryng said deianyra haue prerogacion knowe hertes thoughtes men yf shold saie yow tenthe parte loue desire haue yow ye mighte beleue hit haue goon many contre seen many royame many tresour haue desired many thynge come myn aboue neuer grete thought gete grace oure hercules spack hym self deyanyra ydell hercules mynde remembrance herte beyng ryche wyth poyntes loue sowen bytwene variacions hope despayr esprysed alle vaynes wyth heete fyre brenneth amerous hertes fire brennyng stronge right hard quenche right percyng spa cle leyde doun vpon grasse began saye engyne ala hercules shal deianira doo may come attaine vnto loue wonte longe syn dayne behold men said tht neuer prince ne kynge shold haue loue another nature ne desyre thynge myght wyf supposed haue remayned contynued stable virgine disdaineuse men agayn requestes amonycions ladyes ben well tydynges thyse wordes cesed litil began thynke many thynges poynt thought hercules hercules tidinges cam theder achelous cam theder tassiege cyte lande see right nyghe ffor tidynges aroos pallays ryght grete murmure cam cere hercules deyanyra spyrites trauersyd suche facion hercules lefte beholde deyanyra damoysell lefte thynke hercules bothe two wente vnto kynge oeneus anone hercules cam vnto kyng kynge sawe hym wente ayenst hym said hym enemyes right nyhe cyte hercules answerd ioyously hyt behoueth goo feste hem doo putte hys peple armes answere hercules kynge dyde dosowne armes sowne calcedonye meuyd eche man adoubed hym hercu e grekes redy lityll space calcedonyens assemblid grete companyes palais whan assemblid kynge hercules brought ffelde hercules put hem ordenaunce doon dide hem marche exployted calcedonyens grekes dyner cam fond enemyes approchyd nyhe ther nothyng doo smyte laye hercules maad two bataylles oon fyrste peple calcedonyens whan cam poynte mete hercules wente calcedonyens presence kynge sayd lo ye may see enemyes sette lytill yow ffor ben come lordshypp assaill yow pray yow grete oultrage abate nemynusshe youre corages ye oughte haue fyerste lyon puyssance ellephant appetyte gryffon delyuere yow wyth oute ende fro enemyte kyng achelous keping contre domynacon honour tresours wyues chyldren lyues bee ye enuyous well ye aglouted wyth desyre vengeance ye coueytous gete worshyp glorye yf ye esuertue self tyme ye may haue mendicyte seruytude deth ffor enemyes shall doo vnto yow euyll world yf haue victorie ouer yow thise wordes wroughte hertes calcedonyens gaf corage merueylously full oon ryght good desired medles whan hercules achieuyd exortacon wente bataill hit point fighte ther grete cryes oon side tabour trompettes clarion horne busynes began sowne knyghtes began meue thentree bataill hercules grekes shotte drewe largely vpon enemyes made achelous abasshid moche hoped haue found grete resistence calcedonyens casted eyen vpon banyer hercules seeyng grete lyon paynted therm began ymagyne myght hercules spoken thurgh oute world vertues strengthe whan thus ymagenyng shotte failled grete occision party achelous whan shotte faylled hercules toke swerd fourroied amonge achaye first fronte batayll achelous maad hoole grete calcedonyens yconyens wan vpon first ioynyng e partye recule go backe wherof achelous grete sorowe toke hym xx knyghtes whiche chosen cam reng ith hercules defrayed brake batayll achayens approuuyd corage amorous stronge geant cheualerye vayllyantly grekes entryng taryed abode also hercules ffor dyed swerdes erthe blood bete doun many yconyens stryff grete men myght see nothynge ellys heedes armes fflee ffelde hercules smote strook hit coste achelous deth man achelous like wyse strook strook smote doun oon enemyes residue folke dide best cowde uow behynde yet myght neuer thachayens confounde put aback theyr aduersaryes howe hit allwey fowre agaynst oon th chonyens also myght preuaill vpon achayens fo moche grete nombre alleway fressh peple newe maner two puissance fought geder foure oures loue wrought sore hercules achelous bothe two made swerdes florisshe couerid blood mette ofte tymes smote eche neuer durst achelous abide fore swerd hercules orrible strookes sawe hercules gyue putted hym prees sone smyten hym greuyd hym bataill hercules dide wondres meruailles oeneus toke grete playsir behold hym thachayens therin displaisir ffor seyghe hym assewrid escape deth feleth swerd nekke hand tyrant res yuid man strook hym abood place made grete slaughter man well write ende kynge oeneus calcedoniens cam bataill comyng achaiens reseyuid losse vpon losse parill vpon parill kyng oeneus made many enemyes dye hercules shewid puyssance well doyng putte thachayens alle oute araye flyghte losse felde torned gretly vnto dommage kynge achelous ffor hercules chassed hym hountously hys shyppy maad hym lese twelue thousand achayens etc phow hercules put vtterance kyng achelous espowsed deyanyra etc vitorye whan hercules sawe kynge achelous sauyd hym self see called kynge oeneus sayd hym wold poursiewe enemye wold delyuere world hym toke two honderd chosen men toke leue kynge oeneus wente see folowyng achelous recomandyng hym gorge deyanira nyght oeneus departyng hercules retorned calcedonye tolde wyf doughters hyhe prowes hercules doon batayll chaced enemyes goon two honderd men ladyes gorge deyanyra right ioyous victorye hit anoyed hem sore hercules wyth lytyll companye poursyeued achelous aboue alle deyanyra gretly anoyed greuyd thempryse hercules sore wente chambre constrayned wepe haue ioye hert retorne hercules ffor retorne vnto purpoos hercules whan put vnto poursiewt achelous said entrid royame siewed hym nyhe constraynd wythdrawe hym ryght stronge castell standyng see hercules aseged achelous castell whan achelous sawe hercules poursiewed hym lityl companye wyth two honderd men callid hys frendes hys conduytours amonge thynges told hem hit shame suffre asseged wyth lytyll nombre peple answerd sayd trouthe concluded oure wold yssue reyse breke syege forthwith sowned armes wyth shorte counceyll hyt longe yssued castell hercules aspyed hem knewe cam bataylle sette hys men araye wente allone fore vnto enemyes dowted thynge whan achelous sawe hym come began make grete sighe escryed peple vpon hym sayyng hit clubbe chassed hym calcedonye promysed grete yeftes vnto beste furnysshid hym stroke whan folk knewe hit hercules made curtoisie eche go afore tremblyng leef tree durst abide weight clubbe withoute smytyng ony strook torned backes fledde vnto castell achelous seeyng poure conduyte hys folke drede feer hercules wende shold haue deyd sorowe wente entryd agayn wyth castell hercules retorned wyth peple lawghyng poure guydyng enemyes hercules began thynke deyanyra achelous began ymagyne myghte adommage calcedonyens oon hys captayns sayd vnto hym syre ye knowe well strength may compare vnto strength enemyes ben ten agaynste oon may thynge helpe v ffor allonly clubbe myghty geant wyth ynowh burye v alle also destroye royame consydere ye syn hit open puissance playn descouerte strength eye may vsed tyme hyt expedyent ymagyne subtylte greue calcedonyens hyt myn adnys shall maad grete flamyng light see suche shall well deuyse moyen haue beseged v may ben deceyuyd lightly flamyng light muste nyght hit shall grete inpetuous shall make hit secretly anone oure enemyes shall see hit shall lepe oute tentes shall goo vnto see see meruaille parauenture oute ony armes ffor drede ne fere v shall spryng shall fynde disgarnysshid vnpurueyed theyr armes consequently hyt may ensiewe alle shall make notable delyuerance etc whan achelous herd counceyll hyt semed hym good wolde hit put effecte suche wyse deuysed deuyser dide make honderd torch whiche achyeuyd fyften dayes duryng thyse fyften dayes hercules assaylled many tymes castell achelous myght neuer thynge therto ffor fortresse stode vpon see strong contree myght goten assault achelous myght haue socours fro parte ffor betwene castell achaye grete contrey whan fyften dayes passid torch maad night whan hit paisible wynd storme conduyted torch yssued castell four vnto hauen wher left oon lityl boot whiche ground longe tyme afore put see yf ye demande shippes become achelous brought poort saye yow hercules take sente hem see thentent achelous shold ascape hym ner take away shippys nyght achayens comen lityll boot lyyng ground dide moche brought hit flote see also secretly coude entrid therin necessarye kynge achelous putte hym self busshement thousand men place nyghe hym semed calcedonyens wold goo see lyght shold made whan e knewe hit tyme lighte torch sette fire sette round boute masre made many hooles torch ymagyned dyde anone knyghtes kepte wacche oost hercules sawe hit sore meruaylled light awooke hercules felawes shewed light clerte etc anone hercules sawe resplendissour torch wold knowe hit approched ryue see felawship hym ben longe whan kynge achelous dide lyghte honderd torch pourueyed sprange enbusshement wyth thousand men ran vpon hercules assailled hym men fiersly whan hercules sawe discouere sette peple ordenance beste wise might light sterres receyuid enemy frely wherof began right dolorous bataill ffor oon smote right felonsly ther many wounded deed scarmousshe grete achelous wende escarmousshe scarmousshid hym self vnto theffusion hys blood ffor hercules amonge alle
