whyche desired strongly rescowe kynge abandoned lyues heet whan torch quenchid lityll lityll began coole wythdrewe sawe drope whan wythdrawen hercules assemblid folke said wold goo assaye yf myghte take castell trowble shold folowe hym hardily fiersly anone sawe enemyes retorne vnto castell ran retayned hem putte hym self thikkest smyting wyth clubbe right syde lifte syde made right large place way thi waye ladde hys peple vnto yate castell entrid fledde maad grete occysion enemyes wyth lityll resistence nyght putte deth twelfe h nderd fledde cyte patrace fro whens batayll batayll ben calcedonye alle men achaye slayn reseruyd aboute foure honderd whiche saued fleeyng ffor achelous taken men hym contre hys cyte patrace destroyed whan hercules taken castell wente contre cyte patrace entryng place oute ony resistence translated roiame hand kyng oeneus abood longe subdned royame departed retorned calcedome hasteli myght see deyanira receyuyd grete glorye ioye tryumphe noman reherce ne write poetes escryue write conquest hercules made vpon achelous ffaynyng achelous fought first guyse man vaynquysshyd chaungyd hym self guyse serpent vnderstande subtyllesse malyce dide assaillyng hercules night ffinably fought guyse booll hercules brak oon horne vnderstand laste achelous fiers booll ffor deyde well nyhe pryde sorowe taken hercules brake hys horne vnderstande brak royame destroyed hit phow nessus rauysshid deyanira fro hercules whan passid wyth ouer ryuer howe hercules slewe nessus arowe grete ffeste kynge oeneus maad victoryes hercules achyeuyd vpon kynge achelous doubted hym passyng sore hercules hys comyng presented hym achelous royame said hym shold haue hit oute ony reffuse kyng oeneus sente kynge achelous exyle helde hym self gretly bounden beholden hercules honoured meruaillously hercules toke herte agayn ryght amorows regardes also likewyse dide deyanyra souerayn ioye see hercules desired none thynge see hym shall make longe processe whan hercules ben space requyred kynge oeneus wold gyf hym doughtre wyue oeneus wyth right good agreed acorded hym deyanyra consented better wyll weddyng solempnysed pomp sly solempnly wente bedde laye geder sone whan hercules sawe fader lawe roiame pea toke leue kynge oeneus departed fro calcedonie deyanira peple goo lande royame yconye hercules allwey iourney deyanyra hym louyd sore grete solas beaute yf studied athlas coude haue absteyned hym beholde beaute passyng tyme plesauntly manyer folke ben newe maryed hercules iourneyed ferre cam quarter thessaylle ryuer hebenus renneth arryued ryuer whiche depe brood rennyng inpetuously nether brigge ne plancke passe ouer centaure named nessus practyqued lyf mene lityll boot whiche sad peple ouer ryuer etc whan hercules founde passager nessus cam hym demaunded hym hys folke myght passe ryuer nessus knewe hercules syn tyme vaynquysshyd felawis weddyng pyrothus answerd hym myght passe ryuer lityll boot yf wold passe wold wyth good hym pleasir sette hym ouer hercules thanked nessus moche sawe boote lityll tyme disposed rayne wold deyanyra damoyselles shold passe fyrst deyanyra maydens entryd boote whan therin nessus rowed rowyng behelde deyanyra sawe moche beawte deceyuid hym ffor sone come ouer syde toke deyanyra sayd shold wyf rauysshyng toke hys sholders bare way wherfore deyanyra damoyselles made grete cryes hercules seeyng olde geant bare away deyanira whiche wold resiste power bende bowe shotte arowe vpon geant grete myght connyng smote hym ryght syde vnto herte gaf hym dethes wounde thee bowe hercules grete stronge man coude bende hyt hym self hyt nessus hys wounde hercules gaf hym began fele thappchyng deth suffre sharp anguissh allway ran grete vnto valeye ouerthrewe considering lyf rescows enploied ende lyf ymagine might displaisir hercules remembrid terryble poysen vpon hym mortall sayd deyanyra grete malyce lady loue yow hath caused resseyue deth whyche displeseth sore doth cruel hercules shall reioysse yow whyche worthy haue worthy man hercules trewe husbonde vntrewest wyf euer moche haue synguler pyte yow beaulte constrayneth yow pleasyr shall gyue yow precious thynge hauyng suche vertu yf ye boyll hit oon shertes hercules blood renneth wounde yf ye gyue sherte hercules hit shall neuer loue woman ner lady yow thise wordes geant toke poison temprid hyt wyth blood wonde hit lynnyn cloth gaf hyt deyanyra folish deyanyra adioustyng credence geant toke poyson geant charged man shold towche hit bare sayng hit shold lose vertu towchyng gaf vp goste dyed pytously deyanyra ascapyd fro handes pourposyng wold kepe poyson secrtly alauenture helpe self yf hit nede mene whyle thynges befell betwene deyanyra geant hercules hertes ease deyanyra grete dystresse whan sawe nessus away wyf assone smyten hym right side arowe said vnclothed despoilled hym self caste gowne harnoys clobbe ouer water grete strength sterte water swamme ouer vnto side dide arayment agayn deyanira acompanyed damoyselles folowed cam agayn ryuer garnysshid cursid poyson whan hercules sawe deyanira retorne ymagyned anone slayn geant wente ayenst demanded traytre deyanira answerd fyrst thys demande sayd hym ala lord parill haue ben oppression destruccion ioye hath destrayned myn herte traches myn armes yet seen prynte handes geant shewe displaisir haue cursed glouton geant bare vnto depthe depe valeye deth procedyng strook arowe made hym falle doun wold neuer late goo vnto laste syghe deth certes haue suffrid grete ieoparde thankyng goddes syn haue found yow agayn knowe ye veryly auenged myn enemye haue seen depe miserably wherof reioyed glad agayn phow hercules fought agaynst serpent palu lerne slewe hym etc deyanira hercules kyssid eche right grete loue hercules wente place geant laye ded moche fond hym priued lyf lete hym lye bestes birdes toke arowe tht laie hym thys arowe achilles slayn temple phebus troie loue polixene hercules deiamra cam agayn ryuer hercules sette ouer men wente fro place cyte lerne kynge thys cyte dide grete honour hercules receyuyd hym honourably myght cowde amonge dyuerce deuyses hercules demaunded hym hys tydynges kynge answerd sayd knewe none grete palus dwellyd abood monstre half man half serpent wasted destroyed royame comun murdre ffor said men woman chyldren thys monstre fynde sleeth hem tayll enuenymed hande armed deuoureth destroyeth teth ther escapeth none hit behoueth thys contre deserte ffor laboureurs ne marchans dare go contre lasse acompanyed two honderd men yf lasse monstre assaylleth destroyeth lyke hath doon many etc hercules passyng glad ioyous tidynges sayd kynge syre haue labourd yet hederto comyn wele many royames yet haue wyll perseuere werkes vertu knowe ye syn arryued shall somwhat wele contre lyke haue doon many haue entencion putte deuoyr morn waye toward monstre abyde thauenture vaynquysshe hym vaynquysshid hym monstre called ydre moche dwellyd water whan deyanyra herde thentreprise hercules wold go allone abandonne hym self grete parill began wepe make grete sorowe man myghte pea ner make stynte wepyng hercules conforted beste wyse coude athlas philotes conforted lykewise shewed right hyhe glorious dedes hercules ffor gyue hope hys aduenture myght helpe ner auaylle louyd hercules herte wyth myght puyssance required hym eyen charged full teeres wold absteyne hym fro hyhe enterpryse saying tht hit wisedom man expose hym self euydent terryble daungers goddes sente monstre contre corryge chastyce peple alleway hyt hercules sore ardaut loue yet teres wepte ne prayer ne remonstrance myght cause hercules breke pourpose achyeue aduenture morn erly adoubyd hym departyd fro lerne toke way toward palus monstre thys palus longe thre myle compaas croniques spayne reherce enuyroned fontaynes sprang hyhe montaygnes myddis palus grete lake ponde wherin dwellyd ydre drye lande whan hercules come palus ydre tht neuer slepte wyth bothe eyen alewey nekke stracchid hihe eeres open anone aspied hym sodainl cam ayenst hym rennyng grete radeure hercules abode whan aspyed meruaillous monstre grete playsir see hym ten foote heyghte longe taylle fowle couerd heer body armed right hande helde naked glayue lyfte hand bare shelde hercules thus beholdyng hym suffryd hym come hym monstre spack hym sayd poure geant whyder goste thou behold glayue sharp bothe sydes cuttyng yet ther neuer man herde speke dyed poynt thys glayue ffor moche moste wyse creature euer nature maad acustomed make questyon suche men fynde destroye yf answer therto moche ne fynde royame peple bestes oute entendement haue therfore destroyed blood shall thyn yf thou anste assoylle sophyme shal make thou man serpentyne sayd hercules thyn eloquence thy prudence thy cruell glayue foule pollute infinytes homycides make thyng abaisshed ne discorage seke comen hether destroye shall assoylle oonly oon thy sophymes many thou canst thynke wole well thou knowe yf force thy sophymes fallacious argumentes thou make innocent shall doo vnto lyke thou woldest yf hit happe thy scyence may ouercome yet woll well thou defende armes thou kepe thy lyf well thou canst etc wyth wordes monstre maad vnto hercules seuen sofymes oon fallacio fo subtyll whan hercules gyuen solucion oon monstre replyed seuen argumentes allway hercules full philosophie expert scyence answerd solempnly fallacious argumentes surmouted hym cause poetes fayne ydre seuen heedes hyt appereth first tragedye seneca sayen whan hercules smiten oon heedes seuen heedes cam agayn place ende poursiewe matere whan hercules desputed ayenst serpent yelded hym ryuage see wyth blood fledde whan nyght come hercules grekes withdrewe hem galeyes ete dranke suche made ioyous chere hurte men remembrid conforted victorye werye men forgate labour doon rested hem trauayll passed nyght ouer whan hit day morn hercules yssued galeye beholdyng porte hym semed cyte shold stande well sayd wold make oon concluded begynne hit sente vnto place wiste ony peple aboutes gaf eche man knowleche make cyte first persone wold come put hand therto shold haue domynacon thynge knowen galyce many cam theder woman named coroigne fyrst cam therfore hercules gaf vnto domynacon made begynne cyte named hit coroigne reme brance fo victorye vpon body gerion founded tour arte composed made lampe brennyng contynually day nyght wyth oute puttyng ony thyng therto whiche brennyd afterward space thre honderd yere ouer vpon somette toppe tour maad ymage copre lokyng see gaf hym hand myrrour hauyng suche vertue yf hit happend ony men warre see entencion ony harme cyte sodaynly oost theyr comynge shold appere thys said myrrour dured vnto tyme nabugodonosor aduertysed properte myrrour fyllyd hys galeyes wyth whyte thynges grene bowes leeues hyt semed wode myrrour ne apered none thynge wood wherfore coroignyens knowyng myrrour shewyd hem garnysshid wyth men armes like ben accustomed doo whan enemyes cam thus nabugodonosor toke cyte morenyng destroyed myrrour lampe whan tour maad hercules made come theder maydens contre dide hem make solempne feste remembrance deth gerion departed frothens wente vnto megida presentyd hym honderd ox fayrest world phow hercules assaylled kynge cacus bataill ayenst hym ouercam hym cacus began tyrannyse italye etc conqueste hercules entended peple enhabite newe contrey tydynges cam hym cyte cartagene kynge geant regned named cacus whiche passyng euyll full tyrannye slayn cursidnes kynges aragon nauerre wyues child possessid seignouryes also helde subieccion alle contrey ytaly hercules receyuyd right ioyously tydynges sayd playsir goddes shall assaye yf may take vengeance deth kynges arragon nauare disposed hym vnto werkes hauyng appetite correcte kynge cacus sone excersite myght redy wente vnto royame castylle kynge cacus cyte cartagene stood beside montaigne named monchaio passid many roiames dide hym obeyssance vertuous renomee whan cam approche cartagene kynge cacus cam agaynst hym desobeysance armes ffor ben aduertysed comyng entred frontier sente vnto hym oon knyghtes sayd hym wordes folowe hercules open tyrant haste herte gretter thy body thou woldest assaille heuenes conquere yf goddes gyuen wynges flee byrddes haue yf thou seke pee loue vnto kynge cacus thy semblable complexion fortune salewe name yf thou come otherwyse vnto hym enemye deffye hys name wyse thou hardy entre contrey yf thou entre knowe thou thou shalt fynde cacus castyllyens oon hard encountre euyll aduenture shall man thy companye quyte etc nyght answed hercules som euer ye ye shewe ye haue herte noblesse ffor hit foule alle men especyall noble man myssaye speke euyll another man ye haue callyd open tyrant publicque also ye haue compared vnto tyrant cacus answer yow thys artycle tyrant destroyer tyrantes therfore ye shall retorne agayn vnto cacus sygnefye hym haue intencion shewe hate haue vnto tyrantes fewe dayes may proue vpon v hard encountre wherof haue receyuid menace answer castylian departed fro presence hercules retorned vnto kynge cacus tolde hym worde worde hercules sayd hym whan cacus herde alle thys abaisshid notwithstandyng stronge geant puyssant neuer founden man strenger hym self ffor renome hercules grete vnyuersel world moste stronge moste assewryd armes moste happy doubtyd hym tremblyd heryng speke dedes hit cacus toke corage hym self musyng abaisshement presence noble said blessid next hasty dayes nature fortune shall brynge v make proef force strength behoueth castyle secylle shewe thexcesse armes deffende kyng cacus fro clawes enemyes hit necessite semblably kynge cacus peple desploye putte forth abisme strength forth brethern frendes ben comen warre grekes come vpon castile oute ony quarele late v goo agaynst hem fighte contre birdes fyght oon ayenst nestes dombe bestes cauernes nature entroduceth hem doo yf haue nature tyme come oughte doo etc whan castelians aragonnoys herd cacus speke preysid gretly corage answerd oon wy redy assaylle enemyes answer kynge cacus dide dislogge oost feldes wente forth ayenst hercules straytest way cowde kynge cacus putte way desiryng sore fynde hercules hercules side cam ayenst cacus wente longe oon ayenst sone sawe eche nyghe place hercules founded cyte whiche named terracene assone sawe eche began make grete ioye make showtes cry renged hem ordenance bataill marched oon ayenst hootly sharply fillid ayer sodaynly shotte arowes caste stone dartes begynnyng bataylle castelyens bare hem valiantly mony theyr partye slayn moo hardynes drede ffor put hem fer forth doubted shotte grekes shotte hem sore thykke ground made reed blood casteliens whiche ferre goon sore chauffid muste nede resorte back agayn theyr felawis whan kynge cacus sawe folke sore bestad hard reculed fro shotte grekes grete sorowe herte wist neuer entende entretene holde bataill fledde reculid wente aback fill doun erthe ded sore hurte batayll dured longe thys poynt allway sorowe kynge cacus ende shotte grekes faylled castelyens cacus recouerid newe strength manyer cam fyghte hand hand swerdes shedde spradde largely blood tyre one whiche firste fronte batayll hercules noyse aroose grete ther many sheldes broken many skynnes lyous cutte peces cacus approchid hyt semed tempest grete stronge fiers oultragious smytyng eche stroke deth greke ende dide moche cryes boute hym mountyd hyghe ayer casteliens well wende haue wonne began make ioye good fortune escryyng grekes deth euen like wyse right clere day otherwhile troblid auenturous black clowde semblably allonli comyng hercules cam rescousse ioye troblid torned mortall losse ffor mortall arme hercules enuertued terribly bete doun casteliens like mowar sithe bete doun grasse medowe whan cacus sawe hercules foundre bete doun men blood hym changed blood meuyd coragious man presentid hym self fore fronte hercules smote hym glayne sore harde clefte shelde two partis casteliens seeyng shelde hercules flee peces thought anon cacus slayn put deth hercules made crye ioye hit dured longe ffor hercules lyfte vp armes clubbe smote cacus vpon comble helme suche strength hit semed cacus sawe honderd thousand candellis smyten doun gretteste roche spayne notwithstandyng cacus abood standyng place escryed hercules vnto deth smote hym myght assaillyng castelyens hopyng fortune cacus assaillid hercules hercules gon ferre amonge enemyes allone companye whan herd cacus escryed hym deth sawe casteliens assayllid hym cam hym fro side herte fyld solas abandonned durete hardnes skyn lyon swerdes withoute reuengyng hym saue ayenst cacus thus began batayll betwene hercules cacus stroke grete ferdfull oute mesure cacus foughte spryrite tyrant chauffid desyred sore ouercome hercules tyrannyse tryumphe aboue hym hercules fought vertuous herte founded nourisshid vertu enemye vyces assayllid vicyous kynge bothe two grete fyers stronge grete corages certes whan tasted ynowh eche atte longe stroke hercules grete peysant sholdres cacus ne hys heed myght bere ne puyssance susteyne ende suche batayll dured two oures cacus lefte hym myght suffre hym fledde wente waye etc whan hercules sawe cacus fledde daygned folowe notwythstandyng haue victorye iourney began hewe castelians aragonnoys suche might fynde lefte man lyue fore hym yonge ne olde feble ne stronge hyspan side made feetes armes floryssh shyne batayll sharp grekes dowblid redoublid stroke slewe many enemyes ende whan cacus take hys breth put hym agayn medlee oon side folk fledd maad hem tarye smytyng betyng grekes terribly doon fore wherof cryes aroos highe hercules fightyng syde herd crye ran theder alle auenture anone espyed cacus wente fore hym brake prees smote doun sore cacus knewe hercules durst abide hym fledde agayn euyll happe grekes maad crye ioyous noyse alle castelians fledde grete hurte losse cacus ffor peple ther left moo fifty whiche sauyd hem self vpon mount monchayo whiche stood ther grete effusion blood castile wend haue mounted vp wyth semed ben grete sprynge blood cauernes valeye remplenesshid wyth blood hit cacus flee well sauyd hymself fyfty men vpon montaigne cronicles spaigne reherce whan aboue sewr place retorned sawe doun foot hyll sawe many castelyans oute nombre ded danger dye grete sorowe herte pyte dispyte dauger sawe redy muste passe anone sawe fro ferre champaigne eche quarter place couert party blood also sawe fledde taken brought pestelence termes consideryd desolacon domynacon punycon hys tyrannye hym euydent tought hercules shold lightly conquere contrey ffor obeyed hym tyrannye naturell loue notwithstandyng despaired well sawe alle puyssance men destroyed clubbe hercules knewe myght regne contrey ded bataill retorned vnto scyence thus sorowfull entrid hows first comysed twelue men kepe passage mounte whiche also strayte narow myght goo vp oon man one whan hercules men putte deth alle enemyes hercules wold assaylle roche began mounte goo vpon degree steyres sodaynly kepte paas caste vpon hym grete stone grete habon dance force constrayned descende whan hercules sawe muste withdrawe hym obeyed fortune notwithstandyng made avowe tht wold neuer departe fro foot roche vnto tyme constrayned cacus descende come doun famyne wise auowe made hercules cam vnto foot hille oc ision slaughter ben made place made clene purgid ded bodyes blood laye ded dide make tente bowes leeues bedd fressh grasse comanded eche man shold logge tyme nyght cam day faillid grekes wery day laboured armes wold fayn haue reste maad good chiere ordeyned sette wacche well kepe oost kepe roche cacus come doun leyde hem doun vpon grasse suche wyse acustomed whan warre slepte passid nyght morn hercules deted oste tweyne sente hispan oon arragon nauarre abode hispan name hercules ioyously receyuyd nauarroys aragonnoys made hym obeyssance knowlechyng hercules lord moste vertuous prynce weste whan hispan subdued sayd retorned vnto hercules hercules laye yet styll fore monchayo helde cacus suche subieccion myht yssue cacus folk grete myschief vytayll wist ete ne drynke deferryd longe myghte hopyng hercules shold anoye hym longe ende whan vytaill fayled sawe muste nedes aventure hem self come doun cacus scyence made certayn secrete thynges go doun stomakes put therto fyre taught soo sodaynly felte fyre yssue oute mowthes fumee smoke suche habondance hit semed alle lyght fyre counceyll cacus aduentured hem self descende doun rennyng castyng fyre fumee impetuousement hercules grekes wende hyt ben orage lyghtnyng heuen brente montaigne made hym place ffor hit thyng make men asore basshid thus escaped daunger hercules tyme ffor duryng day roche full smoke fumee cacus made smoke materyell hit semed tenebres derkenes whan cacus folk thus escaped passid oost hercules grekes hercules moste wyse clerk world passetemps enployed studye toke bookes began practyse howe rayson descended roche redde torned many leeves alle thynge well considerid fonde fumee cam naturell thynge wherof grete meruayll sente athlas allway loggyd behynde ooste solytayre whan athlas come shewid hym smoke fumee yet dured tolde lyghtnyng passid oost demanded hym oppynyon athlas knewe incontynent fumee answerd hercules certes sone thou arte sharpe scyence myn age may atteyne hyghe thynges thy yongthe hyt moche knowe growyng thynge longe tyme paste shall telle shall saie thou shall fynde trewe suppose thou shalt vnderstande thys fumee thynge artefysiall maad crafte wlcan fader cacus whiche exellent maystre scyence inventour therof maad certayn montaigne cecylle brenne shall alleway contynuelly brenne vnto ende world cacus whiche arte crafte fader hath maad fumee escape fro thy handes descended wyth hys felawshp forme lyghtnyng tempest thus thy strength deceyuyd scyence whan hercules vnderstood athlas said hym gretly e meruailled scyence cacus myght beleue hit knowe trouthe toke clubbe wente vp thurgh smoke fumee vnto toppe roche sekyng cacus fonde nether beste ne man retorned vnto athlas lawghyng confessid hym hadd sayd trouth sayd wold make poursiewt hym moche gentylmanly escaped day pa ouer spekyng comynyng cacus hys fader wlcan day folowyng whan smoke fumee goon vanysshd away hercules began beholde contre sawe hit comodious ffertyle ende shold euer remembrance memorye hym founded cyte whiche named teracone moche gaf thys contrey sone kynge ancone made hym dwelle peple tyre hercules foundacion wente cyte salamanque moche hit well enhabited peupled wold make solempnell estudye dide make erthe grete rounde hooll maner estudye sette vii scyences lyberall many bookes made contre come theder studye rude dulle wyttes coude compryse ony connyng scyence moche hercules wold departe voyage wold also studye mayntened dide make ymage statue gold vnto semblance lykenes whyche dide sette vp heyght myddes studye vpon pyller made hys crafte arte cam fore ymage haue declaracion ony scyence alle pourposes alle scyences ymage answerd enseygned taught scoliers estudients suche wise hit ben hercules propre personne renomee studye grete alle contree estudye dured vnto tyme saynt iaques convertyd spayne vnto crysten fayth fro salamanque hercules departed wente cateloygne fouded cyte barseloyne whiche right good cyte fynably whan accomplisshid thynges sente athlas home agayn hys contrey helde hym alle hys wryters ffor louyd bookes aboue rychesse world wold gyue leue vnto philotes retorne vnto contrey philotes refused congie leue sayd hym wold serue hym alle lyf reputed felycyte grete seruyse gouerne contre fortune putte hand hercules callid hispan sayd hym hispan knowe thy wytte thy vaylliance haue founde alleway wyse trewe thou arte man auctoryte well knowen thyse march make constitute kynge ouer contrey gyue vnto none charge loue vertue ensiewe honour worshippe whan hispan herde gyfte hercules made hym fyll doun foot thankid hym excused hym grete worshipp hercules sayd hym wold hit shold soo delyuerid hym certayn nombre peple hys felawshyp scrue hym maad hym departe wyth grete syghys sorowe hispan wente contrees tht hercules conquerd vpon geryon vpon cacus fro forthon contrey named spaigne hys name wherof wole tarye conqueste spaigne shall come speke armes hercules dide lombardye deth cacus phow hercules fought ayenst enleuen geantes cremone vaynquysshid ben kynges empereurs sowdans prynces men may speke vertuous liberalite semblable lyke vnto hercules men day fyght oon ayenst another make conquestes ynowhe attrybue vnto synguler proffit resemble vnto hercules neuer fought comyn wele world noble hercules ffor folowe poursiewe mater whan maad hispan kynge regyon hisperye named espaygne sente ox kyen calues departed fro barselone toke waye vnto lombardye wente longe hys iourney cam nyghe vnto cyte cremone whiche daye iourney fro melane ther cyte xi geantes grete mesure xi geantes brethern fones neleo sone saturne callid hem self alle kynges cyte helde estate royall hyt renomes smale lytyll cause theuys robbid neyghebours made hem allday warre whan knewe hercules approchid theyr cyte anone assemblyd counceyll geder demauded oon yf shold suffre hercules entre theyr cyte alle oon oppynyon shold resseyve hym wold sende vnto hym oon whiche named nestor shold entre cremone yf first vaynqusshid b tayll xi brethern nestor comandement geantes departed fro cremone wente vnto hercules fonde lytyll armee thre myle fro cremone spake hercules sayd hym syre haue ten brethern kynges cremone haue sente vnto moche aduertysed thou entrest domynacion charge gyue vnto passage cremone yf thou first ouercome oon batayll therfore chese whether thou wilt haue batayll elli retorne agayn leue viage aduertyse alle geantes grete puyssant syre knyght answerd hercules haue taken way passe cremone late geantes knowe hercules hath intencion speke ner dredeth ne fereth accustomed tyrannyes whiche muste delyuere world foot armes moche ende presume haue ony doubte drede ony manerlye shall saye wyll fighte wyth ten oon another alle attones gyder yow hem yf ye accompanye yow hem shall fynde redy morn erly morow hercules wordes made peple abyde reste nyght nestor retorned brethern sayd brethern haue spoken hercules haue exposed hym comandement hath answerd right hyghe playn corage woll fygte v morn oon another v attones speke playnly hym hath semblante man vertuous armes garnysshid prowesse prynce mewre grete conduyte dispose yow well hit behoueth furnyssh hym batayll certes batayll shall perylous ffor myghtely membrid grete oon v thynketh may compare ne preuaylle ayenst v xi may escape fro force shall persshe hym wyth glayues som euer force strength hym geantes heeryng hym preyse hercules grete meruayll hym myght beleue nestor reported wold fighte alle geder attones ffor none thought hym self stronge ynowhe hercules axed nestor demaunded hym yf sewer haue well vnderstand hercules sayd vnto hym wold fyght ayenst hem alle attones nestor answerd ye herde hym saye hit propre persone wyth answere concluded morn shold arme alle wold goo felde fyghte ayenst hercules yf cam agaynst hem oon geantes sayd vnto brethern morn shall day glorye worshypp shall vaynquysshe vaynquysshour monstres late v make good chiere broder answerd nestor ther doubte shall ouercome brynge vtterance hym tht ye speke moche shall glorye lasse shall xi ayenst oon well said yf fightyng ayenst v xi shall haue lasse honour late v euery man fight hym self broder answerd nestor yf ye seen herde hym haue ye shold hardy ye shewe semblant anoder man ye wene kepe yow offre hath maad lefte hit better haue moste prouffit lasse honour suche caas deuyses passed day wente reste whan oure come morn erly aroos adoubed beste wise coude sente oon men vnto hercules wete yf wold saye ony thyng assone messanger yssued gate first thynge sawe geant armed meruayllously messanger abode auysed hym lityll auysed hym wente vnto geant armed axid hym hercules said geant wole ye saie haue said messanger wyll saye said hercules geantes cremone haue cause lette passage cyte moche dide wete yesterdaye yf wold haue passage hit behoued vaynquissh oon another felde bataill comen hether hope wynne paas ne demande thynge see armes fight gider attones thende haue sooner doon wherfore pray yow goo signefie hem comyng haste thhe messanger wordes retorned vnto geantes tolde founde whan geantes knewe hercules redy felde toke glayues habillemens warre departed fro cyte adressyng ayenst hercules hercules allone place men woman cremone wente vpon wallis towres see batayll philotes noble men grekes vpon hyll ferre ynowh fro place hercules abidyng geantes certes hit fair fight see comyng xi geantes well apoynt well garnysshid helmes enryched gold stone grete stronge oon mesure berded fiers contenances cam marchid sharply aspre corage whan cam nyghe hercules vpon half bowe shotte escryed hym deth made crye grete walles cyte ounded ran ayenst assewrid prynce lyke ben yons hercules heeryng cryes seeyng course foot fermly abode lyftyng vp clubbe ouer heed whan hit cam thassamble hit semed well geantes shold haue frusshid hym glayues ffor smote vpon hym desmesurably tronchons peces flewe ayer stroke grete hercules suffred hem beheld power whan made assayes vpon hym hercules made assaye vpon hem clubbe smote oon geantes vpon helme frusshid helme also heed tht fill doun sodaynly ded whan ten geantes sawe broder ded oon strook grete sorowe blood strongly meuyd nature amonested take vengeance dide hem assayllid eygrely side hercules thus began batayll betwene hercules geantes hercules ne dredde strook glayue spere ne polaxe skyn lyon hard stronge strengthe stable clubbe bare hit nede grete stroke gaf eche geantes dide myght gaf stroke ynowhe hercules coude neuer perce skyn lyon hit hard yet clubbe harder geantes meruailled constance puyssance hercules assone hercules lyfte vp clubbe smyte hys enemyes subtyll lepe side brake strookes hit dide moche lasse oure slewe foure seuen fought afterward suche vigour smote hem clubbe mortall fonde hem fiers etc batayll terryble harde ffor geantes stronge well vsed mestier armes grete payn saue auenge blood brethern haue worship batayll said infortunat whan myght ouer come oon man allone ne mate hym fightyng helped conforted eche alle good corage prouffited grete nombre brethern auailled hem coragious stroke whan approchyng deth hercules alway hercules reioyss hym flote enemyes conforted hym self fortune ffortune helped hym dide meruaylles sydes well coude fighte well defended hym dide well doon alle dide brassid nought worth notwithstandyng myghty hardy lukke good happe hercules broken ne clubbe coude destroyed tryumphed puyssance susteyne furcurs aduersaries myght charge hym stroke meruaill strength myght man puyssance man ellephant skyn lyon semed hit ben tempred quyk harde stele body semed constant ayenst cuttyng glayues euyll willars andue stedy ayenst stroke many hamers marteaul strook enemye hym greuyd toke grete playsir batayll seeyng hym self amonge many geantes gretly reioyssed ther thynge hym greuyng declynyng day whiche began faylle oure whan sonne withhelde rayes torned weste hercules wold make ende spede batayll geantes began cesse smyte ffor fro mornyng vnto euenyng foughte wyth oute ony cessyng hercules envertued hym self suche wyse smytyng vpon oon beyng aboute hym hard sharply wherof hyt befell enfoundred frusshid helmes heedes brake armes sydes meruayllously gaf many grete stroke fynably bete doun frusshed hem reseruid nestor whiche fledde away whan sawe disconfiture therm dide wisely ffor alle brethern slayn hande hercules etc cremone sawe lordes ded sone maad ende wepyng sorowe ben hem hard troblous ende bataill assemblid counceyll whan sawe hercules wonne batayll concluded geder wold yelde hem hercules put mercy conclusion yssued gate grete nombre cam vnto hercules whiche thoo vaynqueur enemyes ffirst kneled fore hym doun ground secondly prayd requyred hym mercy thirdly abandonned hym yte goodes sayd hym wold hold hym lord duryng lyf hercules pietous gentyll vnto meke humelid self receyuyd cremonyens grace maad hem ryse stande vp sente ooste whan come brought hem cremone grete ioye maad vnto ffor glad deth geantes ne man woman ne childe ne thanked goddes manyer hercules kynge cremone enriched newe tytle victorye first nyght entrid cyte restid hym peple also well refresshid right well fested seruyd vitayll morn dide brynge cyte bodyes geantes ded dide burie worshipfully syn founded vpon right grete tour hyghe vpon tour sette xi ymages statue metall facon geantes slayn remembrance victorye edifficacon tour hercules lefte cremone folk gouerne departed then goo forth contre studyed alway neuer ydle studied moche coude make fyre arteficiall well cacus fonde remedy ayenst armes scyence gate right grete loo p yng ytalye wente many place ouerall cam wente dide hym honour reuerence shall make longe processe oute grete auenture wente ferre cam vnto cyte standyng nyghe mounte auentyn regned kynge named euander whiche receyuyd hym solempnly hit wete whan cacus fledd fro monchay sayd vnto mounte cam ytake displaisant haue lost seignourie gaf leue dete fro hym seruantes despaired allone wente mounte auentyn euenyng constrained withdrawe hym theder doubted moche hercules whan comen aboue hyll fonde grete caue wente oute soper began disconforted gretly bitterly said ala exiled banysshid seignouries lordshipp haue socours ne comforte persone dare name kynge wonte name make kynges tremble ala torned reuersid haue thyng ete ner wote logge yf hit bestes poure kynge ony man vnhappy infortunat vnhappy dare seen ne beknowen wordes leyde hym doun vpon bare ground leyde stoon vnder heed right grete payne fill slepe whiche dured longe vaynes strongly meuyd herte quyete body right euyll susteyned anone awoke wente caue loke yf hit nyhe day nyyht anoyed hym hym longe whan comen ayer sawe day appere ne sterres ne mone shyne fonde hit alle derke tenebres thikke grete sawe region ayer couerid clowdes wherof gretly anoyed greuyd wente caue agayn deppest mouth therof sorofull pensif bood oute ony slepyng tyll hit daye whan day apperid cacus yssued agayn caue wente vp vnto toppe hyll began beholde see contre aboute contre semed hym good fayr lyue grete pensifnes many thoughtes concluded hym self wold abyde vnto tyme infortune cessed wold lyue proyes rauayn thefte bethought hym wold goo kynge pryeus calidonie whiche cosyn haue companye lede wyf chosen wold axe demande mariage oon doughters conclusion departed fro mounte auentyn toke waye vnto calidonie wente longe cam theder saye calidonie contre calle nowe calabre whan cacus come calidome kynge prycus resseyued hym hit apperteyned kynge moche knewe hym lignage demanded hym tidynges cacus began syghe whan sawe muste telle myshappe tolde hym recounted fro begynnyng thende hercules taken hym royames ben besieged escaped moche dar abide myn owen contrey comen hether vnto yow refuge telle counte sorowes haue entencion holde mount auentyn cauerne vnto tyme myn enemye hercules shall departe fro myn herytage kepe secrete man world shall haue knowleche therof thende hercules knowe hyt ffor moche hath grete hate hath gretter happe fortune armes haue yf knewe ony place certayn wold come theder destroye considerid haue chosen cauerne hyde haue sayd moche haue sorowe felyng taste requyreth hyt eyen man beyng grete troble reioyssen vysage syght woman ffor woman gladnes comfort man requyre yow praye yow ye gyue wyf oon doughters yf hit plese yow doo certes ye shall grete plaisir moste case may haue presente tyme kynge prycus answerd said cacus ye ben comen extrayt hyghe gentylnes haue grete lordship seignourye hisperye yf fortune agayn yow day hyenes ought therfore vnknowen day haue foure doughters oon named yolee take whome hit pleseth reseruid yolee ffor yet marye yf ye haue ony make ony armee ayenst hercules telle hit playnly shall socoure yow trewe ffrende cacus right well content answer kynge thanked hym sayyng hewold make none armee season wold passe tyme caue like purposid concluded thre doughters kynge prycus sente fore cacus chesse oon whiche wedded laye abode two dayes thende two dayes wold departe toke leue kynge kynge wold haue delyuerid hym ten knyghtes ten squyers haue conueyed hym reffused hem wold none wold haue deliuerid hym certayn lady damoyselles toke none saue two susters wyf whiche wold force goo wyth hym thus departed fro calidoine accompanyed wyth thre susters way sorofull pensif fro forth thus beyng inpacyens vnhapp castyng oute royallte began renne bathed axe blood men woman child mette putte hem alle deth etc cacus began exercyse werkes furour tyrannye goyng vnto mounte auentyn anone come entred caue beste wise coude wyues moste secretly place made neste thefte pytte synnys ffor first nyght logged hys wyues wente hym village stood fast behelde fayrest howse wherin entred wyndowe open slewe alle therin toke goodes moche myghte bere vpon sholdres bare hem caue wyues phow cacus stale away ox kyen longyng hercules hercules fought hym therfore slewe hym morn cacus fonde right grete stone marble whiche toke bare hit vnto caue made therwith dore moste parte tyme cacus helde hym hys caue wente neuer whan wold harme euyll wente feldes sayd slewe mette robbed euery man defowlid woman brent howses townes shortly maad dyde moche harme italy passyd contre supposid behated goddes coude knowe wherof ne fro cam thyse persecusions cacus maad vnto ffor retorne oure purpose hercules cam vnto cyte kynge euander tyme cacus bedewed ytalye blood men fyllid hys caue contynuelle stolen goodes comyng hercules men armes beef ox brought cyte cause kynge euander shold seen hem kynge toke grete plaisir beholde see hem hyghe passyng fayre kynge seen hem hercules demanded hym whether myght sende pasture nyght trouth sire sayd euander yf ye beleue counceyll ye shall lete abyde cyte sende hem feldes wherfore sayd hercules euander answerd said moche whan sende oute bestes knowe become ben stolen dryuen awaye knowe ben robbours oure seruantes ben murdrid howses ben brent peple shold laboure felde ben slayn woman maydens ben villonyed put shame remedye hit ffor haue knowleche actours ne doars therof wherfore men saye wole mayntene ben goddes thus punysshe v oure synnes wherfore pray late bestes abide cyte thende ben robbed yre sayd hercules ye recounte telle grete meruayll beleue well tho thinges ye saye ben veritable notwithstandyng syn goddes haue saued hem vnto day shall kepe yet yf hit plese ffor yf haue also well take cyte feldes yf ther robbeur theef contre take hem away suppose shall fynde hym shall make ytalye quyte hym wordes hercules sente bestes pasture lefte hem wyth oute ony kepars day passid ouer nyght cam nyght cacus yssued oute caue wente contrey pylle robbe yf myght fynde ony proye thus vnhappy secheth euyll ende paid attones trespaces vnhappy aventure broughte hym medowe pastured ox kyen hercules hit nyghe morenyng hym thre wyues assone sawe bestes lyght mone shone cleer knewe hem anone abasshid blood changed visage wyth oute cause ffor sodaynly alle sorowes began ryse hym cam quyknes herte coude speke wyuys seeyng spake word beheld bestes awondred cam hym demanded hym whaat ala answerd cacus syn hyt ye muste nedes knowe telle yow certaynte alle sorowe world aryseth stomacke environneth myn herte ffor see ox tryumphe myn enemye hercules beholdyng renewe loss haue hym honeurs worshippis hath maad lese also royames hath taken away fro grete myserye muste nedes place cursyd hys comynge ffor wote neuer doo signe vengeance shall slee ox kyen whan thre susters herd cacus sorowed counceyllid hym shold slee bestes sayng yf slewe hem hercules shold lese thyng shold ete hit better sayd wyf ye take lede away many ye may brynge caue ffor fy ye soo hercules shall haue domage displaysir ye shall haue plaisir prouffit cacus beleuyd thatthis wyf sayd hym yet loked medowe aboutes yf ony man ben kepe fonde man ne woman cam bestes toke eighte beste coude chese foure ox foure kyen bonde geder corde taylles put corde aboute nekke drewe hem manyer vnto caue well bestes resisted strongly goo backward manyere cacus brought many ere reculyng goyng backward tho bestes staall thende tht man shold folowe hym traches foot bestes whan putte caue bestes hercules said shette doore well man shold neuer haue knowen ne parceyuyd ben ony dore wenyng ben sewer layd hym doun slepte anone sonne rysing hit day hercules desired moche tydynges bestes arose vp dide moche kyng euander brought hym vnto place ox kyen whan comen medowe hercules fonde hym lacked foure ox many kyen wherfore sore troblid knowe yf goddes taken ony theuys stolen comanded shold aspye alle aboute medowe see yf traches thempryntes foot bestes myght seen knowen comandemet oon began seche behelde toward mounte auentyn fonde paas foot ox thoughte paas bestes descended fro mount come medowe whan alle sought longe sawe fonde thynge maad reporte vnto hercules said hym cowde perceyue syde ox yssued syde coude fynde none ensignes ne tokenes bestes goyng pasture right well sayd oon haue founde paas foot certayn ox kyen ben descended mountaigne medowe whan hercules herde saie fro montaigne comen ox medowe called euander demanded hym peple dwellid montaigne euander sayd hym ther ne dwellid man ne beste montaygne inhabited hercules wold goo see paas wente theder hym thoughte well theder myght haue passid eyghte grete bestes nyght trace foot grete newe hee wold wete become fonde well foot bestes toke theyr ende pastured ryght sore esmeruayllid moche strange bestes began thenke whan lityll thoughte behelde mounte said hit muste nedes bee goddes haue rauysshed ox elli ther theef montaigne come hath stolen hem hath ledde hem away reculyng backward moche haue lasse suspecion goddes vpon theef shall neuer departe hen vnto tyme haue serched montaigne oon side ffor herte iugeth bestes ben etc conclusion hercules dide take diuerse calues maad hem faste tyll none whyle duryng sente harnoys armes philotes adoubed made hym redy fighte anone mydday calues began crye blete honger dide brought aboute montaygne passid place caue cryed hyt happend kyen caue herde answerd cryyng lowde sowne passid hook caue cam cere calues also hercules whan hercules herde crye kyen abood calues began crye agayn kyen cryed cacus force cryes awaked allway doubted accused roose vp cutte throtes kyen calues naturelly knowyng moders cryed sore lowde brayed desired mylk lyue hit coude lowde crye moders answerd herof meruaylled moche hercules approchid mounte wente vnto place hym semed herde kyen well thre owres seechyng yf coude fynde ony hoole caue reduyte hit passid many tymes entree caue coude neuer perceyue hit sayd bruyt brayyng herde kyen comen illusion sayd hercules loste labour payne prayd hym leue seke ony thoughte recouerable ende whan hercules herd oon sawe myght come ende desire grete anger toke armes grete tree grewe shoke hit thre tymes grete force thirde tyme ouerthrewe hit rote alle suche wyse roote cam oute erthe maad right grete large hoole parfounde depe botom caue en playnly whan hercules sawe grete hoole root tree maad ryght ioyous glad sayd trewly hit grete theef dwellith muste see yf marchantes enhabite place sayyng wordes hercules bowed doun hys heed beheld oon side caue sawe cacus assone sawe theef knew hym anone wherof ioyous fere escryed hym cacus see thee thou haste fore tyme troblyd royames hesperye innumerable delyctes grete synnes thou madeste openly apperte cause pardicion thy seignourye thou troblest ytaliens tyrannyes hyd vnknowen knowe thy lyf thou mayste denye hit ne forsake hit hit behoueth thou dye therfore make ytalyens franke free thyn horrible odious theftes cursid man yf thy crownes thy diademes thy septres thy bruytes thy ryall men myghte socoure wherfore arte thou wrappid synnes amendest ne correcte pugnycion thou hast suffred yet stede place thou sholdest dispose th apperteyneth kynge pryuce thou haste ben theef stede iustyce thou haste ben murdrer putter fyre brenne village howses thou sholdest haue kept sauyd woman thou hast defowled hem vilonnye kaytyf kynge oute coniuryng pynyng certes see well thou art ytalyens knowe thou hast persecuted hem thy malyce hath ben grete thy subtylte whan vnto thys day thou neuer accused hast doon grete thynge hit grete ner hast hidde thou arte right nyghe perill ffor thou shalt yelde agayn ox ffinably thou shalt put deth thou shalt deye hand thou shalt escape rennyng ne thy subtyll fyres whan cacus vnderstode sentence strongly affrayed neuerthelesse lyfte vp hede seeyng founde hercules man world moste hatid sayd hym ala hercules man corrumped couetyse cursid fortune hath made drawe oute tree wherof parfonde depe rootes hath discouerid reposayll kynge cacus late regnyng pryued fro regnyng bannysshid fro worldly prosperite suffiseth may haue chierte naturell goodes whan thou hast taken alle away fro hit force lyue robberye proye wherof culpe synne ought redonde vpon suffrest thou lyue drawe forth residue poure lyf amonge stone amonge rokkes amonge wormes erthe considere thou haste kynge seke hym thou haste hurted greuyd hym ynowhe hercules answerd cacus yf thou abysmes wrecckidnes myseryes thy demerytes wole accuse ryght sory dolant see kyng hountous shamefull estate whan thou canste aourne thy dayes passid ne presente one good dede remedye thou hast dayly exercysed tyrannye well prosperyte aduersite wote well thou art newe persecutour ytaliens thy hand fowll blood seke ne ytalyens saye thyng moche complayne preiudyce tree hath spoken hys rootes hath discouuerd thyn enbusshe behoueth hyt thou chese wheder thou wilt come fyght ayer large elli come assaylle inne ffor yf hit possible shall delyuere world thy tyrannyes etc answer cacus knewe ther respite foot supposid saue hym doon afore tyme maad crafte grete smoke fumee hit semed come oute hoole tree maad hit ben right pytte helle fumee larded flame brennyng meruayll ffor fumee hercules abandonned neuer cacus leep caue myddell flame fumee maistre crafte anone pourueyed remedyes therto apperteyned wente hym playnly assaylled cacus suche wyse felte fumee ne enpesshement gaf hym grete strook vpon helme clubbe maad hym hurtle heed ayenst oon wallis caue cacus resseyuyng strooke lete fumee disgorge stomack seeyng manyer coude escape toke right grete axe stode hym deffende hym hercules suffrid hym take axe cacus smote vpon hym ffor caue large fought longe therm vnto rescous cacus cam thre susters made reste cacus toke hym grete pryde ffor stronge body hym semed whan restid hercules stronge ben afore tymes myght neuer vaynquysshe hym moche ouercome hym begynnyng presumpsion demanded hercules yf wold achieue batayll wyth oute caue hercules answerd contente answer cacus toke away stone shette caue wente oute goyng oute hym hercules espied hys kyen ded corner ox bounden mosels vnto piler sory whan sawe hys kyen poynt neuertheles passid forth poursiewed cacus racchid oute armes maad hym redy sayd hym thou cursid theef thou haste doon grete displaysir haue slayn kyen ye cursid theef thou thy self answerd cacus yet haste thou doon displaysir haue slayn men taken away royames thou art culpable euyll haue doon deth thy kyen wold hit plesyd goddes well mercy thou sewer thou sholdest neuer take away royame fro man late v achieue oure batayll wordes hercules cacus smote eche right sore grete felonnye stroke cleuyd harnoys sowned sownyng kynge euander grekes cam bataill see hit whiche maad fore thentre caue thre susters passyng desolate cacus enforced hym wyth alle puyssance ffor sawe hit tyme thoo neuer shewe put forth myght handled axe right myghtly well hym nede doo harde boystous gaf many strook hercules hym semed otherwhile sholde confounde hym vnto depe abysme erthe hercules syde faylled yf stronge partye ayenst hym also stronge avenant stronge certayn good helthe cacus smote neuer cacus torned eyen heed made hym stoupe knele oon side goo aback shamefully batayll longe duryng anoyed beholdars sought eche tasted harde bothe side fynably dide moche hit nede reste body swette aboutes hercules sawe yet pryse gyuen nyght approched grete shame hymself hold longe batayll began seche cacus nyghe redowblid stroke suche vigour vpon cacus fiersly laste bare hym doun ground astouyed made hym lese axe syn toke helme thre susters fledde foreste named octa full teeris cryes many grekes wold haue gon hercules made hem retorne callid kynge euander folk said kyng syre lo wonte troble ytalyens secrete murdres conuerte theftes vnknowen defowlyng woman gyue suspecion goddes lo menyster doar thise trespaces haue entencion punysshe hym deserte vnto deth evander answerd hercules sayd prynce exellent worthy aboue ally worthy excessiuely moste beste accomplisshid men flourysshyng armes reuerence due humayne reuerence reuerence dyuyne nature beleue assewridly thou art godde sone godde elli man deyfyed thou especiall haste seen momente eyen generall ytalyens haue seen one yere honderd yere sone noble men stock reluysing shynyng gloryous feetes dedes may thanke gyue lawde deserte grete werke thou bryght shynyng labour hast discombred v derkenes haste gyuen v lyght clerenes thou haste achieuyd grete tourbes assemblees men armes ytalyens sholde haue conne doo haste gooten tryumphe chastysyng geant passing terryble conne gyue reward truly yf thou godde thou haste goddes synguler grace promyse remembrance labour ediffie solempne temple cyte thou shalt haue awter vpon awter shall thy representacion fyn gold representacon tyrant shewyng thou hast vaynquysshid hym thende heyres successours tyme comyng may haue therof knowleche dvryng wordes cacus releuyd hym pytte grekes founden planted cacus inne heed dounward hye vnto ordure benethe ytaliens cam aboute pitte caste many stone vpon hym deyde myserably suche ende poure kynge cacus deyde hooll full ordure styngkynge filthe whan kynge euander sawe ded consente hercules dide hym drawen oute pytte dide hym born cyte hercules receyuyd tryumphantly man reherce feste grete nyght palays kynge euander passid ffor conclusion hercules abode foure dayes fanus comen home fyfthe day consydered myght enioye loue dide nothynge lose tyme toke leue kyng fanus quene facua retorned vnto hows kynge euander helde hym abode vnto tyme temple maad accomplisshid aboute consommacion temple herould calidoine cam vnto hercules signefied hym kynge prycus cam agaynst hym grete puyssance men armes auenge blood cacus cosyn inposed hercules oute cause cruelly put deth one noble kynge cacus yet sayd hym yf wolde susteyne contrarye morn erly shold fynde kynge prycus place blood kyng cacus shedde mortall batayll puyssan e ayenst puyssance wold preue hit trewe sayd whan hercules well herde kynge pricus signefyed hym herte full ioye answerd herauld deth made cacus deye werke iustyce vpon quarell wold furnyssh batayll comanded retorned vnto kynge prycus tolde hym hercules answerd hym shold haue morn batayll kynge pricus supposid haue wonne auantage oost moo thretty thousand men thanked goddes tydynges cam loggid began sowne theyr grete abours wyth sowne theyr men put armes poynt rengid bataylle cam bothe partyes well one place blood kynge cacus hadd ben shedd etc phow hercules fought ayenst kynge prycus batayll fledde cyte hercules allone slewe hym many moo hym aboute fyue clock morenyng hercules pricus assemblid batayll fro fer pricus sawe hercules made meruayllous crye crye calidoniens began renne ayenst hercules maad grete bruyt hit semed peple ynowhe world certayn lyke small rayne abatyth leyth doun grete wynde lyke wise hercules allone layd doun ouer grete booste bruyt ffor assone sawe enemyes renne ayenst hym aboute quarter myle departed fro bataill well sette ordynance comanded folk shold haste thynge began renne ayenst calidoniens swyftely lyke hors lyke herte man myght ouertake kynge euander abasshid see hercules grete legierte swiftenes pricus calidonies whan sawe hym meue oost supposed hit ben hors beste ende whan hercules come nyghe space bowe shote knewe hit hercules sore abasshid comyng pricus escryed men vpon hym shotte arowes casted dartes speres vpon hercules ayenst partyes body neuerthelasse coude neuer persshe ne entre skyn lyon ne neuer rested till parfurnysshid course put hym amonge enemyes myghtely confoundyng fore hym lyke tempeste thonder wente myddes oost chief banyere kynge prycus hercules abood restid began smyte leye vpon one side dye swerd blood calidoniens swerd hevy noman myght susteyne hit hit forfrusshid hit arought hit maad place reed blood cacus shedd blode vpon blode ded men vpon ded shame deth kynge cacus vengid augmentid vpon personnes frendes habondance slaughter occision crye aroose gretly aboute hercules brake rente banyers recognyssances calidoniens conductours ther none hardy withdrewe ther none well as wryd aferd tremblid beste hardiest fledde fore hym made wold enemyes theseus euander cam vnto bataylle recountre ther many spere broken many hawber many helme broken many knyght smyten peces calidoniens grete nombre ther many stronge myghty bataylle ryght stronge myghty fyers kynge pricus put hym surth fore vpon grekes wrought wyth hand right cheuauserously hercules theseus dide worthyly digne memorye ranne fro renge renge disrengyd theyr enemyes hardyed encoraged theyr men shewyd shold doo feetes dedes grete hit inpossible recounte telle lityll tyme put enemyes dispayr shall saye discomfiture calydoniens ffor force armes abode vpon felde moste parte whan kyng pricus sawe peple myghte fyghte loste side fortune ayenst hym poyntes sore labourid nede reste withdrwe hym prees sowned retrayte sowne alle calidoniens tornyd back fledde kynge prycus whan hercules sawe calidonyens withdrewe maad semblable wise hys grekes withdrawe ony nede shewe enemyes wold well reste wise bataill cessed wenyng hercules calidoniens shold reassemble morn whan restid hem withdrewe hem day passid nyght cam kynge prycus assemblad folk shewid vnto losse strength myght grekes especiall hercules said might thynge conquere vpon coude wyselier doo withdrawe hem retorne contrey calidonyens dredd hercules deth tempest thonder heuen grete ioye whan vnderstode kyng pricus answerd one acorde redy put waye answer concluded shold leue tentes carte armour goo lightly secretly toke way conclusion paas paas wente waye oute makynge bruyt noyse dide moche nyght morn ferre fro hercules thys morne whan hercules espied fledde men poursiewid swyftly hit coude ouertake ffor spede matere kynge pricus retorned calidonie hercules poursiewid hym cyte whiche stronge wallis assiegid hym duryng siege ther neuer calidonien durst come hercules ofte tyme assaultid cyte loste tyme ffinably whan sawe coude gete ne wynne vpon enemyes callid grekes sayd man ne aduentureth wynneth thynge soiourne oute doyng ony thynge digne memorye oure enemyes comen vpon v yf fecche hem shall neuer haue ende sortly muste alle wynne lese wherfore aduysed shall disguyse go vnto gate late porter vnderstand haue erand vnto kynge vpon yf may entre goo vnto kyng shall doo yf hit possible shal neuer assault bataill yf hit happen may doo haue deuysed yow tht ye assaill cyte assone shall inn thende calidoniens may haue yow wel haue hem ationes vpon theseus euander vnderstode well hercules wold doo answerd redy obeye comandementis wold assaulte cyte sayyng hercules arayed hym like ben enbassatour theseus grekes dysposid make assault whan redy hercules departed cam knokkyd gate calidonie porter loked litill wyndowe see knokkyd seeyng oon man longe gowne opend hym gate axid hym wold haue hercules answerd sought kynge wold ye hym sayd oon porter certes sayd hercules wold fayn speke vnto persone sayyng wordes porter sawe hercules armed vnder gowne fewe wordes escryed vp hym tasted hym behynde sayyng traytre comen espye cyte whan hercules sawe hym scasid portiers wold grete ioye whiche couerd vnder symple contenance made begynnyng semblant wold haue fledde way escaped employed lityll hys strength portiers brought hym vnto kyng pricus whiche satte halle wyth doughters prynces maad hym presente sayyng syre lo trayttre entrid cyte espye puyssance haue taken hym said wold speke vnto persone well armed vnder mantell ye may see hit ryght euyll tokene ffor man desiryng speke kynge shold wyse armed pryuely ner couert whan kyng vnderstode thaccusacon portiers whilis spake behelde hercules knewe hym sore aferd wist saye hercules esvertued hym self putte hym self holdyng portiers castyng doun ground harde greuously neuer myght releue hem self whan calidoniens halle sawe hym euyll entrete portiers escryed hercules vnto deth assaillid hym side gowne anone rente comyng receyuyd many strook allway defendid hym without disployng puyssance strengthe aweyted tydynges assaulte nyghe affraye grete halle cyte alle party calidoniens ranne vnto palais assayll hercules kynge pricus adoubed hym cam vnto affraye hercules assayllid fiersly certes assaulte coste dere ynowh vnto kyng ffor bien venue hercules approchid vnto tabernacle stode vpon foure grete barres yron wherof toke one bete doun tabernacle lyfte vp hys arme wyth barre smote kyng pricus dismesurably vpon coppe helme withstandyng hys stronge harnoys armures alle frusshid hym doun erthe smote hym sore frusshid brusid fyll dounded betwene two portiers tyme crye aroose grete amonge calidoniens alonly also cyte ffor made wacche sowned armes moche grekes assaillid hastely wallis calidonie terribly troblid calidonyens wiste entende whether hercules assault full heedes armed well palais vpon wallis hercules slayn kynge pricus began smyte vpon enemyes stroke grete eche strook slewe two thre shortly bare hym knighly lityll couerid pament palais ded body calidoniens lyyng oon vp oute ony man myght adomage armoure calidonyens grete corage grete shame myght ouercome hercules allone doon vpon grete empryse assaillid hym grete appetyte caste vpon hym dartes sharp glayues armes sholdres bare dide grete thynges barre gaf grete stroke none hem myght resiste strength pour calidonyes cam theder grete corage desire venge deth kynge hercules put many deth wiste nowher sette foot vpon calidonyens tofore gate palais pyteous noyse wepyngs cryes woman child maad ende whan calidonyens knewe perceyuyd vertue strength hercules labouryd ayn cessid assaill hym fledde hercules yssued palais barre couerd blood assone calidonyens sawe hym escryed vpon hym passyng anguyss hously assaylyd hym newe caste stone dartes vpon hym shotte arowes hym habondantly pourueyed awayted passage assault hercules hadd moche suffre alleway receyuyng moo stroke nombred passid wacche awayted haue slayn hym restid neuer tyll cam vnto gate calidoniens ranne hym men oute drede deth strongly swollen pryde yre began newe smyte vpon sholdres vpon back whan hercules sawe torned fface vnto euyll willars smote vpon hem wyth barre right syde lyfte syde radely dyed barre newe blood maulgre enemye bete hem doun frusshid hem fore hym made hem recule goo aback fourty paas cam gate calidonyens siewed hym agayn er cam vpon hym alle brack brussid frusshid lokkys wekettis dores gate grekes assayllyd wyth alle theyr puyssance bete doun draw brygge callyd assayllans cam vnto hym wyth lityll resistence entryd cyte whiche tyme wyth grete occysion calydonyens wold yelde hem ne putte hem mercy vnto tyme sawe theyr stretes howses full ded bodyes etc phow hercules anamoured yole doughter kynge pricus requyred loue acorded vnto hym bi maner kynge pricus slayn cyte taken hercules tucion slaughter whan calidonyens humelied hercules theseus wente vnto palays came theder poynt fonde doughters kynge pricus ladyes damoyselles sechyne kyng amonge ded bodyes many ded bodyes coude fynde ne knowe hym tht soughte hercules comyng began beholde one soueraynly among caste hys eyen vpon yole doughter kynge ffor moche excellently resplendissant beaulte world none like vnto whan lytyll seen secrete comandement loue drewe hym vnto wenyng haue conforted anone right desolate damoysell sawe hercules approchyng vnto tremblid drede fledde vnto chambre ladyes damoyselles folowid amonge dide hercules shall saye entrid chambre satte doun h r wende haue rysen haue goon way helde clothis said vnto lady ye may flee companye yole spake sayd myserable tyrant sekeste thou troble thou hast slayn fader late suffise madame answerd hercules yf kynge pricus dede hit reson tht moche bewaylid ne bewept ffor wenyng auenge deth tyrant cacus cam longe syn assayll ytalye sayyng vnrightfully cause slayn hym susteynyng contrarye fought hym vpon quarell batayll ended ne put vttrance tyme ffor withdrewe hym peple cam cyte haue poursiewid hym hastely well coude ouertake hym whan sawe leyde siege aboute cyte wold come achyeue batayll duryng siege haue day willid haue ende ffortune hath ben side hath put yow puyssance certes hit muste nedes oute ony remede ye lady loue ffor seeyng synguler beaulte loue hath constrayned pray yow afectuously may ye cesse sorowe ye receyue frende loue ye wepe lasse ye gete wynne contynuell teeris wepynges ne pardurable sighes may neuer reyse fader agayn fayr yole wordes oppressid hoot contrarye ymagynacions herte failled hit pietous thynge beholde frende hercules wold haue taken vp susteyned betwene hys armes wyse lady alleway gouerned cam hym sayd hym knelyng knee syre pray yow name alle goddes ye wyll cesse speke poure damoyselle tyme hath thys day loste fader hyt muste nedes bee nature acquyte ye may wyth owen playsyr late lityll abyde malyncolye alle shall well yf hit plese goddes well yow requeste ladye hercules content late goo tyme recomanded yole vnto goddes wente vnto theseus passe hys tyme ende yole shold goo away ne escape ordeyned twelue grekes kepe comanded vpon payne deth shold suffre woman yssue chambre oute wetyng whether wente night hercules dide dede bodyes oute palais place made clene also ordeyned body kynge pricus shold putte sepulture whan thyse thynges accomplisshid hercules theseus men armes made good chiere suche fonde yole neuer oute remembrance hercules yole certaynly tyme disconforted hit recountid lady gouernance traueyllid ryght sore comforte chyere whan hercules lefte chambre sayd many wordes amonge said doughter ye wepe moche ha madame said yole may lasse doo whan shall haue cause wepe wayle yf haue none fader ded haue loste hym moste louyd world may lese ne gretter thynge ought herte angry sorowfull doughter sayd lady knowe well ye haue moste apparant occacion sorowe ony woman may haue whan hyt muste nedes ye passe thys infortune proffiten yow youre greuous wepynges ther may thynge procede augmentacion melancolye hurtyng appayryng preysid beaulte ye fallen hande prynce man worthy noble aboue loueth yow ye ought thanke goddes gyue hem prcisyngis grace ffor yow ewre happe myshappe yf ye beleue ye shold putte thys suffrance better suffre one euyll two thynketh ye oughte considere estate yf ye considere hit well ye shold payne yow forgete hit madame said yole ala may bee shold haue loue affinyte hauntyse vnto hym hath doon moche harme hath uot taken fro knyght ne vnclene cosyn myn owen propre fader late none speke therof shall mortall enemye longe lyue longe shall lyue shall haue morr prayer promesse ne manace mi doughter sayd lady make ye self bonde ye free faytes dedes loue ben subtyll sodayne loue alleway secrete trone none thynge humelye meke harde hertes bowe stronge hard ne stronge herte amonge humayne creature hit right sone humelyed meked whan hit plaisir ther tour hyghe hyt may beten doun subtyll myne nether wynde grete ne rygorous hit attemperid ther nyght derke hit furmounted wyth day ye hate hercules yf ye haue hauntid hym haue comynycacon hym parauenture ye shall loue hym better euer ye louyd fader moder ony lignage may proue self ffor husbond grete hate first er assemblid wold fayn haue seen hym dye shamefull deth sodaynly whan begon conuerse oon another louyd hym certaynly yf ben day nyght wente shold haue deyed sorowe anoye doughter suche ben toures loue ofte tymes seyth grete hate cometh grete loue glorye hercules clere herte ought enlumyned conqueste hath made cyte shall yow synguler preparacion good wold ye attayne gretter wele felawe loue hym dompter kynges best well faryng man moste tryumphant armes ffor hym thyng inpossible hath conquerid moste parte vnyuersall world doughter reioysse yow fortune shette dore prosite cometh yow hit beleuyd desolacion cyte hath ben deuysed ordeyned parlament goddes faueur yow ar parement none like vnto yow doughters kynges gyue mariage vnto man bi wordes fayre yole stomack enterprised large ymaginacions rose vp fro parte entrid gardero presentacion goddesse dyane whan comen theder knelid doun grete humylyte fore ymage haboundyng syghes wepyng sore doon ony tyme day fore sayd goddesse virgynes shall doo thy right symple ancylle hand mayde ala enlumyne hope beholde myn affliccion poyse myn vnhapp sende thyn eyen secrete myn herte see sorowe bere faveur virgyns kepe body preserue hande hym wold shold wyf hath engendrid rote mortall hate whiche possible anullyd nature iugith hyt possyble may loue myn enemye consequently trouth hate haue ayenst tyrant hercules shall pardurable etc yse prayer lamentacions yolle abode vnto perfoundeur nyght cursyng hercules sayyng hadd leuer deye haue ony loue hym thus desdaynyng loue hercules oute mete drynke passid nyght day folowyng hercules retorned vnto newe prayd wold wyf sayyng wyth oute respyte muste nedes agre thereto right sore displaysant thys requeste excused many facions longe reherce tyme ende prayer requestes hercules loue nspyred suche wyse damoyselle vnderstode well hercules yssued rote noble fader moder acorded doo plaisir shall saye yole comynicqued hercules wyf laye geder acqueyntid eche loue enroted hertes two wyllis lockyd put one hercules forgate deyanyra yole forgate deth fader moche enamoured hercules myght reste place muste allway hym meruaylous thynge rancour hate yole yesterday vnto hercules sodaynly torned loue infallible ffor spede mater duryng yet fyrste dayes loue hercules yole prayer yole hercules gaf susters mariage certayn knightes grekes lefte gouerne contre royame calidonie deted then brought ox kyen wyth hym sente ageyn kynge euander domynacion thankyng hym hys companye honour doon hym ewander gladli conueyed hercules grece hercules wold wyse shold haue trauayll laste euander wyth grete thankyngs hercules armee departid hercules excersite wente vnto see forgate behynde hym fayr yole louyd soueraynly day plesyd hym moche myght doubtyng lese loue dredde deth thus wente see mayntenyng power amerous lyf hercules rencountrid day nyghe hauen good cyte galeye marchauntes hercules made galeye tarye callyd patrone axid hym contre fro whens cam certes syre answerd patrone galeye departed late fro porte trace see well ye estranger ye knowe peryll ye inne wherfore haue pyte yowe youre companye therfore aduertyse yow praye yow next hauen ye shall fynde wyse ye tarye thynge may befall yow ffor also truly ye yf ye goo theder ye shall take harme ffor ther kyng tyrant moste cruell world named diomedes holdeth vnder hym ten thousand theuys makyth warre enst may fynde hath custome putteth men raunson suche hit plesith hym yf putteth suche myserye paye raunson lateth hem go quyte wyth money substance nourysshith theuys horse yf may furnysshe theyr raunson hym self smyteth hem morsellis gyueth hem horse ete deuoure one thynge good yowe ffor thys mornyng goon chasse hunte foreste whiche foure myle trace hym ther ben honderd strongest theuys hath knowe verytably haue seen hem departe passyng thre oures goo etc phow hercules foughte ayenst dyomedes forest trace maad hors ete hym hercules heeryng wordes patrone galeye sayd hym rehercyng lyf diomedes passyng ioyous hys herte syn deth theef cacus hym vertue myght knowe monstre tyrant ony men enpesshyng comyn wele thether wente suche tyrans destroyed thende men shold saye dyde suche werkes couetyse wold neuer holde ne reteyne propre vse thynge goodes conquerid suche wyse gaue hit vnto noble men pre sid thyng vertue wold make seignourye growe ne amasse take hym self royame vpon royame cont nte nature gyuen hym allway wold laboure comyn wele noble herte right wel adressid corage tresuertuous paynem ther none like hym afore hym ne hym ffor holde entretieue mater whan patrone aduertised hym afore sayd tyrant dyomedes goon huntyng foreste honderd theuys dide moche patrone shewyd hym sytuacion foreste way maner myght sonnest come theder gaf leue patrone goo way done callid maryners made seche place assemblid grekes tolde wold shold abide hym hym self wyth oute delaye wold goo foreste patrone enseigned hym seke diomedes sayyng tht wold neuer retorne grece vnto tyme delyuerid contrey tyrant yole began wepe whan herde thentrepryse hercules prayd hym tenderly wepyng wold leue departe hym aventure grete paryll hercules toke rewarde ne hede prayer delyuerid philotes bowe clubbe entrid lytill galeye subtyll lyghte whiche conduyted helpe phylotes ryght nyhe place wold bee toke lande two bowe shotte fer fro foreste settyng foot lande herde bruyt noyse chasse therof grete ioye sayd well adressid toke clubbe lefte bowe philotes entryd foreste ferre rengid foreste whan fonde diomedes honderd theuys dyomedes firste fro ferre espyed hercules knewe estrauger escryed hym sayd geant thou sechest foreste hercules answerd art thou diomedes said kynge trace thou art entrid domynacon oute leue hit displeseth thou must prysonner wher fore yelde hercules said kynge syn thou arte diomedes kynge trace thou art sauns faulte tyrant seke therfore thentencion yelde oute strook smytyng also euyll theef knowe thou shall defende clubbe whyche haue ben accustomed destroye monstres hope daye make thy horse ete deuoure thy body lyke thou haste taught vsid ete thy prysonners whan diomedes herd answer hercules toke ryght grete axe oon hys theuys bare hym lyft hit vp escryyng hercules vnto deth dischargid hard yf hereules torned strook clubbe ben grete peryll diomedes gretenes stature hercules largely strenght puyss nce whan hercules receyuyd strook enhaunced clubbe faillid smyte diomedes ffor gaf hym suche strook vpon stomack heuy torned hym vp doun horse laye astonyed felde honderd theuys meuyd assayllid hercules side redressid diomedes sette hym agayn vpon horse late flee vpon hercules largely arowes dartes brake glayues vpon hym alle thise thynges enpayred thynge armes hercules hawbere nd helme fyn steell forged temprid hard frode amonge lyke montaygne whan suffrid fyrst enuaye assault theuys shewe fought meuyd vpon smote doun right sydes suche vertue sodaynly maad peces flee wode smote doun horse diomedes tyme reysid grete fureur maletalent many complices cam vnto rescows theuys hercules gouernyd wold whi assayllid hym cam behynde smote hym axe vpon helme strook grete fyre sprange oute diomedes well wende haue murdrid hercules well hercules meuyd strook lytill bowed heed lyfte vp clubbe smote amonge theuys maulgre lasse oure holden yren theyr backes honderd slewe syxty alle brussyd frusshyd putte hem flyght diomedes hercules rennyng swyftely hors amonge pour iewid diomedes nyghe raught hym legge pullyd hym doun horse caste hym donn ayenst tre vnto erthe toke hym body vyue force bare hym vnto place batayll ben dyshelmyd hym vnarmed wyth lytyll resistence dyomedes brussyd myght helpe hym self whan hym thus wyll bonde hym foot handes thys assemblid geder twenty horse theuys ranne spark wood cam diomedes said hym thou cursid enemye thy tyme haste enployed tyrannye didest neuer oon good dede thy dayes hast lynyd multeplyyng synnes vice thou hast troublid peple thefte proyes irreparable thou hast nourysshid thy horse wyth mannys flessh cruelte thou haddest supposid haue made dye certes shall iustice vpon shall doo thyn euyll persone like thou woldest haue doon myne hercules leyde tyrant myddes horse whiche grete honger anone deuowred hym louyd mannys flessh thus whan hercules put tyrant deth toke armes syngne victorye retorned vnto philotes abode hym philotes grete ioye whan sawe hercules retorne enquyred hym doon born hym hercules hidde ne concelid thynge hym shall saye grete ioye gladnes retorned vnto grekes dide disancre shippes saillyd aryue porte hauen trace wold hercules hit knowen hit late trace full deth kynge diomedes notwithstandyng hercules toke philotes armes dyomedes sente hym cyte somone gouerned hit yelde hit handes philotes wente palais trace made assemblid pryncipall cyte whan assemblid philotes dide open charge message somoned tracyens shold put cyte handes hercules sayng hercules putte deth diomedes euyll lyuyng loue comyn wele cyte cowde better resseyue hym comyng ffor wold pylle hyt wold onely reduy schit good polycye whan doon somacion ende shold beleue hym discouerd shewid vnto armes diomedes whan tracyens herd philotes sawe armes diomedes complices semblable vocacon diomedes theuys full grete fureur wold haue taken armes fro philotes wyse notable men many yeres desired ende kynge seeyng armes knewe assuridly dyomedes ded full ioye answerd philotes ffor moche hercules kynge grete renomee wysedom done werke grete meryte deth diomedes wold receyue hym good herte cyte wyth oure plente langage tracyens wente vnto gate opend hit philotes retorned vnto hercules tolde hym thyse tydynges hercules grekes wente oute theyr galeyes entrid trace space tyme tracyens brought hem vnto palays yet many theuys hercules putte alle theuys deth nyght duryng space ten dayes soiournyd sette cyte good nature polycye delyueryd hyt euyll theuys maad iuges eleccon playsir peuple whan done alle thynges departyd fro trace grete thankynges well olde yonge mounted vpon see succession tyme ony aventure speke dide moche cam vnto hys royame lycye palais receyuyd grete ioye inhabitaus also neyghbours abode fayr yole whome louyd aboue temporell goody phow deyanira full sorowe moche hercules louyd yole etc theseus retorne hercules seeyng wold abide ther memorye world ony monstre ne tyrant toke leue felawe hercules yole philotes wente athene thebe semblably grekes toke leue euery man retorned contre howse recountynge tellyng place wente grete auentures gloryo werkes hercules renomee renneth fleeth royames empyres lightly wynde also lightly cam hit flewe vnto ycome deyanyra soiourned sayd deyanira hercules retorned fro spaigne grete glorye tryumphe descendid lycye dame deianyra renomee glad also subget grete synguler playsir concluded wold go vnto hym well abasshid signyfied comyng sente sore pensyf dowtyng shold fallen oute grace hercules made redy excersite right noble astate departid fro ycome day goo lycye processe tyme cam nyghe vnto lycye taried attyre araye beste moste fayrest wyse cowde myght callid squyer named lycas comanded hym shold goo lycye signefye hercules comyng comandement deyanyra lycas wente cyte happend hym right gate encountrid mette man knowleche squyer hercules lycas squyer grette salned eche lycas axed squyer demanded hym kynge yf palays ye veryly sayd squyer wote well passith tyme lady yole beste adressid oute mesure moste resplendissaunt lady world grete hit eche man aloweth preyseth thousand tyme deyanyra hercules hath moche grace contynuelly ben geder som euer lady doth hyt agreable vnto hercules ther man saye telle grete loue haue gyder lycas heeryng tydynges squyer toke leue hym maad semblaut haue late falle lefte behynde hym hys bagues iewels moche aduyse ymagynyng hym self hit good signefyed hercules comyng deyanyra vnto tyme aduertysed hys astate pensyf symple cam deyanira attyryng self precyously sayd madame doo ye wherfore answerd deyanyra therfore sayd lycas ther ony thynge sayd deyanira tydynges lycas answerd harde tydynges haue herde saye telle hercules thynges ull suche hardynesse certes hyt ryght greuous saye vnto yow hyt syn ye come thus ferre ye muste nedes knowe vnderstand telle saye yow certaynly lorde hercules hys palays right ioyously hath hym lady fayre excellence loueth aboue thyngis beaute whiche hyghe grete eche man meruaylleth moste souerayne beaute euer seen mannes eye beholde auyse yow ye doo er ye goo ony forther day hit force abyde take counceyll aduyse heryng tidynges deyanira passyng angry bespradd right grete sorow vaynes began quake tremble fayr heer adressid heed drewe hit handes fell maner disatyred smote self fyste grete strook vpon breste fyll doun backward swowne lady damoyselles accompanyed shryked cryed dolorously sore meuyd blood space tyme deyanyra cam self agayn alle pale destaynte thynkynge sorowe engendrid also sorowe comyng spake sayd feble lowe wy poure deyanyra shalt thou whyther shalt thou goo thou fyndest thy self recuylid put back fro loue thy lord hercules ala ala hit possible renouelemet lady may take away husbond herte late ioyned vnto deyanyra shall hit disioyned findyng woman folye shall make separacion auyse hit may bee ffor hercules noble herte loueth vertue yf abandonne gyue ouer shal ayenst vert e noblesse haue affiance hym shall trewe madame say lycas ye faylle thynge saye hercules noble full vertue ffor hath employed tyme vertuous thynges hit man hath taken loue thys newe woman beawte ne affie yow moche vertue affiance begyle deceyue yow ye know well fortune ne entertieneth longe prynces pryncesses toppe aboue whele ther none yet hyghe ne maketh hem somtyme lye benethe amonge suffre beholde see well ye haue doo yf ye go vnto hercules receyue yow hath ben accustomed shall yow tytle dispayre men saye loueth soueraynly new lady hyt aparaut shall sette lytyll stoor youre comynge yf ye goo lady shall euyll content hath bruyt euery man fayn playsir ther shall man hardy welcome yow loue goo theder thanne paryll grete counceyll yow better ye retorne come ye put thynges suffrance attendyng abydyng fyre bruyt lady passe ffor hercules alle parte men shall leue lady lytyll lytyll etc deyanira consideryng licas counceyllyd truly beleuyd well thys counceyll ryght sore wepyng retorned come whan howsse ycome pryuyd alle worldly playsir helde solitaryly oute goyng festes playes thus abidyng solitude greuous annoye grewe ample anoyance constrayned make infynyte bewayllyngis sighes contynuell confort ladyes myght gyue solace innumerable deuyses made vnto eeres make passe tyme myght neuer take away hercules mynde vsid lyuyd many dayes lyf hauyng alleway eere open knowe yf hercules sente ende whan suffrid ynowhe sawe thyng cam neyther man ne woman comyng brynge tydynges fro persone hercules made lettre whiche delyuerid lycas bere vnto hercules chargid hym delyuere hit persone propre hand hym sente hit vnto lycas toke lettre wente vnto lycye two myle nyghe cyte encountrid hercules crosseway hercules cam archade newly slayn wylde boor grete ther neuer none seen lyke hym whan lycas sawe hercules made hym reuerence presentyd lettre hym salewyng hym deyanyra hercules waxe reed changed colour whan herde speke deyanyra receyuyd lettre amyable redde hit fonde therin conteyned folowetth hercules lord man world moste desire yow supplye ye haue recomanded trew seruante indigne deyanyra ala hercules ala become loue tyme paste ye haue soiourned many dayes lycye ye haue lete haue knowleche therof certes right dolorouse auoye suffre bere desire deyfyed ne mounte celestyall manoyrs wyth sonne wyth mone ne sterrys oute rompure brekyng free herte desire solempne comynycacion may fro hen forth fayne hit sayd ye haue another wyf ala hercules haue made ony faulte ayenst reuerence wherfore gyue ye ouer abandoune may ye soo men name yow man vertuous ye abandoue forsake ayenst vertue well ye doo hyt haue seen tyme ye husbond enbrasyng v gyder kyssyng ye shewyd semblaunce solas ioye late ye ye louyd poure femelette ala ben wittenesses maryage eternall serements othes made oon men ben deef blynde goddes see wherfore praye yow ye considere ye ought consydere ye holde youre glorye derer ye doo loue youre newe aqueyntyd maketh yow erre ayenste vertue wherof ye haue grete renomee pray yow ryght hertely sende youre playsir etc whan hercules hadd redde begynnyng ende lettre deyanira yet behelde sawe hyt yole cam vpon hym wyth thre honderd damoyselles feste make chiere hercules hercules closid lettre
