deyanira ffirst tolde tydynges state yole delyuerid lettre conteynyng recomandid hym vnto none wyf prayd sholde gyue none euyll thynkynge leue hope pacyence wyse lady noble oughte bounde doo honour worshippe lettre lityll nought conforted deyanira strongly attaynte ialousye sorowe redowblid grewe redoublyng wrote yet nother lettre whiche sente hercules conteyned wordes folowe hercules ala auaylleth wyf noble husbonde ye noblesse dampnable prouffitable fortune wonte resioye ffor alle daye herde none thynges loanges preysynges yowr prowess right gloryouse dedes feetes wherof worlde enlumyned shoon muste angry take displaisir werkes ben fowle full vyces alle grece murmureth vpon yow peple saie ye wonte vaynquysshour alle thynges wno ye ben vaynquysshid folyssh loue yole ala kynge heuen erthe shall callid hyt alleway happy monte vnto moste hyghe astate ffor fro moche haue mounted heyghte felawe fro ferre fele falle grete peryll hercules yf beaute ye toke wyf may well curse beaute ffor cause greuous shame alle euydente ffor prenostyque myn harme euyll future come astronomyens see wold knewe wote well beaute beaute haue brought herte strayt prysone sorowe oute ende tempestes see falsenesse world myn herte tremblyth hath ryght grete feer ought haue beleue hoope welthe alle remembre mynde thynke daye idreme nyghte thynketh veryly see cuttyng sharpp swerdes entre langyng doughters athlas may fall grete fawte enbrace beclyppe flesshly wyf owne thys withstandyng acertayned trowth ye holde kaytyf yole kaytyf owne wyf pryson playsir chambre parced bedde courteyned auentures warres ben ryght doubteuses daungerous man knoweth may come therof well iniurye grete holde suster grete dishonoure yet wole begynne warre firste yf ye thynke good shall sende moste sage prudent men haue praye requyre rendre yelde agayn suster exione shall contente pardone alle iniuryes etc whan kynge thus fynysshid wordes alle assystents allowed preysyd hys aduyse semed good kynge pryant callid one prynces named anthenor prayd hym swetely wold empryse legacon grece anthenor answerd hym humbly redy doo good playsir shippe made redy belonged conuenyent brynge anthenor grece entrid shippe meyne saillid longe tht arryued porte ssaylle auenture kynge peleus receyuyd ioyously ynowh anthenor demanded hym wherfore come tho party anthenor answerd hym manere syre said messanger kynge pryant hath senteme yow hath comanded saye yow well remembrid grete iniuryes ye haue hym lityl cause occasion haue slayn fader destroyed cyte peple ded ladd seruytude yet worse hold suster fowlly concubynage hym holdeth yet leste ought haue wedded moche ye man grete witte dyscresion kyng lorde prayeth yow warneth hen forth ye sesse rage grete sklaundres may come cause good men ought eschewe theyr power suster delyueryd agayn hym shall pardone ouerplus shall holden hit thyng neuer happend etc whan kynge peleus herde anthenor speke chauffyd hym anone grete anger yre began blame kynge pryant saye witte lighte menaced anthenor comanded hym shold goo anone land yf taryed longe wold slee hym grete tormente anthenor taryed longe entrid hys shyppe wyth oute takyng leue kynge peleus sayllyd soferre see arryuyd salamyne kynge thelamon soiourned anthenor wente vnto hym exposid hym cause comyng manyer syre sayd kynge pryant requyreth effectueusly noblesse suster exione whome ye holde seruyce fowlly ye wold restore vnto hym hyt syttyng ne torneth vnto yow glorye ne worshippe trete doughter suster kynge yssued noble ligne ye bee caas ye restore hym hys suster shall holde alle thynges doon well domaiges dishonour yow haue ben doon hym whan kynge thelamon herde anthenor speke began wexe passyng angry answerd hym right fiersly sayng frende sayd euer thou haue moche meruaylle symplenes thy kynge whome haue none amytye neyther therfore oughte obtempre hys prayer ne requeste thy kynge oughte knowe haue ben venge iniurye hys fader laomedon dide late oure frendes moche entryd firste cyte troyes grete trauayll effusion blood exione thou spekest whyche ryght fayre gyuen vnto guerdoun victorye doo wyth moche well play sir grete beawte remplisshid scyences hit light thinge rendre delyuere agayn thyng fayre auenaut whiche haue conquerid wyth grete payne daunger thou shalt saye thy kynge may neuer recouere poynte swerd repute fooll euer woldest enpryse legacion wherein lyeth thy grete perill thou arte comen amonge peple strongly hate thy semblables therfore go thy waye hastely contre ffor yf thou abyde shall make dye cruell deth etc whan anthenor herd thelamon speke entryd ryght hastely shippe saylyd ferre arryuyd achaye kynge castor kynge polux broder soiourned descended lightly shippe exposed legacyon lyke made kynge castor answerd hym rete yr sayd hym thus ffrende thow te wyll thou knowe wene haue iniuryed kyng pryant wyth cause hit kynge laomedon fader began folye wherfore slayn ffor wronged fyrst certayn moste noble grece therfore desyre euyll wyll thy kynge pryaut hys good loue pee certes hit semeth well chierte whan sente hether message thys contre wherfore rede see well thou abyde longe yf thou goo ncontynent thou shalte dye vylaynsly anthenor parted oute leue entryd shyppe saillyd tyll cam pyllon duc nestor soiourned wyth grete companye noble men anthenor wente vnto hym sayd messanger kynge pryant sayd accountyd hym legacion suche wise sayd yf angry nestor angryd hym self ayenst anthenor sayd hym ha ha ylle varlet maad hardy saye suche thynges fore certes yf hyt noblesse refrayned shold anone arasche thy tonge oute thy hede despyte thy kynge shold force horse alle drawe thy membres one goo thy way hastely syght goddes shall doo doon alle haue sayd etc anthenor alle abasshid horryble wordes du nestor doubtyng furour hys tyrannye retorned vnto see put hym repayre troye ward ben longe see whan grete tempeste aroose ayer began wexe derke rayne thonder right meruayllously make grete wyndes contrarye wexe thykke myste horryble hys shyppe born wawes one tyme hyghe nother tyme lowe grete peryll man sayd shyppe ne suppsid dye ne maad specyall promesses vowes goddes thise parillis thre dayes fourthe day tempeste cessid ayer wexe clere becam paysyble conforted hem self sayllid ferre cam porte troyes wente hem strayte temple yeue thankynges goddes escaped many paryllis ben inne anthenor wente wyth grete companye noble men fore kynge pryant whan baron assemblid alle sone kynge present anthenor tolde alle ordre founden grece lyke hit conteyned fore thise tydynges kynge pryant sore troubd sory obprobrye repreuys doon messanger grece hope ne truste recouure hys suster etc phow kynge pryant assemblid baron knowe whome myght sende grece gete agayn suster exione hector answerd good counceyll parys exposed hys fader vysion promesse goddesse venus etc whan kynge priaut thus adcertayned hate grekes fayr mene coude recouere suster meuyd grete yre thoughte wold sende grete nauye grece hurte domage grekes ala kynge pryant telle mysauenture hath gyuen grete hardynes corage caste oute thy self thy welthe reste maiste refrayne fyrste meuynges thy corage well hyt thy puyssance yet thou oughtest haue take good counceyll meure haue thy mynde men saye comunely man weneth avenge hys sorowe encresyth hit hyt ben sewre thynge haue remembrid prouerbe sayth sytteth well late hym meue elli well e late hym kepe hym alle thynge may suffryd sau welthe man goth vpon playn ground hath thynge stomble thys maner aforesayd kynge pryant thought longe assemblid day hys noble men palays ylyon sayd vnto ye knowe councell anthenor sente grece recouere suster exione fayre manyere ye knowe also retorned wronges obprobres hath founde semeth grekes make lytyll counte iniuryes haue doon v leste yf wordes repente hem yet menasse v strongly euer dide god forbede euer hyt shold come vnto v lyke menasse v pray goddes gyue v puyssance venge v theyr trespaas semeth puyssaut stronge ar also haue moste sewreste cyte best garnysshid world also haue grete lordes ryght grete plente alyed v helpe ayde v nede semeth conclusion haue well puyssance domage hurte enemyes many maners v defende shold hit good begynne shewe puyssance haue greue alle yf ye thynke hit good shal sende men secretli shal grete domage er shall redy defende ye oughte alle employe yow take vengence thise iniuryes ye haue doubte ony thynge moche fyrste victorye ffor hit happeth ofte tymes vaynquers ben vaynquysshid vaynquysshid etc present alowed aduyse kynge offryd euery man hym self employe theyr power wherof kynge priant grete ioy thanked hem lete euery man departe go home theyr owne howses reseruyd onely sone legytisme bastardis whome helde hys palays sayd complaynte grekes wyth wepyng teres manere sone ye haue well memorye deth grantfader seruytude aunte exione holdeth lyuyng manere comyn woman ye puyssant semeth rayson shold enseygne yow employe yow auenge grete iniurye shame yf thys meue yow therto yet ye ought hyt satysfye wyll pleasyr ffor dye sorowe anguyssh whiche ye ought ben bounde remedye power haue yow well nourysshyd brought furth thou hector ryght dere sone art oldeste thy bretherin moste wyse moste stronge praye fyrst thou empryse putte execucion thys wyll thou duc prynce thy bretherin thys werke alle shall obeye gladly vnto lyke wyse shall doo alle royame grete prowesse knowe knowe day forth dispoylle alle thys werke putte hyt vpon arte moste stronge aspre mayntene bataylles auncyent olde may forth helpe self well wonte doo etc wordes answerd hector right sobrely swetely sayng fader ryght dere souerayn lord ther none alle sone hit semeth hym thyng humayne desyre vengeance thyse iniuryes also v ben hyghe noblesse lytyll iniurye ought grete hit qualyte persone groweth mynnyssheth oughte qualyte iniurye yf desyre haue appetite take vengeance iniuryes forsake ne leue nature humayne ffor lyke wyse vsen dombe bestes manyere nature enseigneth gyueth hem therto ryght dere lord fader ther none alle sone oughte desyre vengeance iniurye deth aye l granfader oldeste yf hit plese yow ye considere empryse onely begynnyng also myddell ende thyng may come ffor otherwhyle lityll prouffyten thynges well begonne come vnto euyll ende thynketh hit moche alowable man absteine hym begynne thinges wherof endes ben daungerous wherof may come euyll good ffor thynge sayd ewrous happy vnto tyme hit come vnto good ende saye thyse thynges ony euyll cowardyse onely ende ye begynne thyng specyally thynge ye haue herte put hit lightly ewre ye fyrst well counceyllyd ye knowe well alle affricque europe ben subgettys vnto grekes ben garnysshid knyghtes worthy hardy ryche ryght meruayllously crete day force strenhth v compared vnto force ne vayllyance wherfore yf begynne warre ayenst myght lyghtly come mescheuous shamefull ende ben grete reste ease amongs silf wole seke trouble oure prosperyte welfare exyone hyghe pryse hit behoueth alle v put v peryll doubte deth hath ben longe tyme yet hit better parforme forth tyme trowe hath lityl tyme lyue sholde put v alle suche peryllys mekely beseche yow suppose maner saye thynges cowardyse doubte tournes fortune vnder shadowe thys thynge bete ne destroye youre grete seignourye ne begynne thynge ought leue eschewe grete myschyef etc whan hector maad ende hys ansswer parys thynge well contente therwyth stode vp hys foot sayd thys wyse ryght dere lord beseche yow saye ende ye may come yf ye begynne warre agaynst grekes garnysshid many noble chyualrye ben certes bee whyche alle world none may disconfyte therfore begynne ye hardely empryse ye haue thoughte sende shyppis peple renne grece take peple domage contre yf hyt plese yow sende shall doo hit wyth good wyll herte certayne yf ye sende shall doo grete domage vnto grekes shall take noble lady grece brynge royame comutacion ye may recouere suster exione yf ye wyll vnderstand knowe certayn thynge shall saye hit yow goddes haue promysid hit hit happend late sayd parys tyme comandement lasse ynde begynnyng somer vpon fryday wente hunte foreste ryght erly morenynge fonde thynge torned ony playsyr myddaye fonde grete herte put chasse swyftely lefte alle felawshyp behynde folowed herte moste deserte place alle foreste whyche foreste named yda longe folowed hym cam vnto place tht passyng obscure derke sawe nomore herte chassyd felte sore wery horse also myght go swette side lyghte doun grounde teyde horse tree leyde doun vpon grasse layde vnder heed bow torquoys stede pelowe anone fylle slepe cam visyon god mercurye compayne thre goddess wete venus pallas iuno lefte goddess lityl fro approched sayd wise parys haue brought thise thre goddess vnto grete strif tenchon fallen betwene haue chosen juge determyne thy theyr tenchon stryf suche ete daye geder place sodaynly caste amonge hem apple meruayllous fourme fayrenes beaulte neuer seen non suche forne amongs ther wreton aboute thys forsayd apple grekysh langage hit gyuen fayreste anon eche wold haue hit ony thynge world sayng eche self fayre fayrer myght accorde wherfore ben submysed thy jugement eche hem promytteth sertaynly yefte thy reward tht thou shalt haue withoute faylle iugement apple yf thou iuge iuno fayreste shall make moste noble man world magnyficence yf thou iuge pallas shall make moste wysest man world scyences yf thou iuge venus fayreste shall gyue vnto moste noble lady grece whan herde mercuryus thus speke sayd hym cowde yeue trewe iugement yf sawe hem alle naked fore see better facions bodyes yeue trewe iugement incontynent mercurius dide vnclothe naked behelde hem longe thoughte alle thre passyng fayre yet semed venus exceded beaulte therfore iuged apple apperteyned venus gretly reioyssid iugement confermed promesse mercurye maad fauour awoke anone vene ye right dere fader goddes faylle thynge promysse nay veryly saye yow ende ye sende grece ye may haue ioye shall doo etc parys spacke deyph bus thys manyere ryght dere lorde yf alle werkys men shold begynne men shold auyse particularytres synguler thynges myght happe falle ther shold neuer enterpryse ner foot doon ner maad hardynes yf labourer shold leue ere sowe lande seed birdes recuyelle gadre shold neuer laboure moche ryght dere fader late make redy sende grece shippis ye may beleue better counceyll councel paris hath gyuen yow ffor yf brynge ony noble lady ye may lightly yelde agayn haue agayn suster exione whome suffre vilonye ynowhe spake helenus fourthe sone kyng pryant said thus ha ha right puissant kynge right souerayn domynatour vpon v humble subgettes obeyssant sone beware coueytise vengance put yow suche daunger lyeth herein ye know well knowe scyence knowe thynges future come ye haue prouyd many tymes oute fyndyng fawte goddes forbede hit neuer come parys sente grece ffor knowe ye certayn yf goo make ony assault ye shall see noble worshipfull cyte destroyed grekes troyans slayn alle ben chyldren therfore deporte yow thynges whereof ende shall sorowe grete execucion ryght byttre deth ye youre self wyf ben youre sone may escape trewly yf paris goo grece alle thyse euyllis shall come therof whan kyng herde helenus thus speke abasshid began countrepeyse thynke helde pea spake grete whyle dyde alle arose vp foot troylus yongest sone kynge pryant began speke manyere noble men hardy ye abasshid wordes coward preste hit custome prestes drede bataylles pusillanymyte loue delyces fatte encrasse hem fylle belyes good wynes wyth good metys tht beleuyth ony man may knowe thynges come yf goddes shewe hit hem reuelacion hyt folye tarye vpon thys beleue suche thynges yf helenus ferd late hym goo temple synge dyuyne seruyce late take vengeance iniuryes force armes ryght dere fader lord wherfore art thou troublid wordes sende thy shippis grece thy knyghtes wyse hardy may rendre grekes theyr iniuryes haue doon v alle herde troylus thus speke alowed hym sayng well spoken thus fynysshid parlament wente dyner dyner kynge pryant callid parys deyphebus comanded expresly shold goo vnto partyes panonye hastely fecche assemble knyghtes wyse hardye take hem grece day parys deyphebus departid cyte troye accomplisshe wyll theyr fader day folowyng kynge assemblid counceyll alle cytezeyns cyte troye sayde frendes trewe bourgoys ye knowe alle notoriely grekes theyr pryde haue v grete wronges innumerable domayges hit well knowen alle world ye knowe also holde exione suster seruitude wherfore lyue grete sorowe also ye remembryd haue sente anthenour grece hath nothing doon wherfore sorowe dowblid moche yron ben cured woundes insanable haue purposid sende parys sone men armes puissance grece enuahye assaylle oure enemyes strengthe doo grete domayges assaye yf might take ony noble lady grece sende cyte commutacion myght gete agayn suster exione moche begynne thinge hit may come knowleche firste praye yow ye saye aduys oute yow wyll procede therin moche hit toucheth yow alle well whan kynge thus finysshid wordes eche man helde hym stille grete stode vp knyght named pantheus sone deufrobe philosopher sayde right noble kynge trewe seruant vassale expose yow corage werke also treuly vassale subgette oweth counceyll lorde ye haue well knowleche deufrobe grete philosophre fader liuyd hole sounde nyne skore ten yere wyse philosophye knewe science thynges come saide many tymes affermed trouthe yf parys sone wente grece take ony noble lady vyolence noble cyte shold destroyed brente asshes grekes ye alle yowris shold slayn cruelly therfore ryght sage wyse kynge plese hit noblesse worde beleue wyse men haue sayd also thynge ye may lese leue wherof grete sorowe may ensiewe yf ye perseuere wherfore wyll ye put enbusshement vpon reste put tranquyllite vnder dangereuses auentures fortune leue departe yow yf hit plese yow fro folye parfyne ende lyf reste ewreusly suffre parys goo grece armes yf ye wolle algate sende ye another parys wordes pantheus sourded aroose grete murmures heerers reprouyd prophecyes deufrobe philosopher helde hit mocquerye fable grettest nombre moche consente par e parys comysed go grece wyth men armes parlament fynysshid eche man wente hym home hous place whan conclusion comen knowleche cassandra doughter kynge pryant began make grete sorowe folyssh oute mynde began crye hyghe sayng ha ha right noble cyte troye fayerye hath meuyd brought suche paryllis whiche thou shalt shorte tyme beten doun thyne hyghe tourys ben demolisshid destroyed vnto ground ha ha quene hecuba synne hast thou deseruyd deth thy child whiche shall cruell horrible wherfore destournest thou paris fro goyng grece whiche shall cause euyll auenture whan cryed wente fader kynge wepyng drowned terys prayd hym sholde deporte hym leue empryse wiste scyence grete euyllis harmes comyng cause neuer dissuacions hector ne monyssions ne warnynges cassandra kyng wold change purpoos ne helenus sone ne pantheus etc phow parys deyphebus eneas anthenor polidamas sente grece rauysshyd helayne oute temple venus many prysonne riches brought troye parys espowsed sayd helayne thentre moneth maye whan erthe attyred aourned diuerse flowres parys deyphebus retorned fro panonye brought hem thre thousand knyghtes ght hardy wyse made redy two enty grete shippes chargid leyde alle conuenyent kynge pryant callid eneas anthenor polidamas sone anthenor prayd hem comanded shold go grece parys deyphebus offryd hem self goo wyth good wylle whan alle redy assemblid goo theyr shyppis kynge pryant spake manereshit behoueth replicque many wordes ye knowe well ynowhe cause sende yow grece well haue cause avenge wronges grekes haue v alleway pryncypall cause recouere suster exione lyueth grete fylthe miserye ye owe employe yow wherfore pray yow admoneste yow ye putte alle payne dilygence may recouere suster ye certayn yf ye haue mester nede socours shall socoure yow wyth grete strengthe grekes shall mowe suffre wyll voyage ye holde parys sone duc conduytour bataylle hym deyphebus doo counceyll eneas anthenor wordes parys alle toke leue kynge entryd theyr shyppis drewe vp saylles recomanded hem conduyte iupiter venus saylled ferre hyghe see arryued party grece consteyyng contre hit happend hem day mette shippe whiche one grettest kynges grece named menelaus wente vnto cyte pyre vnto duc nestor sente hym menelaus broder kynge agamenon maryed vnto quene helayne fayrest ladye world men knewe tyme suster kynge castor polus dwellyd geder cyte samestare nourysshyng hem mone theyr nyece doughter sayd helayne menelaus made lityll discouere shippe torne ryght waye one knewe troians sayllyd ferre arryued yle cythare grece ancred theyr shippys wente lande yle temple venus passing auncient grete beaulte full alle riches moche habitantes also contrey theyr deuocion specially vnto venus goddesse sollempnysed festes eche yere gaf answer theyr demandes whan troians arryued halowed moste principall feste venus cause assemblid men woman contre ther aboute made grete feest etc whan parys knewe seest toke beste clothis dyde hem also beste faryng klenliest men wente hym temple entryd therin fayre swete manere made oblacion gold seluer grete largesse parys strongly beholden alle side beaulte one fayrest knyght world richely queyn ly clothed habyllyd hit gaf grete playsir vnto alle beheld hym euery man desired knowe whens cam demanded troians tolde hem hit parys sone kynge pryant troye comen grece comandement fader requyre amyably wolde rendre yelde agayn exione suster gyuen kynge thelamon ferre wente tidyngis comynge troians theyr beaulte hyghe apparayll quene helayne herd speke therof custome woman grete desire knowe experyence yf hit trouthe herde speke disposid go vnto temple vnder colour deuocion accomplissh desire grete folye hit vnto honeste woman wylle goo often tymes vnto festes esbatemens yong peple lityll nought muse deuyse may come theyr desire recche meshyef may folowe body sowle shyppe shold neuer peryssh yf hit abode alleway porte sente oute paryllys see hit good thynge precyous iewell good woman holdeth honestly hows grete domage cam vnto grekes troians helayne wente lyghtly see troians ought specyally absence husbonde hit custome woman wyll brynge theyr desire ende helayne incontynent dyde make redy horse alle convenyent goo vnto temple dyde hem vnderstande wente deuocion temple ferre fro place dwellyd whan alle redy clothyd habyte ryall rood companye vnto ysle cythare entrid vessell brought nyghe temple receyuyd grete worship contrey theyr lady entrid temple right stately made deuocion oblacion grete largesse etc whan parys knewe quene helayne wyf kynge menelaus one moste noble kynges grece comen vnto temple arayed hym moste gentilmanliest wyse coude companye wente temple longe tyme herd speke grete beaulte comen sawe gretly esprised loue began strongly beholde desire see facion body fayr well shapen alle thinges suche wise hit semed properly sawe nature made beholden beseyn thing hit seruyd encrece alle beaulte tht myght befounden woman wherfore parys might forbere beholde sayng hym self neuer seen ne herde speke ony fayre well fourmed behelde like wyse helayne behelde hym also many tymes ofte semed fayrer grete dele ben reported well sayd self sawe neuer man grete beaulte ne plesid well beholde lefte alle deuocion alle thoughtes gaf fors ne raught thing saue beholde parys whan parys knewe sawe grete ioye behelde swetely hym whiche sighte shewyd ynowhe theyr desire one thoughte gretly occasion myght speke gyder longe behelde eche semblaunt helayne made token signe parys approchid anone parys satte doun beside whilis peple playde temple spack wyth softe wy ryght swetely hym exposid eche surprysid loue one myght come ende desire whan spoken ynowgh theyr hote loue parys toke leue yssued temple felawshipp helayne sente hym eyen also fer myghte whan parys comen shippe callyd hym moste noble grettest companye sayd hem manyere frendes ye knowe well wherfore kynge fader hath sente v grece wete recouure exione suster yf may recouure shold domage vnto grekes may recouure exione ouer stronge hand also hit shold ouer grete daunger domage syn kynge thelamon holdeth loueth strongly puyssant owen propre heritage ben thynge puyssant take grece ony noble cyte contre full peple many vayllyant folk semeth good fayr yefft notable goddes hath sente vnto v reffuse see yle comen feste moste grettest cytezeyns temple replenysshid wyth moste noble woman prouynce also quene helayne lady contre wyf kynge menelaus temple also full alle riches yf myght take liue ben temple brynge prysoners v take goodes ther ben gold siluer shall haue conquerd grete gayne riches shold go fecche place yf ye seme good oppynyon nyght shall entre temple alle armed shall take men woman alle shall finde brynge shippes principally helayne yf maye brynge troye kynge pryant may lightly nowh haue agayn suster exione therfore aduyse yow hastely beste whilis hit poynte er escape v blamed thinge allowed hit finably concluded many councellys shold parys deuysed hit happend nyght come mone nyghe goon doun troians armed moste secrete wise cowde lefte kepe theyr shippys wente preuyly vnto temple entryd therin armed lityll deffence toke alle fonde temple alle rychesses therin parys owen hande toke helayne theyr companye broughte theyr shippes alle beste put hit sure garde retorned proye tho began noyse passing grete temple prysonners leuer suffre slayn take prysonners noyse herd ferre suche wyse castell stode therby herde hit incontynent aroose armed hem cam assaylle troians vayllyant tho began medle ryght fyers mortalle troians foure ayenst one slewe many fledde reentryd theyr castell troians toke moche coude fynde good bare hit vnto theyr shippis entryd drewe vp theyr sayllys sayllyd longe seuenth day cam arryuyd porte troye theyr shippes full good prisonners good rychesses abood porte thenedon thre myle fro troye receyuyd wyth grete ioye parys sente propre messanger vnto fader kynge pryant lete hym haue knowleche comynge alle doon grece tidynges kynge gretly reyoyssyd comanded alle cyte make feste solempnly tidynges etc whilys helayne prisonners shippe parys made grete sorowe essid wepe ne bewayle grete sighes husbonde brethern doughter contre frendes grete sorowe lefte ete drynke parys conforted moste swetely tht coude might suffre forbere wepyng parys said manyere lady wherfore demene ye sorowe daye nyght reste man woman might longe endure suffre ne wene ye sorowe hurteth helthe yes verayly lady ye make moche therof wherfore fro hen forth pray yow leue take reste royame ye shall lakke thinge shalle tho prysonners ye wylle haue recomanded ye shall moste renomed lady royame moste ryche meyne ben shall faulte thing wordes answerd helayne parys manyer knowe well sayd muste nedes doo ye wil syn prysonner yf ony good done prysonners hope goddes shall thanke rewarde doo ha sayd parys ne doubte men shall shall plese yow comande toke hand brought secrete place sayd madame wene ye moche hit plesid goddes suffre yow brought prouynce ye loste ye shall ryche honoured ye haue ben royame troye ryche royame achaye yes veryly hit wene ye mayntene yow dishonestly certes nay shal take yow wyf shall ye honoured ye haue ben husbond preysid husbonde yssued noble howse ne vayllyant louyd yow neuer well shall doo therfore cesse ye fro hensforth make suche sorowe beleue haue sayd yow ha sayd abstayne fro making sorow beyng estate ala happend neuer fore syn hit may none otherwyse sore anoyed greuyd shall thynge ye requyre moche haue puyssance resyste hit thus helayne reconfortyd lityll parys dyde playse wyth power etc whan morn cam tyme dyde clothe araye moste honourably myght made sytte vp palefroye rychely arayed aourned dyde prysonners eche degre wente horsback hymself deyphebus broder eneas anthenor polydamas wyth grete companye noble men accompanyed quene helayne departed fro thenadon wente troyes ward ther cam ayenst hem wythoute toun kynge pryant wyth grete companye noble men receyuyd child frendes wyth grete ioye cam helayne bowed ryght swetely dyde grete ioye worshipp whan cam nyghe cyte fonde grete foyson peple made grete feste theyr comyng many manyers instrumentis musycque suche ioye cam vnto pallays kynge pryant hym self lighte doun helpe helayne doun palefroye lad hande vnto wythin halle made ryght grete ioye alle nyght thurgh oute alle cyte tidynges whan hyt cam vnto morn parys agrement consente fader toke helayne hys wyf wedded temple pallas therfore therfore feste lengthyd thurgh oute cyte ioye endured yet eyghte dayes hooll etc whan cassandra knewe trouthe parys broder wedded helayne began make grete sorowe crye braye woman oute witte sayde thus vnhappy troians wherfore reioysse ye yow weddyng parys wherof many euyllys shall come folowe wherfore see ye deth sone shall slayn fore yen husbondes fore theyr wyuys grete sorow ha noble cyte troyes thou shalt destroyed put nought ha vnhappy moders sorowe shall ye see whan ye shall see lityll child taken dismembryd fore yow ha hecuba kaytyf vnhappy shalt thou take water thou shalt wepe deth thy child ha peple blind folissh sende ye incentynent helayne home agayn yelde vnto righte husbond fore swerdes enemyes come slee yow grete sorowe wene ye prynce husbond helayne wole dwelle home oute greuous vengence certes shall dolorouse fyn ende ha vnhappy helayne thou shalt v moche sorowe cassandra said cryed thus hyghe wy grete sorowe kynge pryant knewe h taken prysonner sende praye shold cesse wolde comanded shold fast shette prison yrons kept many dayes pyte hyt troyans beleuyd warnyng amonycion yf beleuyd hyt eschewid right grete euyllis cam vnto shall told fablys wole hem vnto ende world etc phow menelaus sore troblid rauysshyng helayne wyf castor polux brethern poursuyeden parys see theyr deth also condicion manere lordes well grekis troians thynges doon sayd menelaus soiourned pyre wyth duc nestor herde telle trouthe pryse takyng wyf peple wherof sore angry moche abasshyd dolaut sorowfull fylle ground swowne whan come hym self agayn began sore complayne hym demene grettest sorowe world aboue alle thynges moste sory hys wyf bewayllyd beawlte solace myght waye conforted whan duc nestor herd saye therof cam hym hastely conforted hym moste beste wyse cowde louyd hym wyth grete loue menelaus cowde leue hys sorowe toke hys waye vnto hys contre duc nestor conveyed hym wyth grete compayne noble men sente vnto kyng agamenon broder shold come speke hym also sende castor polux brethern helayne shold come also hym anone herd message cam vnto hym whan agamenon sawe broder demene suche sorowe heuynesse sayd hym broder wherfore demenest thou suche sorowe suppose cause iuste allewaye wyse man ought shewe suche semblant outeward shewing suche sorow outeward hit causeth frendes sorowfull enemyes ioyous therfore fayne thy sorowe kele thy corage make semblant thou raughtest thing befalle wepyng ne demenyng sorowe thou mayst neuer come honour ne vengence alonely force naked swerd thou shalt awake thy corage shalt thou take vengance harmes ben thou knowest puyssance haue helpars aydeurs shall fynde venge v iniurye toucheth kynges prynces grece assone shall requyre helpe ther shall one shall helpe v power shall goo grete puyssance fore troye shall slee oure enemyes doo wille shall destroye cyte yf hit happen tht may take parys actour hurtis yllys whe shall hange hym make hym dye euyll deth cesse thy sorowe late v beknowen alle kynges prince grece iniurye requyre helpe v take vengance menela reconforted wyth wordes broder anone sente lettres vnto alle baron grece theyr sendyng cam alle fyrst achylles patroclus dyomedes many assone knewe wherfore sente fore sayde wold go troyes wyth alle theyr strength auenge shame recouere helayne chasse agamenon chyef prynce theyr ooste wyse prudente good counceyll hyt happend kynge castor kynge polux brother quene helayne sone herd saye suster rauysshid entryd theyr shippys wente troians wyth grete companye men armes see yf myght recouere thyrde daye see ther roose grete torment see ther wyth cam grete rayne thonder theyr shippes caste wawes one another mastes broken theyr saylles rente fynably alle perysshid drowned neuer none seen payenems saye two brethern translated goddes heuen zodyacque retorned signe two iumentis moche brethern germayn thus endeth theyr lyues occasion pryse suster poetes faynen brother ben translatyd two sterrys north sterre south sterre whiche ben named castor pollux place declareth dare book facions grekes fore troye moste notable sawe hem behelde hem many tymes duryng triews often tymes betwene bothe party duryng siege fore cyte begynneth speke helayne sayth fayr world man coude fynde fayrer woman ne better fourmed alle membres agamenon longe whyte body strong membres well fourmed louyng labour discrete hardy passing well bespoken menelaus mene stature hardy armes corageous achilles right grete beaulte blonke heeris cryspe gray eyen grete amyable sighte large brestes brode sholdres grete armes raynes hyghe ynowh hyghe man grete stature parcyll ne like hym amonge alle grekes desiryng fighte large yeftes outerageous dispense tantal grete body right strong veritable humble fleyng noyses yf iuste trewe ayax grete stature grete large sholdres grete armes alleway well clothyd richely grete empryse spack lightly thelamon ayax moche fayr knyght black heeris herd gladly songe sauge hym self gladly well grete prowesse good man warre oute pompe vlixes moste fayr man among grekes deceyuable subtyll sayd thynges ioyously right grete lyar well bespoken none felawe ne like hym dyomedes grete brode breste meruayllous stronge fiers regard sight false promesses worthy armes desirous victorye dredde redoubted gretly iniuryons seruantes luxuryous wherfore suffryd many paynes duc nestor grete membrys longe well bespoken discrete prouffitable gaf alleway good counceyll anone sone strongly angry anone peasid agayn moste trewe frend world protheselaus fayr fayr stature right noble light armes neptolonyus grete black heer grete eyen ioyous well chieryd wynbrowes ioyned stameryng wordes wyse lawe palamydes sone kynge naulus ryght fayr shapp lene hardy amyable good man large polydaryus passing grete fatte swollen hardy orguyllous proude withoute trouthe mathaon mene stature powde hardy lityll slepte nyght brysayda doughter calcas passing fayr mene stature white medlid reed well made swete pytouse whome many men louyd beawte loue cam kynge perse ayde grekis vnto siege fore troye within troye dare sayth fyrste kynge pryant longe gresle fayr lowe wy ryght hardy gladly eete erly morenyng man wyth oute drede hated flaterers verytable good iustycyer gladly herde synge sownes musycque strongly louyd knyghtes enrichid alle sone ther none hardy hector oldest sone kyng pryant passid tyme alle knyghtes puyssance lityll besgue grete harde membres myght souffre moche payne moche heery crispe lisped ther yssued neuer oute troye stronge man ne worthy ne ther yssued neuer oute mouthe vyllaynous worde neuer wery fightyng bataylle ther neuer knyght better belouyd peple parys passing fayr knyght strong soft heerid trewe swyft swete speche tote mowthed well drawyng bowe wyse hardy batayll well assewryd couetous lordship deyphebus helenus passing like facion suche wyse man myghte well knowe oon fro resamblid passing well kynge pryant theyr fade deyphebus wyse hardy marmes helenus moche wyse clerk troylus grete grete corage well attempryd sore belouyd yonge maydens force gladnesse resamblid moche hector seconde hym prowesse ther alle royame strong ne hardy yong man eneas grete body discrete meruayllously werkis well bespoken attempryd wordes full good counceyll science connyng visage ioyouse eyen clere graye richest man troye kyng pryant townes castellys anthenor long lene spacke moche discrete grete industrye kynge pryant louyd gretly gladly playd amonge felawship ryght wyse man polydamas sone goodly yong man fayr hardy good maners longe lene lyke fader brown stronge puyssance armes well attempryd wordes kynge menon grete goodly knyght large sholdres grete armes hard breste grete prowesse brought many knyghtes vnto troye quene hecuba rude woman semed better man woman noble woman passinge sage bonayre honeste louyng werkes charyte andrometha wyfe hector passing fayr woman whyte fayr eyen fayr heer amonge alle woman ryght honeste attempryd werkes cassandra fayr stature clere round mouthed wyse shynyng eyen louyd virgynyte knewe moche thynges come astronomye science polyxena moche fayr doughter tendre verray raye beawte whome nature fayllyd nothynge saue made mortall fayrest mayde tyme beste fourmed many moo wythin towne wythoute duryng siege thise pryncypall grettest name therfore dare declareth facion reherceth phow kynges duke erles boron grece assemblid alle theyr nauye forethe cyte athene come troye many shippis eche man brought vnto helpe kynge menelaus whan hit cam ende feuerer wynter passid kinges prince prouynces grece assemblid gyder porte athene go troye hit mynde ony man syn begynnyng world many shippes knyghtes assemblid tyme first agamenon chyef prynce alle oost grekes brought fro royame michames honderd shippys full armed knyghtes kynge menelaus broder brought fro royame sparte lx shippis archelaus prothenor fro royame boecye fifty shippis duc ascalapus erle helmins fro prouynce orconomye thretty shippis kynge epistrophus kynge sedius fro royame cyden thretty shippis kynge thelamon salamyne fifty shippis companye duc thent r duc amphymacus erle polixeme erle thephus many noble men auncient duc nestor fro prouynce pillon fifty shippis kynge thoas tholye fifty shippis kynge doxunois fifty shippis kynge thelamon chyleus sixe thritty shippes polibetes amphymacus fro prouynce calydone two thretty shippis kynge ydumeus kynge mereon crete four score two shyppis kynge vlixes trace two fyfty shippis duc tynelus fro cyte frygis twelue shippis prothocathus prothesalus duke philaca brought wyth hem two fyfty shippis collesis brought four twenty shippis fro royame cresome brought kynge machaon kynge ollydrys sone thre thretty shyppes achilles brought fro noble cyte phaces two twenty shippes kynge thelaphus brought fro rodes two twenty shippes eruphylus fro orchomene two fyfty shyppis duc anthypus duc amphymacus rusticane threttene shyppis kynge polibetes rythee duc lopms broder lawe wedded suster lxij shippis kynge dyomedes arges four score two shippis companye thelamus euryalus kynge poliphebus nyne shippis kynge fureus thretten shippes kynge prothoylus chemenense two fyfty shippes kynge carpenor carpadye lij shippis kynge theorius breysse four twenty shippes kynges duke comen theder sixty nyne ther assemblyd porte athene twelfe honderd four twenty shippis wythoute comprysyng shippis duc palamydes sone kynge naulus cam wyth astate shall sayd etc phow grekes sente achilles vnto delphos god appollo knowe ende theyr warre fonde calcas sente fro troians wente wyth hem athene whan kynge prynces thus assemblid porte athene kynge agamenon chief alle ooste taught alleway coduyte ooste meurely assemblid vnto counceyll playne withoute cyte alle noble men theyr ooste whan assemblid aboute hym siege doo make sayd manere ye noble men one wylle volente ben assemblid oost grete puyssance ye knowe well mynde ony man sawe euer many noble men assemblid tachieue ony werke ne many yong knyghtes deliuere armes tassaylle theyr enemyes well oute mynde presumeth reyse hym self ayenst v begynne warre verayly doubte one honderd copanye suffysant ynowh bringe werke ende whiche alle assembled hit well knowen eche yow grete iniuries grete domagies troians haue v wherfore haue iuste cause take vengance force armes ende fro hen forth ne ne empryse vpon v ony manere yf sholde suffre suche iniuryes dissimulacion myghte yet greue v haue hit custome noble men grece late passe suche wronges dissimulacion therfore hit shold v grete vilonye many haue assemblid grete strengthe dissimule quarelle yet ther nacion world ne dredeth oure puyssance saue thyse ol sshe peple troye euyll counceyll haue meu ayenst v also haue enterprysid vpon v dide fyrst kynge laomedon iniuryed oure peple lityll occasion wherfore receyuyd deth reward cyte destroyed peple slayn brought seruytude ben yet certes hit dyfficyle hard v ben puyssante take vengeance troians hit foure prynces lasse puyssance cam theyr aboue moche troians knowe veryly ben assemblyd goo vpon ben strongly garnysshid men armes ayenst comyng alle suche behoueth deffende wyth semed good yf hit playse yow er departe fro porte sende ysle delphe specyall messangers haue answer god appolyn doo empryse ther none allowed approued wordes agamenon cheese incontynent achilles patroclus goo ysle heere answere appolyn anon departed wente cam sone theder sayd yle y hit myddes yles ciclades locana enffanta appolyn dyane ther ryche temple whiche godde payenems worshippid gaf answere peple suche thynge demanded hym yle fyrst callyd delos moche saye greke manifestacion moche yle paynems sawe fyrst sonne mone deluuye therfore supposyd ben born theyr moder appollo sonne diane mone theyr langage calle yle ortygye moche byrdes tht men calle ortiges englissh ben quayles first seen paynems gaf appollo dyuerce name dyuerce operacions sonne temple grete ymage composid made alle fyn golde worshippe god appolyne well ymage deef dombe yet allwaye ydolatrye regned suche wyse tyme world deuyll put hym ymage gaf answer paynems thingis demanded hym dide deuyll abuse folissh peple tyme beleuyd ymage verray god etc upon parte auctor declareth fro whens cam firste ydolatrye fynde historia ecclisiastica whan herodes deceyuyd thre kynges retorned agayn hym worshippid lord ihesu criste conteyned gospell departid waye etc herodes purposid haue slayn child ihesus therfore gloryouse virgyne lady saynte marie moder ioseph bare hym egypte sone lord entryd egypte alle ydoles egypte fyll doun erthe alle broken brusyd prophesie ysaye sayd thus ascendet dominus nubem leuem et ingredietur egyptum mouebuntur simulacrum egipti en demonstrant shewyng comyng saueour ihesus criste alle ydolatrye sholde haue ende amonge iewes ysmaell first made ydole erthe promotheus made fyrste amonge paynems taughte maner make hem ryght begynnyng ydolatrye cam belus kynge assirye tht fader kynge nynus whiche belus whan dede sone nynus dyde burye hym ryche sepulture dyde make ymage fyn golde semblaunt lykenes fader haue consolacion memorye hym worshippid hym god compellyd folk worshippe hym anone euyll spyryte entryd wythin ymage gaf peple answer theyr demandes thus ensample hym payenems made worshippe theyr frendes worshippid thus proceded ydolatrye ther none goddes propice gaf theyr answer theyr demandes engyne enemye deceyued broughte dampnacion enuye yet hath vpon lygne humayn god made fullfylle siege paradys fro whens caste oute pryde ayer derkenes day iugement abyde helle pardurably companye dampned men whan achilles patroclus arryued yle delphe wente grete deuocion temple appolyn made theyr oblacions grete largesse demanded hym answere theyr affayres werkes appolyn answerd wyth lowe wy achilles retorne grekes haue sente hether saye hem come shal happen certayn shall go sauely troye shall make many bataylles tenthe yere shall haue victorye destroye cyte shall slee kynge pryant wyffe chyldren moste grete contrey ther shall none escape saue onely whome wylle saue forsayd answere achilles passing ioyouse hit happend whilis yet temple bysshoppe troye named chalchas sone man named thistram passing wyse man whiche entryd temple sente also fro kynge pryant haue answere appolin troye made oblacions demandes troye appollyne answerd hym calchas calchas beware thou retorne gayn troye go thou wyth achilles vnto grekes departe neuer fro grekes shall haue victorye troians agreement goddes thou shalt ryght necessarye counseyll doctrine anone calchas knewe achilles temple approchid hym made acqueyntance hym accompanyed gyder fayth oth told eche ydole sayd wherof achilles grete ioye made right grete chiere feste calchas toke hym wyth hym yllyd longe arryued porte atthenes sauely whan yssued shippes achilles toke calchas hande presentid hym kynge agamenon tolde trouthe answere appollo shold haue victorye troians appollyn bad hym shold retorne agayn troye holde hym wyth grekes duryng warre tydynges grekes gretly reioyssed made solempne feste receyuyd calchas theyr companye fayth othe promysid hym rewarde hym well hym good etc phow grekes wyth grete naueye wente saylled toward troye arryueden porte thenedon thre myle fro troye whiche conqueryd bete doun erthe feste grekes made good answer appolyn calcas wente hym morenyng companye achilles patro lu vnto tente agamenon alle moste noble ooste assemblid salewed right courtoysly sayng noble kynges prynces ben assemblyd vengeance grete iniuryes yow doon troyans wherfore tarye ye goddes haue yeuen theyr answere wene ye kynge pryant hath espyes amonge yow whilys ye soiourne garnysshith contre cyte vytayll wyth horse wyth necessaryes hit grete parte somer passed ye haue yet thynge enterprysid vpon enemyes ware ye ben vnkynde ingrate answere goddes tht negligence change answere contrarye ther fore tarye ye lenger shippe yow hors goo ye see cesse vnto tyme promessis goddes accomplisshyd whan calchas thus spoken eche man sayde well sayd spoken agamenon sente vnto alle ooste comanded trompette euery man shold make hym redy remeue anone entryd theyr shippis disancryd drewe vp theyr sayllys wente alle vnto see longe sayllid passing myle fro atthenes ayer fore clere fayr began wexe troblous thykke began ryght grete tempeste see wynde rayne thounder moche ther none hardy hadd fere wende haue deyde theyr shippes caste see one supposid none certayn haue ben drowned sayd calchas hym cause tempeste moche dyane goddesse wroth angry vpon cause departyd fro atthenes made sacrifyce appese wrath hit behoueth kynge agamenon sacrefye owen hand effygenye doughter yong virgyne tendre age otherwyse tempeste shold neuer cesse spede sacrefyse counseyllyd torne nauye applye hit yle andylle temple goddesse dyane etc whan kynge agamenon vnderstode thynge alle marrid passyng sorowfull corage louyd doughter effigeme grete loue side prayed requyred alle kynges prynces grece wold gyue none enpesshement grete enpryse wythstande sacrefyse wherfore vaynquysshid sayd prynces loue contrey toke sayd doughter effygenye presence many grete kynges prynces sacrefyed vnto goddesse deane anone tempest cessyd ayer becam nette clere see well attempryd tranquyllyte pee wente agayn shippe alle lyke wyse drewe vp theyr sayllys sayllyd fore wynde ferre arryued porte royame troyes nyghe vnto castell named sarabana dare ne putteth determynatly wherof kynge agamenon made sacrefyce dyane ouyde twelf book methaphormose sayth hit effygenye doughter boue sayd whan castell sawe grete nauye porte armed cam vnto porte wenyng deffende theyr londe agayn grekes assaylled tho descended lande yet wery trauayll see grekes yssued anone oute theyr shyppys grete plente alle armed slewe chassyd vnto theyr castell slewe fleeyng entryd castell wyth put alle deth toke proye bete doun castell vnto erthe reentryd theyr shippis agayn sayllyd ferre arryued porte thenedon ankryd theyr shippis etc porte passing stronge castell well peupled full grete rychessys thre myle fro troyes whan castell sawe grekes ran armes garnysshid theyr castell wyth good fyghtars yssued cam vnto porte fonde grekes yssued theyr shippes alle armed grete plente toke cowde fynde thus began batayll betwene right fyers mortall ynowhe slayn dede bothe party many moo grekes troians assone grete strengthe grekes descended troians myght lenger suffre ne abide put hem flyghte somme castell fledde vnto troye grekes put hem beleyde castell round aboute assayllyd hit alle sydes within deffended hit passing well vpon wallis slewe many shotte engyns grekes dressyd theyr engyns alle aboute castell sette theyr ladder vnto wally wente vp alle sydes wythin defended hem vaylliantly made hem falle doun theyr dyches dede hurte grekes grete nombre sente allewaye newe folke thassault wherof within wery reculed wente aback fro theyr deffences grekes entryd force castell slewe alle fonde wyth oute sparyng man woman toke pylled alle fonde good bete doun castell howse vnto erthe putte fyre brente vp reentryd theyr shippis ioyous gayne goten castell phow grekes sente dyomedes vlixes vnto kynge pryant haue agayn helayne prisonners answere hadd whan grekes demolysshid beten doun thus castell ediffyces thenedon sarabana refresshid medowe thenedon agamenon charge alle ooste conduyte hit well good captayn ought doo comanded alle butyn gayne two castellys shold brought forth hit doon anone comanded wyse kynge distrybued gayn eche man deserte qualyte dide crye alle ooste alle noble men ooste shold assemble playn thenedon fore kynge agamenon whan alle comen kynge agamenon spack sayd manere frendes felawis ben assemblid iuste cause eche yow knoweth grete puyssance shall tydynges therof alle world alleway stronge puyssance hit plese goddes hit bee wyth oute pryde felonnye hit synne pryde growealle vyces goddes resiste wythstonde orguyllous prowde peple therfore oughte put away pryde fro oure werkes especiall werke vse ryght waye iustice ende man may reprehende v ne blame ye knowe well ben comen thus ferre take vengeance iniuryes wronges kynge pryant hath v haue hym grete hurte domayge ye may well knowe trouthe haue assemblid cyte troye grete power deffende ayenst v also cyte passing grete stronge ye knowe well ben vpon theyr propre herytagye thynge dowblith theyr force strength ye may take ensample crowe otherwhyle deffendeth well neste agayn fawcion ne saye thynges ony doubte haue shall haue victorye ne shall destroye theyr cyte well hit stronge onely oure worshippe ende recomanded haue conduyted werke grete discrecion oute pryde often tymes ouer lyght hasty enterpryse thyng grete poyse oute mewre counceyll may come myschieuous ende ye knowe well longe agoo kynge pryant dide requyre v specyall messangers sholde rendre hym suster exione orguyell pryde wolde delyuere agayn yf deliueryd sente home agayn euylly neuer happend yle cythare quene helayne moste noble grece neuer rauysshyd ne ladde awaye also enterprysed payne ne laboure ben ther none v knoweth shall happen hym good euyll therfore yf ye seme good myghte retorne contrey oute suffrynge payne oure honoure worshippe shall sende vnto kynge pryant oure specyall messangers bidde hym sende renvoye v helayne freely restore v domayges parys hath doon yle cythare yf wyll doo oure retorne shall honourable may axe hym ryght yf reffuse thys shall haue two thynges shall fyghte v iustyce oure trewe quaryll oure puyssance excusid whan men shall oure offres shall gyue wronge blame troians v loose preysyng shall ben excused alle domayges shall doon thyse offres therfore auyse yow amonge self thynge ye wyll doo felonnes blamed counceylle alowed hit fynably concluded soo agamenon sayd cheese theyr messangers dyomedes vliyes goo troye make theyr legacion whiche toke theyr horse wente incontynent theder cam troye aboute mydday wente strayt pallays kynge pryant toke theyr horse kepe gate wente vp halle goyng vp meruayllyd hem gretly ryche werke sawe alle pallays specially tree sawe playn whiche made arte mathematycque meruayllously composed grete beaulte tronchon stock benethe gretter gretenes spere passing longe hyghe aboue braunches gold siluer leeuys spradde ouer pallais saue lityll hit coueryd alle fruyte tree dyuerse precyous stone gaf grete lyght bryghtnes gaf grete solace behelde hit wente fer forth cam grete halle kynge pryant accompanyed noble men wyth oute salewyng kynge ne vlixes sayd hym manyere kinge pryant meruaylle nothyng haue salewid moche thou arte oure enemye mortell kynge agamenon whome ben messangers sendeth comandeth v thou renuoye sende hym quene helayne whome thou haste rauysshid betaken fro husbonde thou restore alle domages parys thy sone hath done grece yf thou doo trowe thou shalt doo wyse man yf thou doo beholde euyllys may come thyne thou shalt dye euyll deth alle thy men noble cyte shall destroyed whan kynge pryant herde vlixes thus speke answerd contynent vlixes wyth oute demandyng counceylle meruaylle gretly thy wordes requyrest thynge man vaynquysshid myght deffende hym self wyth grete payne wolde accorde beleue grekes haue suche puyssance doo thynge thou haste sayd requyre reparacion oughte demande haue slayn fader brethern ladde away suster seruytude whome daigne marye honourably holde mayntene comyn woman haue agayn haue sente anthenor wold haue pardoned surplus ye knowe vilonnyes menace dyde messanger therfore ought ony thynge ye saye leuer dye vylaynsly agree requeste late agamenon knowe desire neuer haue pea ne loue wyth grekes haue doon many dysplaysirs yf hit ye ben messangers shold make yow dye euyll deth therfore go ye way anone may see yow wyth oute displaysir myn herte began dyomedes lawghe despyte sayd thus ha kynge yf oute displaysir mayste see v ben tweyne thou shalt wythoute displaysir alle dayes thy lyf thou shalt see fro hensforth fore thyn eyen grete puissance grekes whiche shall come fore thy cyte shall cesse tassaylle hit contynuelly ayenst whome thou mayste longe deffende thou thyne finably shall receyue bytter deth therfore thou sholdest take counceyll thy werkes yf thou well auysed many troians wolde haue ronne vpon grekes drewe theyr swerdes haue slayn kynge pryant destourned hem sayd hem sholde late two fooles saye theyr folye hit nature fole shewe folye wyse man suffre hit ha syre sayd eneas ye saye men shold shewe foole folye truly yf h presence felawe hath spoken folyly fore yow shold receyue deth hande hit pperteyneth hym saye yow suche venymous wordes ne menace therfore auyse hym go way anone yf cesse speke folyly dyomedes thyng abasshyd answerd eneas sayd euer thou thou shewest well thy wordes thou arte right yll auysed hoot thy wordes desire may one fynde place couenable may rewarde wordes thou hast sayd see well kynge well ewrous happy haue suche counceller thou arte counceyllest hym vylonnye vlixes brack wordes dyomedes ryght wysely prayd hym holde pea saide kynge pryant haue vnderstand alle thou haste sayd shall goo reporte hit vnto prynces incontynent wente toke theyr horse retorned vnto theyr ooste fonde alle noble assemblyd fore kynge agamenon sayde answere kynge pryant wherof grete meruaylle deuysed longe gyder conduyte well theyr werkes syn ad certayned warre troians phow agamenon assemblyd counceyll grekes haue vitaylles sente achilles thelephus vnto royame se slewe kynge tentram bataylle telephus made kynge kynges cam ayde helpe kynge pryant thynges agamenon callid folk counceyll playne theneden sayd amonge alle thynges hit behoueth v necessaryly auysed duryng siege fore troye ooste shall socouryd vytayll therfore yf ye seme good shall sende vnto royame messe haue fro then vitaylles contynuelly hit contre right fertyle comodyous shall goo theder shall take sewerte contre shall fayll sende vitaill ooste longe shall contrey counceyll plesid moche grekes chese incontynent achilles thelephus sone hercules furnysshe message goo theder grete companye men armes prouynce regned kynge name theutram longe regned pee contre peplid good hardy knyghtes whan achilles thelephus thre thousand knyghtes fiers hardy arryued yle messe yssued oute theyr shippes descended lande ther cam ayenst kynge theutram grete companye men fote horse back began bataylle right fiersly assamble ther many knyghtes slayn bothe side well grekes lasse nombre deffended hem well theyr defence auayllyd ne ben grete prowesse achilles dide right meruayllys body stronge moste vayllyant grekes whome araug wente therfore ther myghte man endure fo hym whan achilles espyed kynge theutram myddes peple dide grete domage folke thressid grettest prees enemyes bete doun fore hym fonde vnto cam kynge theutram gaf hym many stroke hewe helme smote hym doun ground slayn hym contynent ne thelephus ha e ben whiche put hym betwene prayde achilles humbly wold slee hym ner harme kynge hym self cryed achilles mercy sayd achilles thelephus meueth pyte ayenst oure enemye mortall come assaylle v grete felonnye hit rayson falle pytte made redy v ha syre sayd thelephus kynge ryght famylier fader hercules also dyde tyme grete honour londe therfore may suffre see hym slayn fore myn eyen well sayd achylles take hym wyth hym thou wilte bataylle fynysshid grekes cessid kynge thentram born pallays dede achilles brussyd hym frusshid hym kynge prayd achilles thelephus wold goo wyth hym whiche wente receyuyd wyth grete ioye honour hit longe kynge thentram wounded deth woundes achilles gyuen hym sente achilles thelephus said hem frendes may longe lyue sayd thelephus frende may lenger lyue haue lawfull eyre body may leue royame haue goten wyth grete labour loste longe syn ne ben moste worthy alle worthy thy fader hercules whyche waranted shelde ayenst alle wolde haue taken hit fro dyde fayt wold haue taken hit whan thy fader grete prowesse slewe hem enchassed hem oute syn haue kepte hit paysybly thynge meryte vertue thy fader syn hyt soo thy fader hath conqueryd thys royame haue none eyre hit well right rayson thou herytier thy fader moche laste worde leue royame myn goodes euer bee make myn herityer praye thou burye honourably hit apperteyneth kynge sone finysshid wordes deyde thelephus noble contrey dide burye hym honourably leyde hym moche ryche sepulture wher vpon wreton epithaphye lieth kyng thentram achilles slewe whiche lefte royame thelephus thelephus afore duc made kynge messe noble contre dide hym homage peple promysed hym fayth seruyse achilles dide charge shippes wyth vytaill ordeynd thelephus shold abide newe royame whiche dide sore anoyed prayd hym also comanded name grekis shold diligence sende vnto ooste grekis often tymes vitayllis promysid hym doo wolde wythoute ony fawte achylles toke leue hym retorned shippes sayllyd longe felawship arryued poort thenedon sauely fonde ooste yet soiournyng anone descended wente strayt vnto tente kynge agamenon alle prynces kynges assemblid receyuyd wyth grete ioye alle ooste loued moche grete strengthe prowesse achilles tolde arryued messe batayll thelephus made kynge promysid furnysshe ooste vitaylles tidynges grekes grete ioye alowed preysid moche vaylliance achilles theyr parlament eche man wente vnto pauyllon achilles receyuyd grete ioye myrondynes moche louyd hym place auctour nameth kynges prynces cam helpe ayde kynge pryant troye alle moste notable fyrst cam vnto ayde kynge pandorus kynge galior kynge adrastus thre thousand knyghtes armed fro prouynce tholoson cam foure kynges wyth fyue thousand knyghtes armed kynge carras kynge amasius kynge nestor moche stronge man kynge amphymacus fro royame licye cam kynge glauton wyth thre thousand knyghtes sone sarpedon one strengest knyghtis world cosyn kynge pryant fro royame lichaon cam kynge ensemus thre thousand knyghtes ryght expert armes fro royame larysse cam two kynges wyth fyften honderd knyghtes kynge imstor moche grete man kynge capidus fro royame thaborye cam kynge remus thre thousand knyghtes companye cam foure duke seuen erles feyd kynge pryant bare armes colour asure oute signe therby kynge remus peple knowen bataylle fro royame trachie cam kynge pilex duc alchamas xi honderd knyghtis fro royame pauonye cam kynge pessemus duc stupex cosyn wyth thre thousand knyghtes right expert iouste shote wyth bowe moche wylde contre forestes montaygnes lityll peple ynowhe wylde bestes byrdes fro prouynce boecye cam thre duke twelue honderd knyghtes duc ansermms duc fortunus duc sammus fro royame burtyn growe good espices cam two kynges brethern thousand knyghtes kynge bo te kynge episteus fro regne paphagore sonne rysyng eeste full alle riches cam right riche kynge philemeus thre thousand kngyhtes sheldes hydes fysshis couerd gold precyous stone kynge grete geant fro regne ethiope cam kynge perseus kynge thiction hym right hardy wyse thre thousand kngyhtes companye many duc many erle also wyth hem simagon sone kynge thiction fro royame cheres cam kynge theleus archilogus sone affinyte kynge pryant brought thousand knyghtes fro yle argreste cam two kynges haue name wyth xii honderd knyghtes fro regne eliane beyonde royame amasonne cam auncyent kynge ryght wyse discrete named epistropus brought thousand knyghtes meruayllous beste tht callyd sagittayre behynde myddes hors fore man beste heery lyke hors eyen reed coole shotte right well abowe beste made grekes sore aferd slewe many hem wyth bowe thus nombre alle knyghtes cam ayde kynge pryant two thertty thousand wyth oute royame uroye ynde myneur hit founde wrytyng syn creacion world many noble knyghtes assemblid one place meuyd quarelle lityll occasion kynges prynces oughte take hede well auysed meue warre also ferre myght amende hit waye comyng duc palamydes grekes departed fro porte thenadon counceyll dyomedes cam toke lande stronge cyte troye troians receyuyd batayll right vigorously grekes yet partyd fro thenedon whan palamides sone kynge naulus cam arriued porte thenedon thretty shippis full knyghtes armed alle noble hardy men comyng grekes grete ioye murmured fore cause taryed longe wherof excusid hym sekenes palamides holden grete worshippe amonge grekes seconde kynge agamenon puyssant discrete armes moche riche comyng anone chosyn counceyllour ooste thus grekes many day many nyght porte thenedon often tymes assemblid counceyll aduyse beste manere assege cyte troye finably many oppynyons helde hem counceyll dyomedes said alle ye kynges prynces baron ben assemblid ought alle haue grete shame vilonye whan hit yere goon syn descended londe haue yet ben fore troye verayly haue gyuen oure enemyes grete auantage syn hit soo tyme duryng ben pourueyed grete aydes alle cyte strongly fortefyed renforced wally bulwerkis haue good leyzer make verrayly semeth ben hardy come vnto therfore delaye v goo theder encreseth oure shame domage trowe yf goon theder whan cam first contre shold haue esely descended taken lande shall doo ben better garnysshid tyme alle suche thyng behoeffyd deffende hem therfore counceylle yow morn tymes putte v waye good ordenance late v sette siege fermly hastely may oughte well knowe shall doo wyth oute grete bataylle fore hit behoueth eche man employe hymself putte behynde alle fere drede none waye may exployte werke ne better ne honourably myn aduys etc counceyll dyomedes plesid alle baron ooste also morn erly reentryd theyr shippis sayllyd strayt vnto poort troye brought theyr shippes good ordenance one another first fronte putte honderd shippis right well garnysshid knyghtes banyers wauyd wynde putte honderd alle ordre ferre sayllyd sawe noble cyte troye approchid therto hastely myghte whan troians sawe grekes approche cyte ran armes mounted vpon theyr horse alle armed wente forth wyth oute ordenance vnto porte whan grekes sawe troians come grete nombre deffende theyr porte ther none hardy ferde moche coude descende land force armes armed hem incontynent contended descende take lande force etc fyrst honderd shippis chief captayn kynge prothesalaus philarde dyde grete payne diligence brynge shippis wythin porte wynde stronge blewe hem porte strongly ayenst ryuage many brake brussyd many grekes drownyd myght take lande toke hit anone slayn troians wyth grete torment grete nombre grounde reed theyr blood hyt mynde ony man euer ony nauye wan land wyth grete myschef dyde nauye grekes first honderd shippes cam arryued folowed hem wyth garnysshyd grete arblasters shotte slewe many troians constrayned go back toke grekes lande couryd firste foughte grete myschief began bataylle mortall kynge protheselaus descended wyth firste dyde right meruaylles wyth body slewe day troians wyth oute nombre yf allone ben alle grekes descended lande ben slayn myght deffence helpe whan seuen thousand grekes faughte ayenst honderd thousand troians saye yow grete danger wher felte hem self solde theyr lyues dere abidyng socours kynge archela kynge prothenor anon arryued wolde troians descended toke londe socourid theyr peple vayllyantly began agayn cruell bataylle etc arryued duc nestor folk threstid amonge enemyes right fiersly ther many spere broken many arowe shotte knyghtes fyll doun dede bothe side crye grete hit meruayllous heere slewe many troians archelaus prothenor arryuyd kynge ascalus kynge agalus wyth theyr shippis descended lande assayllid troians grete fiersnes force made hem recule go back cam bataylle grete foyson newe troians began bataylle grete hit ben alle daye fore moche grekes reculed force vnto theyr shippis arryuyd vlixes wyth grete companye knyghtes threstyd anone bataylle grekes recoueryd lande theyr comyng assayllyd troians made vlixes grete effusion blood enemyes anone ensigne knowen amonge whan kynge philomenus sawe vlixes slewe theyr peple adressid hym vnto hym bete hym doun horse lityll wounded vlixes smote hym agayn harde gaf hym grete wounde vpon throte cutte two orygynall vayne smote hym half dede troians ran toke hym fro grekes bare hym vpon shelde cyte ne aduenture kynge grekes ben disconfited troians entended strongly saue hym arryued kynge thoas kynge agamenon kynge menelaus kynge thelamon ayax wyth theyr power descended lande medlid hem batayll brack theyr speres vpon troians bete doun many dede hurte ioynyng many troians slayn whan kynge prothesalus departid fro bataylle ben syn begynnyng take breth whan cam porte fonde alle men nyghe dede whome wepte pytye toke agayn corage auenge deth men wente agayn bataylle grete yre slewe many troians wounded hem smote doun many theyr horse cam bataylle partye troians kynge perses wyth grete companye knyghtes comyng ethyopyens began bataylle mortall many grekes slayn force made hem goo back oute fayll disconfited ne worthy palamydes sone descended lande comyng grekes recomforted also palamydes made right meruayllys wyth hand addressid hym ayenst sagamon broder kynge menon neuewe kynge perse sore greuyd grekes smote hym sore wyth spere pershid hym thurgh oute body smote hym ded doun erthe smote grete presse bete doun alle mette eche man knewe hym made hym waye roose crye vpon troians myght suffre strengthe palamydes reculed force ben alle desconfited moste worthy alle worthy hector whan herd crye vpon peple yssued oute cyte wyth grete companye knyghtes entryd bataylle armed ryche armes bare shelde golde lione gowles strengthe anone knowen amonge grekes encountryd mette comyng kynge prothesalaus alle day cessid sle troians smote hym wyth swerd grete myght vpon helme clefte hym vnto nombryll notwythstandyng armour fyll doun dede erthe hector threstid grettest prees many grekes araught wyth swerde slewe eche man fledde fro hym makyng hym waye demaunded grekes one another greuyd hem anon knewe hit hector moste stronge man world none hardy durst abyde strook hit happend hector wente oute lityll refresshe hym grekes reprised corage vp troians happend day eyghte ten tymes hit aboute oure euensonge tyme hector departid fro batayll reentrid cyte grekes wyth disconfited arryued right stronge achilles wyth myrondones entryd anon batayll well wyth thre thousand good knyghtes wyth hym troians alle sydes beten doun slayn ayenst achilles endured man beten doun erthe sore hurte arryued nauye grekes knyghtes go lande medlid batayll wherfore troians moche suffre ferre muste nedes flee theyr cyte achilles slewe fleeyng grete crye hurte men ther achilles alle dyed wyth blood troians slayn grete occision entre cyte sawe faders child slayn fore eyen occysion slaughter ben grete ne yf troylus parys deyphebus grete companye fyerse newe ne comen oute yssued cyte resisted grekes made thoccision cesse also nyght nyghe eche man wyth drewe hym place troians shytted cyte dyde make good wacche achilles wyth grekis retorned theyr tentes wyth grete glorye yet dressyd kynge agamenon dyde dresse hem incontynent made eche man take place couenable astate tentes ne pauyllons loggyd vnder leues beste wyse coude theyr horse ankryd theyr shippis well myght toke oute alle necessarye thus made grekes theyr siege nyght sette hit fore cyte troye made meruayllous grete fyres ooste made hit light hit day logged nyghe gyder made ryght good wacche well none assaultes nyght alle nyght trompettis menestrellys grete plente agamenon ordeyned conforte ooste restid nyght alle armed beste wyse coude fyrst bataylle grekes troians theyr comyng etc pof seconde bataylle fore troye whiche many kynges grete baron slayn worthy hector troians ben victoryous theyr enemyes ne ben prayer thelamon ayax cosyn hector etc whan nyght passid hector charge alle cyte ordeyned right erly batailles grete playn cyte putte fyrst bataylle two thousand good knyghtes whiche betoke lede conduyte tweyn kynnysmen wete glaucon sone kynge keye afiamolor bastard broder assigned kynge thesus trahie archilogus broder wyse vay liant made hem yssue gate named da dane stode ayenst oost grekes seconde batayll put thre thousand good knyghtes stronge toke conduyte kynge exampitus frigie kynge alcanus knyghtes grete strengthe recomanded garde goddes made yssue good ordenance thirde batayll toke troyllus broder coduyte thre thousand knightes wise hardy said hym departyng right dere broder leysse herte putteth doubte thy gret hardynes wherfore pray thou gouerne wysely batayll suche wyse thou enterpryse suche thynges thou maiste achieue tht thou put thy body dauger deth ouer moche wenyng wherby thou myghtest gyue ioye thyn enemyes owres go thy waye name goddes tht conduyte kepe fro paryll encombrance ha syre broder answerd troylus hit nedeth yow doubte shall doo tht right ye haue comanded wente forth companye bare shelde thre lyon golde hector put fourthe bataill thre thousand knyghtes seuen honderd toke conduyte kynge huppon larisse kynge huppon moste stronge troians next hector companye vailliant knyght bastard broder hector wise hardy named dyma cu v bataill hector deliuerid conduyte kynge cisayne folk meruayllous stronge grete geantis kyng bare shelde asure ony difference hector comisid batayll polidamas bastard broder kyng yssued sixte bataylle ledde kynge precemessus peple well induced shote drawe boowe wente wyth oute armes bataylle mounted vpon good light horse hector comysid deyphebus broder conduyte yssued bataylle adiousted hector alle cheuallerye royame agreste vnder conduyte kynge esdras kynge philon kynge philon meruayllous chare alle yuorye gold siluer precyous stone chare conduyted two stronge knyghtes wyth thyse two kynges hector put epitagoren bastard broder yssued seuenth batayll ladde eneas noble admyrall named enfrene wente eyghte bataylle ladde kynge perse named perses parys chief captayne hector prayd parys broder shold assemble vnto grekes vnto tyme cam hym self wolde folowe hym anone nyneth batayll laste ladde hector hym self ten bastarde brethern hym alle beste knyghtes cyte chosen bataylle nombre fyue thousand etc whan hector rychely ar yed armed good harnoys scewre mou ted vpon horse named galathe one moste grete strengest horse world armed mounted rood vnto kynge fader sayd hym ryght dere fader reteyne yow thousand fyue honderd knyghtis alle men foote cyte holde yow wythoute fore syght grekes meue yow yf sende yow worde ende yf haue necessite ye oure reffuge shall sende yow alle way amonge messangers shall saye yow state bataylle take ye good heede garde oure enemyes take cyte cautele trayson kynge answerd hym sone shall doo alle thou haste sayd next ayde helpe goddes thou arte alle hope truste haue fayth vertue thyn armes grete discrescion thy wytte praye goddes ryght humbly wylle kepe hoole sounde preserue fro encombrance wordes hector wente hym forth hector moche coragyous stronge victoryous batayll right wyse conduytour men armes shelde alle gold myddell lyon gowles well laste yssued hous cyte yet passid allewaye alle bataylles cam putte hym self afore fyrst bataylle woman cyte alle wente vpon wally beholde batayles th doughters kynge wyth qu ne hel yne grete doubte dyuerce ymagynacyons self whylis hector ordeyned bataylles kynge agamenon ydle ordeyned ryght erly peple sixe twenty bataylles putte fyrst bataylle patroclus wyth hys peple wyth folk achylles whiche day batayll woundes dyde hele hem tente patroclus moche noble due ryche louyd moche achylles bothe one alyance seconde bataylle kynge men kynge ydumeus thre thousand knyghtes ther hem due atthenes wyth alle peple thirde bataylle ledde kynge achalaphus sone phimenus wyth peple fourth bataylle ladde kynge archelaus kynge prothenor broder securidam right stronge knyght peple boecye fyfthe batayll ladde kynge menelaus wyth alle peple sperte sixthe bataylle ladde kynge epistropus kynge celidus wyth alle peple seuenth batayll ladde thelamon ayax wyth alle peple salamyne foure erlis hym wete thesus amphymacus dorius polidarius eyghte ledde kynge thoas nynthe ledde ayax aleus tenthe ladde kynge philotus enleuenth kyng ydumeus kynge meron twelfth duc nestor thrittenth lad kynge exiones fourt nth kyng vlixes fyftenth kyng humerus sixtenth folke prothesclaus moche desiryng auenge deth theyr lord seuententh ladde kynge polidarius kynge machaon eyghtenth kynge rodes nynetenth yng sampitus kynge lidorus twentythe kynge ger pulus one twentythe kyng philotetes larisse two twentyth dyomedes thre twentythe kynge oeneus cypre foure twentythe kynge prothalus fyfe twentythe kynge carpenor sixe twentythe last bataylle ladd kynge agamenon emperour alle ooste whan alle bataylles ordeyned one side thyng tassemble auauncyd hym hector alle ther fyrst patroclus cam ayenst hym moche horse myghte renne smote hym strongly wyth spere shelde perchid hit thurgh harme dyde hector assayllid patroclus wyth swerde gaf hym grete strook vpon heed clefte hit two peces patroclus fyll doun dede ground whan hector sawe hym ded coueyted armes ryght queynte ryche lightid doun horse take kynge menon cam vpon hym wyth thre thousand good knyghtes deffende kynge patroclus ayenst hector sayd hym thus ha wolf rauysshyng insacyable certes behoueth seke thy praye place geteste thou none assayllyd hym alle side wolde haue taken fro hym galathee hors hector prowesse remounted wolde wende haue vengid hym kynge menon kynge glancion kynge thesus archilogus sone cam wyth thre thousand fightars hector leyd bete doun alle afore hym fyrst mette gaf grete stroke slewe hym hym many mo bete doun slewe thus began bataylle bothe side hector cam agayn body patroclus haue armes kyng ydumeus crete cam ayenst hym two thousand fyghtars kynge menon allway eye hector letted hym waye hector myght haue armes sore desired suffryd grete payne moche foote enforced hym wyth alle corage began slee man hors smyte heedes legges foot armes slewe fyften strengest assayllyd hym mene kyng menon toke body patroclus fore hym bare hit vnto tente grekes contended greue hector take away horse ther amonge right stronge knyght named creon de la plerre greuyd hym moste one seruauntis hector adressid hym agayn creon gaf hym grete stroke wyth spere smote hym doun dede erthe smote doun another escryed troians right lowde shold come socoure hector wyth cry cam first securabor one bastard brethern hector threstid grettest prees ferre cam vpon greuyd hector slayn moo thretty dide moche force made grekes recule hector remounted vpon horse threstid amonge grete fierste slewe grete plente desplaysir might haue armes patroclus recountryd none slewe hym bete hym doun hurte eche man made hym waye dredde hym etc cam bataylle menesteus duc atthenes cam ioyned hym bataylle troyllus dyde meruaylles hym kynge sampitus kynge machaon kynge alcanus tho began fyerse bataylles menesteus adressid hym ayenst troyllus faught ayenst hym grete force bete hym doun horse grete prees folke menesteus contended wyth alle strength moche toke hym lad hym toward theyr tentes wyth grete companye knyghtes imseres troye escryed troians troyllus prysonner shold dishonoured yf suffred hym ledd away kynge alcanus toke spere right stronge adressid hym vnto hem helde troyllus smote first doun dede erthe smote another sore wounded hym dide moche ayde men troyllus rescowed sette agayn vpon hors also helpe kynge sampitus cam alle peple gaf grete strook menesteus ouerthwart yf well armed ben slayn escryed menesteus peple began amonge mortall bataylle many slayn one side amonge thynges menesteus sory loste prysonner recountryd miseres whome loste hym anone knewe hym adressid hym hym bete hym doun tyme smote doun another knyght tham cam batayll hupon hiripisus two thousand fightars ayenst cam menelaus prothenor wyth theyr folke began mortall medle etc anone cam polidamas sone anthenor wyth grete companye threstid side amonge enemyes cam kynge remus fro troye wyth thre thousand fightars ayenst cam menelaus wyth alle peple saide menelaus adressid hym ayenst kynge remus iusted gyder smote eche ground adressid hym polidamas remus agaynst neuewe helayne yong man twenty yere olde remus gaf hym grete strook wyth spere smote hym doun dede erthe wheerof menelaus grete sorowe louyd hym moche grete yre gaf grete stroke remus wyth swerde smote hym doun dede whan kynge remus beten doun men wende ben dede wold haue fledde ne ben polidamas retayned hem wyth grete payne dide moche toke theyr kynge h rte bare hym home saefte kynge celidus moste fayr kynge world adressid hym polidamas smote hym wyth spere coude remeue hym polidamas gaf hym grete stroke wyth swerde smote hym doun dede erthe amonge thyngis hector wente cam fowlyng sleyng enemyes made waye fore hym sleyng knyghtes betyng doun ferre cam vpon salamyne kynge thelamon conduyted slewe many troians bete doun prowesse kynge thenter gaf grete stroke spere hector made hym depe wounde hector grete yre encountrid admyrall grekes slewe hym cruelly swerd hector closid enemyes party grekes kynge thesus sayd hector warned hym shold go oute bataylle sayd hit domage alle world lese suche knyght hector thankid hym right courtoisly menelaus thelamon assayllid polidamas thelamon adressid hym first smote hym spere gaf hym many stroke moche brake laas helme toke hym lad hym away ne hector haue whiche ferre smote amonge helde hym slewe hurte many dide moche vaylliance tht slewe thretty fledde lefte polidamas hym ther putte hem gyder kynge epistropus kynge menelaus kynge thelamon alle peple smote amonge troians grete fierste made hem go back maulgre notwythstandyng grete prowesse hector wyth dyde meruayllys sone good hors galathe slayn vnder hym deffended hym foote meruaillously ther none hardy grekes tht durste approche hym whan krethern knewe right grete dauger tht ran parte tho thelamon sore hurte dinadorus one bastard brethern hector gaf grete stroke polixenus noble man slewe hym bete hym doun grete strong hors whervpon satte toke stede hector mounted vpon hym contynent meruaylles armes done bastardis cam deyphebus wyth alle ooste grete foyson archer hurted slewe grete foyson grekes deyphebus made gaf kynge thenter grete wounde visage tho began batayll also mortall hit ben malle day thesus assayllyd quyntelynus one bastard brethern hector kynge moderus taken lad away hector delyueryd hym alle quyte courtosye done hym lytyll fore cam bataylle partye grekes kynge tho kynge phylota kynge thoas adressid hym ayenst cassilanus one bastard brethern hector gaf hym grete stroke slewe hym doun erthe seeyng hector whiche smote angerly amonge grekes anone slewe many put hem alle flight cam bataylle nestor wyth sixe thousand knyghtes kynge esdras kynge phylon dide grete meruaylles armes cam ayenst hem assemble ther many knyghtes slayn beten doun one partye kynge philon dide right meruaylles armes enclosid wyth grekes alle side slayn yf iecomas kynge esdras fader ne deliueryd hym fro theyr handes hector broder dyde meruaylles polidamas put grekes f ght menelaus thelamon resisted strongly cam eneas bataylle alle oost putte hym inne wyth hector force put grekes playn flight wherof ayax moche grete sorowe also behelde behynde hym sawe banyers cam batayll yet haue ben alle floure cheualerye grece prayd h fledde wolde abide recomence begynne newe bataylle ayax eneas entrecountred harde fylle bothe erthe cam philotras wyth thre thousand knyghtes made troians goo backe smote hector spere might remeue hym hector gaf hym
