grete stroke swerde bete hym sore hurte cam batayll kynge humerus kynge vlixes wyth alle theyr peple kyng hamelius well ooste ten thousand knyghtes whiche dide troians moche sorowe moche wery theyr socours cam parys batayll comyng smote harde kynge frigie cosyn vlixes slewe hym bete hym doun wherof grekes moche sorowe vlixes supposid haue smyten parys wyth spere smote horse slewe hym parys fyll erthe troyllus gaf vlixes grete stroke wounded hym visage made blood sprynge oute lyke wyn kenneth tonne etc vlixes hurted hym agayn truly troians fledde ne ben grete prowesse hector brethern hector ne cessid put hym self grettest prees eche man knewe hym made hym waye whan sawe peple myght suffre grete strengthe grekes wythdrew side tolde iniuryes grekes hem wolde yf cam theyr aboue amonested warned hem well brought hem avaleye right side assaylle theyr enemyes grete occision grekes ther kynge thoas assayllid bastard brethern hector auenge deth cassibelanus theyr broder slayn bete hym doun horse rasyd helme fro hede slayn hym incontynent yf duc atthenes come threstid amonge hem gaf grete stroke one bastardis quyntylynus fyll doun ground sore hurte parys smote duc wyth arowe side made hym grete wounde duc sore hurte sette therby magre alle deliueryd kynge thoas fro theyr handes hector dyde grete payne put grekes vnto flighte kynge humerus shotte arowe vnto hector hurted hym visage hector ran vpon hym grete yre smote hym sore vpon hede clefte hit vnto teeth fyll doun dede blowyng horn cam seuen thousand grekis tassaylle hector defended hym ayenst meruayllously wente litill fader toke thre thousand knyghtes freshe fiers brought hem bataylle theyr comyng made grete occision grekes etc ayax hector iusted geder fought eche wyth menelaus slewe ioynyng admyrall troye celidones slewe mole oreb neuewe kynge thoas mandon smote oute eye kynge cedonyus sadellus slewe admyrall grekes thelamon bete margareton sore wounded hym famuell bete kynge prothenor erthe kynge gaull iusted ayenst menesteus menesteus hurte hym nose swerde deanor seeyng broder hurte adressid hym menesteus smote hym doun erthe ran vpon hym thre brethern wold haue slayn hym taken hym deffended hym vaylliantly anone socourid kynge thenter hector assailled hem bothe oute faulte escaped hym ne ayax stronge knyght haue comen rescows thousand knyghtes companye tho cam kynge perse fyue thousand knyghtes parys ladde dide alle troians made grekes recule goo back force dare writeth book hector slewe thousand knyghtes assaulte amonge alle thynges hector encountryd kyng menon fore tente said hym ha euyl traytre oure comen tht thou shalt receyue thy reward thou restournest take armes patroclus smote hym grete strook fyll doun ground hector alightid doun smote heed wolde haue taken armes hym menesteus letted hym smote vpon hector ouerthwart suche force tht gaf hym grete wounde wente way oute taryyng doubtyng fureur hector hector wente oute stowre dyde bynde wounde hit bledde wente agayn stoure slewe comyng many grekes dare sayth bounden wounde slewe daye thousand knyghtes ther none corage auenge hym ayenste hym deffende putte hem alle flight troians entryd theyr tentes pyllid robbed toke beste cowde fynde etc day troians vittorye alle grekes yf fortune dyuerse wylle consentyd myght haue slayn hem alle eschewyd grete euyllys cam certes hit wysedom whan ony man fyndeth enemye grete perylle fortune offre power deliuere hym therof hit happeth ofte tymes shall neuer recouere haue enemye caas fortune torne backe thus hit happend day vnhappy hector aboue enemyes myght haue slayn hem alle yf wolde soughte thynge flee whan grete mysaventure cam afore hym encountre thelamon ayax sone kynge thelamon exione cosyn germayn hector brethern whiche wyse vayllyant whiche adressid hym ayenst hector deliueryd hym grete assault hector hym valyant bothe two fightyng spak geder therby hector knewe cosyn germaine sone aunte hector curtoisye enbraced hym armes made hym grete chiere offryd hym playsir yf desired ony thynge hym prayd hym wolde come troye hym see lignage hys moder syde sayd thelamon entended thynge auantage sayde wolde goo thys tyme prayd hector sayng yf louyd hym moche sayde wolde sake instance cesse bataill day troians shold leue grekes pee vnhappy hector accorded hym requeste blewe horn made alle peple withdrawe cyte troians begonne putte fyre shippes grekes alle brente hem ne hector callyd fro then wherof troians sory rapeell cause wherfore troians lost haue victorye whiche myght neuer atteyne ne come fortune contrarye therfore virgile sayth non est misericordia bello saye ther mercy bataill man ought take misericorde take victorye may gete hit pof first triews two monethis demanded grekes thirde batayll betwene whiche hector bare achilles grounde twyes slewe kyng prothenor smote hym one stroke two party hit cam morn betymes troians armed goo assayll grekes grekes sente tymes kynge pryant demanded triews two monethes agreed said triews dede bodyes gaderid well partye buryed brente achilles sorowfull deth patroclus coude wyse confortyd made body buryed moche riche sepulture dyde kynge prothes laus kynges pryn e slayn hurte wounded dide helid duryng trews pryant kynge dide burye bastard sone cassibelanus ryght honourably temple venus toke grete sorow deth dyde alle etc whan cassandra herde doell sorow troians made deth theyr frendes escried sayd meshaut troians make sorow self lyke wise shall hit happen come yow frendes shall deth ala ne seche ye pee grekes fore er euyllys come yow er noble cyte destroied ala ne yelde agayn helayne kynge fader dyde rauysshe force wherfore ye shall alle destroyed amonge al thinges palamides murmured strongli seignourye agamenon sayng worthy haue grete domynacion aboue alle hym self worthy haue seignourye ooste agamenon g e consente prince onely thre foure tht tyme ther thyng proceded whan trews faylled kynge agamenon charge alle ooste ordeyned ryght erly hys bataylles gaf fyrst achylles seconde dyomedes thirde menelaus fourth menesteus duc athene alle ordeyned good captayns conduytours hector ordeyned batayllys lyke wyse sette fyrst troyllus alle sette good captayns hardy made alle batayllis yssue sette hym self fronte fore whan achylles sawe hym ran ayenst hym hector ayenste hym smote eche erthe ryght sore hector remounted fyrst lefte achylles lyynge erthe smote amonge moste grettest prees raught knyght slewe hym bete hym doun wente tourgh oute bataylle made reed blood slayn whan achilles remountid threstid amonge troians grettest prees slewe many wente ferre encountrid hector agayn ran hym hector hym achilles born doun grounde hector wolde haue taken hors myght grete socours achilles whan remounted assaylled hector swerd gaf grete stroke hector nyhe beten hym hector gaf hym grete stroke vpon helme enfoundrid hym made blood sprynge heed thus bataill mortall two knyghtes yf ben departid one slayn theyr peple departid cam dyomedes batayll troillus syde whiche smote eche erthe dyomedes remounted fyrste assayllyd troylus foote deffended hym vayllyantly slewe hors dyomedes theyr men remounted bothe two force began agayn medle dyomedes taken ladde away troyllus yf troians hadd put hem paryll deth rescowe hym many slayn cam bataylle menelaus grekes side parys side goyng comyng hector cessid slee bete doun knyghtes ther newe knyght named bretes assayllyd hym fiersly hector ryght grete yre smote hym vpon helme grete stroke clefte heed vnto nombryll fyll doun dede seeyng kynge archylogus cosyn hector wold haue taken hors kynge archylogus deffended hym moche myghte hector ran vpon hym smote hym harde smote body two peces notwythstandyng harnoys kynge prothenor adressid hym hector toke garde ne hede smote hym doun erthe hector remounted anone vpon horse gaf kynge prothenor grete stroke myght clefte bodye two halues seeyng achilles paret cosyn grete sorowe kynge archelaus contended auenge deth troians cam vpon grete strength grekes muste nedes flee troians folowed hem vnto tentes nyght cam made hem departe troians retorned cyte phow grekes helde parlament myght slee worthy hector retourned fourthe bataylle whiche parys menelaus encountryd kynge thoas brought prysoner troye bataylle whan nyght come alle kynges prynces baron grekes assemblid tente kynge agamenon helde theyr parlament myghte slee hector sayde well longe lyue cam batayll ayenst myght neuer vaynquysshe troians sholde doo grete domaige brynge thynge ende requyred achilles wold take hit vpon hym well strenght wisedom achylles enterprysed gladly wi te hector desired deth deth ony also hector myght sonnest lose lyf counceyll wente reste tyll morn tymes armed hem hector yssued oute cyte wyth bataylles well diligently ordeyned hym self fore alle fyrste bataylle hym eneas parys deyphebus hym troyllus hym folowyng eche ordre ioyned alle troians geder honderd thousande fyghtyng men tho began bataylle horryble mortall parys wyth perce good knyghtes slewe shotte many grekis hurted hector encountrid kynge agamenon bete hym wounded hym sore achilles assayllyd hector gaf hym many stroke brake helme eneas troyllus cam rescows hector dyom cam vpon adressid hym eneas bete hym sayd hym mocquerye ha good counceller gauyst counceyll thy kynge offende greue knowe thou trouthe yf thou come ofte bataylles may mete thou shalt escape oute deth amonge thynges hector assaylled achilles gaf hym many stroke russhid brake helme wende haue taken hym sone guideus ran vpon hector gaf hym grete strok wyth swerd hurted hym sore hector yre recountryd dyomedes gaf hym grete stroke bete hym doun grounde troyllus alightyd descended doun fygh e dyomedes foote dyomedes deffended hym vayllyantly hit uaylle beside fought gyder hector achilles cam medlee kynges prynces grece wyth grete companye men armes fro partye troians cam alle baron comen theyr ayde began meruayllously bataylle kynge agamenon kynge pandelus fought geder kyng men laus recountrid parys knewe eche well menelaus smote hym harde wyth spere made hym grete wounde smote hym doun wherof parys alle shamed vlixes bete kynge arastous toke horse good sente hit tente polimytes ayllyd huppon auncyent slewe hym kynge archilogus fought geder polidamas bete palamydes wounded hym sore mocqued hym reproche kynge scelenus kynge carras encountrid geder carras sore beten wounded philemenus bete anthenor philoteas kynge remus fought geder kynge thesus kynge eryalus fought geder bothe sore hurte bastardes kynge pryant dyde meruaylles slewe many grekes hurte many kynges kynge thelamon kynge sarpedon iusted sore one ayenste fylle bothe sore hurte alle astonyed angwysshe kynge thoas achilles cosyns assaylleden hector gaf hym many stroke drewe helme fro hede hurted hym many place hector gaf hym grete strook swerd tht cutte half nose rescows hector cam bastard brethern slewe many grekes toke kynge thoas wounded bete kynge agamenon suche wise born tentes dede kyng thoas ladde prisonner troye menelaus contended greue parys parys shotte hym arowe enuenymed wounded hym suche wise tht born tente sone menelaus bouden wounde cam agayn batayll greue parys yf fouden hym fonde hym assayllid hym eneas put hym self betwene hem bothe moche parys vnarmed auente hym eneas lad hym cyte ende menelaus shold slee hym hector assayllyd menelaus wende haue taken hym ther cam rescows grete plente chyualrye grekes wherfore hector myght come entente threstid smote amonge dide moche helpe folke grekes fledde nyght cam made batayll cesse phow pryant wolde kynge thoas prisoner shold haue ben hanged retorned fyfthe bataylle whiche hector slewe wi h hand thre kynges dyomedes slewe sagittarye etc whan hit cam morn tymes kynge pryant wold shold fight day sente counceyll wete hector parys troylus deyphebus eneas anthenor polidamas sayd ye knowe holde prisoner kynge thoas wyth oute cause haue deseruyd come destroye v therfore thynketh good make hym dye euyll deth saye ye therto ha sire sayde eneas god forbede noblesse shold suche vilonye syn hit kynge thoas one noble kynges grece myght happe grekes myght take one oures whome myght doo semblable wyse wherof ye myght take grettest sorowe world hit better thynketh ye kepe ryght well kynge thoas wyth oute mysdoynge hym yf fortune one oures taken myghte make change take one counceyll semed good hector kynge pryant sayd yet yf ye thus hit shall seme grekes doubte v dare put theyr folk deth notwithstandyng shall doo counceyll counceyll fynysshid eneas toke troyllus anthenor wente see helayne whome fonde grete halle ylion wyth quene hecuba many noble ladyes made grete sorowe supposid haue conforted dyde quene hecuba sayde shold take thoughte ne sorowe cyte shold well deffende amonge thynges grekes complayned hem sore deth theyr frendes troians slewe thus helde hem self chyldren put hem suche dauger wherof well passid ben deliueryd yf good counceyll yet hit happend nyght ther cam grete wynde grete rayne tentes ware alle torned vp doun erthe semed world shold haue ended grete storme wherof sorowe doublid whan hit cam morenyng whan tempeste passyd armed hem alle thurgh oute ooste wente hem ayenst troians tho yssued batayll achilles adressid hym first huppon grete geant kynge larrysse smote hym sore wyth spere breste slewe hym bare hym doun erthe hector slewe comyng kynge athomeus dyomedes slewe kynge antipus kynge epistropus kynge cedus assaylleden hector epistropus iusted ayenst hector brak spere vpon hym said hym many vilayns wordes wherof hector angry grete yre gaf hym grete strook tht slewe hym sayd hym sholde goo saye vilaynous wordes dede suche wonte saye lyuyng men cedeus passyng sorowfull deth broder amonestid thousand knyghtis slee hector assayllyd hym anone bete hym hors cryed kynge cedeus sle hector whan hector apperceyuyd tht gaf hym grete strook cutte arme wherof fyll angwyssh felte anone hector slewe hym eneas slewe medlee kynge amphymacus ther wente gyder alle puyssant grekes assaylled troians slewe many wente grete force tht put troians chasse whiche achilles slewe kynge philis wherof hector grete sorowe yre slewe kynge dalpmee kynge doreus thus puyssance hector troians recouerd felde slewe many grekes etc yssued oute troye kynge epistropus thre thousand knyghtes foureyed threstyd amonge grekes reculed theyr comyng moche brought wyth hym sagittarye afore made mencion sagittarye armed bare stronge bowe turquoys full arowes shotte strongly whan knyghtes grekes sawe meruayllous beste wyll goo forth afore began wythholde hem wente aback amonge thynges hector slewe polixenes noble due fought sore ayenst hym strenghte troians horrour sagittarye grekes reculyd vnto theyr tentes hyt happend dyomedes fore one tentes assayllyd sagittarye beste fore hym troians back behoued hym shewe puyssance sagittarye tho shotte arowe hym dyomedes well assewryd auaunfid hym nyghe vnto hym gaf hym grete stroke wyth swerde whiche armed slewe hym tyme hit paste myddaye grekes recoueryd felde made troians flee entrecountryd hector achylles wyth force theyr speres faught bothe two fylle bothe erthe achilles fyrst remounted supposid haue ladde awaye galathe good horse hector hector escryed hys folke sholde suffre hym lede hym awaye ran vpon achilles dyde moche rescowed galathe rendryd hym hector right glad hym medle anthenor taken sente tentes notwit standyng polidamas sone dyde meruaylles armes resscowe hym myght thus faught grete domage one partye vnto nyght departed hem pof trewes betwene hem whiche began bataylle agayn fro morn euyn wyth grete domage one partye troyans loste grekes morn betymes grekes sente diomedes vlixes vnto kynge pryant haue tryews thre monthes kynge pryant assemblid counceyll vpon thynge eche man agreed saue hector sayde grekes fayned wylle burye theyr dede bodyes cawtele lackyd vytaylle therfore requyred tryews ende duryng tyme pourueye vytayll dayly waste owres wherof may sone haue scarcete hit wolde abide onely entente ayenst tho ppynyon many wyse men agreed triews accorded thre monethes triewes duryng kynge tho deliueryd stede anthenor held prisoner sente troians calcas comandement appolyn lefte troians passing fayr doughter wyse named breseyda chaucer booke made troylus named creseyda whiche doughter prayd kynge agamenon prynces wolde requyre kynge pryant sende breseyda hym prayde ynow kynge pryant instance calcas troians blamed sore calcas callid hym euyll fals traytre worthy dye lefte hys owne lande naturell lord goo companye mortall enemyes alleway petycion grekes kynge pryant sente breseyda fader triews duryng hector wente hym day vnto tentes grekes achylles behelde hym gladly moche neuer seen hym vnarme requeste achylles hector wente hys tente spack totgeder many thynge achylles sayde hector haue grete playsir see vnarmed moche neuer seen fore yet shall haue playsir whan day shall come thou shalt dye hande whyche thynge moste desire knowe moche stronge haue often tymes prouyd hit vnto effusion blood wherof haue grete anger yet haue grete sorowe moche thou slewest patroclus hym moste louyd world thou mayste beleue certayn fore thys yere past deth shall auengyd vpon hande also wote well thou desirest slee hector answerd sayde achilles yf desire thy deth meruaylle nothynge therof moche thou deseruest myn enemye mortall thou art come lande destroye myne wyll well thou knowe thy wordes fere nothynge yet haue hope wyth two yere yf lyue swerde faylle thou shalt dye myn handes thou allonely alle moste grettest grekes amonge yow ye haue enterprysid grete folye hit may none otherwyse come yow therby deth assewrid thou shalt dye hande er shall dye thyne yf thou wene thou stronge thou maiste defende ayenste make hit alle baron thyn ooste promyse accorde fighte body ayenst body yf hit happen thou vaynquysshe frendes shall bannysshid oute royame shalle leue hit vnto grekes therof shall leue good plegge herein thou mayste prouffite many may renne grete danger yf haunte batayll yf hit happen vaynquysshe make alle ooste departe hen suffre v lyue pee achilles achauffid hym sore wordes offryd hym doo batayll gaf hector gayge whiche hector toke resseyuyd gladly etc whan agamenon knewe haytye bargayn wente hym hastely vnto tente achylles grete companye noble men whiche wolde wise accorde ne agree batayll sayng wold submytte hem many noble men vnder strenghte one man troians sayden lyke wyse saue kynge pryant wolde gladly agreed grete strenghte felte sone hector thus champe broken hector departed wente agayn troye fro grekes whan troylus knewe certaynly breseyda shold sente fader made grete sorowe souerain lady loue semblable wyse breseyda louyd strongly troylus made also grettest sorowe world leue souerayn lord loue ther neuer seen moche sorowe made betwene two louers departyng lyste alle theyr loue late hym rede booke troyllus chawcer made wherin shall fynde storye hooll whiche longe wryte fynably breseyda ledde vnto grekes whome receyued honourably amonge diomedes anone enflamed loue breseyda whan sawe fayr ridyng side shewid alle corage made many promesses specially desired loue whan knewe corage diomedes excused sayng wolde agree hym ne reffuse hym tyme herte disposed tyme answere otherwyse answere dyomedes grete ioye moche reffusid vtterly accompanyed vnto tente fader halpe doun hors toke fro one glouys helde handes souffryd hym swetely calcas resceyuyd wyth grete ioye whan pryuete betwene hem bothe breseyda saide fader semblable wordes fader thy wytte fayllyd wonte wyse moste honoured belouyd cyte troye gouernest alle wyth inne haddest many riches possession haste ben trayttre thou oughtest haue kepte thy rychesses deffended thy contree vnto deth thou louest better lyue pouerte exyle amonge mortall enemyes thy contree shall thys torne grete vylonnye certes thou shalt neuer gete moche honour thou haste goten vylonnye thou shalt blamed thy lyf thou shalt also thy deth dampned helle semeth yet hit ben better haue dwellyd oute peple vpon yle see dwelle dishonoure vylonnye wenest thou grekes holde trewe faithfull arte openly false vntrewe thy peple certes hit god appollo thus abusid hyt companye deuyllys thus spack fader wepte strongly displaysyr hadde etc ha doughter sayd calcas wenest thou sewre thynge despyte answer goddes specyally thyngeth towcheth helthe knowe certaynly answer warre shall dure longe cyte ne shall destroyed noble also burgeyses therfore hit better v sauf slayn wyth fynysshid parlament comyng breseyda plesid moche alle grekes cam theder fested demaunded tydynges troye kynge pryant wyth inne sayd vnto hem moche knewe curtoysly alle grettest promysyd kepe holde dere doughter eche man wente hys owne tente ther none hem gaf iewell departyng hit plesid well abide dwelle wyth grekes forgate anone noble cyte troye loue noble troyllus sone purpos woman chaungid torned certes sonner man saie thinke late breseyda blamed fader vyce trayson whiche self excersised forgetyng contre trewe frende troyllus etc phow grekes troians began sixthe bataylle dured space thretty dayes whiche many kynges prynces ded one syde diomedes smote doun troillus horse sente hit breseyda loue receyuyd hit gladly etc thre monethis triews passid morn tymes troians apparayllid bataill whan hector ordeyned batayllis yssued fyrste toke wyth hym fyftene thousand fyghtyng men troyllus folowed hym wyth ten thousand knyghtes hym cam paris thre thousand fyghtyng men good archer well horsed cam deyphebus thre thousand fyghtars hym cam eneas alle ordre many thys daye partye troians honderd thousand good fyghtyng men hardy partye grekes cam alle ther fyrste menelaus wyth seuen thousand knyghtes hym dyomedes wyth many achilles lad also seuen thousand kyng pampitus grete multitude knyghtes lyke ordeyned kynge philis aduaunced hym alther fyrste hector cam ayenst hym stronge slewe hym spere ther roos grete crye deth amonge grekes occysion slaughter began grete hyt horryble syght see well one syde kynge pampitus slewe many troians venge deth vncle assayllyd hector hector gaf hym grete strooke wyth hys swerd sleewe hym also avenge deth grekes slewe many troians achilles slewe many noble men amonge whyche slewe duc biraon cuforbe moche noble man hector day sore hurte visage bledde grete plente blood wyste doon hyt therfore troians reculed vnto walles whan hector behelde sawe vpon wallis quene hecuba hys moder susters grete shame grete yre assayllid kynge menon cosyn achilles gaf hym many stroke wyth swerd vpon hys helme slewe hym seeyng achilles wende haue enraged toke stronge spere ranne ayenst hector brake hys spere vpon hym coude remeue hym hector gaf hym wyth hys swerd grete strooke maad hym tomble vnder hys horse sayd hym achilles achilles thou contendest approche knowe thou approchest thy deth achilles wold haue answerd hector troyllus cam vpon betwene wyth grete nombre knyghtes putte hym myddes slayn fyue honderd knyghtes grece put back force menelaus cam rescows wyth thre thousand fyghtyng men partye troians cam kynge ademon iusted ayenst menelaus smote hym hurted hym vysage troylus toke hym lad hym away yf dyomedes come sonner grete companye knyghtes fought troillous comyng smote hym doun toke hys horse sente hit breseyda dyde saye seruant hyt troyllus horse loue beten hym prowesse prayd fro forth wold holde hym loue frende etc breseyda grete ioye tydynges sayd seruaut shold saye vnto lord myght hate hym wyth good herte louyd whan diomedes knewe answer right ioyous threstid amonge enemyes troians stronger maad grekes goo back recule vnto tentes slayn hem yf kynge agamenon socowred hem right grete strength began batayll horryble mortall grekes recoueryd felde rebowted put troians aback vnto theyr dyches cam palidamas rescows wyth grete nombre multitude knyghtes dyde fayre appertyses warre dyomedes adressid hym hym beten palydamas toke horse dyomedes toke hit troyllus fought fote mounted anone ther vpon cam achilles ayenst troyllus troyllus receyuyd gladly bete doun achilles whiche remountyd lyghtly assaillid troyllus swerd troyllus defended hym right vaylliantly cam hector stowre slayn thousand knyghtes grekes defended achilles oppressid vnnethe myght defende hym ben slayn taken yf kynge thelamon duc atthenes socourid hym sette hym agayn hors grete payne nyght cam departed fougght thus thretty dayes contynuelly grete domage bothe partyes ther slayn sixe bastard sone kynge pryant hector hurte visage therfore kynge pryant demauded trews grekes sixe monethis agreed accorded hym etc phow grekes troians began seuenth batayll dured twelue dayes began eyghte batayll moche domageous troians ffor hector slayn achilles rebowted cyte force grete domage dvryng sixe monthes triews aforsaid hector dide hym heled woundes playd noble halle ylyon hystorye sayth moste ryall halle fayre alle world thus duryng trewes kynge pryant dyde burye hys sixe bastard sone eche sepulture hym self ryght honourably amonge thynges diomedes suffred grete sease loue brescida myght ete ne reste thynkyng requyred many tymes loue answerd hym right wysely gyuyng hym hope wyth oute certaynte ony poynte whyche dyomedes enflamed alle poyntes loue whan sixe monthes passid began fyghte space twelue dayes contynuelly fro mornyng vnto euenyng many slayn one syde cam grete mortalite amonge grekes oost grete hete tho therfore kyng agamenon requyred tryews whyche agreed accorded hym etc whan triews passid nyght fore andrometha wyf hector hadd two fayr sone hym wherof one name la medon astromatas andrometha sawe nyght meruayllous vysion semed yf hector wente day folowyng bataylle shold slayn grete fere drede husbond wepyng sayd hym prayng hym wold goo batayll day wherof hector blamed wyf sayng shold beleue ne gyue fayth dremes wold abyde ner tarye therfore whan hyt morenyng andrometha wente vnto kynge pryant quene tolde veryte vysion prayd wyth alle herte wold doo moche hector shold day go bataylle etc hit happend day fayre cleer troians armed troyllus yssued fyrste batayll hym eneas parys deyphebus polidamas kynge sarpedon kynge epistropus kynge croys kynge philomenus alle prynces comen ayde troians eche man good ordenance kyng pryant sente hector shold kepe hym well day fro goyng batayll wherfore hector angry sayd wyf many wordes reprochable knewe well defence cam requeste hyt notwithstandyng deffence armed hym whan andromeda sawe hym armed toke lytyll chyldren fyll doun foot husbond prayd hym humbly wold take armes wold doo hyt sayd hym leste yf ye wyll haue mercy haue pytie lytyll child dye bitter deth shall ledde seruytude bondage strange contreyes poynt cam vpon quene hecuba quene helayne susters hector knelid doun fore foot prayd hym wyth wepyng teerys wold doo harnoys vnarme hym come wyth halle neuer wold doo hit prayer descended palays thus armed toke hys horse wold haue goon bataylle requeste andromeda kynge pryant cam rennyng anone toke hym brydell sayd hym many thynges one maad hym retorne wyse wold vnarme hym amonge thynges batayll mortall grekes troians diomedes troyllus iusted geder assemble greuyd eche wyth oute faylle eche slayn yf menelaus come departid kynge myseres frygye bete menelaus taken hym whan eneas cam distrowblid wold haue slayn hym sayd troyllus delyueryd hem slewe many grekes cam kynge thelamon thre thousand fyghtyng men stid hys comyng ayenst polidamas put hym worse vnhorsid hym troyllus socourid hym made hym remounte hors cam parys achilles side smote amonge troians grete forcewyth helpe hys peple putte hem flyght vnto cyte chasse achilles slewe margareton one bastardes kynge pryant whan hector knewe achylles slayn margareton grete sorowe dyde anone lase hys helme wente hym batayll hys fader knewe hys comyng slewe two noble duke grekes duc coryphus duc bastidus threstid grettest prees grekes slewe many coude areche grekes fledde afore hym ther none hardy tht durst abide stroke thus troians retorned slewe grekes side grekes toke polidamas lad hym away ne hector haue ben whiche delyuerid hym slewe many grekes admyrall grece named leocides assayllid hector hector slewe hymanone whan achilles sawe hector slewe thus noble grece many meruayll beholde thought yf hector slayn grekes shold neuer haue victorye also moche slayn many kynges prynces ranne vpon hym meruayllously noble duc grece hym named polyceus come loue achilles whyche promysyd gyue hym hys suster maryage hector slewe duc anone seeyng achilles achilles wenyng avenge deth policeus assayllyd hector grete yre hector caste hym darte fiersly made hym wounde thye achilles yssued batayll dide bynde hys wounde toke grete spere purpose slee hector yf myght mete hym amonge thynges hector taken moche noble baron grece moche queyntly rychely armed lede hym oute ooste ease caste shelde behynde hym backe lefte breste discouerte thys poynte toke none hede achylles cam pryuely vnto hym putte thys spere wyth body hector fyll doun dede ground whan kynge menon sawe hector dede assayllyd achylles grete yre bete hym doun ground hurte hym strongly men bare hym tente vpon hys shelde deth hector alle troians disconfyte reentryd theyr cyte beryng body hector wyth grete sorowe lamentacion pof ryche sepulture hector grete lamentacions wepynges troians maad deth palamydes chosen duc governour oost grekes whan hector ded body born cyte ther tonge coude expresse sorowe maad cyte generally men woman ther none lever haue loste owen sone hym sayd then forth loste alle hope truste deffence thus demened ryght longe sorowe noble kynges prynces bare body vnto palais ylyon whan kynge pryant sawe hym fyll doun swowne vpon body ded sorowe vnnethe coude take hym awaye force demened grete sorowe brethern myght men saye sorowe moder quene made hys susters sorowe maad hys wyf certes man expresse alle lamentacions maad moche body myght longe endure wyth oute corrupcion kynge pryant toke counceyll many wyse maysters myght kepe body hector wyth oute corrupcion wyth oute sepulture dyde make counceyll ryche sepulture vpon foure pylers gold lyfte vp heyghte vpon whyche maad moche ryche tabernacle gold precyous stone foure corner tabernacle foure ymages gold semblauce angellis aboue tabernacle ther grete ymage gold maad semblance hector vysage torned toward grekes helde naked swrde semed manaced grekes ther myddes tabernacle place wyde maysters setted putte body hector flesshe bone cladde beste garementes robe stood right vp foot myght endure longe tyme wyse oute corupcon certayn scyence maystres sette sommet toppe hede hector wete vessell hole bottom whiche vessell alle ffull fyn banie stylled dropped place aboue heed spradde doun alle membres bodye well wyth iu oute fyllyd often tymes vessell wyth bame thus body myght enpayre grete vertue bame alle peple wold see hector sawe hym veryly lyke wyse ben lyue thys sepulture maysters maad lampe fyn gold brennyng contynuelly wyth oute gooyng oute quenchyng maad closure ende man sholde approche ne goo vnto thys tabernacle wyth oute lycence leue temple kynge pryant ordeyned sette grete plente prestes praye godde oute sessyng hys sone hector gaf good rente amonge thynges kynge agamenon assemblid kynges noble ofte said hem manere frendes ye kynges prynces baron oughte rendre yelde thankynges goddes humbly deuoute herte right hard enemye hector haue suffred slayn hande achilles ffor longe lyue neuer esperance haue comen aboue oure enemyes may troians fro hen forth hope truste onely destruccon may shorte tyme hope victorye vpon moche achilles strongly hurte may goo batayll yf ye thynke good whylis may heled also ben hurte whome haue many also burye ded bodyes shall sende kynge pryant haue triews two monethis counceyll semed good hem sente anone kynge pryant tryews accorded two monethis dvryng triews palamydes murmured ayen seygnourye agamenon day gyder palamides spack thys mater kynge agamenon answerd hym sage presence alle sayd hym palamydes wenest thou haue grete ioye seygnourye gyuen begynnyng haue occupyed thys present tyme well hyt requeste haue none avayll ne prouffit therby haue grete charge breke many slepes thende neclygence ooste goo declyne ner disworshyppe certes hit well suffisid haue ben vnder governauce fere man may accuse ony euyll wyll necligence haue fayllid ony thynge yf thou gauyst thy consente myn eleccion thou darst esmaye therof ffor thou yet tyme comen hit two yere er thou cam therfore yf shold haue abyden thy comyng ben yet poort atthenes moche thou shalt wene haue ioye office desiryng haue honour contente another chosen redy consente moste wy whan agamenon thus spoken ther proceded tht day matere euen agamenon dide crye oost tht eche man shold morn betymes fore tente parlament whan hit cam morenyng assemblid agamenon sayd brethern frendes haue vnto thys tyme charge werke grete trauayll conduyte hit well suche wise suffrance goddes haue brought hit honour vnto thys tyme moche hit leeffful tht vnyuersite answere alway one maister euery man enploye hym beste power moche haue conduyted oost longe tyme wyll chese another may conduyte hyt dyscretely whan agamenon fynysshid wordes sayng plesid euery man chee palamydes duc gouernour wente vnto tente achilles laye seke woundes angry deposyng agamenon sayd fore alle wold hyt palamydes thyng lyke vnto agamenon wytte discrecion ought change hym palamydes moche alle peple consentid abode therby also etc phow kynge pryant yssued batayll auenge vpon grekes deth sone hector prowessis dide annyversarye sayd hector whyche achilles esprysed loue polixena doughter kynge pryant suche wyse myght dure ne reste whan two monthis triews paste kynge pryant desiryng avenge deth sone hector ordeyned owen persone bataylles sette eche batayll good conduytours hym self wente ledde hym fyve twenty thousand good knyghtes chosen beste dare sayth book ther yssued troye day honderd fyfty thousand men deiphebus formeste parys hym cam kyng pryant troyllus eneas menon polidamas wente hem vnto tentes grekes palamydes ordeyned bataylles began batayll grete mortall kyng pryant smote doun palamides comyng smote grettest prees grekes slewe many bete hem doun dyde moche armes day wyth grete payne man sholde beleue hyt man auncyent olde myght doo dyde day kynge sarpedon troye assaylled kynge neptolonyus passyng stronge knyght kynge sarpedon born erthe defended hym vailliantly gaf grete stroke vnto kynge neptolonyus maad hym grete wounde thye cam batayll kynge parce remounted kynge sarped n wyth ayde folke menelaus duc atthenes assaylleden kynge perce enclosed hym peple amonge hem slewe kynge perce maad troians recule force dyde meruaylles armes kynge sarpedon kynge pryant bastard sonnes folowed hym cessid slee grekes ther none day dide moche armes dyde kynge pryant sorowe yre maad hys strengthe growe grekes auysed hem take way whiche troians shold retorne vnto cyte wente theder grete nombre whan troians reculeden goo place fonde hem self myddell enemyes tho began mortall batayll ther cam vpon kyng pryant grete nombre fyghtyng men one wynge parys cam trauerse wyth grete foysson good fyghtars grete foysson archer slewe many grekes hurted hem dyde well hat force grekes muste recule theyr tentes troians reentrid cyte kyng pryant loo pryse batayll sente grekes demande triews agreed acorded hym fynde longe triews endured etc amonge thynges kynge pryant dyde carye land body kynge perse buryed hys contre tho wepyng sorowe grete troye especyall parys louyd hym strongly duryng thys triews annyversarye hector approchid shold moorne fyftene dayes grete sorowe shold halowe grete feste funerall hit tyme guyse custome kynges prynces duryng tryews grekes wente cam cyte sauely dide troians vnto tentes grekes achilles grete desire goo troye see cyte feste annyversarye hector whome slayn wente alle vnarmed vnto temple appolyn sepulture hector fonde grete foyson men woman noble wepte maad grete sorowe fore sepulture whiche man myght see side alle hool like wyse fyrst vertue bame quene h cuba polixena doughter passyng foyre grete companye noble ladyes alle theyr heer spartled hangyng aboute sholdres demened ryght meruayllous sorowe well polyxena maad grete sorowe yet loste thynge beawte semed ande shewid self fayre alle membres well colowred nature formed neuer none fayrer etc whan achilles well aduysed seen polixena sayd hym self neuer seen fayre woman ne better fourmed ne made wyth one moste noble woman fo worlde achilles shoten darte loue stack hym herte meruayllously coude cesse beholde behelde desired asottyd thought none thynge abode temple vnto euenyng longe quene whan wente oute conueyed eye vpon polixena ferre myght see thys cause begynnyng hys meschief thys sorowe achilles retorned vnto tente whan leyde slepe nyght ther cam many thynges mynde thoughte knewe dauger polixena putte hym inne thought hym self moste stronge men world coude ner mowe vaynquysshe hym regarde syghte frayll mayde vaynquisshid ouercome hym hym semed ther medecyne world myght hele hym saue sayd prayer strengthe ne rychesse may thynge meue haue pyte wote neuer devyll hath putte thys daunger loue hateth sore mortall hate right good cause ffor comen hether sle kyune cosyus late haue slayn noble brother hector certes see remedye syn moste noble fayreste world torned hym walle fyll wepyng drowned hym self teres necessite muste thynke myght come loue polixene coueryd hydde corage well myghte phow achylles sente secrete messanger vnto hecuba quene troye requyre doughter polixena answer loue said achilles assemblid cost grekes cou ceyllid hem departe haue pee troians nyght folowyng achilles leyde bedde myght slepe thought wold sende tymes hys messanger vnto quene hecuba knowe yf myght fyne wyth wold gyue hym doughter polixena wyve wold moche wold make grekes reyse theyr syege goo agayn theyr contrees hastely pee shold maad betwene alle thus thought nyght put execucion sente trewe messanger vnto quene requyre doughter sayde promyses lord comanded hym whan quene vnderstande wordes messanger answerd hym discretly well hated achilles ony man world sayng frend moche redy doo thyng thy mayster requyreth saye vnto hym may doo thynge allone self shall speke lorde parys sone thou shalt come thirde day agayn shall saye thyn answere whan messanger herde quene speke retorned vnto lord said hym founde thus began achylles haue hope come entente quene hecuba wente anone vnto kynge pryant husbond paris tolde achilles sente kynge henge doun heed longe whyle wyth oute sayng ony worde said wyf hyt thynketh herde thynge resceyue frendship amytye hym hath grete offence hath taken away lyght myn eyen sleyng dere sone hector hath therin gyuen hope grekes haue victorye alleway eschiewe moste grete peryll thende myn sone lose theyr lyf may haue reste myn olde dayes consente yow haue requyreth alleway forseen doo fyrste thynge hath promysid wyth oute ony decepcion parys agreed thynge lyghtly moche promesses achilles thynge spoken quene helayne etc thirde daye achilles sente agayn hys messanger vnto quene sone cam fore sayd hym haue spoken husbonde also sone parys requeste also promesse thy lorde contente hys requeste agreed hym doo fyrst thynge hath promysed thou mayst saye hym may come chief ende desire conduyte wysely secretly thys thynge moche hym messanger toke leue quene cam anone hys mayster counted hym alle quene sayd hym began achilles strongly thynke myghte performe promysed kynge pryaut hyt greuous thynge doo hit alle hys puyssance hit propre vyce vnto folissh lover promyse thynge hard brynge aboute dyfficyle come effecte loues lyke wyse gloryfyed hym achilles hys merytes gyuyng hys ayde grekes wold make leue theyr syege achilles counceyll palamydes assemblid kynges noble men oost parlament sayd manere mi frendes assemblid brynge warre ende thenke ye otherwhile self grete legyerte lyghtnes folye recouere wif menelaus haue lefte oure contrees landes oure wyves oure chyldren ben comen thys stronge lande haue dyspendyd owrys folyly putte oure bodyes daunger deth grete infynyte laboure syn haue ben comen hether ther ben ryght many kynges prynces ded self haue shedde moche blood tht neuer shold haue happend yf begonne folye lay e nothyng grete pry ther behoueth dye many noble men ther ben ynowhe world noble fayr woman whome menelaus myght haue one two yf wolde hit light thynge ouercome troians haue stronge cyte well garnysshid good fightars horse backe foote hit ought suffise v haue slayn hector many theyr noble whiche myghte retorne wyth oure honoure worshippe yf leue helayne haue exione whome helayne may compare noblesse meuyd duc atthenes kynge thoas contraryed strongly wordes achilles dyde alle sayd sayde neyther fayr ne well wherof achilles grete sorowe comanded myrondones shold arme ayenst troians shold gyue counceyll ne ayde vnto grekes amonge thynges vytaylles began faylle amonge grekes grete famyne assemblid palamydes alle moste noble oost counceyll theyr counceyll kynge agamenon sente vnto cyte messe kynge thelephus charged laded shippes vitayll cam sauely agayn ooste grekes receyuyd wyth grete ioye amonge thynges palamydes dyde theyr shippes reparyed ende myght redy yf nede etc pof deth deyphebus son kynge pryant parys slewe palamydes troians rebouted grekes theyr tentes sette fyre theyr shippis alle thynges achilles wold goo batayll loue polixene whan triews passid began fighte ben acustomed deyphebus assayllid domyng kynge cressus grece adressid hym hym gladly iusted one ayenst deyphebus bete kynge cressus dede doun ground wherof grekes sore trowblid put hem flight palamydes dyomedes cam wyth fyue twenty thousand fyghtyng men resisted troians wyth noble kynge thelamon ayax adressid hym ayen efronyus one bastard sone kynge pryant smote hym hard bete hym doun dede ground seeyng deyphebus grete furour ran vpon thelamon bete hym sore hurte hym whan palamydes sawe stroke toke grete spere adressid hym deyphebus smote hym harde breste spere entryd body spere brake trouchon bood body deyphebus whan parys sawe broder hurte deth toke hym ladde hym vnto gate cyte toke hym men kepe deyphebus opend eyen sawe parys broder said hym broder shalt thou late descende helle auengyng deth pray may er trouchon betaken oute body thou moche thy hande thou slee hym hath slayn parys promysid hym wold power retorned hym bataylle ryght angry broder sayd hym self desired lenger lyue tyll auengyd deth broder sought palamydes alle abowtes fonde hym foughte agaynst kynge sarpedon assayllyd sle hym palamydes deffended hym vayllyantly grete fureur gaf grete strooke wyth swerde kynge sarpedon cutte sholdre fro body anone kynge sarpedon fyll doun dede parys seeyng grete domage palamydes dyde also prowesse putte troians flight cessid slee smyte doun allway bende stronge bowe auysed well palamydes leyzer shotte hym arowe enuenymed smote hym throte cutte two maistre vayne palamydes fyll doun dede erthe who deth grekes made moche sorowe lefte batayll wente vnto theyr tentes helde stale ayenst troians deffended strongly descended troians fote entryd theyr tentes toke alle fonde good parys troyllus wente side waye vnto porte dyde putte fyre shippis brente grete plente men mighte see flame ferre rescowse shippis cam kynge thelamon grete companye fightars began batayll horrible grete occision slaughter bothe side verayly shippis ben alle brente ne ben prowesse kynge thelamon tht dide meruaylles body euer dyde ther fyue honderd shippes brente grete occision grekes many hurte ebes sone kynge trace sore hurte wyth spere bare tronchon body poynte wente tente achylles restid hym day reffused goo bataylle loue polixene ebes reprochid strongly achylles suffryd destroye peple contre dye vyllaynsly myght well helpe hem yf wolde sone fynysshid wordes one toke oute tronchon body anone fyll doun dede presence achilles anon cam fro batayll oon varlettis seruauntes achilles achilles demaunded hym tydynges ooste ha syre sayd hit day myshappid oure folk grete multitude troians ben comen vpon haue slayn alle cowde mete wyth trowe ther lefte oon home men troye euery man come bataylle therfore yf hit plese yow whilis troians ben wery come bataylle ye shall gete yow perpetuell memorye worshyppe glorye prowesse ye shall lytyll space haue alle vaynquysshid hem shall dare deffende hem ayenst yow ben wery neuer wolde achylles wordes varlet ne deth ebes chaunge corage dissimyled alle seen herde grete loue polixene amonge thynges bataylle ryght sharpe endured vnto nyght grete domage grekes nyght departed yet deyphebus dede drewe toward ende whan parys troyllus sawe hym sorowe began crye make grete sorowe deyphebus opend lytyll eyen demanded parys wyth feble voys yf dede slayn hym parys sayd hym ye deyphebus dyde drawe oute hede spere wyth tronchon anone deyde wherfore troians made grete sorowe hit nede holde longe parlament sorowe kynge pryant fader made ne wyf susters hit moche also deth kynge sarpedon partye grekes made grete sorowe deth palamydes made body buryed worshypfully myght longe wyth oute heed gouernour counceyll duc nestor agamenon remysed dignyte fore day folowyng troians erly morenyng yssued oute cyte good ordenance grekes cam ayenst hem tho began batayll mortall grete slaughter bothe side hit rayned moche day grekes wythdrewe hem theyr tentes troians folowed rayne grete muste nedes leue bataylle retorne theyr cyte morn betymes began fighte slewe day many baron grekes fought euen faughte space seuen dayes contynuelly grete occision one moche grekes myght suffre stenche dede bodyes demaunded triews two monethis whiche accorded hem kynge pryant dvryng triews kynge agamenon sente duc nestor vlixes dyomedes speke achilles praye hym amoneste hym come ooste deffende hem ayenst troians slewe hem ouer meruayllously whan come vnto hym resseyuyd hem wyth grete ioye vlixes sayd hym syre achilles ne hit entencion also owres alle ooste leue oure contre come renne vpon kynge pryant destroye hym force armes bete doun cyte fro whens cometh newe corage many hurtes domages haue resseyuyd lande troians haue slayn many kynges prynces pylled robbed oure tentes brente oure shippes hope haue vaynquysshid hem ye force valeur haue slayn hector rray tutor troians also deyphebus dede troians ben therwyth put vnder foote ye haue goten grete trauayll grete worshippe good renome wyll ye lese alle attones suffre peple slayn cruelly ye haue longe deffended effusion blood plese hit yow fro hensforth entretene kepe good renome defende peple wyth oute yow may longe defende hem ayenst enemyes ende may come victorye prowesse whiche hope attayne come sire vlixes sayd achilles yf come lande tho cause ye haue declared maye saye grete folye amonge v wyf one v wete syre menelaus many kynges hyghe prince paryll deth hit ben moche wysdom noble palamydes haue abyden pea contree slayn kynges prynces lyke wyse certes grete partye worlde noble men ben assemblid yf dye many ben redy dede hit muste nedes folowe contrees shall replenysshid gouerned villayns hector noble worthy dede lyke wyse may dye lightly stronge therfore moche ye requyre goo bataylle moche payne laboure lese ye haue entencion putte danger loue better lese renomee lyf ende ther prowesse hit forgoten nestor dyomedes contendeden ynowh drawe achilles quarellis myght neuer enduce hym theyr porpose ne wordes agamenon neyther sayd hem shold make pee troians fore alle slayn etc retorned thre prynces vnto agamenon sayde hym alle founde achilles agamenon dyde hit knowen prynces ooste assemblid cause demanded theyr auyse stode vp menelaus sayng hit shold v grete vylonnye seke pee wyth troians syn hector deyphebus ben dede slayn theyr deth troians repute vaynquysshid wyth achilles sholde well mayntene warre agaynst troians answerd vlixes nestor sayde hit meruayll though menelaus desired warre affeccion recouere wyf troye disgarnysshid newe hector troyllus lityll lasse stronge worthy hector ther also another deyphebus parys oughte dowte moche therfore couceyllid pee retorne hom agayn grece escryed false traytour calcas whiche traytour troians said ha noble men thinke ye doo ayenst comadement goddes haue promisid yow victorie ye leue hit certes tht shold grete folye take agayn corage fighte ye agaynst troians stronglye ye haue doon fore cesse tyll ye haue victorie goddes haue promisid yow wordes said calcas grekes toke herte hem sayng veryly wold mayntene warre ayenst troians whether achilles helpe hem wold leue pof many bataylles made one side tht bothe grete domage certayn triew deth noble troyllus achylle slewe ayenst promys drewe hym horse tayll thurgh oost achilles slewe kynge menon etc whan triews two monethis passid began fyghte bataylle right sharpely dyde troyllus meruaylles armes venge deth broder dare saith book slewe day thousand knyghtes grekes fledde fore hym bataylle endured nyght departed hem day folowyng fourtenth bataylle began harde sharpe dide dyomedes meruaylles armes slewe many troians hurte hem adressid hym ayenst troyllus one tyme smote hym harde smote hym doun erthe sore hurte reprochid hym loue breseyda grekes ran grete strength toke dyomedes vp bare hym vpon shelde vnto tente menelaus sawe dyomedes beten adressid hym ayenst troyllus troyllus yet spere hole smote hym harde bete hym doun erthe sore hurte born tente men vpon shelde agamenon assemblid alle strengthe threstid amonge troians slewe many troyllus cam ayenst hym smote hym doun hors anon remounted helpe folk thus finysshid bataylle day agamenon sente haue triews sixe monethis whiche agreed accorded kynge pryant hit hit semed counceyll tht shold accorded longe amonge thinges breseyda ayenst fader wente see diomedes laye sore hurte tente knewe well troyllus loue hurte hym retorned corage many purpose ende sawe might neuer recouere troyllus therfore sone diomedes hole wolde gyue hym loue wyth oute lenger taryyng amonge thinges kynge agamenon trasported hym vnto tente achilles companye duc nestor achilles receyuyd hem wyth grete ioye agamenon prayd hym wolde come forthon bataylle suffre peple thus slayn achilles wold neuer molefye corage wordes well moche louyd agamenon agreed consentid men shold go batayll oute hym wherof agamenon nestor cowde hym grete thanke thanked hym ynowhe retorned theyr tentes whan triews passid agamenon ordeyned peple batayll achilles sente hym mirondones habilled ensigned reed signe knowen tho began batayll harde sharpe grete domage bothe party troylus bete doun duc atthenes slewe many mirodones hurte fought thus tyll nyght departed morn tymes began batayll sharpe mortall kynge philomen polidamas toke kynge thoas lad hym away ne mirodones haue rescowed hym troylus smote among hem slewe many hurted hem deliueryd hym grete assault slewe horse wolde haue taken hym whan parys bastard brethern smote amonge hem brake remysed troyllus horse ther fiers medlee slew myrundones emargeron one bastardis kynge pryant troyes wherof troyllus grete sorowe ayde peple smote amonge hem slewe hurte many deffended hem vayllyantly helde hem gyder troyllus cessid greue hem entre amonge hem often tymes tho cam bataylle agamenon menelaus thelamon vlixes dyomedes wyth alle peple began harde medlee ther grekes dyde troians suffre moche payne troyllus socouryd hem vayllyantly put hym self alleway moste nede slewe bete doun fonde dide moche prowesse grekes fledde vnto theyr tentes thelamon deffended hem vayllyantly made hem recouere felde prowesse sixtenth bataylle whiche dyed many knyghtes bothe side troyllus cessid greue myrundones ther none puyssant ne stronge myght dure agaynst hym dide moche remysed grekes flighte toke honderd noble men brought cyte whan bataylle fynysshid ayenst euen myrundones retorned vnto tente achilles ther founden many hurte ther honderd hem dede wherof achilles moche sorowe hit nyght wente bedde many thoughtes purposid one go bataylle auenge deth men another tyme thoughte beawte polixene thoughte yf wente shuld lese loue alleway kynge pryant wyf shold holde hym deceyuour promysid sholde helpe grekes well sayd hym self sente men theyr ayde thought chilles many dayes moche day cam seuententh batayll began moche horryble dured seuen dayes contynuelly many grekes ayn wherfore agamenon requyred triews troians agreed lenger triews tyll buryed theyr dede bodyes whan dayes passid eyghtenth batayll began ryght aspre fiers menelaus parys iusted gyder bete well eche polidamas vlixes faught gyder grete whyle menesteus bete doun eneas wyth iustynge kynge phylomenus bete agamenon sore hurte hym yf thelamon come smote ground phylomenus sore wounded archylogus sone duc nestor assayllyd one bastardis kynge pryant named brum smote hym harde wyth spere bare hym doun ground slewe hym wherof troians grete sorowe aboue alle troyllus angry smote amonge grekes put hem flight ne mirondanes haue ben resisted hym therfore troyllus smote amonge slewe many bete doun dyde moche moche made grekes rebonte hem theyr tentes descended fote entryd tentes slewe hem alle side grete crye sowne cam achilles rested hym tente demanded one seruantes ther hit sayd hym troians vaynquysshid grekes slewe theyr tentes whiche myghte deffende wene ye sewre nay ye shall see anone fourty thousand troians shall slee yow vnarmed tyme haue slayn parte myrundones cesse slee ther shall abide one lyue yf socouryd wordes achilles quoke yre sette behynde hym loue polixene dyde arme hym hastely mounted hors ran araged lyon smote amonge troians pershid hem slewe hurte suche wyse anone swerde knowen blood ran felde alle aboute wente whan troyllus knewe achilles faught swerde adressid hym hym gaf hym grete strooke made hym grete wounde depe muste nedes cesse many dayes comyng bataylle troyllus hurte also hand achilles thynge sore bothe fyll doun ground bataylle dured vnto nyght morn began agayn endured vnto euen thus faught sixe dayes contynuelly wherfore ther many slayn eyther partye kynge pryant grete sorowe achilles ayenst promyse come batayll wende made hym vnderstand thynge rather deceyue hym otherwyse reprochid wyf beleue lightly hym polixene sorowed ynowhe plesid haue achilles husbond achilles amonge thynges dyde hele woundes duryng sixe monethes triews goten whiche woundes troyllus gyuen hym porposid auenge hym troyllus shold dye villaynsly hande thynges nynetenth batayll began wyth grete occision afore achilles entryd bataylle assemblid myrondones prayd hem wolde entende none thynge enclose troyllus holde hym wyth oute sleynge tyll cam wolde fer fro hem promysid hym wolde smote bataylle syde cam troyllus began slee bete doun alle raughte dyde moche aboute mydday put grekes flight myrondones well two thousand fyghtyng men forgete comandement theyr lord threstid amonge troians recouerid felde helde hem geder sought man troyllus fonde hym tht foughte strongly enclosid party slewe wounded many allone amonge hem man socoure hym slewe horse hurte hym many place araced heed helme coyffe yron deffended hym beste wyse cowde cam achilles whan sawe troyllus alle naked ran vpon hym rage smote heed caste hit vnder foot horse toke body bonde hit taylle horse drewe hit hym thurgh oute ooste vylonnye hit drawe sone noble kynge worthy hardy certes yf ony noblesse ben achilles wold haue done vylonye whan parys knewe achilles thus vylaynsly slayn troyllus grete sorowe eneas polidamas dyde grete payne recouere body myght grete multytude grekis resisted hem parte kynge menon deyde sorowe deth troyllus assayllyd achylles sayd hym reproche ha euyll trayttre cruelte hath meuyd bynde taylle thy horse sone noble prynce kynge pryantis drawe hym moste vylayne worlde certes thou shalt abyd hit ran vpon hym smote hym harde wyth spere breste made hym grete wounde gaf hym many stroke wyth swerde bete hym doun ground body troyllus recoueryd wyth grete payne folke achylles releuyd theyr lord sette hym agayn horse sone strength cam hym agayn cam agayn stoure recountryd kynge menon assayllyd hym strongly kynge menon defended hym vayllyantly hurted achilles many place cam moche peple one side departed cam nyght departed made cesse faught thus space seuen dayes seuenth day whan achilles heled woundes desiryng auenge hym kynge menon sayd folke yf myght recountre hym shold holde hym cloos lyke dyde troyllus began bataylle right aspre achilles menon faught gyde grete felonye bete doun eche foote myrundones enclosid hym toke hym force man socoure hym achilles seeyng kynge menon dauger ran vpon hym slewe hym wyth grete martyre menon gaf hym fore many grete woundes wherof laye longe amonge thynges menelaus menesteus grete companye kynges prynces many fightyng men threstyd stoure put many troians flight whiche entred theyr cyte grete myschief moche grekes chassed hem nyghe slewe hurted many phow parys ennortement hecuba moder slewe achilles temple appollo sone due nestor parys apax slewe eche bataylle deth troyllus kynge pryant wyf child habitantes cyte made grete sorowe meruayllously sayde alle syn lost hector deyphebus troyllus then forthon hope theyr lyf theyr deth kynge pryant demanded tryews hit greed accorded grekes duryng whiche dyde burye honourably body troyllus body kynge menon quene myght appeasid ner conforted deth chyldren toughte many maner wy myght auengyd achylles thus slayn sone cruelle tyrannye fynably called parys sore wepyng said hym secretly wordes ryght dere sone thou knowest traytte achilles hath slayn trayson forseen thy brethern child wyth lace lyf moche hath slayn hem trayson semeth good also iuste right slayn trayson shall telle hit shall doon vnhappy man hath many tymes requyred haue wyf doughter polixene haue gyuen hym good esperan e haue purposed sende hym feall messanger bidde hym come speke temple appolyn wyll right dere sone thou awayte good companye knyghtes whan shall comen ye renne vpon hym slee hym escape wyth lyf parys answerd wolde thynge suche wyse deuysed ther vpon assemblyd twenty good knyghtes whome affyed hym moche wente hem forth temple appolyn assone achilles herde messanger speke cam quene hecuba foole beyng euyll counceyllid toke wyth hym sone duc nestor wente bothe vnto temple appolyn sone comen parys knyghtes ran vpon hym parys caste hym thre dartes wherwyth hurte hym sore achilles drewe oute swerde armour wrapped arme mantell smote amonge knyghtes right fiersly slewe seuen fynably sone duc nestor archilogus achilles bothe slayn temple anone parys comanded tht body shold caste oute houndes byrdes request helenus put place fore temple kepte troians grete ioye saide forthon charge grekes ne sette nought hem whan agamenon knewe therof sente vnto kynge pryant haue bodyes burye hem kynge pryant made deliuerid born tentes tho aroose grete sorowe amonge grekes sayd hadde alle loste duc nestor myght comforted deth sone made achilles noble sepulture consentement kynge pryant leyde cyte thentre gate tymbre thynges kynge agamenon assemblid counceyll noble coste shewid deth achilles moste parte disconforted distalentid warre therfore demanded yf hit good leue warre entertene hold hit among dyuerse opynyons alowed warre blamed hit finably concluded alle geder one acorde mayntene warre sayyng yf achilles fayllyd yet sholde faylle promesses goddes stode vp ayax among said yf achylles dede late sende sone kynge nycomedes beell sire norisshith techith foot armes trowe wyth oute hym may haue victorye troians counceyll semed good agrement euery man menelaus chosen goo fe che neptolonyus sone achylles named wyse pyrrus amonge thynges whan tryews faylled xvi day iuyn whan dayes ben lengest alle yere troians began twentyth bataylle ayenst grekes ryght sharpe harde day wente ayax grete folye bataylle wyth oute armes bare nothynge swerde troians loste theyr beste defendours hardy wonte saue theyr lyues foughte myghtyly parys wyth alle peple perse beste archer slewe many grekes kynge phylomenus foughte strongly paphaghone cam slewe many grekes e made recule menesteus iusted agaynst polidamas bete hym ryght fiersly ran vpon hym wyth swerde taken slayn hym ne kynge phylomenus deliueryd hym fro handes ayax made day meruaylles armes thus vnarmed slewe many troians yet hurte ende smote amonge perse parys ladde slewe many made hem torne flight whan parys sawe peple thus slayn shotte ayax arowe enuenymed raught hym betwene racke side ayax anone felte hurte deth thought wolde dye tyll auengid hym hym slayn hym dyde moche fonde parys sayd hym thou haste slayn wyth thyn arowe fore dye shall slee also thy cause ben many noble men slayn gaf hym grete strook cutte two visage depe fyll doun dede erthe ayax fyll doun hym troians toke body parys wepyng teres bare hit vnto cyte folowed vnto gate next nyght folowyng agamenon made ooste aproche ner cyte pyght tentes troians kepte wally day nyght troians esperance ne hope theyr lyues whan sawe alle sone kynge pryant dede ther tonge expresse lamentacions kynge pryant made wyf doughters quene helayne deth parys aboue alle helayne made moste grettest sorowe kynge dyde burye parys right riche sepulture sette temple iuno honourably etc p quene panthasile cam amazonne thousand maydens socoure troye bare vayllyantly slewe many grekis slayn pyrrus sone achilles two monethis duryng hoole yates troye opend troians dide thynge goo cyte lamented sorowed kynge agamenon sente ofte tymes vnto kynge pryant shold sende men batayll kynge pryant doubtyng destruccon wold hit moche abood socours quene amasone way come vnto socours kynge pryant amazoue prouynce ne dwellyd woman oute men enduced warre fyght nyghe contre ysle men dwellid accustomed thre tymes yere go thether appryll maye iuyn vnto men haue theyr companye retorned amazonne ensayanted chylde yf bare sone gaf hem sowke certayn tyme sente hem faders yf hit doughter helde hit dide brenne right pappe bere better spere taught foot armes prouynce lady quene moche noble virgyne strong fightar name panthasilee louyd moche hector good renomee whan knewe grekes assaillid troyes grete strength wente theder socour hit thousand vyrgynes loue hector whan comen knewe ded made grete sorowe praid kyng pryant wold late yssue bataill ayenst grekes tht myht shewe hem maydens coude bere armes prayer panthasilee morn tymes gate opend yssued oute kynge philemen paphaghone eneas polidamas peple quene panthasile wyth maydens grekes anone redy began batayll harde sharpe menesteus adressid hym panthasile hym anon smote menesteus ground toke hys horse gaf hym one maydens cam dyomedes ayenst receyuyd hym gladly smote hym strongly torned vp doun fro hors toke fro dyomedes shelde fro hys necke delyueryd hit one maydens whan thelamon sawe dide suche appertyses armes adressid hym ayenst ayenst hym thelamon born doun ground ladde hym cyte diomedes cam rescows grete deffence escryed maydens smote amonge grekes suche sierte yre torned hem flight chassed hem sleyng betyng hem vnto tentes slayn hem yf diomedes gretly resisted hem mayntened stowr vnto nyght tht departed quene panthasilee retorned cyte wyth grete glorye kyng pryant resceyuyd grete ioye gaf many fayr iewellis ryche hym semed well shold avenge hym sorowes fought thus many tymes longe menelaus retorned fro kynge nycomedes brought ooste neptolonyus sone achilles otherwyse named pyrrus thys pirrus receyuyd grete glorye alle baron ooste aboue alle myrundones passyng ioyous helde hym lord desyueryd pirrus conduyte men armes made hym knyght hande noble thelamon prayd goddes gyue hym strength corage gyrdyng swerd wold gyue hym vyctorye honour avenge deth fader two prynces sette sporres golde kynge agamenon gaf hym alle armes achilles fader hys baghes iewellis newe knyght feste chyualerye grekes maad many dayes grete gladnesse ioye etc thynges cam day fyghtyng bataylles redy one side tho began batayll ryght hard pirrus wad armed propre armes fader recountrid polidamas comyng slayn hym wyth grete stroke swerd gaf hym kynge philemenis cam vpon delyueryd hym pirrus smote fro hors philemems lad hym away ne paphaghone rescowed hym grete trauayll amonge thynges quene pantasilee entred bataill maydens smote amonge myrundoues slewe many cam vpon kynge thelamon smote ground quene pantasilee gaf hym grete strook swerd tht bete hym doun erthe like wise maydens releuyd sette agayn horse smote among myrondones helde kynge phylomems grete dangier many slewe hurted hem whan pyrrus sawe men euyll entretyd escryed hem sayd oughte haue grete shame suffryd hem vaynquysshid woman lefte kynge phylemems deffende men ayenst mayde adressid quene panthasilee nyghe pyrrus reproched hym fader slayn hector trayson world ought renne vpon hym pyrrus grete sorowe thyse wordes adressid hym ayenst anone bare hym doun erthe anone releuyd hym assayllid panthasile hys swerd hym grete strength pyrrus remounted ayde hys myron doues cam batayll agamenon dyomedes menelaus menesteus duc atthenes peple dyde prynces baron amonge thynges kynge phylomems delyuered myrondones gaf grete thankyngys vnto quene panthasilee sayd haue ben ben slayn cam batayll alle troians tho began showre sharpe mortall recountrid pirrus glacon sone anthenor broder polidamas moder gaf hym grete stroke slewe hym fylle doun ded erthe adressid panthasilee vnto pyrrus bete doun eche erthe remoutyd anone began medle geder agayn cam vpon moche peple bothe partyes departyd polidamas avenge deth brother slewe day many grekes hurte dide moche armes panthasilee put grekes flyght cam rescows pirrus diomedes thelamon maad fledde abyde susteyne stour dide vnto nyght eche man wente hys place faught thus euery day moneth longe whiche tyme slayn ten thousand fyghtyng men bothe partyes panthasilee loste many maydens whan restyd moneth began batayll ryght sharpe assamble cam one ayenst pirrus panthasilee brake theyr speres oute fallyng pyrrus sore hurte tronchon spere abode wyth body wherfore crye arose gretly amonge grekes ran vpon panthasilee grete strengthe brake lase helme pirrus tht grete furour toke none hede wounde ne sette therby tronchon body assayllid strongly panthasilee tho helme broken wende haue smyten hym pirrus araught first gaf grete stroke wyth hys swerde cutte arme body wherof sayd panthasilee fyll doun dede erthe pirrus yet content smote body cuttid two peces anon grete effusion blood ran fro wounde fyll doun ded amonge peple toke hym vp leyde vpon shelde bare hym hys tente maydens panthasilee avenge deth quene smote amonge myrondoues grete fureur slewe many hurte hit prouffited lytill troians afewe ayenste grete multitude grekes ther slayn troye day batayll ten thousand men withdrewe hem cyte saue hem self shette closid faste gate entencion yssu oute batayll ayenst theyr enemyes etc phow anthenor eneas spack geder amonge delyuere cyte vnto grekes trayson dyde hit vnder symylacion pea kyng pryant agayn said hem som bastardis grete rude wordes troians moche grete sorowe whan sawe hem myschef ffor hope haue ony socours ony place contended thynge kepe well cyte garnyssh hem well wyth vytayll ffor fered ne dredde hem nought ony assault amonge thynges grekes wold haue caste dogges body panthasilee moche hadd slayn many noble men grece pyrrus agayn sayd hyt honour worshyppe nob esse fynably concluded caste hit stagne nyghe cyte anchyses wyth hys sone eneas anthenor sone polidamas wente counceill gyder aduyse myght haue theyr lyues sauyd ayenst grekes theyr goodes rather fayle hereof wold betraye cyte concluded shold speke kynge pryant counseylle hym take pea poyntement wyth grekes restoryng helayne husbond domage parys dide yle cetharys yf kynge pryant ben happy haue doon plesid grekes begynnyng sauyd lyf hys wyues lyf hys child sauyd cyte cytezeyns eschewid myschyeuys cam afterward therfore saie men prouerbe concordes pea sone taken ben good ffor hit hard thynge repease suche maner domages hym tht hath avauntage warre ffor wyth grete payne wold grekes haue ben content tho aboue wyth offres moche suffred many hurtes domages tofore troye ffor semed well poynt destroye cyte inhabytautes whan forsayd named traytours spake mater thende vnder colour pea myght betraye cyte yf wyse myght saue theyr lyues wente hem fore kynge pryant amphymacus one bastard sone spake thys purpose tofore many noble men cyte anon kynge pryant hadd herde hem speke purchasyng pea wyth grekes thought sayd thys thynge grete felonye began syghe said wold aduysed take counceyll fyrs e sayd hym thus yf thou wo te oure counceyll vpon thys thynge take hede shall saye yf hit plese vse counceyll kynge sayd wold well theyr counceyll wold wete semed hem good sayd semeth yow good spack anthenor sayng kynge ye may dissymyle ye yowres ben envoluped wyth youre enemyes ben cyte desyryng deth destruccion ye may yssue ben moo fyfty kynges desire thynge destroye cyte yow dwelle therin ye may resiste ye dar open gate thus late v enclosid ought two euyll thynges chese lasse ylle therfore haue pea wyth grekes yf ye seme good shall rendre helayne menelaus husbond syn parys ded also restorre domage parys dyde grece rather shold suffre oure self put deth etc wordes arose vp amphymacus one bastard sone kynge pryant reprouyd strongly wordes anthenor sayd hym truste hope may lorde fader haue syn thou oughtest haue ferme corage vnto hym thys cyte see thus recreaunt oughtest lyue dye wyth v thou counceylle make pea wyth grekes oure grete dishonoure shame trewly fore kynge shall ther shall dye twenty thousand men thynge thou counceyllest kynge cometh trayson many iniuryous wordes sayd amphymacus anthenor eneas began refrayne hym sayng ye knowe well may hen forth goo batayll ayenst grekes dare open oure gate wherfore hit behoueth v fynde manyer haue pea wyth hem kynge pryant grete yre sayd anthenor eneas haue ye shame self speke ye dye sorowe ffor haue doon yet hetherto haue hyt counceyll anthenor whan thou retornest fro grece sente requyre exyone suster counceyllest thou shold sende parys grece endomage grekes neuer taken vpon haue meuyd warre ayenst ne hadd thy false counceyll haue ben whyche meuyd sende thether thou eneas ala whan sente wyth parys grece thou pryncypall counceyll parys shold rauysshe helayne brynge royame thou heel pest therto wyth thy persone yf thou woldest haue ben contrarye therto haue lettyd hit helayne neuer seen walles troye thys haue slayn chyldren haue doon moche domage hurte ye counceyll ayenst honour make pea wyth grekes haue cruelly destroyed certes counceyll fynysshith lyf grete sorowe dishonour etc wordes eenas strongly angry wrothe answerd kynge wordes sharpe poynant ynowhe departed anthenor kynge evyll contente whan goon kynge began wepe dredde shold delyuere cyte handes grekes whyche shold slee hym incontynent thoughte wold doo hem dye fyrste callyd hym amphymacus sayd hym ryght dere sone thy fader ought supporte eche vnto deth knowe certaynly anthenor eneas contenden slee v grekes delyuere cyte therfore hyt shold ylle doon make falle pytte haue maad redy fore er doo ony suche evyll shall telle manere morne even shall come counceyll thou shalt enbusshyd wyth inne shalt haue wyth good knyghtes whan shall comen thou shalt renne vpon hem slee hem amphymacus answerd vnto hym sayd wold doo wyth good wylle well ther moo thys counceyll kynge hys sone yet ther thynge secrete otherwhile knowen eneas knewe well trouthe thys thynge hyt knowen whome knewe hyt anone anthenor theyr conplices spack furth trayson cyte swore eche sayd yf wente counceyll kynge wold goo wyth grete companye men armes ffor eneas moste noble troye moste ryche nexte kynge beste lynage myght l compare kynge anthenor also ryche puyssant frendes cyte theyr trayson suche wold delyuere cyte handes enemyes alle lignage sholde haue theyr lyues theyr goodes sauyd herof toke good sewerte grekes amonge thynges kynge pryant sente anthenor eneas come counceyll performe thynge purposid cam agrete companye men armes therfore kynge sente amphymacus shold leue hys empryse daye folowyng kynge sente alle troians counceyll whan assemblid fore hym eneas stode vp amonested make pea grekes accorded saue kynge said hym eneas syre kynge werfore consentest thou thou thou shall trete pea shall make hyt magre whan kynge sawe contradiccon myght thynge auaylle leuer consente hym cause destruccon said eneas late hit made ye shall thynke hit may expedient pea shall holde hit agreable counceyll anthenor chosen goo grekes trete pea troians toke braunches palme syngne pea wente vpon walles cyte shewid sygne vnto grekes wihche shewyd well wolde entende pea anthenor aualed fro wallis late doun presented kynge agamenon kynge agamenon comysid werke kynge crete dyomedes vlixes thoo thynges thre kynges shold besoyne anthenor alle grekes promysid holde hyt agreable sware hyt vpon theyr lawe etc whan foure assembled anthenor replenesshid wyth barate promysed delyuere cyte trayson doo hit wylle playsir saue wold assure hym eneas theyr kynnysmen parentele wold chese eneas shold haue possession oute ony lo se thre kynges grece swore anthenor th wold doo holde sayd one thynge muste scerete vnto tyme hyt brought aboute thende kepe trayson secrete anthenor prayd grekes wold delyuere hym kynge cassilus moche auncyent man goo wyth hym troye thentente myght better beleuyd knewe wyll troians wete yf wold haue pea grekes also saye wyll desire grekes demanded anthenor body panthasile whiche grekes agreed hym gladly thynges anthenor kynge cassilyus entryd cyte dyde hyt knowen kyng comynge morn tymes kynge pryant assemblid alle troians answer anthenor whiche sayd kynge otherwyse founden makyng longe sermone couere wyth hys felonnye spack longe puyssance grekes theyr trouthe theyr promesses holden tryews maad lyyng fore cyte ben faythfully gouerned oute brekyng spake ffeblenes troians grete daungers inne thys concluded forthon hit prouffitable seke pea come therto sayd hyt coude yf gaf grete quantyte gold syluer vnto grekes restore grete domages loss hadd warre auysed kynge eche hym self employe hym thys thynge wyth oute ony sparynge moche sayd anthenor knowe thys tyme alle theyr wylle wolde ye wold late eneas goo wyth vnto knowe better theyr wylle thende beleuyd v better every man alowed wordes anthenor wente eneas vnto grekes wyth hem kynge cassilyus whan counceyll fynysshyd alle doon kynge pryant entryd hys chambre began wepe right strongly apperceyuyd well trayson playned sore deth hys sone also grete domage bare yet worste muste bye hys pea haue doon hym domage hurte gyue alle tresour longe tyme gadryd gyder become poure olde auncyent dayes yet sewre lyf muste nedes wyll shall betraye hym syde whan helayne knewe anthenor shold goo grekes prayd hym right effectuously wold make pea ayenst menelaus husbond wold haue pyte promysid wold doo power whan eneas anthenor comen ooste grekes treted theyr trayson wyth thre kynges grekes hadd comysyd maad pea helayne toke good sewerte theyr parlament grekes ordeyned dyomedes vlixes shold goo troye wente ther grete ioye whan herde theyr comyng theyr cyte wenyng troians haue pea moche desyred morn erly comandement kynge pryant alle troians assembled hys palays spake vlixes sayd grekes demanded two thynges wete restytucion theyr domages grete quantyte gold syluer also demanded amphymacus shold bannysshid ever oute cyte troye wyth oute ony truste euer come agayn thys purchasyd anthenor amphymacus moche contraryed hym afore hit grete paryll speke lyghtly tyme parturbacion sedicion alle assemblid parlament herde sodeynly meruaylous crye dyomedes vlixes hadd grete drede peple wold haue slayn said wold take two kynges stede amphymacus ende shold bannysshid alleway ther coude man knowe n wete whens noyse cam ne wherfore therfore departid euery man wente hys place etc anthenor drewe parte dyomedes vlixes speke felonnye sayd hym vlixes wherfore taryest thou longe delayest doo thou hast promysed anthenor answerd sayd goddes knowe eneas attende none thynge doo haue promysid yow ther meruayllous thynge enpessheth v shall saye yow hit certayn whan kynge ylyon fouded fyrst palays ylion cyte establisshid name pallas grete temple cyte whan hit redy made saue tour meruayllous thynge descendid fro heuen stack walle temple wyth grete aroter hyt hath ben tyll thys tyme none may bere hit away saue kepe hyt matere tree woode ther man knoweth woode ne hit maad goddesse pallas sente hyt theder gaf nto thys thynge grete vertue sayd thynge shall inne temple wythin cyte wythin wallis troians may lese theyr cyte ne kynges ne eyre thynge holdeth troians sewerte therfore may better kepe hyt thyng hath name palladyum moche goddesse pallas sente hit sayd dyomedes yf thynge suche vertue thou sayst lose oure payne sayd anthenor ought thynge esmaye eneas attended fulfylle promesse ffor haue late spoken preest kepeth hit thende delyuer hyt stelthe haue verray truste shall delyuere hit grete gold haue promysid hym assone shall haue hyt shall sende hit yow oute cyte shall performe thynge haue promysid yow er ye goo hen couere hyde oure werke shall goo vnto kynge pryant shall hym vnderstande haue spoke longe yow knowe quantyte gold ye demande hyt doon anthenor purposid phow trayttre anthenor bought preest palladyum gaf hyt vlixes horse brasse grekes brought temple pallas beyng full men armes cyte troye taken brente kynge p yant slayn etc whan dyomedes vlixes retorned oost anthenor wente hym vnto kynge pryant said hym shold assemble folk counceyll whan alle comen anthenor sayd hem come pea grekes muste nedes paye twenty thousand mar gold good poys moche syluer also honderd thousand quarter whete muste maad redy certayn terme whan haue shall sette sewrte holde pea wyth ony frawde malengyne ordeyned shold beleueyed whylis besy ther abowtes anthenor wente preest tht kepte palladyum whiche preest name thoant bare hym grete quantite gold two counceill anthenor sayd hym shold take gold wherof shold ryche hys lyf shold gyue hym palladyum noman shold knowe therof ffor haue sayd grete fere moche drede thou ony man shold knowe therof shall sende hit vlixes shall bere blame vpon hym euery man shall saye vlixes shall haue stolen hyt shall quyte therof bothe two etc thoant preest resisted longe wordes anthenor ende couetyse grete gold anthenor gaf hym consentyd shold take palladyum bere hyt away anthenor toke hyt anone sente hyt vnto vlixes nyght wy ranne amonge peple vlixes subtilite taken born awaye palladyum troye trayson thys preest louyd better covetyse betraye cyte leue gold gyuen hym certes hyt afoule vyce preest synne couetyse fewe haue ben fore thys tyme fewe ben yet yf ben attaynte therwyth wherof hyt grete pyte syn hyt auaryce moder vyces whilis troians gadryd gyder gold syluer put hyt temple mynerve kepe vnto tyme hyt alle assemblid hit playsid offre make sacrefyse theyr god appolyn whan hadd slayn many bestes sacrefyce put vpon awter hadd sette fyre brenne hit happend ther cam two meruayllis fyrste fyre wold alyghte ne brenne began make fyre ten tymes alway hyt quenchid myght neuer brenne sacrefyce seconde myracle meruaylle whan appoynted entraylles bestes theyr sacrefyce grete eygle descended fro ayer cryyng gretly toke wyth foot said entraylles bare hem shyppes grekes two thinges troians sore abasshid esmayed said goddes wroth wyth hem demanded cassandra thinges signefied sayd god appolyn wroth hem theffusion blood achylles shedde wherwith temple defowlid violid firste ye muste go fecche fyre sepulture achilles lighte sacrefyce ther hit shal quenche dide sacrefyce brente cleer second myracle sayd hem certayn trayson maad cyte wyth grekes whan grekes herde speke myracles demauded calcas hyt signefyed sayd hem tradicion cyte shold come shortly amonge thynges calcas crisis preest councellyd grekes shold make grete hors brasse muste grete myght holde hit thousand knyghtes armed sayd hyt playsir goddes hors made passyng wyse mayster apius who name synon maad hyt subtylly wyth oute forth man coude parceyue ne see entree ne yssue wythin hyt apperyd closid ther yssue whan wold etc whan hors full maad thousand knyghtes therin counseyll crysis prayed kynge pryant wold suffre thys hors entre cyte hit myght sette temple pallas moche sayd maad hyt hanour pallas vowe maad restytucion palladyum hadd doon taken oute temple etc amonge thynges prynces yet troye whan sawe kynge fowle shamefully trayted grekes wente oute troye toke theyr men kyng philemenus ladde moo hym two honderd fyfty men sixty maydens amazone lefte
