thousand cam wyth quene panthasile caryed bodye hem rood moche cam vnto theyr contre cam day grekes shold swete pea faynedly vpon playn felde vpon sayntuaryes kynge pryant yssued cyte peple sware eche partye holde pea fermly fro forthon dyomedes swore fyrste grekes whan broken pea treatid anthenor thyng made therfore mayntene forsworne colour therfore sayth proverbe swerith cawtele malicyously malice forswerith hym self diomedes sware lyke wyse kynges prynces grece kynge pryant troians swore good fayth knewe thynge grete trayson theyr othes thus maad kynge pryant delyueryd helayne menelaus husbond prayd hym kynges prynces grece wold pardone helayne wyth oute suffryng doon ony iniurye hurte promysid hym faynedly wold wronge prayd grekes myghte sette hors brasse wyth temple pallas ffor restytucion palladyum thende goddesse pallas myght aggreable retourne kynge pryant answerd therto eneas anthenor sayd hym hit shold well doon hit shold honour cyte hyt kynge pryant accorded hyt wyth euyll wyll grekes receyuyd gold siluer whete promysid sente hyt putte hit shyppis thynges wente maner procession deuocyon wyth theyr prestis began strength cordes drawe horse brasse vnto tofore gate cyte moche gate hyt myght entre cyte hit grete therfore brake walle cyte lengthe heyght suche wyse hyt entryd town troians receyuyd hyt wyth grete ioye custome fortune suche grete ioye endeth tristres sorowe troians maad ioye hors wherin closid theyr deth knewe nothynge hyt hors subtill man named synon bare keyes horse opene hyt whan troians aslepe restyd hem nyght assone yssued horse gaf token fyre feldes ende shold come cyte putte hyt alle destruccion day grekes fayneden goo vnto thenadon sayd wolde resseyve helayne sette saefte cause peple shold renne vpon grete evyllys hurtes fallen thus departyd porte troyes wyth saylles drawen vp cam fore sonne goyng doun thenedon troians grete oye whan sawe grekes departe sowped euenyng wyth grete gladnes grekes sone come thenedon armed euenyng wente hem stylly pryuely toward troye whan troians well sowped wente bedde slepe synon opend hors wente oute lyghte fyre shewyd hit oute anone oute delaye wayte entryd cyte gate broken brynge hors brasse thousand knyghtes yssued fonde troians slewe hem howsis slepte thought thinge thus entrid grekes cyte slewe men woman chyldren wyth oute sparyng ony toke fonde howses slewe many er hyt daye slayn moo twenty thousand pylled robbed temple crye aroose moche horryble slewe whan kynge pryant herde crye knewe anone eneas anthenor betrayed hym aroose anone hastely wente hym hys temple appolyn wythin hys palays esperance ne hope hys lyf knelid fo e hyghe awter cassandra fledde syde one ben oute witte temple mynerue wepyng demenyng grete sorowe noble woman abood styll palays wepynges teeris hyt cam morn grekes conduyte eneas anthenor open traytours vnto theyr cyte also theyr kynge lord cam entrid palays ylyon fonde deffence put deth fonde pyrrus entryd temple appolyne fonde kynge pryant abidyng deth ran vpon hym nakyd swerd seeyng eneas anthenor guyded hym slewe kynge pryant tofore hyghe awter whiche bebledd blood quene hecuba polixene fledde wyste neuer whyder goo happend mette eneas sayd hecuba hym grete fureur ha felon trayttre fro whens comen grete cruelte thou hast brought haue slayn kynge pryant hath doon moche good hath sette magnyfycence also hast betrayed contre thou born cyte thou oughtest kepe left late hit suffise refrayne thy corage haue pyte thys vnhappy polixene thende amonge many euyllis thou haste done thou mayst haue grace haue doon one good dede saue fro deth er grekes slee eneas meuyd pyte resseyuyd polixene hys garde putte secrete place amonge thynges kynge thelamon sette temple mynerue kepyng andrometha wyf hector cassandra fonde ylyon putte fyre cyte partyes brente noble cyte reseruyd howses trayttres whiche kepte reseruyd whan cyte troye brente kynge agamenon assemblid moste noble grece temple mynerue whan alle assemblid requyred two thynges one shold holde fayth throuthe trayttres shold take aduyse good manere departe proye cyte answere suche grekes wold hold fayth trayttres fyrst poynte second euery man shold brynge proye comyn departe eche man hys meryte deserte spake thelamon sayd shold brenne helayne whome moche hurte euyll comen many worthy kynges prynces deyd fore ther grete murmure vpon grete payne agamenon vlixes menelaus myght saue vlixes fayre langage said hem moche dyuerce thynges contente helayne shold haue harme agamenon dide moche reward doughter kynge pryant cassandra deliuerid hym whilis grekes helde yet parlament cam eneas anthenor aduertysed hem helenus alway blamed troians thempryse made ayenst grekes counceyllid put body achilles sepulture whiche wold haue gyuen houndes praid hem therfore wold saue lyf hit accorded agreed andrometha helenus prayd two sonnes hector whiche sauyd well pyrrus ther agaynst debated hit lityll ende agreed hyt child respited fureur ordeyned noble woman escaped fro deth shold goo whyder wold freely dwelle styll yf hit plesid thynges doon purposid departe troye grete tempeste began aryse tyme endured moneth hole fore myght goo see demanded grekes calcas cause enpesshement dured longe answerd puyssan e infernal yet oppesid theffusion blood achilles shedde temple appollyn loue polixene tappese goddes hit behoveth sacrefye polixene achilles deyde pyrrus enquyred dyligently polixene becomen cause deth fader ffor ther tydynge whether alyue ded agamenon demanded anthenor whiche said hym knewe wherof lyed yet make ende hys euyllis enquyred moche polixene founden pryson olde auncient towr putte inne wente theder drewe oute force armes presented vnto kynge agamenon whyche anone sente pyrrus whiche sente sepulcre achilles slayn ledde ther ne kynge ne prynce grete sorowe see fayr figure woman loste withoute deseruyd hyt delyuerid fro hande pyrrus yf calcas ben sayd alleway tempeste shold cesse vnto tyme ded whan fayre polixene fore sepulture achilles excusid moche humbly deth achilles said moche wroth sory deth kynges prynces grece suffryd dye ayenst iustyce wyth oute culpe trespaas well leuer haue deth lyve taken away slayn frendes whan fynysshid wordes pyrrus smote wyth swerd seeyng quene moder slewe cruelly cutte peces caste hem alle aboute sepulture fader whan hecuba quene sawe thus fayre doughter slayn fyll doun aswowne wente oute wytte becam madde began renne vacabonde araged assaylled wyth teth nayles myght come casted stone hurte many grekes toke force ladde yle stoned deth thus quene hecuba ended fynysshyd lyf grekes maad noble sepulture putte body therm sepulcre appereth yet yle vnto thys day etc pof dissencion meuyd palladyum betwene kyng thelamon vlixes eneas anthenor exylled troye grekes retorned adventure whhylis grekes soiourned yet troye myght departe grete tempeste destroyed cyte taken fonde good kynge thelamon made quarell fore kyng agamenon palladyum vlixes well deseruyd hit hadd many tymes socowryd oost vytayll also defendid hyt grete prowesse oost grekes ben danger haue ben loste ne ben sayd slayn kynge polmestor whome kynge pryant put polidorus hys sone slayn polidorus hadd brought grete tresour fonde vnto oost grekes also slayn kynge frygye brought goodes ooste aleggyd goten many royames seygnourye grece many vayllyances doon honour grekes sayd vlixes hym prowesse ne vaillyance onely subtylte fayre spekyng deceyue men hym haue goten v grete villonnye myght haue vaynquysshid troians armes haue vaynquysshid hem dysceyte barate etc wordes answerd vlixes sayd vayllyance wytte troians vaynquysshid yf hadd ben troians yet astate glorye cyte sayd thelamon certes palladyum neuer nquerid prowesse wytte grekes wyste neuer hit ne vertue hit whan dyde hem knowe therof fyrste dylygence dyde therto whan knewe cyte troye myght taken longe hyt wente secretly cyte dyde moche hyt delyueryd vnto toke cyte answerd thelamon iniuryously vlixes hym lyke wyse moche becam enemyes mortall eche thelamon manacyd vlyxes deth openly allewaye mater well discuted agamenon menelaus iugyd palladyum shold abyde wyth vlixes sayd maad iugement moche vlyxes hys fayre spekyng sauyd fro deth helayne thelamon wold haue hadd ded thys iugement myght contente moste grettest parte ooste sayd thelamon oughte better haue palladyum vlixes therfore thelamon sayd agamenon menelaus many iniuryous wordes sayd vnto hem wold theyr mortall enemye fro forth thys sayd cause agamenon menelaus vlixes helde hem alle thre nyghe gyder hadd allewaye wyth grete nombre multytude knyghtes hit happed morn erly thelamon founde slayn bedde woun many place body werof roos grete crye ooste maad grete sorowe gaf alle blame vnto thre kynges fore rehercyd pyrrus louyd strongly kynge thelamon sayd many iniuryous wordes vlixes vlyxes doubted hym next nyght folowyng men entryd shippes secretly wente see retourne homward lefte wyth dyomedes hys frende palladyum pyrrus dyde doo brenne body thelamon put asshes ryche vessell gold bere wyth hym hys contrey burye hyt honourably hate grete betwene pyrrus kynge agamenon hys broder anthenor maad pea day gaf dyner vnto alle noble grece dyde serue hem wyth many mete gaf fayre yeftes etc amonge thynges grekes reprochyd en hadd falsyd hys othe hyded polixene cause banysshi hym oute troye euer whan eneas sawe myght abyde prayd hem moche wold accorde agree myght haue two twenty shipp parys hym grece agreed hym requeste gaf hym foure monethes space repayre garnysshe lacked anthenor departed troye wyth hys good wylle ladd hym grete nombre troians hist ye telleth whether wold goo eneas hated strongly anthenor moche hym banysshyd oute troye grete sorowe anthenor well banysshid cause eneas assemblid troians sayd frendes brethern syn fortune hath put v state ben inne may lyue oute heed gouernour yf ye wyll counceyll ye shall chese anthenor make hym kynge ffor wyse ynowhe governe yow thys counceyll semed good troians sente anthenor retorned anone vnto assone come eneas assemblid grete nombre peple renne vpon hym myhhty troye troians prayed hym wold cesse syn warre fynysshid wold begynne hyt agayn sayd eneas shold spare one feloue trayttre hys grete felonnye hath causid dye polixene fayre doughter kynge pryant hym bannysshid oute troye shold haue counceyllid holpen yow nowe muste nedes leve yow eneas sayd moche troians bannysshid anthenor euer oute troye constrayned hym anone goo way towne etc anthenor entryd see wyth grete companye troians sayllyd ferre fylle amonge men warre pyrates see ranne vpon hym slewe many hys men hurte robbed pyllid shyppis ende anthenor escapyd saillid ferre arryuyd prouynce named gerbandye wherof kynge tetides lord kyng iuste man debonayre thys lande aryved anthenor fewe shyppis rested syde grete yle nyghe vnto porte sawe contre fayre puyssant woodes lande foutaynes edyffied cyte hym peple fortefyed hit wyth wallis good towrys whan troians knewe therof many wente theder dwellid anthenor cyte grewe strongly full peple anthenor governyd hym wysely lande well grace kynge tetydes seconde kynge hys royame named cyte cortirem erralum cassandra lefte troye grete sorowe grete myschyefs fallen frendes cessid wepe waylle whan demeuyd longe sorowe grekes demanded theyr estate theyr retournyng home whyche sayd shold suffre many paynes grete paryllis er come theyr contre sayd agamenon owne hows shold slee hym hyt happyd hym lyke cassandra deuysyd sayd kynge thelamon lefte two sone two quenes eldest named hermycides quene glausta quene thymyssa name anchisatus two child norysshid kynge theuter longe tyll grete bere armes amonge thynges agamenon menelaus demanded congye retorne theyr landes moste grete ooste gaf hem leue sore anoyed ffor moche ben taken suspecte deth thelamon vlixes whiche stolen away lyke theef wherfore shewyd well culpable deth thus two brethern putte hem see retorne home thus thentree wynter whan see moste dangerouse anone grekes entryd see fooles euyll aduysed doubtes see shippes alle charged laden wyth rychesses wherof hadd despoylled ryche cyte royame troye grete desyre hadd ben home theyr contre began retorne thus myddes wynter sette aparte alle danger paryllis whiche fyll vnto gretly whan hadd sayllyd foure dayes foure nyghtes fyfthe daye see egee aboute houre none cam grete tempeste supprysed sodaynly wyth grete rayne thonder wyth wynde grete wawes see casted shyppes see many brake theyr mastes alle rente theyr saylles whan nyght cam whyche longe derke shyppes lefte eche saillyng fore wynde one place many brente lyghtnyng thonder tht fyll vpon hem many drowned sonken see therm ded drowned grete rychesses troye loste oyleus ayax xxxii shippes companye shyppes brente perisshid hym self forse armes legges alle naked swymyng cam arryued lande swollen water dronken laye grete vpon gravell hopyng deth lyf anone cam lyke wyse sauyd swymmyng whiche disconfortid maleheurte vnhappynes myschief cam ayax moche drewe cassandra temple mynerue hyt happeth often tyme many punysshid synne trespace one man etc phow kynge naulus cetus sonne dide doo perysshe see many shippes grekes theyr retourne deth sone palamydes deth kynge agamenon thexyle dyomedes hys rapeell egee wyf etc thys tyme ther kynge grece named naulus moche ryche puyssaut hys royame stode vpon syde see grece toward south whyche see grete roches hyghe many montaygnes hylles sande whyche ryght peryllous kynge fader palamides slayn fore troye yet sone named cetus ther non grece ryche ne puissant kyng ther euyll peple coude ease greuyng anoyng whiche made said kynge naulus vnderstand sone kynge cetus palamides slayn batayll wy ran slayn couertly vlixes diomedes agamenon menelaus made contryued false lettre conteyned palamydes wold haue betrayd ooste grekes whylis emperour oost grete quantyte gold made lettre put side knyght slayn vlixes tretyd suche wyse wyth one secretayres palamydes grete money suche lettres conteyned secretarye thynduccion vlixes put money vnder heed palamides whilis slepte sone secretarie said vlixes doon vlixes slewe secretarye pryuely forth dide moche lettre cam handes grekes redde hit abasshid whan sawe wryting trayson teyned leye vnder heed wente anone tente fonde trouthe thinge wold haue ronne vpon palamides offred hym hymself deffende hit ayenst tht euer wold proue hit ther none durst fight ayenst hym vlixes dide moche hys fayre langage thynge repeasid semed hyt beste palamydes shold abyde dignyte thynge thus repeasid vlixes diomedes day dide palamydes vnderstand knewe pytte moche tresour wold parte shold goo nyght folowyng whan nyght come wente thre allone oute companye offryd palamydes goo doun pytte fyrste sayd wold folowe assone wythin two caste stone vpon hym many slew hym retorned tentes pryuely thynge sayd enuyous men kynge naulus cetus deth palamydes false kyng sone began strongly thynke myght avenge hem grekes knewe well grekes retourne herte wynter muste passe royame kyng naulus dide crye royame men shold make grete fyres euery nyght vpon montaigne stode see side dide thende whan grekes shold see fyre nyght shold come theder wenyng fynde good hauen yf cam shold fynde harde rockkes montaigne sande shold escape oute deth hit thus doon naulus deuysed ther well two honderd shippis grekes broken ayenst rokkes therin drowned whan shippis tht folowed herde noyse shippis broken crye drowned torned borde made see ward sauyd hem self escaped agamenon menelaus diomedes shall named cetus otherwyse callid pellus grete sorowe whan knewe agamenon escaped thoughte longe myght avenge hym whan shold come home descended owen lande dyde wryte lettre clytemestra wyf agamenon lettre conteyned certayn agamenon husbond espowsyd one doughters kynge pryant louyd strongly brought hym contre make quene put oute clitemestra doo slee therfore cetus aduertysed thende myght pourveye self clytemestra anone beleuyd lettres thanked cetus ynowhe thought wold avenge husboond clitemestra absence husbond louyd man named egystus whome hadd doughter named erygona loved loue gystus euer dyde husbond well comen lowe blood hyt custome woman doth mysse take one lasse value husbond tretyd egistus fyrst nyght agamenon shold lye shold renne vpon hym slee hym thinge doon like wise purposid agamenon slayn put erthe anone clitemestra toke husbond loue egystus kynge mychames agamenon thus slayn sone thys clytemestra named horestes yonge chylde whiche calcybus parent toke kepyng toke hym moder thende shold slee hym sente hym kynge crete ydumeus hys vncle grete ioye hym wyf tharasis also loved hym moche clitemestra doughter hadd moo child fayr yonge mayde thus cetus wryton clitemestra wyf agamenon lyke wise wrote wyf dyomedes named egee doughter kyng polymytes arsymens suster assandrus retorned fro troye wyth dyomedes broder lawe hit happed theyr retournyng descended lande kynge thelepus whyche euyll contente wente ayenst hem wyth grete companye men armes assayllid deffended hem strongly assandrus slewe many knyghtes thelepus wherof hadd grete sorowe angry toke grete spere adressid hym ayenst assandrus grete force smote doun erth slewe hym dyomedes avenge deth broder lawe slewe many knyghtes thelepus recoueryd body assandrus grete payne bare hyt shippe etc thus deyde assandrus hit reported thus egee hys suster hit sayd dyomydes husbond doon slee hym haue seygnourye archimens wherof assandrus one half ayenst suster egee thyse tydynges cetus wreton egee moche wroth angry diomedes husbond procured moche ayenst peple promysed wold resseyue dyomedes lord thus whan dyomedes retorned wyf ne hys folke wold resseyue hym banysshid hym oute contre archymens euer hit happyd hym arryued salamyne kynge theuter broder kynge thelamon thys kynge herde saye dyomedes culpable deth broder vlixes comanded dyomdes shold taken dyomedes herde hereof fledde then kynge demephon kynge athamas whan arryued theyr landes banysshid semblable manere arryued lande duc nestor whiche resseyuyd hem wyth grete ioye two kynges purposid goo theyr landes wyth men armes take vengeance peple duc nestor blamed hem therof counceillid shold sende fyrst amoneste warne hem resseyue theyr lordes promyse grete fraunchyses lybertees thus dyde nestor councellyd hyt longe theyr peple resseyuyd hem fore sayd etc whan eneas biden troye repayre hys shyppis suffryd many assault hys neyghbours wold haue taken proye alle remenant troians moche myghte abyde lenger hys terme assigned vnto hym grekes assemblid troians counceyllid shold sende fecche dyomedes kynge sayd hem wold come gladly moche putte contrey wyse hardy deffende sente seche dyomedes fonde hym cam gladly wyth good wyll fonde troians half assiegid neyghbours yet eneas presente appoynted hem batayll ayenst enemyes fought many dayes whiche diomedes dide many prowess slewe many theyr enemyes many toke many henge theuys fyfthe bataill dyde moche prowesse cam aboue enemyes alle vaynquyshid wherfore ther neuer none heer neyghbours ner none aboute durste assaylle troians dwellid pea amonge thynges nauye eneas redy entryd therm anchyses fader toke see many troians goo whyther goddes wold consente shold dwelle abyde fonde many peryllous aventures see ende sayllid see hellesponte sayllyd ferre aryved ytalye toscanne hys aventures arryuyd cartage ytalye wyll see hyt late hem rede virgyle eneydos shall fynde hyt whan egee wyf dyomedes knewe troians resseyuyd dyomedes hadd desconfyted enemyes doubted dyomedes wold take vengeance counceyllid wyth peple counceyll sente fecche hym cam wyth good wyll resseyuyd wyth grete ioye lyke wyse hadd exyled theyr lordes retourn fro troye callid hem home agayn euery man retorned hys seygnourye escaped fro paryllis see phow horrostes sone kyng agamenon toke cruell vengeance deth hys fader kynge vlixes many dyuerse adventure retorned seygnourye royame whan horrestes sone kynge agamenon foure twenty yere age kynge ydumeus nourysshid hym made hym knyghte maad grete feste newe chyualerye horrestes horrestes prayd hym wold helpe hym wyth peple take vengeance deth fader recouere lande kynge ydumeus delyuerd hym thousand knyghtes wyse hardy horrestes assemblid thousand many place toke way vnto mychames goyng thederward passid cyte trasem wherof kynge forensis lord halpe hym wyth thre honderd knyghtes moche hated egystus cause sayd egystus trouth plight hys doughter whyche lefte loue clytemestra wente horrestes make warre egistus whan sette forth theyr way hyt thentre moneth may whan cam fore mychames wyth inne cyte wold yelde hit vnto hym sette siege round aboute hit horestes answer goddes hym self shold take vengeance moder hys handes notwythstandyng closid cyte egisteus goon feche socours assamble knyghtes deffende cyte ayenst comyng horestes hys enemye instygacion counceyll clitemestra hys wyf anone horestes knewe therof sette grete nombre knyghtes wayte take hym retournyng maad cyte assayllid often tymes moche hit well garnysshid horestes toke hit wyth assault xv daye siege comysyd hys peple kepe yates thende none shold yssue ne entre wente hym palays ryall made take moder sette wre pryson toke dyde taken alle felte culpable deth fader rebell ayenst hym day egistus retournyd wyth hys socours fyll handes peple horestes tht slewe peple ke hym lyue brought hym horestes handes bounden behynde hym backe morn horestes dide moder clitemestra brought fore hym naked handes bounden assone sawe ran vpon naked swerd cutte two pappes slewe handes maad drawen feldes houndes ete deuowre byrdes dyde dispoylle egistus drawe hym thurgh cyte dide hange hym forke lyke wyse dyde alle culpable deth hys fader thus vengid horrestes deth good kynge agamenon fader etc menelaus grete paryllis see aryued crete wyth hym dame helayne hys wyf whan knewe deth hys broder vengeance sayd horrestes taken euyll contente wyth nevewe taken cruell vengeance moder came menelaus grettest lordes grece see helayne grekes suffrid many hurtes domages crete menelaus wente aryued poort michames sayd horrestes worthy kynge lord moche hadd taken cruell vengeance moder avenge thys tyrannye menelaus assemblid noble grece atthenes thende horestes shold declarid pryuyd seygnourye cruelte doon ayenst hys moder horestes excusid hym therof sayng doon goddes comanded hym avau ced hym due atthenes offryd horestes yf ther ony man wold proue horestes done well wold deffende hym none wold preue hit therfore horrestes assaylled restablisshyd hys seygnourye bare heuy herte vncle menelaus cause kynge ydumeus cam mychames maad pea betwene hem bothe horestes toke hermone doughter menelaus helayne wyf erigone doughter egistus clytemestra grete sorowe whan sawe horestes grete seygnourye henge strangled self amonge thynges vlixes cam crete wyth two marchautes shippes hyred ffor loste shippes alle inne pyrates robb ur see robbyd hym robbed hyt myshappid hym arryued lande kynge thelamon taken loste resydue goodes contre hanged hym industrye subtylte wytte escaped right poure aryuyd lande kynge naulus whiche hated hym deth sone palamydes alleway dide moche connyng witte escaped moche pourly cam aryued crete kynge ydumeus resseyuyd hym ioyously ynowh moche esmayed sawe hym poure demauded hym aduentures syn departed fro troye vlixes tolde hym longe many daungers meruaylles loste men grete rychesse brought fro troye kyng ydumeus pyte vlixes honoured hym moche longe wold abide hym whan departed gaf hym two shippes full suche thynge behoved goo alle hys contrey gaf hym goodes ynowhe prayd hym wold goo royame alcynous hys waye wold see hym gladly etc thus departed vlixes fro crete wente hym kyng alcynous wiche resseyuyd hym wyth grete ioye herde hym gladly speke herde vlixes tydynges penolope wyf many notable men requyred wold neuer entende man moche chaste certayn sone helde partye lande ayenst wyf cam vlixes thelamotus hys sone acertayned hym thinges tht trewe cause vlixes prayd alcynous wold accompanye hym vnto royame grete nombre knyghtes alcinous agreed hym gladly sayllid longe nyght aryued contre entryd cyte howses hys enemyes slewe morn day vlixes thus accompanied entrid palays resseyuyd kynge lord wyth grete ioye aboue penolope wyf grete ioye longe desired hym peple cam fro sydes ranne see hym lord gyuyng hym grete ryche yeftes thus vlixes moche honouryd exalted hys royame treted moche alcinous gaf doughter naufica maryage thelamotus sone grete solempnyte weddyng alcynous wente hym hys contre vlyxes abood royame grete pea pof feetes pyrrus syn hys retournyng fro troye horrestes sone agamenon slewe hym delphos rauysshyng hermone hys wyf moo aduentures etc pirrus sone achilles dyadamie doughter kynge lychomedes hys moder syde kynge lichomedes sone kynge achastus lyued yet tyme kynge achastus moche olde auncyent hated strongly pyrrus historye telleth wherfore ne cause hate cam kynge achastus put kynge peleus oute royame thesaylle sente hym exyle sette espyes many place slee pyrrus retourne fro troyes pirrus comyng fro troye passid many paryllis see caste see beste iewellis hadde arryuyd molose descended dide repayre shippis soiourned knewe kynge achastus sente kynge peleus grauntfader exyle fader achilles sette espyes slee hym hereof grete sorowe moche wroth kynge peleus wyste holde hym doubte two sone achastus one named philistenes menelapus fere yf fonde hym wold sle hym avisid hym olde auncyent ediffice half myle fro cyte thessaylle betwene see cyte olde closure wallis rockes aboute ther moo howses ther hadd ben tyme paste celiers vnder erthe wher men myght entre secretly hole apperyd lytyll busshes thornes etc place dwellid kynge peleus abydyng retornyng nevewe pyrrus troye myght avenge hym enemyes wente ofte tyme vpon ryuage see see yf hys nevewe myght come whan shyppis pyrrus repayred toke hys way toward thessaylle auenge hym kyng achastus doo thynge wysely sente thessayll two hys secretaryes one named cryspus adrastus wyse subtyll vnto hyghe myghty man cyte named assandrus tyme trewe frende hym kynge peleus haue hys aduyse wente theder whan herde speke assandrus retorned vnto pyrrus tolde hym founden anone pyrrus maad drawe vp theyr saylles saylled toward thessaylle grete tempeste arose see dured thre dayes fourth day arryued poort sepehadem half myle thessaylle nyghe vnto caue peleus helde hym pyrrus descended lande reste hym trauayll hadd see take ayer lande aduenture wente strayte caue peleus thornes busshes hyded hym hoole fyll ther inne fonde hys belefader peleus anone peleus knewe hys nevewe ffor moche resemblyd ryght well vnto fader achylles beclipte hym aboute necke kyssed hym exposyd vnto hym alle hys malehurte grete vnhappynesse wherof pyrrus grete sorowe wente vp wente hys shyppes cam tydynges philistenes menalipus sone kyng achastus comen hunte foreste fast pyrrus vnclothid hym dyde olde roobe broken rente toke swerd sayd peple shold abyde hym allone wold goo foreste ferre goon encountrid two brethern demanded hym fro whens cam whyder wold goo sayd grece retorned fro troye shyppe wold haue goon agayn contre tempeste see trauaillid ther wer well fyve honderd personnes alle ded ther man escaped allone grete adventure hadd dronken moche water see haue loste muste goo begge fro dore dore tyll come contre yf ye haue brought thys foreste ony thynge ete praye yow ye wyll gyue therof two brethern sayd hym shold abyde etc whylis spake thus gyder grete herte passyd fore menalapus put hym chasse lefte hys broder wyth pyrrus allone hyt happyd phylistenes alyght doun hys horse reste hym assone descended pyrrus ranne vpon hym wyth hys naked swerd hande slewe hym whan menalipus retorned pyrrus assayllid hym slewe hym thus slewe pyrrus two vncles brethern thetys moder achilles hys fader retorned encountrid chinaras houshold kyng achastus pirrus demanded kynge achastus answerd hym faste ferre fro then assone sayd pyrrus slewe hym wente agayn hys shyppis cladde hym precyouse robe retorned agayn vnto foreste mette wyth kynge achastus demanded hym sayd one sone kynge pryant troye prisonner pyrrus pirrus said kyng ensigned hym toward see kyng torned hym see thederward pyrrus drewe oute swerd wold haue slayn hym thetys present escryed hym knewe hym sayng ha ryght dere neuewe wolte thou doo wylte thou sle fader thou haste slayn two brethern thyne vncles thus sayng helde hym arme helde hys swerde pyrrus answerd kynge achastus thy fader hath exylid kynge peleus thyn husbond hath trespaste offended yf wole pardoune peleus hys maletalent euyll wylle wyll pardoue hym myn kynge achastus well content peleus cam fore hym pea made betwene hem whan retorned geder wyth good loue kynge achastus sayd auncyent feble may helpe self therfore wyll discharge charge governement thys royame haue loste shold haue governed hyt moche pirrus right dere nevewe nexte eyer sease hym therin peleus sayd gyue hym ryght tytle haue therin wyll pyrrus kynge comanded kynge achastus baron thesaylle shold make homage pyrrus kyng therof grete ioye dyde hit gladly thus pyrrus crowned kynge thessaylle taken redoubtyd kynge thessaylle grece ydumeus kynge crete deyde anone lefte two sone hym merion loarca loarca deyde sone hym merion made kynge thelamotus sone naufica hys wyf whiche named deyphebus amonge thynges kyng achastus dide burye two sone thesayll agrement pirrus hit happend whan pirrus thus enhaunsid highe seygnourye becam amorouse herimone doughter helayne wyf horestes dide moche rauysshid force brought thesayll toke wyf horestes passing sorouful thyng durste assaylle pirrus royame said yf myght lyue wold avenge hym tyme place hyt happyd pyrrus wente yle delphe thanke god appolyn thys hadd taken vengeance deth hys fader achylles lefte hys pallays andrometha wyf hector lityll sone said hector named laomedon lefte andrometha wyth chyld werkes wherof herimone euyll contente sente menelaus fader pyrrus alle lefte loue andrometha shold come theder leue thynge whilis pyrrus oute sle andrometha sone laomedon menelaus wente anone thessaylle doo thynge doughter requyred hym ran vpon andrometha whiche toke sone betwene armes ran cyte requyryng helpe peple ayenste menelaus wold slee chyld peple armed anone ran vpon menelaus dyde moche menelaus muste retorne contrey wyth oute doyng ony thynge whan horestes knewe pyrrus yle delphe wente theder assayllid pyrrus slewe hym wyth owen hande maad hym buryed anone horestes recoueryd hys wyf brought hys royame whan pyrrus ded peleus thetis toke andrometha wyth chyld pyrrus laomedon lytyll sone sente hem cyte molose andrometha delyueryd fayre sone whiche named achilleydes whiche whan grete crowned broder laomeden kyng royame thesaill wold loue hym troians shold frauchised sai historye suster kynge menon achilles slewe fore troye kyng pryant dyde burye byside troyllus sone sayd suster cam troye moche rychely arayed dyde open sepulcre broder toke bone chat fonde assone hem helde hem vanysshyd sodaynly away neuer man wyste became ne bone taken said sawe thys goddesse doughter goddesse phow thelagonus sone vlixes quene cyrces cam fynde hys fader vlixes slewe hym wetyng avysion cam sayd vlixes slepyng vlixes slepte nyght bedde meruayllous vysion hym semed sawe ymage meruayllo fourme fayrest euer seen desyred sore towche ymage wold haue enbraced ymage wold suffre hym wythdrewe afterward approchid demanded hym wylt thou answerd wyll conioyned geder may knowe flesshly said ymage thy requeste harde bytter ffor oure conionccion shall vnhappy ffor one v two shall deye hym semed ymage helde spere aboue heed pensell maad wyth fysshis moche subtylly sawe ymage wld goo sayd hym departyng signe signefieth ylle destruccion shall v two whan vlixes awaked meruayll thys dreme thoughte sore hyt myght signefye sente deuyns saages hys royame demanded wat hys vysion myght signefie whan lytyll taken hede therof said owen sone shold slee hym vlixes grete drede feer sone made hym taken kepte sewerly chese place ferre fro peple dwellyd wyth trewe frendes dyde fortefye place hyghe towres closid hit water round bowte ther myght man entre drawe bryge wyket made kepte man shold entre brought wyth hym hit happend vlixes whan retorned fro troye fortune brought hym yle circe dwellid whiche lady whyche knewe moche enchantements ony woman world arte helde vlixes nyghe yere vlixes gate sone whiche named thelagonus thus tyme vlixes dwellid place stronge thelagonus sone knewe yet fader whan cage bere armes demanded often tymes hys moder hys fader yf alyue dwellyd longe prayd sayd hym vlixes hys fader tolde hym dwellyd etc whan thelagonus ryght ioyous desired strongly see fader toke leue moder wente many iourneyes cam achaye whan knewe vlixes dwellid wente theder whan comen monday morenyng brygge stode kepte hyt diligently prayd hem wold late hym passe see vlixes wold agree hym manere prayd hem putte hym back felonsly rudely wherof ryght angry wroth ran vpon one gaf hym grete strook wyth fyste vpon canell necke fyll doun ded assayllyd caste hem doun brygge began crye moche lowde whan castell herde noyse ran armes cam assaylle thelagonus avauncyd hym one toke swerd hym dide moche lytyll slewe fyftene hurte hym many place crye grewe vlixes aroose vp doubtyng hyt thelamotus hys sone yssued oute pryson cam noyse darte hande whiche caste ayenst thelagonus whan sawe hys men slayn hurted hym lityll knewe thelagonus receyuyd darte caste hyt ayenst vlixes knewe smote sore betwene sydes hurted hym vnto deth fyll erthe spack wyth grete payne demaunded thelagonus ffor moche hys vysion cam hys mynde thelagonus demaunded syde spack hym answerd hym hyt vlixes began thelagonus make grettest sorowe world sayng ala caytyf come see fader lyue hym ioye haue slayn hym sone sayd soo fyll doun swowne whan hys herte cam hym agayn began rente gowne bete hys vysage wyth hys fystes fylle wepyng approchid hys fader said hym vnhappy thelagonus sone quene circe prayd goddes wold suffre hym dye wyth fader etc whan vlixes knewe hit hys sone reconforted hym self sente anone fecche thelamotus sone cam incontynent whyche wold haue slayn thelagonus auenge deth hys fader vlixes repeasid hym sayd hym broder prayd hem wold loue eche vlixes brought achaye lyuyd thre dayes sone buryed hym honourably thelamotus helde royame achaye fader helde wyth hym thelagonus nyghe yere half made hym knyght grete honour wold shold dwelle wyth hym moche moder wrote hym often tymes shold retorne contre dide moche departed wyth grete honour ffor hys broder dyde hym haue alle hym behoued way gaf hym many ryche yeftes departyd one wepyng teeres thus thelagonus retorned yle aulides vnto circe moder moche grete ioye comyng hit longe cyrces hys moder deyde thelagonus maad kynge thys yle wher lyved sixty yere grete prosperyte deyde thelamotus regned achaye sixty ten yere augmented encresid seygnourye strongly whan vlixes slayn foure score thryttene yere olde partye dare fynysshid hys book syege troye speketh theyr aduentures fore said wrote dictes greke hys booke conteyned fore wreton two bookes founde accordyng moste partye dare putte ende hys booke siege endured ten yere ten monethis twelue dayes grekes slayn siege fore troye eyghte honderd sixe thousand fyghtyng men troians defended hem ayenst grekes slayn sixe honderd sixe fyfty thousand fightyng men saith furthermore whan eneas departed troye excyle ladde wyth hym two honderd shippes anthenor ladde wyth hym fyue honderd troians eneas ladde remenant wyth hym etc thys recyteth dare hys booke laste ende whome moste noble kynges prynces one partye also slayn sayth hector prynce chyvalerye world slewe wyth hys hande good loyall fayte eyghtene kynges hys prowesse wyth oute malengyne wete kynge archylogus kynge protheselaus kynge patroclus kynge menon kyng prothenor kynge archymenus kyng polemon kyng epistropus kyng ecedyus kynge doccius kynge polixenus kyng phybus kynge anthypus kynge lenutus kynge polibetes kynge humerus kynge fumus kynge exampitus parys slewe palamydes emperour ooste grekes kynge achilles kynge ayax ayax parys slewe eche eneas slewe kyng amphymacus kynge nercus achylles slewe kynge cupemu kynge yponeus kynge plebeus kynge austerus kynge lymonyus kynge euforbius kynge menon kynge neptolonyus also slewe hector toke none hede hym troyllus myrondones enclosid vnarmed pyrrus sone achylles slewe quene panthasilee also slewe noble kynge pryant fonde vnarmed wyth oute deffence cruell tyrant slewe fayre mayde polixene beste manerd world dyomedes slewe kynge antypus kynge escorpus kynge prothenor kynge obtyneus etc thus ende book whyche haue translated myn auctor nyghe god hath gyuen connyng gyuen laude preysyng moche wrytyng penne worn myn hande wery stedfast myn eyen dimed ouermoche lokyng whit paper corage prone redy laboure hit hath ben age crepeth dayly febleth bodye also cause haue promysid dyuerce gentilmen frendes adresse hem hastely myght sayd book therfore haue practysed lerned grete charge dispense ordeyne said book prynte maner forme ye may see wreton penne ynke bokes ben thende euery man may haue attones ffor bookes storye named recule historyes troyes thus enpryntid ye see begonne oon day also fynysshid oon day whiche book haue presented sayd redoubtid lady fore sayd hath well acceptid hit largely rewarded wherfore beseche almyghty god rewarde euerlastyng blisse lyf prayng said grace shall rede book desdaigne symple rude werke nether replye agaynst sayyng mater towchyd book thauwh hyt acorde vnto translacon whiche haue wreton hit ffor dyuerce men haue made dyuerce bookes whiche poyntes acorde dictes dare homerus ffor dictes homerus grekes sayn wryten fauorably grekes gyue worship troians dare wryteth otherwyse doo also propre name hit wonder acorde ffor oon name thyse dayes haue dyuerce equyuocacions contrees dwlle alle acorde conclusion generall destruccion noble cyte troye deth many noble prynces kynges duke erles baron knyghtes comyn peple ruyne irreperable cyte neuer syn reedefyed whiche may ensample men duryng world dredefull ieopardous begynne warre hormes loss deth foloweth terfore thapostle saith wreton wreton doctryne whyche doctryne comyn wele beseche god maye taken suche place tyme shall moste nedefull encrecyng pea loue charyte whyche graunte v suffryd crucyfied rood tree saye alle amen charyte pergama flere volo fata danais data solo solo capta dolo capta redacta solo causa mali talis meretrix fuit exicialis femina letalis femina plenum mali si fueris lota si vita sequens bona tota si eris ignota non eris ab que nota passa prius paridem idis modo thesia pridem e factura fidem ne redeas idem rumor de veteri faciet ventura timeri cras poterunt fieri turpia sicut heri scena quid euadis morti qui cetera tradis cur tu non cladis concia clade cadis femina digna mori reamatur amore priori reddita victori deliciis que thori
